Component: Split Text

Installation:
npm install gsap @gsap/react

Usage:
1import SplitText from "./SplitText";
2
3const handleAnimationComplete = () => {
4  console.log('All letters have animated!');
5};
6
7<SplitText
8  text="Hello, you!"
9  className="text-2xl font-semibold text-center"
10  delay={50}
11  duration={1.25}
12  ease="power3.out"
13  splitType="chars"
14  from={{ opacity: 0, y: 40 }}
15  to={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
16  threshold={0.1}
17  rootMargin="-100px"
18  textAlign="center"
19  onLetterAnimationComplete={handleAnimationComplete}
20  showCallback
21/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4import { SplitText as GSAPSplitText } from 'gsap/SplitText';
5import { useGSAP } from '@gsap/react';
6
7gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger, GSAPSplitText, useGSAP);
8
9const SplitText = ({
10  text,
11  className = '',
12  delay = 50,
13  duration = 1.25,
14  ease = 'power3.out',
15  splitType = 'chars',
16  from = { opacity: 0, y: 40 },
17  to = { opacity: 1, y: 0 },
18  threshold = 0.1,
19  rootMargin = '-100px',
20  textAlign = 'center',
21  tag = 'p',
22  onLetterAnimationComplete
23}) => {
24  const ref = useRef(null);
25  const animationCompletedRef = useRef(false);
26  const onCompleteRef = useRef(onLetterAnimationComplete);
27  const [fontsLoaded, setFontsLoaded] = useState(false);
28
29  // Keep callback ref updated
30  useEffect(() => {
31    onCompleteRef.current = onLetterAnimationComplete;
32  }, [onLetterAnimationComplete]);
33
34  useEffect(() => {
35    if (document.fonts.status === 'loaded') {
36      setFontsLoaded(true);
37    } else {
38      document.fonts.ready.then(() => {
39        setFontsLoaded(true);
40      });
41    }
42  }, []);
43
44  useGSAP(
45    () => {
46      if (!ref.current || !text || !fontsLoaded) return;
47      // Prevent re-animation if already completed
48      if (animationCompletedRef.current) return;
49      const el = ref.current;
50
51      if (el._rbsplitInstance) {
52        try {
53          el._rbsplitInstance.revert();
54        } catch (_) {
55          /* noop */
56        }
57        el._rbsplitInstance = null;
58      }
59
60      const startPct = (1 - threshold) * 100;
61      const marginMatch = /^(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)(px|em|rem|%)?$/.exec(rootMargin);
62      const marginValue = marginMatch ? parseFloat(marginMatch[1]) : 0;
63      const marginUnit = marginMatch ? marginMatch[2] || 'px' : 'px';
64      const sign =
65        marginValue === 0
66          ? ''
67          : marginValue < 0
68            ? `-=${Math.abs(marginValue)}${marginUnit}`
69            : `+=${marginValue}${marginUnit}`;
70      const start = `top ${startPct}%${sign}`;
71
72      let targets;
73      const assignTargets = self => {
74        if (splitType.includes('chars') && self.chars.length) targets = self.chars;
75        if (!targets && splitType.includes('words') && self.words.length) targets = self.words;
76        if (!targets && splitType.includes('lines') && self.lines.length) targets = self.lines;
77        if (!targets) targets = self.chars || self.words || self.lines;
78      };
79
80      const splitInstance = new GSAPSplitText(el, {
81        type: splitType,
82        smartWrap: true,
83        autoSplit: splitType === 'lines',
84        linesClass: 'split-line',
85        wordsClass: 'split-word',
86        charsClass: 'split-char',
87        reduceWhiteSpace: false,
88        onSplit: self => {
89          assignTargets(self);
90          const tween = gsap.fromTo(
91            targets,
92            { ...from },
93            {
94              ...to,
95              duration,
96              ease,
97              stagger: delay / 1000,
98              scrollTrigger: {
99                trigger: el,
100                start,
101                once: true,
102                fastScrollEnd: true,
103                anticipatePin: 0.4
104              },
105              onComplete: () => {
106                animationCompletedRef.current = true;
107                onCompleteRef.current?.();
108              },
109              willChange: 'transform, opacity',
110              force3D: true
111            }
112          );
113          return tween;
114        }
115      });
116
117      el._rbsplitInstance = splitInstance;
118
119      return () => {
120        ScrollTrigger.getAll().forEach(st => {
121          if (st.trigger === el) st.kill();
122        });
123        try {
124          splitInstance.revert();
125        } catch (_) {
126          /* noop */
127        }
128        el._rbsplitInstance = null;
129      };
130    },
131    {
132      dependencies: [
133        text,
134        delay,
135        duration,
136        ease,
137        splitType,
138        JSON.stringify(from),
139        JSON.stringify(to),
140        threshold,
141        rootMargin,
142        fontsLoaded
143      ],
144      scope: ref
145    }
146  );
147
148  const renderTag = () => {
149    const style = {
150      textAlign,
151      overflow: 'hidden',
152      display: 'inline-block',
153      whiteSpace: 'normal',
154      wordWrap: 'break-word',
155      willChange: 'transform, opacity'
156    };
157    const classes = `split-parent ${className}`;
158    const Tag = tag || 'p';
159
160    return (
161      <Tag ref={ref} style={style} className={classes}>
162        {text}
163      </Tag>
164    );
165  };
166  return renderTag();
167};
168
169export default SplitText;
170

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Blur Text

Installation:
npm install motion

Usage:
1import BlurText from "./BlurText";
2
3const handleAnimationComplete = () => {
4  console.log('Animation completed!');
5};
6
7<BlurText
8  text="Isn't this so cool?!"
9  delay={200}
10  animateBy="words"
11  direction="top"
12  onAnimationComplete={handleAnimationComplete}
13  className="text-2xl mb-8"
14/>

Code:
1import { motion } from 'motion/react';
2import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useMemo } from 'react';
3
4const buildKeyframes = (from, steps) => {
5  const keys = new Set([...Object.keys(from), ...steps.flatMap(s => Object.keys(s))]);
6
7  const keyframes = {};
8  keys.forEach(k => {
9    keyframes[k] = [from[k], ...steps.map(s => s[k])];
10  });
11  return keyframes;
12};
13
14const BlurText = ({
15  text = '',
16  delay = 200,
17  className = '',
18  animateBy = 'words',
19  direction = 'top',
20  threshold = 0.1,
21  rootMargin = '0px',
22  animationFrom,
23  animationTo,
24  easing = t => t,
25  onAnimationComplete,
26  stepDuration = 0.35
27}) => {
28  const elements = animateBy === 'words' ? text.split(' ') : text.split('');
29  const [inView, setInView] = useState(false);
30  const ref = useRef(null);
31
32  useEffect(() => {
33    if (!ref.current) return;
34    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
35      ([entry]) => {
36        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
37          setInView(true);
38          observer.unobserve(ref.current);
39        }
40      },
41      { threshold, rootMargin }
42    );
43    observer.observe(ref.current);
44    return () => observer.disconnect();
45  }, [threshold, rootMargin]);
46
47  const defaultFrom = useMemo(
48    () =>
49      direction === 'top' ? { filter: 'blur(10px)', opacity: 0, y: -50 } : { filter: 'blur(10px)', opacity: 0, y: 50 },
50    [direction]
51  );
52
53  const defaultTo = useMemo(
54    () => [
55      {
56        filter: 'blur(5px)',
57        opacity: 0.5,
58        y: direction === 'top' ? 5 : -5
59      },
60      { filter: 'blur(0px)', opacity: 1, y: 0 }
61    ],
62    [direction]
63  );
64
65  const fromSnapshot = animationFrom ?? defaultFrom;
66  const toSnapshots = animationTo ?? defaultTo;
67
68  const stepCount = toSnapshots.length + 1;
69  const totalDuration = stepDuration * (stepCount - 1);
70  const times = Array.from({ length: stepCount }, (_, i) => (stepCount === 1 ? 0 : i / (stepCount - 1)));
71
72  return (
73    <p ref={ref} className={className} style={{ display: 'flex', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
74      {elements.map((segment, index) => {
75        const animateKeyframes = buildKeyframes(fromSnapshot, toSnapshots);
76
77        const spanTransition = {
78          duration: totalDuration,
79          times,
80          delay: (index * delay) / 1000
81        };
82        spanTransition.ease = easing;
83
84        return (
85          <motion.span
86            className="inline-block will-change-[transform,filter,opacity]"
87            key={index}
88            initial={fromSnapshot}
89            animate={inView ? animateKeyframes : fromSnapshot}
90            transition={spanTransition}
91            onAnimationComplete={index === elements.length - 1 ? onAnimationComplete : undefined}
92          >
93            {segment === ' ' ? '\u00A0' : segment}
94            {animateBy === 'words' && index < elements.length - 1 && '\u00A0'}
95          </motion.span>
96        );
97      })}
98    </p>
99  );
100};
101
102export default BlurText;
103

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Circular Text

Installation:
npm install motion

Usage:
1import CircularText from './CircularText';
2  
3<CircularText
4  text="REACT*BITS*COMPONENTS*"
5  onHover="speedUp"
6  spinDuration={20}
7  className="custom-class"
8/>

Code:
1import { useEffect } from 'react';
2import { motion, useAnimation, useMotionValue } from 'motion/react';
3
4import './CircularText.css';
5
6const getRotationTransition = (duration, from, loop = true) => ({
7  from,
8  to: from + 360,
9  ease: 'linear',
10  duration,
11  type: 'tween',
12  repeat: loop ? Infinity : 0
13});
14
15const getTransition = (duration, from) => ({
16  rotate: getRotationTransition(duration, from),
17  scale: {
18    type: 'spring',
19    damping: 20,
20    stiffness: 300
21  }
22});
23
24const CircularText = ({ text, spinDuration = 20, onHover = 'speedUp', className = '' }) => {
25  const letters = Array.from(text);
26  const controls = useAnimation();
27  const rotation = useMotionValue(0);
28
29  useEffect(() => {
30    const start = rotation.get();
31    controls.start({
32      rotate: start + 360,
33      scale: 1,
34      transition: getTransition(spinDuration, start)
35    });
36  }, [spinDuration, text, onHover, controls, rotation]);
37
38  const handleHoverStart = () => {
39    const start = rotation.get();
40    console.log('CircularText mounted with text:', text);
41    if (!onHover) return;
42
43    let transitionConfig;
44    let scaleVal = 1;
45
46    switch (onHover) {
47      case 'slowDown':
48        transitionConfig = getTransition(spinDuration * 2, start);
49        break;
50      case 'speedUp':
51        transitionConfig = getTransition(spinDuration / 4, start);
52        break;
53      case 'pause':
54        transitionConfig = {
55          rotate: { type: 'spring', damping: 20, stiffness: 300 },
56          scale: { type: 'spring', damping: 20, stiffness: 300 }
57        };
58        scaleVal = 1;
59        break;
60      case 'goBonkers':
61        transitionConfig = getTransition(spinDuration / 20, start);
62        scaleVal = 0.8;
63        break;
64      default:
65        transitionConfig = getTransition(spinDuration, start);
66    }
67
68    controls.start({
69      rotate: start + 360,
70      scale: scaleVal,
71      transition: transitionConfig
72    });
73  };
74
75  const handleHoverEnd = () => {
76    const start = rotation.get();
77    controls.start({
78      rotate: start + 360,
79      scale: 1,
80      transition: getTransition(spinDuration, start)
81    });
82  };
83
84  return (
85    <motion.div
86      className={`circular-text ${className}`}
87      style={{ rotate: rotation }}
88      initial={{ rotate: 0 }}
89      animate={controls}
90      onMouseEnter={handleHoverStart}
91      onMouseLeave={handleHoverEnd}
92    >
93      {letters.map((letter, i) => {
94        const rotationDeg = (360 / letters.length) * i;
95        const factor = Math.PI / letters.length;
96        const x = factor * i;
97        const y = factor * i;
98        const transform = `rotateZ(${rotationDeg}deg) translate3d(${x}px, ${y}px, 0)`;
99
100        return (
101          <span key={i} style={{ transform, WebkitTransform: transform }}>
102            {letter}
103          </span>
104        );
105      })}
106    </motion.div>
107  );
108};
109
110export default CircularText;
111

Extra Config/Code:
1.circular-text {
2  margin: 0 auto;
3  border-radius: 50%;
4  width: 200px;
5  position: relative;
6  height: 200px;
7  font-weight: bold;
8  color: #fff;
9  font-weight: 900;
10  text-align: center;
11  cursor: pointer;
12  transform-origin: 50% 50%;
13  -webkit-transform-origin: 50% 50%;
14}
15
16.circular-text span {
17  position: absolute;
18  display: inline-block;
19  left: 0;
20  right: 0;
21  top: 0;
22  bottom: 0;
23  font-size: 24px;
24  transition: all 0.5s cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0, 1);
25}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Text Type

Installation:
npm install gsap

Usage:
1import TextType from './TextType';
2
3<TextType 
4  text={["Text typing effect", "for your websites", "Happy coding!"]}
5  typingSpeed={75}
6  pauseDuration={1500}
7  showCursor
8  cursorCharacter="_"
9  texts={["Welcome to React Bits! Good to see you!","Build some amazing experiences!"]}
10  deletingSpeed={50}
11  variableSpeedEnabled={false}
12  variableSpeedMin={60}
13  variableSpeedMax={120}
14  cursorBlinkDuration={0.5}
15/>

Code:
1'use client';
2
3import { useEffect, useRef, useState, createElement, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
4import { gsap } from 'gsap';
5import './TextType.css';
6
7const TextType = ({
8  text,
9  as: Component = 'div',
10  typingSpeed = 50,
11  initialDelay = 0,
12  pauseDuration = 2000,
13  deletingSpeed = 30,
14  loop = true,
15  className = '',
16  showCursor = true,
17  hideCursorWhileTyping = false,
18  cursorCharacter = '|',
19  cursorClassName = '',
20  cursorBlinkDuration = 0.5,
21  textColors = [],
22  variableSpeed,
23  onSentenceComplete,
24  startOnVisible = false,
25  reverseMode = false,
26  ...props
27}) => {
28  const [displayedText, setDisplayedText] = useState('');
29  const [currentCharIndex, setCurrentCharIndex] = useState(0);
30  const [isDeleting, setIsDeleting] = useState(false);
31  const [currentTextIndex, setCurrentTextIndex] = useState(0);
32  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(!startOnVisible);
33  const cursorRef = useRef(null);
34  const containerRef = useRef(null);
35
36  const textArray = useMemo(() => (Array.isArray(text) ? text : [text]), [text]);
37
38  const getRandomSpeed = useCallback(() => {
39    if (!variableSpeed) return typingSpeed;
40    const { min, max } = variableSpeed;
41    return Math.random() * (max - min) + min;
42  }, [variableSpeed, typingSpeed]);
43
44  const getCurrentTextColor = () => {
45    if (textColors.length === 0) return 'inherit';
46    return textColors[currentTextIndex % textColors.length];
47  };
48
49  useEffect(() => {
50    if (!startOnVisible || !containerRef.current) return;
51
52    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
53      entries => {
54        entries.forEach(entry => {
55          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
56            setIsVisible(true);
57          }
58        });
59      },
60      { threshold: 0.1 }
61    );
62
63    observer.observe(containerRef.current);
64    return () => observer.disconnect();
65  }, [startOnVisible]);
66
67  useEffect(() => {
68    if (showCursor && cursorRef.current) {
69      gsap.set(cursorRef.current, { opacity: 1 });
70      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, {
71        opacity: 0,
72        duration: cursorBlinkDuration,
73        repeat: -1,
74        yoyo: true,
75        ease: 'power2.inOut'
76      });
77    }
78  }, [showCursor, cursorBlinkDuration]);
79
80  useEffect(() => {
81    if (!isVisible) return;
82
83    let timeout;
84    const currentText = textArray[currentTextIndex];
85    const processedText = reverseMode ? currentText.split('').reverse().join('') : currentText;
86
87    const executeTypingAnimation = () => {
88      if (isDeleting) {
89        if (displayedText === '') {
90          setIsDeleting(false);
91          if (currentTextIndex === textArray.length - 1 && !loop) {
92            return;
93          }
94
95          if (onSentenceComplete) {
96            onSentenceComplete(textArray[currentTextIndex], currentTextIndex);
97          }
98
99          setCurrentTextIndex(prev => (prev + 1) % textArray.length);
100          setCurrentCharIndex(0);
101          timeout = setTimeout(() => {}, pauseDuration);
102        } else {
103          timeout = setTimeout(() => {
104            setDisplayedText(prev => prev.slice(0, -1));
105          }, deletingSpeed);
106        }
107      } else {
108        if (currentCharIndex < processedText.length) {
109          timeout = setTimeout(
110            () => {
111              setDisplayedText(prev => prev + processedText[currentCharIndex]);
112              setCurrentCharIndex(prev => prev + 1);
113            },
114            variableSpeed ? getRandomSpeed() : typingSpeed
115          );
116        } else if (textArray.length >= 1) {
117          if (!loop && currentTextIndex === textArray.length - 1) return;
118          timeout = setTimeout(() => {
119            setIsDeleting(true);
120          }, pauseDuration);
121        }
122      }
123    };
124
125    if (currentCharIndex === 0 && !isDeleting && displayedText === '') {
126      timeout = setTimeout(executeTypingAnimation, initialDelay);
127    } else {
128      executeTypingAnimation();
129    }
130
131    return () => clearTimeout(timeout);
132    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
133  }, [
134    currentCharIndex,
135    displayedText,
136    isDeleting,
137    typingSpeed,
138    deletingSpeed,
139    pauseDuration,
140    textArray,
141    currentTextIndex,
142    loop,
143    initialDelay,
144    isVisible,
145    reverseMode,
146    variableSpeed,
147    onSentenceComplete
148  ]);
149
150  const shouldHideCursor =
151    hideCursorWhileTyping && (currentCharIndex < textArray[currentTextIndex].length || isDeleting);
152
153  return createElement(
154    Component,
155    {
156      ref: containerRef,
157      className: `text-type ${className}`,
158      ...props
159    },
160    <span className="text-type__content" style={{ color: getCurrentTextColor() || 'inherit' }}>
161      {displayedText}
162    </span>,
163    showCursor && (
164      <span
165        ref={cursorRef}
166        className={`text-type__cursor ${cursorClassName} ${shouldHideCursor ? 'text-type__cursor--hidden' : ''}`}
167      >
168        {cursorCharacter}
169      </span>
170    )
171  );
172};
173
174export default TextType;
175

Extra Config/Code:
1.text-type {
2  display: inline-block;
3  white-space: pre-wrap;
4}
5
6.text-type__cursor {
7  margin-left: 0.25rem;
8  display: inline-block;
9  opacity: 1;
10}
11
12.text-type__cursor--hidden {
13  display: none;
14}
15

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Shuffle

Installation:
npm install gsap @gsap/react

Usage:
1import Shuffle from './Shuffle';
2
3<Shuffle
4  text="Hello World"
5  shuffleDirection="right"
6  duration={0.35}
7  animationMode="evenodd"
8  shuffleTimes={1}
9  ease="power3.out"
10  stagger={0.03}
11  threshold={0.1}
12  triggerOnce={true}
13  triggerOnHover
14  respectReducedMotion={true}
15  loop={false}
16  loopDelay={0}
17/>

Code:
1import React, { useRef, useEffect, useState, useMemo } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4import { SplitText as GSAPSplitText } from 'gsap/SplitText';
5import { useGSAP } from '@gsap/react';
6import './Shuffle.css';
7
8gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger, GSAPSplitText, useGSAP);
9
10const Shuffle = ({
11  text,
12  className = '',
13  style = {},
14  shuffleDirection = 'right',
15  duration = 0.35,
16  maxDelay = 0,
17  ease = 'power3.out',
18  threshold = 0.1,
19  rootMargin = '-100px',
20  tag = 'p',
21  textAlign = 'center',
22  onShuffleComplete,
23  shuffleTimes = 1,
24  animationMode = 'evenodd',
25  loop = false,
26  loopDelay = 0,
27  stagger = 0.03,
28  scrambleCharset = '',
29  colorFrom,
30  colorTo,
31  triggerOnce = true,
32  respectReducedMotion = true,
33  triggerOnHover = true
34}) => {
35  const ref = useRef(null);
36  const [fontsLoaded, setFontsLoaded] = useState(false);
37  const [ready, setReady] = useState(false);
38
39  const splitRef = useRef(null);
40  const wrappersRef = useRef([]);
41  const tlRef = useRef(null);
42  const playingRef = useRef(false);
43  const hoverHandlerRef = useRef(null);
44
45  useEffect(() => {
46    if ('fonts' in document) {
47      if (document.fonts.status === 'loaded') setFontsLoaded(true);
48      else document.fonts.ready.then(() => setFontsLoaded(true));
49    } else setFontsLoaded(true);
50  }, []);
51
52  const scrollTriggerStart = useMemo(() => {
53    const startPct = (1 - threshold) * 100;
54    const mm = /^(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)(px|em|rem|%)?$/.exec(rootMargin || '');
55    const mv = mm ? parseFloat(mm[1]) : 0;
56    const mu = mm ? mm[2] || 'px' : 'px';
57    const sign = mv === 0 ? '' : mv < 0 ? `-=${Math.abs(mv)}${mu}` : `+=${mv}${mu}`;
58    return `top ${startPct}%${sign}`;
59  }, [threshold, rootMargin]);
60
61  useGSAP(
62    () => {
63      if (!ref.current || !text || !fontsLoaded) return;
64      if (respectReducedMotion && window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches) {
65        setReady(true);
66        onShuffleComplete?.();
67        return;
68      }
69
70      const el = ref.current;
71
72      const start = scrollTriggerStart;
73
74      const removeHover = () => {
75        if (hoverHandlerRef.current && ref.current) {
76          ref.current.removeEventListener('mouseenter', hoverHandlerRef.current);
77          hoverHandlerRef.current = null;
78        }
79      };
80
81      const teardown = () => {
82        if (tlRef.current) {
83          tlRef.current.kill();
84          tlRef.current = null;
85        }
86        if (wrappersRef.current.length) {
87          wrappersRef.current.forEach(wrap => {
88            const inner = wrap.firstElementChild;
89            const orig = inner?.querySelector('[data-orig="1"]');
90            if (orig && wrap.parentNode) wrap.parentNode.replaceChild(orig, wrap);
91          });
92          wrappersRef.current = [];
93        }
94        try {
95          splitRef.current?.revert();
96        } catch {
97          /* noop */
98        }
99        splitRef.current = null;
100        playingRef.current = false;
101      };
102
103      const build = () => {
104        teardown();
105
106        splitRef.current = new GSAPSplitText(el, {
107          type: 'chars',
108          charsClass: 'shuffle-char',
109          wordsClass: 'shuffle-word',
110          linesClass: 'shuffle-line',
111          smartWrap: true,
112          reduceWhiteSpace: false
113        });
114
115        const chars = splitRef.current.chars || [];
116        wrappersRef.current = [];
117
118        const rolls = Math.max(1, Math.floor(shuffleTimes));
119        const rand = set => set.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * set.length)) || '';
120
121        chars.forEach(ch => {
122          const parent = ch.parentElement;
123          if (!parent) return;
124
125          const w = ch.getBoundingClientRect().width;
126          const h = ch.getBoundingClientRect().height;
127          if (!w) return;
128
129          const wrap = document.createElement('span');
130          Object.assign(wrap.style, {
131            display: 'inline-block',
132            overflow: 'hidden',
133            width: w + 'px',
134            height: shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down' ? h + 'px' : 'auto',
135            verticalAlign: 'bottom'
136          });
137
138          const inner = document.createElement('span');
139          Object.assign(inner.style, {
140            display: 'inline-block',
141            whiteSpace: shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down' ? 'normal' : 'nowrap',
142            willChange: 'transform'
143          });
144
145          parent.insertBefore(wrap, ch);
146          wrap.appendChild(inner);
147
148          const firstOrig = ch.cloneNode(true);
149          Object.assign(firstOrig.style, {
150            display: shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down' ? 'block' : 'inline-block',
151            width: w + 'px',
152            textAlign: 'center'
153          });
154
155          ch.setAttribute('data-orig', '1');
156          Object.assign(ch.style, {
157            display: shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down' ? 'block' : 'inline-block',
158            width: w + 'px',
159            textAlign: 'center'
160          });
161
162          inner.appendChild(firstOrig);
163          for (let k = 0; k < rolls; k++) {
164            const c = ch.cloneNode(true);
165            if (scrambleCharset) c.textContent = rand(scrambleCharset);
166            Object.assign(c.style, {
167              display: shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down' ? 'block' : 'inline-block',
168              width: w + 'px',
169              textAlign: 'center'
170            });
171            inner.appendChild(c);
172          }
173          inner.appendChild(ch);
174
175          const steps = rolls + 1;
176
177          if (shuffleDirection === 'right' || shuffleDirection === 'down') {
178            const firstCopy = inner.firstElementChild;
179            const real = inner.lastElementChild;
180            if (real) inner.insertBefore(real, inner.firstChild);
181            if (firstCopy) inner.appendChild(firstCopy);
182          }
183
184          let startX = 0;
185          let finalX = 0;
186          let startY = 0;
187          let finalY = 0;
188
189          if (shuffleDirection === 'right') {
190            startX = -steps * w;
191            finalX = 0;
192          } else if (shuffleDirection === 'left') {
193            startX = 0;
194            finalX = -steps * w;
195          } else if (shuffleDirection === 'down') {
196            startY = -steps * h;
197            finalY = 0;
198          } else if (shuffleDirection === 'up') {
199            startY = 0;
200            finalY = -steps * h;
201          }
202
203          if (shuffleDirection === 'left' || shuffleDirection === 'right') {
204            gsap.set(inner, { x: startX, y: 0, force3D: true });
205            inner.setAttribute('data-start-x', String(startX));
206            inner.setAttribute('data-final-x', String(finalX));
207          } else {
208            gsap.set(inner, { x: 0, y: startY, force3D: true });
209            inner.setAttribute('data-start-y', String(startY));
210            inner.setAttribute('data-final-y', String(finalY));
211          }
212
213          if (colorFrom) inner.style.color = colorFrom;
214          wrappersRef.current.push(wrap);
215        });
216      };
217
218      const inners = () => wrappersRef.current.map(w => w.firstElementChild);
219
220      const randomizeScrambles = () => {
221        if (!scrambleCharset) return;
222        wrappersRef.current.forEach(w => {
223          const strip = w.firstElementChild;
224          if (!strip) return;
225          const kids = Array.from(strip.children);
226          for (let i = 1; i < kids.length - 1; i++) {
227            kids[i].textContent = scrambleCharset.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * scrambleCharset.length));
228          }
229        });
230      };
231
232      const cleanupToStill = () => {
233        wrappersRef.current.forEach(w => {
234          const strip = w.firstElementChild;
235          if (!strip) return;
236          const real = strip.querySelector('[data-orig="1"]');
237          if (!real) return;
238          strip.replaceChildren(real);
239          strip.style.transform = 'none';
240          strip.style.willChange = 'auto';
241        });
242      };
243
244      const play = () => {
245        const strips = inners();
246        if (!strips.length) return;
247
248        playingRef.current = true;
249        const isVertical = shuffleDirection === 'up' || shuffleDirection === 'down';
250
251        const tl = gsap.timeline({
252          smoothChildTiming: true,
253          repeat: loop ? -1 : 0,
254          repeatDelay: loop ? loopDelay : 0,
255          onRepeat: () => {
256            if (scrambleCharset) randomizeScrambles();
257            if (isVertical) {
258              gsap.set(strips, { y: (i, t) => parseFloat(t.getAttribute('data-start-y') || '0') });
259            } else {
260              gsap.set(strips, { x: (i, t) => parseFloat(t.getAttribute('data-start-x') || '0') });
261            }
262            onShuffleComplete?.();
263          },
264          onComplete: () => {
265            playingRef.current = false;
266            if (!loop) {
267              cleanupToStill();
268              if (colorTo) gsap.set(strips, { color: colorTo });
269              onShuffleComplete?.();
270              armHover();
271            }
272          }
273        });
274
275        const addTween = (targets, at) => {
276          const vars = {
277            duration,
278            ease,
279            force3D: true,
280            stagger: animationMode === 'evenodd' ? stagger : 0
281          };
282          if (isVertical) {
283            vars.y = (i, t) => parseFloat(t.getAttribute('data-final-y') || '0');
284          } else {
285            vars.x = (i, t) => parseFloat(t.getAttribute('data-final-x') || '0');
286          }
287
288          tl.to(targets, vars, at);
289
290          if (colorFrom && colorTo) {
291            tl.to(targets, { color: colorTo, duration, ease }, at);
292          }
293        };
294
295        if (animationMode === 'evenodd') {
296          const odd = strips.filter((_, i) => i % 2 === 1);
297          const even = strips.filter((_, i) => i % 2 === 0);
298          const oddTotal = duration + Math.max(0, odd.length - 1) * stagger;
299          const evenStart = odd.length ? oddTotal * 0.7 : 0;
300          if (odd.length) addTween(odd, 0);
301          if (even.length) addTween(even, evenStart);
302        } else {
303          strips.forEach(strip => {
304            const d = Math.random() * maxDelay;
305            const vars = {
306              duration,
307              ease,
308              force3D: true
309            };
310            if (isVertical) {
311              vars.y = parseFloat(strip.getAttribute('data-final-y') || '0');
312            } else {
313              vars.x = parseFloat(strip.getAttribute('data-final-x') || '0');
314            }
315            tl.to(strip, vars, d);
316            if (colorFrom && colorTo) tl.fromTo(strip, { color: colorFrom }, { color: colorTo, duration, ease }, d);
317          });
318        }
319
320        tlRef.current = tl;
321      };
322
323      const armHover = () => {
324        if (!triggerOnHover || !ref.current) return;
325        removeHover();
326        const handler = () => {
327          if (playingRef.current) return;
328          build();
329          if (scrambleCharset) randomizeScrambles();
330          play();
331        };
332        hoverHandlerRef.current = handler;
333        ref.current.addEventListener('mouseenter', handler);
334      };
335
336      const create = () => {
337        build();
338        if (scrambleCharset) randomizeScrambles();
339        play();
340        armHover();
341        setReady(true);
342      };
343
344      const st = ScrollTrigger.create({
345        trigger: el,
346        start,
347        once: triggerOnce,
348        onEnter: create
349      });
350
351      return () => {
352        st.kill();
353        removeHover();
354        teardown();
355        setReady(false);
356      };
357    },
358    {
359      dependencies: [
360        text,
361        duration,
362        maxDelay,
363        ease,
364        scrollTriggerStart,
365        fontsLoaded,
366        shuffleDirection,
367        shuffleTimes,
368        animationMode,
369        loop,
370        loopDelay,
371        stagger,
372        scrambleCharset,
373        colorFrom,
374        colorTo,
375        triggerOnce,
376        respectReducedMotion,
377        triggerOnHover,
378        onShuffleComplete
379      ],
380      scope: ref
381    }
382  );
383
384  const commonStyle = useMemo(() => ({ textAlign, ...style }), [textAlign, style]);
385
386  const classes = useMemo(() => `shuffle-parent ${ready ? 'is-ready' : ''} ${className}`, [ready, className]);
387
388  const Tag = tag || 'p';
389  return React.createElement(Tag, { ref, className: classes, style: commonStyle }, text);
390};
391
392export default Shuffle;
393

Extra Config/Code:

2  display: inline-block;
3  white-space: normal;
4  word-wrap: break-word;
5  will-change: transform;
6  line-height: 1;
7  font-size: 4rem;
8  font-family: 'Press Start 2P', sans-serif;
9  text-transform: uppercase;
10  visibility: hidden;
11}

14  visibility: visible;
15}

19  overflow: hidden;
20  vertical-align: baseline;
21  position: relative;
22}

25  display: inline-flex;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Shiny Text

Installation:
npm install motion

Usage:
1import ShinyText from './ShinyText';
2
3<ShinyText
4  text="✨ Shiny Text Effect"
5  speed={2}
6  delay={0}
7  color="#b5b5b5"
8  shineColor="#ffffff"
9  spread={120}
10  direction="left"
11  yoyo={false}
12  pauseOnHover={false}
13  disabled={false}
14/>

Code:
1import { useState, useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import { motion, useMotionValue, useAnimationFrame, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
3import './ShinyText.css';
4
5const ShinyText = ({
6  text,
7  disabled = false,
8  speed = 2,
9  className = '',
10  color = '#b5b5b5',
11  shineColor = '#ffffff',
12  spread = 120,
13  yoyo = false,
14  pauseOnHover = false,
15  direction = 'left',
16  delay = 0
17}) => {
18  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);
19  const progress = useMotionValue(0);
20  const elapsedRef = useRef(0);
21  const lastTimeRef = useRef(null);
22  const directionRef = useRef(direction === 'left' ? 1 : -1);
23
24  const animationDuration = speed * 1000;
25  const delayDuration = delay * 1000;
26
27  useAnimationFrame(time => {
28    if (disabled || isPaused) {
29      lastTimeRef.current = null;
30      return;
31    }
32
33    if (lastTimeRef.current === null) {
34      lastTimeRef.current = time;
35      return;
36    }
37
38    const deltaTime = time - lastTimeRef.current;
39    lastTimeRef.current = time;
40
41    elapsedRef.current += deltaTime;
42
43    if (yoyo) {
44      const cycleDuration = animationDuration + delayDuration;
45      const fullCycle = cycleDuration * 2;
46      const cycleTime = elapsedRef.current % fullCycle;
47
48      if (cycleTime < animationDuration) {
49        // Forward animation: 0 -> 100
50        const p = (cycleTime / animationDuration) * 100;
51        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? p : 100 - p);
52      } else if (cycleTime < cycleDuration) {
53        // Delay at end
54        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? 100 : 0);
55      } else if (cycleTime < cycleDuration + animationDuration) {
56        // Reverse animation: 100 -> 0
57        const reverseTime = cycleTime - cycleDuration;
58        const p = 100 - (reverseTime / animationDuration) * 100;
59        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? p : 100 - p);
60      } else {
61        // Delay at start
62        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? 0 : 100);
63      }
64    } else {
65      const cycleDuration = animationDuration + delayDuration;
66      const cycleTime = elapsedRef.current % cycleDuration;
67
68      if (cycleTime < animationDuration) {
69        // Animation phase: 0 -> 100
70        const p = (cycleTime / animationDuration) * 100;
71        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? p : 100 - p);
72      } else {
73        // Delay phase - hold at end (shine off-screen)
74        progress.set(directionRef.current === 1 ? 100 : 0);
75      }
76    }
77  });
78
79  useEffect(() => {
80    directionRef.current = direction === 'left' ? 1 : -1;
81    elapsedRef.current = 0;
82    progress.set(0);
83    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
84  }, [direction]);
85
86  // Transform: p=0 -> 150% (shine off right), p=100 -> -50% (shine off left)
87  const backgroundPosition = useTransform(progress, p => `${150 - p * 2}% center`);
88
89  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
90    if (pauseOnHover) setIsPaused(true);
91  }, [pauseOnHover]);
92
93  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
94    if (pauseOnHover) setIsPaused(false);
95  }, [pauseOnHover]);
96
97  const gradientStyle = {
98    backgroundImage: `linear-gradient(${spread}deg, ${color} 0%, ${color} 35%, ${shineColor} 50%, ${color} 65%, ${color} 100%)`,
99    backgroundSize: '200% auto',
100    WebkitBackgroundClip: 'text',
101    backgroundClip: 'text',
102    WebkitTextFillColor: 'transparent'
103  };
104
105  return (
106    <motion.span
107      className={`shiny-text ${className}`}
108      style={{ ...gradientStyle, backgroundPosition }}
109      onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter}
110      onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
111    >
112      {text}
113    </motion.span>
114  );
115};
116
117export default ShinyText;
118

Extra Config/Code:
1.shiny-text {
2  display: inline-block;
3}
4

Component: Text Pressure

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/TextPressure-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// Component ported from https://codepen.io/JuanFuentes/full/rgXKGQ
2// Font used - https://compressa.preusstype.com/
3  
4import TextPressure from './TextPressure';
5
6// Note:
7// Make sure the font you're using supports all the variable properties. 
8// React Bits does not take responsibility for the fonts used
9
10<div style={{position: 'relative', height: '300px'}}>
11  <TextPressure
12    text="Hello!"
13    flex
14    alpha={false}
15    stroke={false}
16    width
17    weight
18    italic
19    textColor="#ffffff"
20    strokeColor="#5227FF"
21    minFontSize={36}
22  />
23</div>

Code:
1// Component ported from https://codepen.io/JuanFuentes/full/rgXKGQ
2
3import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
4
5const dist = (a, b) => {
6  const dx = b.x - a.x;
7  const dy = b.y - a.y;
8  return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
9};
10
11const getAttr = (distance, maxDist, minVal, maxVal) => {
12  const val = maxVal - Math.abs((maxVal * distance) / maxDist);
13  return Math.max(minVal, val + minVal);
14};
15
16const debounce = (func, delay) => {
17  let timeoutId;
18  return (...args) => {
19    clearTimeout(timeoutId);
20    timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
21      func.apply(this, args);
22    }, delay);
23  };
24};
25
26const TextPressure = ({
27  text = 'Compressa',
28  fontFamily = 'Compressa VF',
29  fontUrl = 'https://res.cloudinary.com/dr6lvwubh/raw/upload/v1529908256/CompressaPRO-GX.woff2',
30
31  width = true,
32  weight = true,
33  italic = true,
34  alpha = false,
35
36  flex = true,
37  stroke = false,
38  scale = false,
39
40  textColor = '#FFFFFF',
41  strokeColor = '#FF0000',
42  className = '',
43
44  minFontSize = 24
45}) => {
46  const containerRef = useRef(null);
47  const titleRef = useRef(null);
48  const spansRef = useRef([]);
49
50  const mouseRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
51  const cursorRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
52
53  const [fontSize, setFontSize] = useState(minFontSize);
54  const [scaleY, setScaleY] = useState(1);
55  const [lineHeight, setLineHeight] = useState(1);
56
57  const chars = text.split('');
58
59  useEffect(() => {
60    const handleMouseMove = e => {
61      cursorRef.current.x = e.clientX;
62      cursorRef.current.y = e.clientY;
63    };
64    const handleTouchMove = e => {
65      const t = e.touches[0];
66      cursorRef.current.x = t.clientX;
67      cursorRef.current.y = t.clientY;
68    };
69
70    window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
71    window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove, { passive: true });
72
73    if (containerRef.current) {
74      const { left, top, width, height } = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
75      mouseRef.current.x = left + width / 2;
76      mouseRef.current.y = top + height / 2;
77      cursorRef.current.x = mouseRef.current.x;
78      cursorRef.current.y = mouseRef.current.y;
79    }
80
81    return () => {
82      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
83      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
84    };
85  }, []);
86
87  const setSize = useCallback(() => {
88    if (!containerRef.current || !titleRef.current) return;
89
90    const { width: containerW, height: containerH } = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
91
92    let newFontSize = containerW / (chars.length / 2);
93    newFontSize = Math.max(newFontSize, minFontSize);
94
95    setFontSize(newFontSize);
96    setScaleY(1);
97    setLineHeight(1);
98
99    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
100      if (!titleRef.current) return;
101      const textRect = titleRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
102
103      if (scale && textRect.height > 0) {
104        const yRatio = containerH / textRect.height;
105        setScaleY(yRatio);
106        setLineHeight(yRatio);
107      }
108    });
109  }, [chars.length, minFontSize, scale]);
110
111  useEffect(() => {
112    const debouncedSetSize = debounce(setSize, 100);
113    debouncedSetSize();
114    window.addEventListener('resize', debouncedSetSize);
115    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', debouncedSetSize);
116  }, [setSize]);
117
118  useEffect(() => {
119    let rafId;
120    const animate = () => {
121      mouseRef.current.x += (cursorRef.current.x - mouseRef.current.x) / 15;
122      mouseRef.current.y += (cursorRef.current.y - mouseRef.current.y) / 15;
123
124      if (titleRef.current) {
125        const titleRect = titleRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
126        const maxDist = titleRect.width / 2;
127
128        spansRef.current.forEach(span => {
129          if (!span) return;
130
131          const rect = span.getBoundingClientRect();
132          const charCenter = {
133            x: rect.x + rect.width / 2,
134            y: rect.y + rect.height / 2
135          };
136
137          const d = dist(mouseRef.current, charCenter);
138
139          const wdth = width ? Math.floor(getAttr(d, maxDist, 5, 200)) : 100;
140          const wght = weight ? Math.floor(getAttr(d, maxDist, 100, 900)) : 400;
141          const italVal = italic ? getAttr(d, maxDist, 0, 1).toFixed(2) : 0;
142          const alphaVal = alpha ? getAttr(d, maxDist, 0, 1).toFixed(2) : 1;
143
144          const newFontVariationSettings = `'wght' ${wght}, 'wdth' ${wdth}, 'ital' ${italVal}`;
145
146          if (span.style.fontVariationSettings !== newFontVariationSettings) {
147            span.style.fontVariationSettings = newFontVariationSettings;
148          }
149          if (alpha && span.style.opacity !== alphaVal) {
150            span.style.opacity = alphaVal;
151          }
152        });
153      }
154
155      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
156    };
157
158    animate();
159    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
160  }, [width, weight, italic, alpha]);
161
162  const styleElement = useMemo(() => {
163    return (
164      <style>{`
165        @font-face {
166          font-family: '${fontFamily}';
167          src: url('${fontUrl}');
168          font-style: normal;
169        }
170
171        .flex {
172          display: flex;
173          justify-content: space-between;
174        }
175
176        .stroke span {
177          position: relative;
178          color: ${textColor};
179        }
180        .stroke span::after {
181          content: attr(data-char);
182          position: absolute;
183          left: 0;
184          top: 0;
185          color: transparent;
186          z-index: -1;
187          -webkit-text-stroke-width: 3px;
188          -webkit-text-stroke-color: ${strokeColor};
189        }
190
191        .text-pressure-title {
192          color: ${textColor};
193        }
194      `}</style>
195    );
196  }, [fontFamily, fontUrl, textColor, strokeColor]);
197
198  const dynamicClassName = [className, flex ? 'flex' : '', stroke ? 'stroke' : ''].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
199
200  return (
201    <div
202      ref={containerRef}
203      style={{
204        position: 'relative',
205        width: '100%',
206        height: '100%',
207        background: 'transparent'
208      }}
209    >
210      {styleElement}
211      <h1
212        ref={titleRef}
213        className={`text-pressure-title ${dynamicClassName}`}
214        style={{
215          fontFamily,
216          textTransform: 'uppercase',
217          fontSize: fontSize,
218          lineHeight,
219          transform: `scale(1, ${scaleY})`,
220          transformOrigin: 'center top',
221          margin: 0,
222          textAlign: 'center',
223          userSelect: 'none',
224          whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
225          fontWeight: 100,
226          width: '100%'
227        }}
228      >
229        {chars.map((char, i) => (
230          <span
231            key={i}
232            ref={el => (spansRef.current[i] = el)}
233            data-char={char}
234            style={{
235              display: 'inline-block',
236              color: stroke ? undefined : textColor
237            }}
238          >
239            {char}
240          </span>
241        ))}
242      </h1>
243    </div>
244  );
245};
246
247export default TextPressure;
248

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Curved Loop

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/CurvedLoop-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import CurvedLoop from './CurvedLoop';
2
3// Basic usage
4<CurvedLoop marqueeText="Welcome to React Bits ✦" />
5
6// With custom props
7<CurvedLoop 
8  marqueeText="Be ✦ Creative ✦ With ✦ React ✦ Bits ✦"
9  speed={2}
10  curveAmount={400}
11  direction="right"
12  interactive
13  className="custom-text-style"
14/>
15
16// Non-interactive with slower speed
17<CurvedLoop 
18  marqueeText="Be ✦ Creative ✦ With ✦ React ✦ Bits ✦"
19  speed={2}
20  curveAmount={400}
21  interactive
22/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect, useState, useMemo, useId } from 'react';
2import './CurvedLoop.css';
3
4const CurvedLoop = ({
5  marqueeText = '',
6  speed = 2,
7  className,
8  curveAmount = 400,
9  direction = 'left',
10  interactive = true
11}) => {
12  const text = useMemo(() => {
13    const hasTrailing = /\s|\u00A0$/.test(marqueeText);
14    return (hasTrailing ? marqueeText.replace(/\s+$/, '') : marqueeText) + '\u00A0';
15  }, [marqueeText]);
16
17  const measureRef = useRef(null);
18  const textPathRef = useRef(null);
19  const pathRef = useRef(null);
20  const [spacing, setSpacing] = useState(0);
21  const [offset, setOffset] = useState(0);
22  const uid = useId();
23  const pathId = `curve-${uid}`;
24  const pathD = `M-100,40 Q500,${40 + curveAmount} 1540,40`;
25
26  const dragRef = useRef(false);
27  const lastXRef = useRef(0);
28  const dirRef = useRef(direction);
29  const velRef = useRef(0);
30
31  const textLength = spacing;
32  const totalText = textLength
33    ? Array(Math.ceil(1800 / textLength) + 2)
34        .fill(text)
35        .join('')
36    : text;
37  const ready = spacing > 0;
38
39  useEffect(() => {
40    if (measureRef.current) setSpacing(measureRef.current.getComputedTextLength());
41  }, [text, className]);
42
43  useEffect(() => {
44    if (!spacing) return;
45    if (textPathRef.current) {
46      const initial = -spacing;
47      textPathRef.current.setAttribute('startOffset', initial + 'px');
48      setOffset(initial);
49    }
50  }, [spacing]);
51
52  useEffect(() => {
53    if (!spacing || !ready) return;
54    let frame = 0;
55    const step = () => {
56      if (!dragRef.current && textPathRef.current) {
57        const delta = dirRef.current === 'right' ? speed : -speed;
58        const currentOffset = parseFloat(textPathRef.current.getAttribute('startOffset') || '0');
59        let newOffset = currentOffset + delta;
60
61        const wrapPoint = spacing;
62        if (newOffset <= -wrapPoint) newOffset += wrapPoint;
63        if (newOffset > 0) newOffset -= wrapPoint;
64
65        textPathRef.current.setAttribute('startOffset', newOffset + 'px');
66        setOffset(newOffset);
67      }
68      frame = requestAnimationFrame(step);
69    };
70    frame = requestAnimationFrame(step);
71    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
72  }, [spacing, speed, ready]);
73
74  const onPointerDown = e => {
75    if (!interactive) return;
76    dragRef.current = true;
77    lastXRef.current = e.clientX;
78    velRef.current = 0;
79    e.target.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
80  };
81
82  const onPointerMove = e => {
83    if (!interactive || !dragRef.current || !textPathRef.current) return;
84    const dx = e.clientX - lastXRef.current;
85    lastXRef.current = e.clientX;
86    velRef.current = dx;
87
88    const currentOffset = parseFloat(textPathRef.current.getAttribute('startOffset') || '0');
89    let newOffset = currentOffset + dx;
90
91    const wrapPoint = spacing;
92    if (newOffset <= -wrapPoint) newOffset += wrapPoint;
93    if (newOffset > 0) newOffset -= wrapPoint;
94
95    textPathRef.current.setAttribute('startOffset', newOffset + 'px');
96    setOffset(newOffset);
97  };
98
99  const endDrag = () => {
100    if (!interactive) return;
101    dragRef.current = false;
102    dirRef.current = velRef.current > 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
103  };
104
105  const cursorStyle = interactive ? (dragRef.current ? 'grabbing' : 'grab') : 'auto';
106
107  return (
108    <div
109      className="curved-loop-jacket"
110      style={{ visibility: ready ? 'visible' : 'hidden', cursor: cursorStyle }}
111      onPointerDown={onPointerDown}
112      onPointerMove={onPointerMove}
113      onPointerUp={endDrag}
114      onPointerLeave={endDrag}
115    >
116      <svg className="curved-loop-svg" viewBox="0 0 1440 120">
117        <text ref={measureRef} xmlSpace="preserve" style={{ visibility: 'hidden', opacity: 0, pointerEvents: 'none' }}>
118          {text}
119        </text>
120        <defs>
121          <path ref={pathRef} id={pathId} d={pathD} fill="none" stroke="transparent" />
122        </defs>
123        {ready && (
124          <text fontWeight="bold" xmlSpace="preserve" className={className}>
125            <textPath ref={textPathRef} href={`#${pathId}`} startOffset={offset + 'px'} xmlSpace="preserve">
126              {totalText}
127            </textPath>
128          </text>
129        )}
130      </svg>
131    </div>
132  );
133};
134
135export default CurvedLoop;
136

Extra Config/Code:
1.curved-loop-jacket {
2  min-height: 100vh;
3  display: flex;
4  align-items: center;
5  justify-content: center;
6  width: 100%;
7}
8
9.curved-loop-svg {
10  user-select: none;
11  width: 100%;
12  aspect-ratio: 100 / 12;
13  overflow: visible;
14  display: block;
15  font-size: 6rem;
16  fill: #ffffff;
17  user-select: none;
18  -moz-user-select: none;
19  -webkit-user-select: none;
20  font-weight: 700;
21  text-transform: uppercase;
22  line-height: 1;
23}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Fuzzy Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/FuzzyText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import FuzzyText from './FuzzyText';
2  
3<FuzzyText 
4  baseIntensity={0.2}
5  hoverIntensity={0.5}
6  enableHover
7>
8  404
9</FuzzyText>

Code:
1import React, { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2
3const FuzzyText = ({
4  children,
5  fontSize = 'clamp(2rem, 10vw, 10rem)',
6  fontWeight = 900,
7  fontFamily = 'inherit',
8  color = '#fff',
9  enableHover = true,
10  baseIntensity = 0.18,
11  hoverIntensity = 0.5,
12  fuzzRange = 30,
13  fps = 60,
14  direction = 'horizontal',
15  transitionDuration = 0,
16  clickEffect = false,
17  glitchMode = false,
18  glitchInterval = 2000,
19  glitchDuration = 200,
20  gradient = null,
21  letterSpacing = 0,
22  className = ''
23}) => {
24  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
25
26  useEffect(() => {
27    let animationFrameId;
28    let isCancelled = false;
29    let glitchTimeoutId;
30    let glitchEndTimeoutId;
31    let clickTimeoutId;
32    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
33    if (!canvas) return;
34
35    const init = async () => {
36      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
37      if (!ctx) return;
38
39      const computedFontFamily =
40        fontFamily === 'inherit' ? window.getComputedStyle(canvas).fontFamily || 'sans-serif' : fontFamily;
41
42      const fontSizeStr = typeof fontSize === 'number' ? `${fontSize}px` : fontSize;
43      const fontString = `${fontWeight} ${fontSizeStr} ${computedFontFamily}`;
44
45      try {
46        await document.fonts.load(fontString);
47      } catch {
48        await document.fonts.ready;
49      }
50      if (isCancelled) return;
51
52      let numericFontSize;
53      if (typeof fontSize === 'number') {
54        numericFontSize = fontSize;
55      } else {
56        const temp = document.createElement('span');
57        temp.style.fontSize = fontSize;
58        document.body.appendChild(temp);
59        const computedSize = window.getComputedStyle(temp).fontSize;
60        numericFontSize = parseFloat(computedSize);
61        document.body.removeChild(temp);
62      }
63
64      const text = React.Children.toArray(children).join('');
65
66      const offscreen = document.createElement('canvas');
67      const offCtx = offscreen.getContext('2d');
68      if (!offCtx) return;
69
70      offCtx.font = `${fontWeight} ${fontSizeStr} ${computedFontFamily}`;
71      offCtx.textBaseline = 'alphabetic';
72
73      let totalWidth = 0;
74      if (letterSpacing !== 0) {
75        for (const char of text) {
76          totalWidth += offCtx.measureText(char).width + letterSpacing;
77        }
78        totalWidth -= letterSpacing;
79      } else {
80        totalWidth = offCtx.measureText(text).width;
81      }
82
83      const metrics = offCtx.measureText(text);
84      const actualLeft = metrics.actualBoundingBoxLeft ?? 0;
85      const actualRight = letterSpacing !== 0 ? totalWidth : (metrics.actualBoundingBoxRight ?? metrics.width);
86      const actualAscent = metrics.actualBoundingBoxAscent ?? numericFontSize;
87      const actualDescent = metrics.actualBoundingBoxDescent ?? numericFontSize * 0.2;
88
89      const textBoundingWidth = Math.ceil(letterSpacing !== 0 ? totalWidth : actualLeft + actualRight);
90      const tightHeight = Math.ceil(actualAscent + actualDescent);
91
92      const extraWidthBuffer = 10;
93      const offscreenWidth = textBoundingWidth + extraWidthBuffer;
94
95      offscreen.width = offscreenWidth;
96      offscreen.height = tightHeight;
97
98      const xOffset = extraWidthBuffer / 2;
99      offCtx.font = `${fontWeight} ${fontSizeStr} ${computedFontFamily}`;
100      offCtx.textBaseline = 'alphabetic';
101
102      if (gradient && Array.isArray(gradient) && gradient.length >= 2) {
103        const grad = offCtx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, offscreenWidth, 0);
104        gradient.forEach((c, i) => grad.addColorStop(i / (gradient.length - 1), c));
105        offCtx.fillStyle = grad;
106      } else {
107        offCtx.fillStyle = color;
108      }
109
110      if (letterSpacing !== 0) {
111        let xPos = xOffset;
112        for (const char of text) {
113          offCtx.fillText(char, xPos, actualAscent);
114          xPos += offCtx.measureText(char).width + letterSpacing;
115        }
116      } else {
117        offCtx.fillText(text, xOffset - actualLeft, actualAscent);
118      }
119
120      const horizontalMargin = fuzzRange + 20;
121      const verticalMargin = 0;
122      canvas.width = offscreenWidth + horizontalMargin * 2;
123      canvas.height = tightHeight + verticalMargin * 2;
124      ctx.translate(horizontalMargin, verticalMargin);
125
126      const interactiveLeft = horizontalMargin + xOffset;
127      const interactiveTop = verticalMargin;
128      const interactiveRight = interactiveLeft + textBoundingWidth;
129      const interactiveBottom = interactiveTop + tightHeight;
130
131      let isHovering = false;
132      let isClicking = false;
133      let isGlitching = false;
134      let currentIntensity = baseIntensity;
135      let targetIntensity = baseIntensity;
136      let lastFrameTime = 0;
137      const frameDuration = 1000 / fps;
138
139      const startGlitchLoop = () => {
140        if (!glitchMode || isCancelled) return;
141        glitchTimeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
142          if (isCancelled) return;
143          isGlitching = true;
144          glitchEndTimeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
145            isGlitching = false;
146            startGlitchLoop();
147          }, glitchDuration);
148        }, glitchInterval);
149      };
150
151      if (glitchMode) startGlitchLoop();
152
153      const run = timestamp => {
154        if (isCancelled) return;
155
156        if (timestamp - lastFrameTime < frameDuration) {
157          animationFrameId = window.requestAnimationFrame(run);
158          return;
159        }
160        lastFrameTime = timestamp;
161
162        ctx.clearRect(
163          -fuzzRange - 20,
164          -fuzzRange - 10,
165          offscreenWidth + 2 * (fuzzRange + 20),
166          tightHeight + 2 * (fuzzRange + 10)
167        );
168
169        if (isClicking) {
170          targetIntensity = 1;
171        } else if (isGlitching) {
172          targetIntensity = 1;
173        } else if (isHovering) {
174          targetIntensity = hoverIntensity;
175        } else {
176          targetIntensity = baseIntensity;
177        }
178
179        if (transitionDuration > 0) {
180          const step = 1 / (transitionDuration / frameDuration);
181          if (currentIntensity < targetIntensity) {
182            currentIntensity = Math.min(currentIntensity + step, targetIntensity);
183          } else if (currentIntensity > targetIntensity) {
184            currentIntensity = Math.max(currentIntensity - step, targetIntensity);
185          }
186        } else {
187          currentIntensity = targetIntensity;
188        }
189
190        if (direction === 'horizontal') {
191          // Horizontal: shift each row left/right
192          for (let j = 0; j < tightHeight; j++) {
193            const dx = Math.floor(currentIntensity * (Math.random() - 0.5) * fuzzRange);
194            ctx.drawImage(offscreen, 0, j, offscreenWidth, 1, dx, j, offscreenWidth, 1);
195          }
196        } else if (direction === 'vertical') {
197          // Vertical: shift each column up/down
198          for (let i = 0; i < offscreenWidth; i++) {
199            const dy = Math.floor(currentIntensity * (Math.random() - 0.5) * fuzzRange);
200            ctx.drawImage(offscreen, i, 0, 1, tightHeight, i, dy, 1, tightHeight);
201          }
202        } else {
203          // Both: shift each row horizontally, then shift each column vertically
204          // First pass: draw with horizontal displacement to a temp position
205          for (let j = 0; j < tightHeight; j++) {
206            const dx = Math.floor(currentIntensity * (Math.random() - 0.5) * fuzzRange);
207            ctx.drawImage(offscreen, 0, j, offscreenWidth, 1, dx, j, offscreenWidth, 1);
208          }
209          // Second pass: read what we just drew and apply vertical displacement
210          const tempData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, offscreenWidth + fuzzRange, tightHeight + fuzzRange);
211          ctx.clearRect(
212            -fuzzRange - 20,
213            -fuzzRange - 10,
214            offscreenWidth + 2 * (fuzzRange + 20),
215            tightHeight + 2 * (fuzzRange + 10)
216          );
217          ctx.putImageData(tempData, 0, 0);
218          for (let i = 0; i < offscreenWidth + fuzzRange; i++) {
219            const dy = Math.floor(currentIntensity * (Math.random() - 0.5) * fuzzRange * 0.5);
220            const colData = ctx.getImageData(i, 0, 1, tightHeight + fuzzRange);
221            ctx.clearRect(i, -fuzzRange, 1, tightHeight + 2 * fuzzRange);
222            ctx.putImageData(colData, i, dy);
223          }
224        }
225        animationFrameId = window.requestAnimationFrame(run);
226      };
227
228      animationFrameId = window.requestAnimationFrame(run);
229
230      const isInsideTextArea = (x, y) => {
231        return x >= interactiveLeft && x <= interactiveRight && y >= interactiveTop && y <= interactiveBottom;
232      };
233
234      const handleMouseMove = e => {
235        if (!enableHover) return;
236        const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
237        const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
238        const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
239        isHovering = isInsideTextArea(x, y);
240      };
241
242      const handleMouseLeave = () => {
243        isHovering = false;
244      };
245
246      const handleClick = () => {
247        if (!clickEffect) return;
248        isClicking = true;
249        clearTimeout(clickTimeoutId);
250        clickTimeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
251          isClicking = false;
252        }, 150);
253      };
254
255      const handleTouchMove = e => {
256        if (!enableHover) return;
257        e.preventDefault();
258        const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
259        const touch = e.touches[0];
260        const x = touch.clientX - rect.left;
261        const y = touch.clientY - rect.top;
262        isHovering = isInsideTextArea(x, y);
263      };
264
265      const handleTouchEnd = () => {
266        isHovering = false;
267      };
268
269      if (enableHover) {
270        canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
271        canvas.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
272        canvas.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove, { passive: false });
273        canvas.addEventListener('touchend', handleTouchEnd);
274      }
275
276      if (clickEffect) {
277        canvas.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
278      }
279
280      const cleanup = () => {
281        window.cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId);
282        clearTimeout(glitchTimeoutId);
283        clearTimeout(glitchEndTimeoutId);
284        clearTimeout(clickTimeoutId);
285        if (enableHover) {
286          canvas.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
287          canvas.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
288          canvas.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
289          canvas.removeEventListener('touchend', handleTouchEnd);
290        }
291        if (clickEffect) {
292          canvas.removeEventListener('click', handleClick);
293        }
294      };
295
296      canvas.cleanupFuzzyText = cleanup;
297    };
298
299    init();
300
301    return () => {
302      isCancelled = true;
303      window.cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrameId);
304      clearTimeout(glitchTimeoutId);
305      clearTimeout(glitchEndTimeoutId);
306      clearTimeout(clickTimeoutId);
307      if (canvas && canvas.cleanupFuzzyText) {
308        canvas.cleanupFuzzyText();
309      }
310    };
311  }, [
312    children,
313    fontSize,
314    fontWeight,
315    fontFamily,
316    color,
317    enableHover,
318    baseIntensity,
319    hoverIntensity,
320    fuzzRange,
321    fps,
322    direction,
323    transitionDuration,
324    clickEffect,
325    glitchMode,
326    glitchInterval,
327    glitchDuration,
328    gradient,
329    letterSpacing
330  ]);
331
332  return <canvas ref={canvasRef} className={className} />;
333};
334
335export default FuzzyText;
336

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Gradient Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/GradientText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import GradientText from './GradientText'
2
3// For a smoother animation, the gradient should start and end with the same color
4  
5<GradientText
6  colors={["#5227FF","#FF9FFC","#B19EEF"]}
7  animationSpeed={8}
8  showBorder={false}
9  className="custom-class"
10>
11  Add a splash of color!
12</GradientText>

Code:
1import { useState, useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import { motion, useMotionValue, useAnimationFrame, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
3import './GradientText.css';
4
5export default function GradientText({
6  children,
7  className = '',
8  colors = ['#5227FF', '#FF9FFC', '#B19EEF'],
9  animationSpeed = 8,
10  showBorder = false,
11  direction = 'horizontal',
12  pauseOnHover = false,
13  yoyo = true
14}) {
15  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);
16  const progress = useMotionValue(0);
17  const elapsedRef = useRef(0);
18  const lastTimeRef = useRef(null);
19
20  const animationDuration = animationSpeed * 1000;
21
22  useAnimationFrame(time => {
23    if (isPaused) {
24      lastTimeRef.current = null;
25      return;
26    }
27
28    if (lastTimeRef.current === null) {
29      lastTimeRef.current = time;
30      return;
31    }
32
33    const deltaTime = time - lastTimeRef.current;
34    lastTimeRef.current = time;
35    elapsedRef.current += deltaTime;
36
37    if (yoyo) {
38      const fullCycle = animationDuration * 2;
39      const cycleTime = elapsedRef.current % fullCycle;
40
41      if (cycleTime < animationDuration) {
42        progress.set((cycleTime / animationDuration) * 100);
43      } else {
44        progress.set(100 - ((cycleTime - animationDuration) / animationDuration) * 100);
45      }
46    } else {
47      // Continuously increase position for seamless looping
48      progress.set((elapsedRef.current / animationDuration) * 100);
49    }
50  });
51
52  useEffect(() => {
53    elapsedRef.current = 0;
54    progress.set(0);
55  }, [animationSpeed, progress, yoyo]);
56
57  const backgroundPosition = useTransform(progress, p => {
58    if (direction === 'horizontal') {
59      return `${p}% 50%`;
60    } else if (direction === 'vertical') {
61      return `50% ${p}%`;
62    } else {
63      // For diagonal, move only horizontally to avoid interference patterns
64      return `${p}% 50%`;
65    }
66  });
67
68  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
69    if (pauseOnHover) setIsPaused(true);
70  }, [pauseOnHover]);
71
72  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
73    if (pauseOnHover) setIsPaused(false);
74  }, [pauseOnHover]);
75
76  const gradientAngle =
77    direction === 'horizontal' ? 'to right' : direction === 'vertical' ? 'to bottom' : 'to bottom right';
78  // Duplicate first color at the end for seamless looping
79  const gradientColors = [...colors, colors[0]].join(', ');
80
81  const gradientStyle = {
82    backgroundImage: `linear-gradient(${gradientAngle}, ${gradientColors})`,
83    backgroundSize: direction === 'horizontal' ? '300% 100%' : direction === 'vertical' ? '100% 300%' : '300% 300%',
84    backgroundRepeat: 'repeat'
85  };
86
87  return (
88    <motion.div
89      className={`animated-gradient-text ${showBorder ? 'with-border' : ''} ${className}`}
90      onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter}
91      onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
92    >
93      {showBorder && <motion.div className="gradient-overlay" style={{ ...gradientStyle, backgroundPosition }} />}
94      <motion.div className="text-content" style={{ ...gradientStyle, backgroundPosition }}>
95        {children}
96      </motion.div>
97    </motion.div>
98  );
99}
100

Extra Config/Code:
1.animated-gradient-text {
2  position: relative;
3  margin: 0 auto;
4  display: flex;
5  max-width: fit-content;
6  flex-direction: row;
7  align-items: center;
8  justify-content: center;
9  border-radius: 1.25rem;
10  font-weight: 500;
11  backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
12  transition: box-shadow 0.5s ease-out;
13  overflow: hidden;
14  cursor: pointer;
15}
16
17.animated-gradient-text.with-border {
18  padding: 0.35rem 0.75rem;
19}
20
21.gradient-overlay {
22  position: absolute;
23  top: 0;
24  left: 0;
25  right: 0;
26  bottom: 0;
27  border-radius: inherit;
28  z-index: 0;
29  pointer-events: none;
30}
31
32.gradient-overlay::before {
33  content: '';
34  position: absolute;
35  left: 0;
36  top: 0;
37  border-radius: inherit;
38  width: calc(100% - 2px);
39  height: calc(100% - 2px);
40  left: 50%;
41  top: 50%;
42  transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
43  background-color: #060010;
44  z-index: -1;
45}
46
47.text-content {
48  display: inline-block;
49  position: relative;
50  z-index: 2;
51  background-clip: text;
52  -webkit-background-clip: text;
53  color: transparent;
54}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Falling Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/FallingText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import FallingText from './FallingText';
2  
3<FallingText
4  text={`React Bits is a library of animated and interactive React components designed to streamline UI development and simplify your workflow.`}
5  highlightWords={["React", "Bits", "animated", "components", "simplify"]}
6  highlightClass="highlighted"
7  trigger="hover"
8  backgroundColor="transparent"
9  wireframes={false}
10  gravity={0.56}
11  fontSize="2rem"
12  mouseConstraintStiffness={0.9}
13/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useState, useEffect } from 'react';
2import Matter from 'matter-js';
3import './FallingText.css';
4
5const FallingText = ({
6  className = '',
7  text = '',
8  highlightWords = [],
9  highlightClass = 'highlighted',
10  trigger = 'auto',
11  backgroundColor = 'transparent',
12  wireframes = false,
13  gravity = 1,
14  mouseConstraintStiffness = 0.2,
15  fontSize = '1rem'
16}) => {
17  const containerRef = useRef(null);
18  const textRef = useRef(null);
19  const canvasContainerRef = useRef(null);
20
21  const [effectStarted, setEffectStarted] = useState(false);
22
23  useEffect(() => {
24    if (!textRef.current) return;
25    const words = text.split(' ');
26    const newHTML = words
27      .map(word => {
28        const isHighlighted = highlightWords.some(hw => word.startsWith(hw));
29        return `<span class="word ${isHighlighted ? highlightClass : ''}">${word}</span>`;
30      })
31      .join(' ');
32    textRef.current.innerHTML = newHTML;
33  }, [text, highlightWords, highlightClass]);
34
35  useEffect(() => {
36    if (trigger === 'auto') {
37      setEffectStarted(true);
38      return;
39    }
40    if (trigger === 'scroll' && containerRef.current) {
41      const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
42        ([entry]) => {
43          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
44            setEffectStarted(true);
45            observer.disconnect();
46          }
47        },
48        { threshold: 0.1 }
49      );
50      observer.observe(containerRef.current);
51      return () => observer.disconnect();
52    }
53  }, [trigger]);
54
55  useEffect(() => {
56    if (!effectStarted) return;
57
58    const { Engine, Render, World, Bodies, Runner, Mouse, MouseConstraint } = Matter;
59
60    const containerRect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
61    const width = containerRect.width;
62    const height = containerRect.height;
63
64    if (width <= 0 || height <= 0) {
65      return;
66    }
67
68    const engine = Engine.create();
69    engine.world.gravity.y = gravity;
70
71    const render = Render.create({
72      element: canvasContainerRef.current,
73      engine,
74      options: {
75        width,
76        height,
77        background: backgroundColor,
78        wireframes
79      }
80    });
81
82    const boundaryOptions = {
83      isStatic: true,
84      render: { fillStyle: 'transparent' }
85    };
86    const floor = Bodies.rectangle(width / 2, height + 25, width, 50, boundaryOptions);
87    const leftWall = Bodies.rectangle(-25, height / 2, 50, height, boundaryOptions);
88    const rightWall = Bodies.rectangle(width + 25, height / 2, 50, height, boundaryOptions);
89    const ceiling = Bodies.rectangle(width / 2, -25, width, 50, boundaryOptions);
90
91    const wordSpans = textRef.current.querySelectorAll('.word');
92    const wordBodies = [...wordSpans].map(elem => {
93      const rect = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
94
95      const x = rect.left - containerRect.left + rect.width / 2;
96      const y = rect.top - containerRect.top + rect.height / 2;
97
98      const body = Bodies.rectangle(x, y, rect.width, rect.height, {
99        render: { fillStyle: 'transparent' },
100        restitution: 0.8,
101        frictionAir: 0.01,
102        friction: 0.2
103      });
104
105      Matter.Body.setVelocity(body, {
106        x: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 5,
107        y: 0
108      });
109      Matter.Body.setAngularVelocity(body, (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.05);
110      return { elem, body };
111    });
112
113    wordBodies.forEach(({ elem, body }) => {
114      elem.style.position = 'absolute';
115      elem.style.left = `${body.position.x - body.bounds.max.x + body.bounds.min.x / 2}px`;
116      elem.style.top = `${body.position.y - body.bounds.max.y + body.bounds.min.y / 2}px`;
117      elem.style.transform = 'none';
118    });
119
120    const mouse = Mouse.create(containerRef.current);
121    const mouseConstraint = MouseConstraint.create(engine, {
122      mouse,
123      constraint: {
124        stiffness: mouseConstraintStiffness,
125        render: { visible: false }
126      }
127    });
128    render.mouse = mouse;
129
130    World.add(engine.world, [floor, leftWall, rightWall, ceiling, mouseConstraint, ...wordBodies.map(wb => wb.body)]);
131
132    const runner = Runner.create();
133    Runner.run(runner, engine);
134    Render.run(render);
135
136    const updateLoop = () => {
137      wordBodies.forEach(({ body, elem }) => {
138        const { x, y } = body.position;
139        elem.style.left = `${x}px`;
140        elem.style.top = `${y}px`;
141        elem.style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(${body.angle}rad)`;
142      });
143      Matter.Engine.update(engine);
144      requestAnimationFrame(updateLoop);
145    };
146    updateLoop();
147
148    return () => {
149      Render.stop(render);
150      Runner.stop(runner);
151      if (render.canvas && canvasContainerRef.current) {
152        // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
153        canvasContainerRef.current.removeChild(render.canvas);
154      }
155      World.clear(engine.world);
156      Engine.clear(engine);
157    };
158  }, [effectStarted, gravity, wireframes, backgroundColor, mouseConstraintStiffness]);
159
160  const handleTrigger = () => {
161    if (!effectStarted && (trigger === 'click' || trigger === 'hover')) {
162      setEffectStarted(true);
163    }
164  };
165
166  return (
167    <div
168      ref={containerRef}
169      className={`falling-text-container ${className}`}
170      onClick={trigger === 'click' ? handleTrigger : undefined}
171      onMouseEnter={trigger === 'hover' ? handleTrigger : undefined}
172      style={{
173        position: 'relative',
174        overflow: 'hidden'
175      }}
176    >
177      <div
178        ref={textRef}
179        className="falling-text-target"
180        style={{
181          fontSize: fontSize,
182          lineHeight: 1.4
183        }}
184      />
185      <div ref={canvasContainerRef} className="falling-text-canvas" />
186    </div>
187  );
188};
189
190export default FallingText;
191

Extra Config/Code:
