--------------------------------------------------

Component: Text Cursor

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/TextCursor-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import TextCursor from './TextCursor';
2
3<TextCursor
4  text="⚛️"
5  spacing={80}
6  followMouseDirection
7  randomFloat
8  exitDuration={0.3}
9  removalInterval={20}
10  maxPoints={10}
11/>

Code:
1import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'motion/react';
3import './TextCursor.css';
4
5const TextCursor = ({
6  text = '⚛️',
7  spacing = 100,
8  followMouseDirection = true,
9  randomFloat = true,
10  exitDuration = 0.5,
11  removalInterval = 30,
12  maxPoints = 5
13}) => {
14  const [trail, setTrail] = useState([]);
15  const containerRef = useRef(null);
16  const lastMoveTimeRef = useRef(Date.now());
17  const idCounter = useRef(0);
18
19  const handleMouseMove = e => {
20    if (!containerRef.current) return;
21    const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
22    const mouseX = e.clientX - rect.left;
23    const mouseY = e.clientY - rect.top;
24
25    const createRandomData = () =>
26      randomFloat
27        ? {
28            randomX: Math.random() * 10 - 5,
29            randomY: Math.random() * 10 - 5,
30            randomRotate: Math.random() * 10 - 5
31          }
32        : {};
33
34    setTrail(prev => {
35      const newTrail = [...prev];
36
37      if (newTrail.length === 0) {
38        newTrail.push({
39          id: idCounter.current++,
40          x: mouseX,
41          y: mouseY,
42          angle: 0,
43          ...createRandomData()
44        });
45      } else {
46        const last = newTrail[newTrail.length - 1];
47        const dx = mouseX - last.x;
48        const dy = mouseY - last.y;
49        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
50
51        if (distance >= spacing) {
52          let rawAngle = (Math.atan2(dy, dx) * 180) / Math.PI;
53          const computedAngle = followMouseDirection ? rawAngle : 0;
54          const steps = Math.floor(distance / spacing);
55
56          for (let i = 1; i <= steps; i++) {
57            const t = (spacing * i) / distance;
58            const newX = last.x + dx * t;
59            const newY = last.y + dy * t;
60
61            newTrail.push({
62              id: idCounter.current++,
63              x: newX,
64              y: newY,
65              angle: computedAngle,
66              ...createRandomData()
67            });
68          }
69        }
70      }
71
72      return newTrail.length > maxPoints ? newTrail.slice(newTrail.length - maxPoints) : newTrail;
73    });
74
75    lastMoveTimeRef.current = Date.now();
76  };
77
78  useEffect(() => {
79    const container = containerRef.current;
80    if (!container) return;
81
82    container.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
83    return () => container.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
84    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
85  }, []);
86
87  useEffect(() => {
88    const interval = setInterval(() => {
89      if (Date.now() - lastMoveTimeRef.current > 100) {
90        setTrail(prev => (prev.length > 0 ? prev.slice(1) : prev));
91      }
92    }, removalInterval);
93    return () => clearInterval(interval);
94  }, [removalInterval]);
95
96  return (
97    <div ref={containerRef} className="text-cursor-container">
98      <div className="text-cursor-inner">
99        <AnimatePresence>
100          {trail.map(item => (
101            <motion.div
102              key={item.id}
103              initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 1, rotate: item.angle }}
104              animate={{
105                opacity: 1,
106                scale: 1,
107                x: randomFloat ? [0, item.randomX || 0, 0] : 0,
108                y: randomFloat ? [0, item.randomY || 0, 0] : 0,
109                rotate: randomFloat ? [item.angle, item.angle + (item.randomRotate || 0), item.angle] : item.angle
110              }}
111              exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0 }}
112              transition={{
113                opacity: { duration: exitDuration, ease: 'easeOut' },
114                ...(randomFloat && {
115                  x: { duration: 2, ease: 'easeInOut', repeat: Infinity, repeatType: 'mirror' },
116                  y: { duration: 2, ease: 'easeInOut', repeat: Infinity, repeatType: 'mirror' },
117                  rotate: { duration: 2, ease: 'easeInOut', repeat: Infinity, repeatType: 'mirror' }
118                })
119              }}
120              className="text-cursor-item"
121              style={{ left: item.x, top: item.y }}
122            >
123              {text}
124            </motion.div>
125          ))}
126        </AnimatePresence>
127      </div>
128    </div>
129  );
130};
131
132export default TextCursor;
133

Extra Config/Code:
1.text-cursor-container {
2  width: 100%;
3  height: 100%;
4  position: relative;
5}
6
7.text-cursor-inner {
8  position: absolute;
9  top: 0;
10  left: 0;
11  right: 0;
12  bottom: 0;
13  pointer-events: none;
14}
15
16.text-cursor-item {
17  position: absolute;
18  user-select: none;
19  white-space: nowrap;
20  font-size: 1.875rem;
21}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Decrypted Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/DecryptedText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import DecryptedText from './DecryptedText';
2
3{/* Example 1: Defaults (hover to decrypt) */}
4<DecryptedText text="Hover me!" />
5
6{/* Example 2: Customized speed and characters */}
7<DecryptedText
8text="Customize me"
9speed={60}
10maxIterations={10}
11characters="ABCD1234!?"
12className="revealed"
13parentClassName="all-letters"
14encryptedClassName="encrypted"
15/>
16
17{/* Example 3: Animate on view (runs once) */}
18<div style={{ marginTop: '4rem' }}>
19<DecryptedText
20  text="This text animates when in view"
21  animateOn="view"
22  revealDirection="start"
23  sequential
24  useOriginalCharsOnly={false}
25/>
26</div>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';
2import { motion } from 'motion/react';
3
4const styles = {
5  wrapper: {
6    display: 'inline-block',
7    whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap'
8  },
9  srOnly: {
10    position: 'absolute',
11    width: '1px',
12    height: '1px',
13    padding: 0,
14    margin: '-1px',
15    overflow: 'hidden',
16    clip: 'rect(0,0,0,0)',
17    border: 0
18  }
19};
20
21export default function DecryptedText({
22  text,
23  speed = 50,
24  maxIterations = 10,
25  sequential = false,
26  revealDirection = 'start',
27  useOriginalCharsOnly = false,
28  characters = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz!@#$%^&*()_+',
29  className = '',
30  parentClassName = '',
31  encryptedClassName = '',
32  animateOn = 'hover',
33  ...props
34}) {
35  const [displayText, setDisplayText] = useState(text);
36  const [isHovering, setIsHovering] = useState(false);
37  const [isScrambling, setIsScrambling] = useState(false);
38  const [revealedIndices, setRevealedIndices] = useState(new Set());
39  const [hasAnimated, setHasAnimated] = useState(false);
40  const containerRef = useRef(null);
41
42  useEffect(() => {
43    let interval;
44    let currentIteration = 0;
45
46    const getNextIndex = revealedSet => {
47      const textLength = text.length;
48      switch (revealDirection) {
49        case 'start':
50          return revealedSet.size;
51        case 'end':
52          return textLength - 1 - revealedSet.size;
53        case 'center': {
54          const middle = Math.floor(textLength / 2);
55          const offset = Math.floor(revealedSet.size / 2);
56          const nextIndex = revealedSet.size % 2 === 0 ? middle + offset : middle - offset - 1;
57
58          if (nextIndex >= 0 && nextIndex < textLength && !revealedSet.has(nextIndex)) {
59            return nextIndex;
60          }
61
62          for (let i = 0; i < textLength; i++) {
63            if (!revealedSet.has(i)) return i;
64          }
65          return 0;
66        }
67        default:
68          return revealedSet.size;
69      }
70    };
71
72    const availableChars = useOriginalCharsOnly
73      ? Array.from(new Set(text.split(''))).filter(char => char !== ' ')
74      : characters.split('');
75
76    const shuffleText = (originalText, currentRevealed) => {
77      if (useOriginalCharsOnly) {
78        const positions = originalText.split('').map((char, i) => ({
79          char,
80          isSpace: char === ' ',
81          index: i,
82          isRevealed: currentRevealed.has(i)
83        }));
84
85        const nonSpaceChars = positions.filter(p => !p.isSpace && !p.isRevealed).map(p => p.char);
86
87        for (let i = nonSpaceChars.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
88          const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
89          [nonSpaceChars[i], nonSpaceChars[j]] = [nonSpaceChars[j], nonSpaceChars[i]];
90        }
91
92        let charIndex = 0;
93        return positions
94          .map(p => {
95            if (p.isSpace) return ' ';
96            if (p.isRevealed) return originalText[p.index];
97            return nonSpaceChars[charIndex++];
98          })
99          .join('');
100      } else {
101        return originalText
102          .split('')
103          .map((char, i) => {
104            if (char === ' ') return ' ';
105            if (currentRevealed.has(i)) return originalText[i];
106            return availableChars[Math.floor(Math.random() * availableChars.length)];
107          })
108          .join('');
109      }
110    };
111
112    if (isHovering) {
113      setIsScrambling(true);
114      interval = setInterval(() => {
115        setRevealedIndices(prevRevealed => {
116          if (sequential) {
117            if (prevRevealed.size < text.length) {
118              const nextIndex = getNextIndex(prevRevealed);
119              const newRevealed = new Set(prevRevealed);
120              newRevealed.add(nextIndex);
121              setDisplayText(shuffleText(text, newRevealed));
122              return newRevealed;
123            } else {
124              clearInterval(interval);
125              setIsScrambling(false);
126              return prevRevealed;
127            }
128          } else {
129            setDisplayText(shuffleText(text, prevRevealed));
130            currentIteration++;
131            if (currentIteration >= maxIterations) {
132              clearInterval(interval);
133              setIsScrambling(false);
134              setDisplayText(text);
135            }
136            return prevRevealed;
137          }
138        });
139      }, speed);
140    } else {
141      setDisplayText(text);
142      setRevealedIndices(new Set());
143      setIsScrambling(false);
144    }
145
146    return () => {
147      if (interval) clearInterval(interval);
148    };
149  }, [isHovering, text, speed, maxIterations, sequential, revealDirection, characters, useOriginalCharsOnly]);
150
151  useEffect(() => {
152    if (animateOn !== 'view' && animateOn !== 'both') return;
153
154    const observerCallback = entries => {
155      entries.forEach(entry => {
156        if (entry.isIntersecting && !hasAnimated) {
157          setIsHovering(true);
158          setHasAnimated(true);
159        }
160      });
161    };
162
163    const observerOptions = {
164      root: null,
165      rootMargin: '0px',
166      threshold: 0.1
167    };
168
169    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(observerCallback, observerOptions);
170    const currentRef = containerRef.current;
171    if (currentRef) {
172      observer.observe(currentRef);
173    }
174
175    return () => {
176      if (currentRef) {
177        observer.unobserve(currentRef);
178      }
179    };
180  }, [animateOn, hasAnimated]);
181
182  const hoverProps =
183    animateOn === 'hover' || animateOn === 'both'
184      ? {
185          onMouseEnter: () => setIsHovering(true),
186          onMouseLeave: () => setIsHovering(false)
187        }
188      : {};
189
190  return (
191    <motion.span className={parentClassName} ref={containerRef} style={styles.wrapper} {...hoverProps} {...props}>
192      <span style={styles.srOnly}>{displayText}</span>
193
194      <span aria-hidden="true">
195        {displayText.split('').map((char, index) => {
196          const isRevealedOrDone = revealedIndices.has(index) || !isScrambling || !isHovering;
197
198          return (
199            <span key={index} className={isRevealedOrDone ? className : encryptedClassName}>
200              {char}
201            </span>
202          );
203        })}
204      </span>
205    </motion.span>
206  );
207}
208

--------------------------------------------------

Component: True Focus

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/TrueFocus-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import TrueFocus from './TrueFocus';
2
3<TrueFocus 
4sentence="True Focus"
5manualMode={false}
6blurAmount={5}
7borderColor="#5227FF"
8animationDuration={0.5}
9pauseBetweenAnimations={1}
10/>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { motion } from 'motion/react';
3import './TrueFocus.css';
4
5const TrueFocus = ({
6  sentence = 'True Focus',
7  separator = ' ',
8  manualMode = false,
9  blurAmount = 5,
10  borderColor = 'green',
11  glowColor = 'rgba(0, 255, 0, 0.6)',
12  animationDuration = 0.5,
13  pauseBetweenAnimations = 1
14}) => {
15  const words = sentence.split(separator);
16  const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0);
17  const [lastActiveIndex, setLastActiveIndex] = useState(null);
18  const containerRef = useRef(null);
19  const wordRefs = useRef([]);
20  const [focusRect, setFocusRect] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0, width: 0, height: 0 });
21
22  useEffect(() => {
23    if (!manualMode) {
24      const interval = setInterval(
25        () => {
26          setCurrentIndex(prev => (prev + 1) % words.length);
27        },
28        (animationDuration + pauseBetweenAnimations) * 1000
29      );
30
31      return () => clearInterval(interval);
32    }
33  }, [manualMode, animationDuration, pauseBetweenAnimations, words.length]);
34
35  useEffect(() => {
36    if (currentIndex === null || currentIndex === -1) return;
37
38    if (!wordRefs.current[currentIndex] || !containerRef.current) return;
39
40    const parentRect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
41    const activeRect = wordRefs.current[currentIndex].getBoundingClientRect();
42
43    setFocusRect({
44      x: activeRect.left - parentRect.left,
45      y: activeRect.top - parentRect.top,
46      width: activeRect.width,
47      height: activeRect.height
48    });
49  }, [currentIndex, words.length]);
50
51  const handleMouseEnter = index => {
52    if (manualMode) {
53      setLastActiveIndex(index);
54      setCurrentIndex(index);
55    }
56  };
57
58  const handleMouseLeave = () => {
59    if (manualMode) {
60      setCurrentIndex(lastActiveIndex);
61    }
62  };
63
64  return (
65    <div className="focus-container" ref={containerRef}>
66      {words.map((word, index) => {
67        const isActive = index === currentIndex;
68        return (
69          <span
70            key={index}
71            ref={el => (wordRefs.current[index] = el)}
72            className={`focus-word ${manualMode ? 'manual' : ''} ${isActive && !manualMode ? 'active' : ''}`}
73            style={{
74              filter: manualMode
75                ? isActive
76                  ? `blur(0px)`
77                  : `blur(${blurAmount}px)`
78                : isActive
79                  ? `blur(0px)`
80                  : `blur(${blurAmount}px)`,
81              '--border-color': borderColor,
82              '--glow-color': glowColor,
83              transition: `filter ${animationDuration}s ease`
84            }}
85            onMouseEnter={() => handleMouseEnter(index)}
86            onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
87          >
88            {word}
89          </span>
90        );
91      })}
92
93      <motion.div
94        className="focus-frame"
95        animate={{
96          x: focusRect.x,
97          y: focusRect.y,
98          width: focusRect.width,
99          height: focusRect.height,
100          opacity: currentIndex >= 0 ? 1 : 0
101        }}
102        transition={{
103          duration: animationDuration
104        }}
105        style={{
106          '--border-color': borderColor,
107          '--glow-color': glowColor
108        }}
109      >
110        <span className="corner top-left"></span>
111        <span className="corner top-right"></span>
112        <span className="corner bottom-left"></span>
113        <span className="corner bottom-right"></span>
114      </motion.div>
115    </div>
116  );
117};
118
119export default TrueFocus;
120

Extra Config/Code:

2  position: relative;
3  display: flex;
4  gap: 1em;
5  justify-content: center;
6  align-items: center;
7  flex-wrap: wrap;
8  outline: none;
9  user-select: none;
10}
11
12.focus-word {
13  position: relative;
14  font-size: 3rem;
15  font-weight: 900;
16  cursor: pointer;
17  transition:
18    filter 0.3s ease,
19    color 0.3s ease;
20  outline: none;

22}
23
24.focus-word.active {

28.focus-frame {

34  border: none;
35}

37.corner {

41  border: 3px solid var(--border-color, #fff);
42  filter: drop-shadow(0px 0px 4px var(--border-color, #fff));
43  border-radius: 3px;
44  transition: none;
45}
46
47.top-left {
48  top: -10px;
49  left: -10px;
50  border-right: none;
51  border-bottom: none;
52}
53
54.top-right {
55  top: -10px;
56  right: -10px;
57  border-left: none;
58  border-bottom: none;
59}
60
61.bottom-left {
62  bottom: -10px;
63  left: -10px;
64  border-right: none;
65  border-top: none;
66}
67
68.bottom-right {
69  bottom: -10px;
70  right: -10px;
71  border-left: none;
72  border-top: none;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Scroll Float

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ScrollFloat-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import ScrollFloat from './ScrollFloat';
2
3<ScrollFloat
4  animationDuration={1}
5  ease='back.inOut(2)'
6  scrollStart='center bottom+=50%'
7  scrollEnd='bottom bottom-=40%'
8  stagger={0.03}
9>
10  React Bits
11</ScrollFloat>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4
5import './ScrollFloat.css';
6
7gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
8
9const ScrollFloat = ({
10  children,
11  scrollContainerRef,
12  containerClassName = '',
13  textClassName = '',
14  animationDuration = 1,
15  ease = 'back.inOut(2)',
16  scrollStart = 'center bottom+=50%',
17  scrollEnd = 'bottom bottom-=40%',
18  stagger = 0.03
19}) => {
20  const containerRef = useRef(null);
21
22  const splitText = useMemo(() => {
23    const text = typeof children === 'string' ? children : '';
24    return text.split('').map((char, index) => (
25      <span className="char" key={index}>
26        {char === ' ' ? '\u00A0' : char}
27      </span>
28    ));
29  }, [children]);
30
31  useEffect(() => {
32    const el = containerRef.current;
33    if (!el) return;
34
35    const scroller = scrollContainerRef && scrollContainerRef.current ? scrollContainerRef.current : window;
36
37    const charElements = el.querySelectorAll('.char');
38
39    gsap.fromTo(
40      charElements,
41      {
42        willChange: 'opacity, transform',
43        opacity: 0,
44        yPercent: 120,
45        scaleY: 2.3,
46        scaleX: 0.7,
47        transformOrigin: '50% 0%'
48      },
49      {
50        duration: animationDuration,
51        ease: ease,
52        opacity: 1,
53        yPercent: 0,
54        scaleY: 1,
55        scaleX: 1,
56        stagger: stagger,
57        scrollTrigger: {
58          trigger: el,
59          scroller,
60          start: scrollStart,
61          end: scrollEnd,
62          scrub: true
63        }
64      }
65    );
66  }, [scrollContainerRef, animationDuration, ease, scrollStart, scrollEnd, stagger]);
67
68  return (
69    <h2 ref={containerRef} className={`scroll-float ${containerClassName}`}>
70      <span className={`scroll-float-text ${textClassName}`}>{splitText}</span>
71    </h2>
72  );
73};
74
75export default ScrollFloat;
76

Extra Config/Code:

2  overflow: hidden;
3}

5.scroll-float-text {
6  display: inline-block;
7  font-size: clamp(1.6rem, 8vw, 10rem);
8  font-weight: 900;
9  text-align: center;
10  line-height: 1.5;
11}
12
13.char {
14  display: inline-block;
15}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Scroll Reveal

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ScrollReveal-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import ScrollReveal from './ScrollReveal';
2
3<ScrollReveal
4  baseOpacity={0.1}
5  enableBlur
6  baseRotation={3}
7  blurStrength={4}
8>
9  When does a man die? When he is hit by a bullet? No! When he suffers a disease?
10  No! When he ate a soup made out of a poisonous mushroom?
11  No! A man dies when he is forgotten!
12</ScrollReveal>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef, useMemo } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4
5import './ScrollReveal.css';
6
7gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
8
9const ScrollReveal = ({
10  children,
11  scrollContainerRef,
12  enableBlur = true,
13  baseOpacity = 0.1,
14  baseRotation = 3,
15  blurStrength = 4,
16  containerClassName = '',
17  textClassName = '',
18  rotationEnd = 'bottom bottom',
19  wordAnimationEnd = 'bottom bottom'
20}) => {
21  const containerRef = useRef(null);
22
23  const splitText = useMemo(() => {
24    const text = typeof children === 'string' ? children : '';
25    return text.split(/(\s+)/).map((word, index) => {
26      if (word.match(/^\s+$/)) return word;
27      return (
28        <span className="word" key={index}>
29          {word}
30        </span>
31      );
32    });
33  }, [children]);
34
35  useEffect(() => {
36    const el = containerRef.current;
37    if (!el) return;
38
39    const scroller = scrollContainerRef && scrollContainerRef.current ? scrollContainerRef.current : window;
40
41    gsap.fromTo(
42      el,
43      { transformOrigin: '0% 50%', rotate: baseRotation },
44      {
45        ease: 'none',
46        rotate: 0,
47        scrollTrigger: {
48          trigger: el,
49          scroller,
50          start: 'top bottom',
51          end: rotationEnd,
52          scrub: true
53        }
54      }
55    );
56
57    const wordElements = el.querySelectorAll('.word');
58
59    gsap.fromTo(
60      wordElements,
61      { opacity: baseOpacity, willChange: 'opacity' },
62      {
63        ease: 'none',
64        opacity: 1,
65        stagger: 0.05,
66        scrollTrigger: {
67          trigger: el,
68          scroller,
69          start: 'top bottom-=20%',
70          end: wordAnimationEnd,
71          scrub: true
72        }
73      }
74    );
75
76    if (enableBlur) {
77      gsap.fromTo(
78        wordElements,
79        { filter: `blur(${blurStrength}px)` },
80        {
81          ease: 'none',
82          filter: 'blur(0px)',
83          stagger: 0.05,
84          scrollTrigger: {
85            trigger: el,
86            scroller,
87            start: 'top bottom-=20%',
88            end: wordAnimationEnd,
89            scrub: true
90          }
91        }
92      );
93    }
94
95    return () => {
96      ScrollTrigger.getAll().forEach(trigger => trigger.kill());
97    };
98  }, [scrollContainerRef, enableBlur, baseRotation, baseOpacity, rotationEnd, wordAnimationEnd, blurStrength]);
99
100  return (
101    <h2 ref={containerRef} className={`scroll-reveal ${containerClassName}`}>
102      <p className={`scroll-reveal-text ${textClassName}`}>{splitText}</p>
103    </h2>
104  );
105};
106
107export default ScrollReveal;
108

Extra Config/Code:
1.scroll-reveal {
2  margin: 20px 0;
3}
4
5.scroll-reveal-text {
6  font-size: clamp(1.6rem, 4vw, 3rem);
7  line-height: 1.5;
8  font-weight: 600;
9}
10
11.word {
12  display: inline-block;
13}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Ascii Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ASCIIText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// Component ported and enhanced from https://codepen.io/JuanFuentes/pen/eYEeoyE
2  
3import ASCIIText from './ASCIIText';
4
5<ASCIIText
6  text='hello_world'
7  enableWaves
8  asciiFontSize={8}
9  text="Hey!"
10/>

Code:
1// Component ported and enhanced from https://codepen.io/JuanFuentes/pen/eYEeoyE
2
3import { useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
4import * as THREE from 'three';
5
6const vertexShader = `
7varying vec2 vUv;
8uniform float uTime;
9uniform float mouse;
10uniform float uEnableWaves;
11
12void main() {
13    vUv = uv;
14    float time = uTime * 5.;
15
16    float waveFactor = uEnableWaves;
17
18    vec3 transformed = position;
19
20    transformed.x += sin(time + position.y) * 0.5 * waveFactor;
21    transformed.y += cos(time + position.z) * 0.15 * waveFactor;
22    transformed.z += sin(time + position.x) * waveFactor;
23
24    gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(transformed, 1.0);
25}
26`;
27
28const fragmentShader = `
29varying vec2 vUv;
30uniform float mouse;
31uniform float uTime;
32uniform sampler2D uTexture;
33
34void main() {
35    float time = uTime;
36    vec2 pos = vUv;
37    
38    float move = sin(time + mouse) * 0.01;
39    float r = texture2D(uTexture, pos + cos(time * 2. - time + pos.x) * .01).r;
40    float g = texture2D(uTexture, pos + tan(time * .5 + pos.x - time) * .01).g;
41    float b = texture2D(uTexture, pos - cos(time * 2. + time + pos.y) * .01).b;
42    float a = texture2D(uTexture, pos).a;
43    gl_FragColor = vec4(r, g, b, a);
44}
45`;
46
47Math.map = function (n, start, stop, start2, stop2) {
48  return ((n - start) / (stop - start)) * (stop2 - start2) + start2;
49};
50
51const PX_RATIO = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.devicePixelRatio : 1;
52
53class AsciiFilter {
54  constructor(renderer, { fontSize, fontFamily, charset, invert } = {}) {
55    this.renderer = renderer;
56    this.domElement = document.createElement('div');
57    this.domElement.style.position = 'absolute';
58    this.domElement.style.top = '0';
59    this.domElement.style.left = '0';
60    this.domElement.style.width = '100%';
61    this.domElement.style.height = '100%';
62
63    this.pre = document.createElement('pre');
64    this.domElement.appendChild(this.pre);
65
66    this.canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
67    this.context = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
68    this.domElement.appendChild(this.canvas);
69
70    this.deg = 0;
71    this.invert = invert ?? true;
72    this.fontSize = fontSize ?? 12;
73    this.fontFamily = fontFamily ?? "'Courier New', monospace";
74    this.charset = charset ?? ' .\'`^",:;Il!i~+_-?][}{1)(|/tfjrxnuvczXYUJCLQ0OZmwqpdbkhao*#MW&8%B@$';
75
76    this.context.webkitImageSmoothingEnabled = false;
77    this.context.mozImageSmoothingEnabled = false;
78    this.context.msImageSmoothingEnabled = false;
79    this.context.imageSmoothingEnabled = false;
80
81    this.onMouseMove = this.onMouseMove.bind(this);
82    document.addEventListener('mousemove', this.onMouseMove);
83  }
84
85  setSize(width, height) {
86    this.width = width;
87    this.height = height;
88    this.renderer.setSize(width, height);
89    this.reset();
90
91    this.center = { x: width / 2, y: height / 2 };
92    this.mouse = { x: this.center.x, y: this.center.y };
93  }
94
95  reset() {
96    this.context.font = `${this.fontSize}px ${this.fontFamily}`;
97    const charWidth = this.context.measureText('A').width;
98
99    this.cols = Math.floor(this.width / (this.fontSize * (charWidth / this.fontSize)));
100    this.rows = Math.floor(this.height / this.fontSize);
101
102    this.canvas.width = this.cols;
103    this.canvas.height = this.rows;
104    this.pre.style.fontFamily = this.fontFamily;
105    this.pre.style.fontSize = `${this.fontSize}px`;
106    this.pre.style.margin = '0';
107    this.pre.style.padding = '0';
108    this.pre.style.lineHeight = '1em';
109    this.pre.style.position = 'absolute';
110    this.pre.style.left = '0';
111    this.pre.style.top = '0';
112    this.pre.style.zIndex = '9';
113    this.pre.style.backgroundAttachment = 'fixed';
114    this.pre.style.mixBlendMode = 'difference';
115  }
116
117  render(scene, camera) {
118    this.renderer.render(scene, camera);
119
120    const w = this.canvas.width;
121    const h = this.canvas.height;
122    this.context.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
123    if (this.context && w && h) {
124      this.context.drawImage(this.renderer.domElement, 0, 0, w, h);
125    }
126
127    this.asciify(this.context, w, h);
128    this.hue();
129  }
130
131  onMouseMove(e) {
132    this.mouse = { x: e.clientX * PX_RATIO, y: e.clientY * PX_RATIO };
133  }
134
135  get dx() {
136    return this.mouse.x - this.center.x;
137  }
138
139  get dy() {
140    return this.mouse.y - this.center.y;
141  }
142
143  hue() {
144    const deg = (Math.atan2(this.dy, this.dx) * 180) / Math.PI;
145    this.deg += (deg - this.deg) * 0.075;
146    this.domElement.style.filter = `hue-rotate(${this.deg.toFixed(1)}deg)`;
147  }
148
149  asciify(ctx, w, h) {
150    if (w && h) {
151      const imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h).data;
152      let str = '';
153      for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) {
154        for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
155          const i = x * 4 + y * 4 * w;
156          const [r, g, b, a] = [imgData[i], imgData[i + 1], imgData[i + 2], imgData[i + 3]];
157
158          if (a === 0) {
159            str += ' ';
160            continue;
161          }
162
163          let gray = (0.3 * r + 0.6 * g + 0.1 * b) / 255;
164          let idx = Math.floor((1 - gray) * (this.charset.length - 1));
165          if (this.invert) idx = this.charset.length - idx - 1;
166          str += this.charset[idx];
167        }
168        str += '\n';
169      }
170      this.pre.innerHTML = str;
171    }
172  }
173
174  dispose() {
175    document.removeEventListener('mousemove', this.onMouseMove);
176  }
177}
178
179class CanvasTxt {
180  constructor(txt, { fontSize = 200, fontFamily = 'Arial', color = '#fdf9f3' } = {}) {
181    this.canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
182    this.context = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
183    this.txt = txt;
184    this.fontSize = fontSize;
185    this.fontFamily = fontFamily;
186    this.color = color;
187
188    this.font = `600 ${this.fontSize}px ${this.fontFamily}`;
189  }
190
191  resize() {
192    this.context.font = this.font;
193    const metrics = this.context.measureText(this.txt);
194
195    const textWidth = Math.ceil(metrics.width) + 20;
196    const textHeight = Math.ceil(metrics.actualBoundingBoxAscent + metrics.actualBoundingBoxDescent) + 20;
197
198    this.canvas.width = textWidth;
199    this.canvas.height = textHeight;
200  }
201
202  render() {
203    this.context.clearRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
204    this.context.fillStyle = this.color;
205    this.context.font = this.font;
206
207    const metrics = this.context.measureText(this.txt);
208    const yPos = 10 + metrics.actualBoundingBoxAscent;
209
210    this.context.fillText(this.txt, 10, yPos);
211  }
212
213  get width() {
214    return this.canvas.width;
215  }
216
217  get height() {
218    return this.canvas.height;
219  }
220
221  get texture() {
222    return this.canvas;
223  }
224}
225
226class CanvAscii {
227  constructor(
228    { text, asciiFontSize, textFontSize, textColor, planeBaseHeight, enableWaves },
229    containerElem,
230    width,
231    height
232  ) {
233    this.textString = text;
234    this.asciiFontSize = asciiFontSize;
235    this.textFontSize = textFontSize;
236    this.textColor = textColor;
237    this.planeBaseHeight = planeBaseHeight;
238    this.container = containerElem;
239    this.width = width;
240    this.height = height;
241    this.enableWaves = enableWaves;
242
243    this.camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(45, this.width / this.height, 1, 1000);
244    this.camera.position.z = 30;
245
246    this.scene = new THREE.Scene();
247    this.mouse = { x: this.width / 2, y: this.height / 2 };
248
249    this.onMouseMove = this.onMouseMove.bind(this);
250  }
251
252  async init() {
253    try {
254      await document.fonts.load('600 200px "IBM Plex Mono"');
255      await document.fonts.load('500 12px "IBM Plex Mono"');
256    } catch (e) {
257      // Font loading failed, continue with fallback
258    }
259    await document.fonts.ready;
260
261    this.setMesh();
262    this.setRenderer();
263  }
264
265  setMesh() {
266    this.textCanvas = new CanvasTxt(this.textString, {
267      fontSize: this.textFontSize,
268      fontFamily: 'IBM Plex Mono',
269      color: this.textColor
270    });
271    this.textCanvas.resize();
272    this.textCanvas.render();
273
274    this.texture = new THREE.CanvasTexture(this.textCanvas.texture);
275    this.texture.minFilter = THREE.NearestFilter;
276
277    const textAspect = this.textCanvas.width / this.textCanvas.height;
278    const baseH = this.planeBaseHeight;
279    const planeW = baseH * textAspect;
280    const planeH = baseH;
281
282    this.geometry = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(planeW, planeH, 36, 36);
283    this.material = new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
284      vertexShader,
285      fragmentShader,
286      transparent: true,
287      uniforms: {
288        uTime: { value: 0 },
289        mouse: { value: 1.0 },
290        uTexture: { value: this.texture },
291        uEnableWaves: { value: this.enableWaves ? 1.0 : 0.0 }
292      }
293    });
294
295    this.mesh = new THREE.Mesh(this.geometry, this.material);
296    this.scene.add(this.mesh);
297  }
298
299  setRenderer() {
300    this.renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: false, alpha: true });
301    this.renderer.setPixelRatio(1);
302    this.renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, 0);
303
304    this.filter = new AsciiFilter(this.renderer, {
305      fontFamily: 'IBM Plex Mono',
306      fontSize: this.asciiFontSize,
307      invert: true
308    });
309
310    this.container.appendChild(this.filter.domElement);
311    this.setSize(this.width, this.height);
312
313    this.container.addEventListener('mousemove', this.onMouseMove);
314    this.container.addEventListener('touchmove', this.onMouseMove);
315  }
316
317  setSize(w, h) {
318    this.width = w;
319    this.height = h;
320
321    this.camera.aspect = w / h;
322    this.camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
323
324    this.filter.setSize(w, h);
325
326    this.center = { x: w / 2, y: h / 2 };
327  }
328
329  load() {
330    this.animate();
331  }
332
333  onMouseMove(evt) {
334    const e = evt.touches ? evt.touches[0] : evt;
335    const bounds = this.container.getBoundingClientRect();
336    const x = e.clientX - bounds.left;
337    const y = e.clientY - bounds.top;
338    this.mouse = { x, y };
339  }
340
341  animate() {
342    const animateFrame = () => {
343      this.animationFrameId = requestAnimationFrame(animateFrame);
344      this.render();
345    };
346    animateFrame();
347  }
348
349  render() {
350    const time = new Date().getTime() * 0.001;
351
352    this.textCanvas.render();
353    this.texture.needsUpdate = true;
354
355    this.mesh.material.uniforms.uTime.value = Math.sin(time);
356
357    this.updateRotation();
358    this.filter.render(this.scene, this.camera);
359  }
360
361  updateRotation() {
362    const x = Math.map(this.mouse.y, 0, this.height, 0.5, -0.5);
363    const y = Math.map(this.mouse.x, 0, this.width, -0.5, 0.5);
364
365    this.mesh.rotation.x += (x - this.mesh.rotation.x) * 0.05;
366    this.mesh.rotation.y += (y - this.mesh.rotation.y) * 0.05;
367  }
368
369  clear() {
370    this.scene.traverse(obj => {
371      if (obj.isMesh && typeof obj.material === 'object' && obj.material !== null) {
372        Object.keys(obj.material).forEach(key => {
373          const matProp = obj.material[key];
374          if (matProp !== null && typeof matProp === 'object' && typeof matProp.dispose === 'function') {
375            matProp.dispose();
376          }
377        });
378        obj.material.dispose();
379        obj.geometry.dispose();
380      }
381    });
382    this.scene.clear();
383  }
384
385  dispose() {
386    cancelAnimationFrame(this.animationFrameId);
387    if (this.filter) {
388      this.filter.dispose();
389      if (this.filter.domElement.parentNode) {
390        this.container.removeChild(this.filter.domElement);
391      }
392    }
393    this.container.removeEventListener('mousemove', this.onMouseMove);
394    this.container.removeEventListener('touchmove', this.onMouseMove);
395    this.clear();
396    if (this.renderer) {
397      this.renderer.dispose();
398    }
399  }
400}
401
402export default function ASCIIText({
403  text = 'David!',
404  asciiFontSize = 8,
405  textFontSize = 200,
406  textColor = '#fdf9f3',
407  planeBaseHeight = 8,
408  enableWaves = true
409}) {
410  const containerRef = useRef(null);
411  const asciiRef = useRef(null);
412
413  useEffect(() => {
414    if (!containerRef.current) return;
415
416    let cancelled = false;
417    let observer = null;
418    let ro = null;
419
420    const createAndInit = async (container, w, h) => {
421      const instance = new CanvAscii(
422        { text, asciiFontSize, textFontSize, textColor, planeBaseHeight, enableWaves },
423        container,
424        w,
425        h
426      );
427      await instance.init();
428      return instance;
429    };
430
431    const setup = async () => {
432      const { width, height } = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
433
434      if (width === 0 || height === 0) {
435        observer = new IntersectionObserver(
436          async ([entry]) => {
437            if (cancelled) return;
438            if (entry.isIntersecting && entry.boundingClientRect.width > 0 && entry.boundingClientRect.height > 0) {
439              const { width: w, height: h } = entry.boundingClientRect;
440              observer.disconnect();
441              observer = null;
442
443              if (!cancelled) {
444                asciiRef.current = await createAndInit(containerRef.current, w, h);
445                if (!cancelled && asciiRef.current) {
446                  asciiRef.current.load();
447                }
448              }
449            }
450          },
451          { threshold: 0.1 }
452        );
453        observer.observe(containerRef.current);
454        return;
455      }
456
457      asciiRef.current = await createAndInit(containerRef.current, width, height);
458      if (!cancelled && asciiRef.current) {
459        asciiRef.current.load();
460
461        ro = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
462          if (!entries[0] || !asciiRef.current) return;
463          const { width: w, height: h } = entries[0].contentRect;
464          if (w > 0 && h > 0) {
465            asciiRef.current.setSize(w, h);
466          }
467        });
468        ro.observe(containerRef.current);
469      }
470    };
471
472    setup();
473
474    return () => {
475      cancelled = true;
476      if (observer) observer.disconnect();
477      if (ro) ro.disconnect();
478      if (asciiRef.current) {
479        asciiRef.current.dispose();
480        asciiRef.current = null;
481      }
482    };
483  }, [text, asciiFontSize, textFontSize, textColor, planeBaseHeight, enableWaves]);
484
485  return (
486    <div
487      ref={containerRef}
488      className="ascii-text-container"
489      style={{
490        position: 'absolute',
491        width: '100%',
492        height: '100%'
493      }}
494    >
495      <style>{`
496        @import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=IBM+Plex+Mono:wght@500;600&display=swap');
497
498        .ascii-text-container canvas {
499          position: absolute;
500          left: 0;
501          top: 0;
502          width: 100%;
503          height: 100%;
504          image-rendering: optimizeSpeed;
505          image-rendering: -moz-crisp-edges;
506          image-rendering: -o-crisp-edges;
507          image-rendering: -webkit-optimize-contrast;
508          image-rendering: optimize-contrast;
509          image-rendering: crisp-edges;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Scrambled Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ScrambledText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// Component inspired by Tom Miller from the GSAP community
2// https://codepen.io/creativeocean/pen/NPWLwJM
3
4import ScrambledText from './ScrambledText';
5  
6<ScrambledText
7  className="scrambled-text-demo"
8  radius={100}
9  duration={1.2}
10  speed={0.5}
11  scrambleChars=".:"
12>
13  Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. 
14  Similique pariatur dignissimos porro eius quam doloremque 
15  et enim velit nobis maxime.
16</ScrambledText>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { SplitText } from 'gsap/SplitText';
4import { ScrambleTextPlugin } from 'gsap/ScrambleTextPlugin';
5
6import './ScrambledText.css';
7
8gsap.registerPlugin(SplitText, ScrambleTextPlugin);
9
10const ScrambledText = ({
11  radius = 100,
12  duration = 1.2,
13  speed = 0.5,
14  scrambleChars = '.:',
15  className = '',
16  style = {},
17  children
18}) => {
19  const rootRef = useRef(null);
20  const charsRef = useRef([]);
21
22  useEffect(() => {
23    if (!rootRef.current) return;
24
25    const split = SplitText.create(rootRef.current.querySelector('p'), {
26      type: 'chars',
27      charsClass: 'char'
28    });
29    charsRef.current = split.chars;
30
31    charsRef.current.forEach(c => {
32      gsap.set(c, {
33        display: 'inline-block',
34        attr: { 'data-content': c.innerHTML }
35      });
36    });
37
38    const handleMove = e => {
39      charsRef.current.forEach(c => {
40        const { left, top, width, height } = c.getBoundingClientRect();
41        const dx = e.clientX - (left + width / 2);
42        const dy = e.clientY - (top + height / 2);
43        const dist = Math.hypot(dx, dy);
44
45        if (dist < radius) {
46          gsap.to(c, {
47            overwrite: true,
48            duration: duration * (1 - dist / radius),
49            scrambleText: {
50              text: c.dataset.content || '',
51              chars: scrambleChars,
52              speed
53            },
54            ease: 'none'
55          });
56        }
57      });
58    };
59
60    const el = rootRef.current;
61    el.addEventListener('pointermove', handleMove);
62
63    return () => {
64      el.removeEventListener('pointermove', handleMove);
65      split.revert();
66    };
67  }, [radius, duration, speed, scrambleChars]);
68
69  return (
70    <div ref={rootRef} className={`text-block ${className}`} style={style}>
71      <p>{children}</p>
72    </div>
73  );
74};
75
76export default ScrambledText;
77

Extra Config/Code:
1.text-block {
2  margin: 7vw;
3  max-width: 800px;
4  font-family: monospace;
5  font-size: clamp(14px, 4vw, 32px);
6  color: #fff;
7}
8
9.char {
10  will-change: transform;
11  display: inline-block;
12}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Rotating Text

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/RotatingText-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import RotatingText from './RotatingText'
2  
3<RotatingText
4  texts={['React', 'Bits', 'Is', 'Cool!']}
5  mainClassName="px-2 sm:px-2 md:px-3 bg-cyan-300 text-black overflow-hidden py-0.5 sm:py-1 md:py-2 justify-center rounded-lg"
6  staggerFrom={"last"}
7  initial={{ y: "100%" }}
8  animate={{ y: 0 }}
9  exit={{ y: "-120%" }}
10  staggerDuration={0.025}
11  splitLevelClassName="overflow-hidden pb-0.5 sm:pb-1 md:pb-1"
12  transition={{ type: "spring", damping: 30, stiffness: 400 }}
13  rotationInterval={2000}
14/>

Code:
1'use client';
2
3import { forwardRef, useCallback, useEffect, useImperativeHandle, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
4import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'motion/react';
5
6import './RotatingText.css';
7
8function cn(...classes) {
9  return classes.filter(Boolean).join(' ');
10}
11
12const RotatingText = forwardRef((props, ref) => {
13  const {
14    texts,
15    transition = { type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 },
16    initial = { y: '100%', opacity: 0 },
17    animate = { y: 0, opacity: 1 },
18    exit = { y: '-120%', opacity: 0 },
19    animatePresenceMode = 'wait',
20    animatePresenceInitial = false,
21    rotationInterval = 2000,
22    staggerDuration = 0,
23    staggerFrom = 'first',
24    loop = true,
25    auto = true,
26    splitBy = 'characters',
27    onNext,
28    mainClassName,
29    splitLevelClassName,
30    elementLevelClassName,
31    ...rest
32  } = props;
33
34  const [currentTextIndex, setCurrentTextIndex] = useState(0);
35
36  const splitIntoCharacters = text => {
37    if (typeof Intl !== 'undefined' && Intl.Segmenter) {
38      const segmenter = new Intl.Segmenter('en', { granularity: 'grapheme' });
39      return Array.from(segmenter.segment(text), segment => segment.segment);
40    }
41    return Array.from(text);
42  };
43
44  const elements = useMemo(() => {
45    const currentText = texts[currentTextIndex];
46    if (splitBy === 'characters') {
47      const words = currentText.split(' ');
48      return words.map((word, i) => ({
49        characters: splitIntoCharacters(word),
50        needsSpace: i !== words.length - 1
51      }));
52    }
53    if (splitBy === 'words') {
54      return currentText.split(' ').map((word, i, arr) => ({
55        characters: [word],
56        needsSpace: i !== arr.length - 1
57      }));
58    }
59    if (splitBy === 'lines') {
60      return currentText.split('\n').map((line, i, arr) => ({
61        characters: [line],
62        needsSpace: i !== arr.length - 1
63      }));
64    }
65
66    return currentText.split(splitBy).map((part, i, arr) => ({
67      characters: [part],
68      needsSpace: i !== arr.length - 1
69    }));
70  }, [texts, currentTextIndex, splitBy]);
71
72  const getStaggerDelay = useCallback(
73    (index, totalChars) => {
74      const total = totalChars;
75      if (staggerFrom === 'first') return index * staggerDuration;
76      if (staggerFrom === 'last') return (total - 1 - index) * staggerDuration;
77      if (staggerFrom === 'center') {
78        const center = Math.floor(total / 2);
79        return Math.abs(center - index) * staggerDuration;
80      }
81      if (staggerFrom === 'random') {
82        const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * total);
83        return Math.abs(randomIndex - index) * staggerDuration;
84      }
85      return Math.abs(staggerFrom - index) * staggerDuration;
86    },
87    [staggerFrom, staggerDuration]
88  );
89
90  const handleIndexChange = useCallback(
91    newIndex => {
92      setCurrentTextIndex(newIndex);
93      if (onNext) onNext(newIndex);
94    },
95    [onNext]
96  );
97
98  const next = useCallback(() => {
99    const nextIndex = currentTextIndex === texts.length - 1 ? (loop ? 0 : currentTextIndex) : currentTextIndex + 1;
100    if (nextIndex !== currentTextIndex) {
101      handleIndexChange(nextIndex);
102    }
103  }, [currentTextIndex, texts.length, loop, handleIndexChange]);
104
105  const previous = useCallback(() => {
106    const prevIndex = currentTextIndex === 0 ? (loop ? texts.length - 1 : currentTextIndex) : currentTextIndex - 1;
107    if (prevIndex !== currentTextIndex) {
108      handleIndexChange(prevIndex);
109    }
110  }, [currentTextIndex, texts.length, loop, handleIndexChange]);
111
112  const jumpTo = useCallback(
113    index => {
114      const validIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(index, texts.length - 1));
115      if (validIndex !== currentTextIndex) {
116        handleIndexChange(validIndex);
117      }
118    },
119    [texts.length, currentTextIndex, handleIndexChange]
120  );
121
122  const reset = useCallback(() => {
123    if (currentTextIndex !== 0) {
124      handleIndexChange(0);
125    }
126  }, [currentTextIndex, handleIndexChange]);
127
128  useImperativeHandle(
129    ref,
130    () => ({
131      next,
132      previous,
133      jumpTo,
134      reset
135    }),
136    [next, previous, jumpTo, reset]
137  );
138
139  useEffect(() => {
140    if (!auto) return;
141    const intervalId = setInterval(next, rotationInterval);
142    return () => clearInterval(intervalId);
143  }, [next, rotationInterval, auto]);
144
145  return (
146    <motion.span className={cn('text-rotate', mainClassName)} {...rest} layout transition={transition}>
147      <span className="text-rotate-sr-only">{texts[currentTextIndex]}</span>
148      <AnimatePresence mode={animatePresenceMode} initial={animatePresenceInitial}>
149        <motion.span
150          key={currentTextIndex}
151          className={cn(splitBy === 'lines' ? 'text-rotate-lines' : 'text-rotate')}
152          layout
153          aria-hidden="true"
154        >
155          {elements.map((wordObj, wordIndex, array) => {
156            const previousCharsCount = array.slice(0, wordIndex).reduce((sum, word) => sum + word.characters.length, 0);
157            return (
158              <span key={wordIndex} className={cn('text-rotate-word', splitLevelClassName)}>
159                {wordObj.characters.map((char, charIndex) => (
160                  <motion.span
161                    key={charIndex}
162                    initial={initial}
163                    animate={animate}
164                    exit={exit}
165                    transition={{
166                      ...transition,
167                      delay: getStaggerDelay(
168                        previousCharsCount + charIndex,
169                        array.reduce((sum, word) => sum + word.characters.length, 0)
170                      )
171                    }}
172                    className={cn('text-rotate-element', elementLevelClassName)}
173                  >
174                    {char}
175                  </motion.span>
176                ))}
177                {wordObj.needsSpace && <span className="text-rotate-space"> </span>}
178              </span>
179            );
180          })}
181        </motion.span>
182      </AnimatePresence>
183    </motion.span>
184  );
185});
186
187RotatingText.displayName = 'RotatingText';
188export default RotatingText;
189

Extra Config/Code:
1.text-rotate {
2  display: flex;
3  flex-wrap: wrap;
4  white-space: pre-wrap;
5  position: relative;
6}
7
8.text-rotate-sr-only {
9  position: absolute;
10  width: 1px;
11  height: 1px;
12  padding: 0;
13  margin: -1px;
14  overflow: hidden;
15  clip: rect(0, 0, 0, 0);
16  white-space: nowrap;
17  border: 0;
18}
19
20.text-rotate-word {
21  display: inline-flex;
22}
23
24.text-rotate-lines {
25  display: flex;
26  flex-direction: column;
27  width: 100%;
28}
29
30.text-rotate-element {
31  display: inline-block;
32}
33
34.text-rotate-space {
35  white-space: pre;
36}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Scroll Velocity

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ScrollVelocity-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import ScrollVelocity from './ScrollVelocity';
2  
3<ScrollVelocity
4  texts={['React Bits', 'Scroll Down']} 
5  velocity={100}
6  className="custom-scroll-text"
7/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useLayoutEffect, useState } from 'react';
2import {
3  motion,
4  useScroll,
5  useSpring,
6  useTransform,
7  useMotionValue,
8  useVelocity,
9  useAnimationFrame
10} from 'motion/react';
11import './ScrollVelocity.css';
12
13function useElementWidth(ref) {
14  const [width, setWidth] = useState(0);
15
16  useLayoutEffect(() => {
17    function updateWidth() {
18      if (ref.current) {
19        setWidth(ref.current.offsetWidth);
20      }
21    }
22    updateWidth();
23    window.addEventListener('resize', updateWidth);
24    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', updateWidth);
25  }, [ref]);
26
27  return width;
28}
29
30export const ScrollVelocity = ({
31  scrollContainerRef,
32  texts = [],
33  velocity = 100,
34  className = '',
35  damping = 50,
36  stiffness = 400,
37  numCopies = 6,
38  velocityMapping = { input: [0, 1000], output: [0, 5] },
39  parallaxClassName = 'parallax',
40  scrollerClassName = 'scroller',
41  parallaxStyle,
42  scrollerStyle
43}) => {
44  function VelocityText({
45    children,
46    baseVelocity = velocity,
47    scrollContainerRef,
48    className = '',
49    damping,
50    stiffness,
51    numCopies,
52    velocityMapping,
53    parallaxClassName,
54    scrollerClassName,
55    parallaxStyle,
56    scrollerStyle
57  }) {
58    const baseX = useMotionValue(0);
59    const scrollOptions = scrollContainerRef ? { container: scrollContainerRef } : {};
60    const { scrollY } = useScroll(scrollOptions);
61    const scrollVelocity = useVelocity(scrollY);
62    const smoothVelocity = useSpring(scrollVelocity, {
63      damping: damping ?? 50,
64      stiffness: stiffness ?? 400
65    });
66    const velocityFactor = useTransform(
67      smoothVelocity,
68      velocityMapping?.input || [0, 1000],
69      velocityMapping?.output || [0, 5],
70      { clamp: false }
71    );
72
73    const copyRef = useRef(null);
74    const copyWidth = useElementWidth(copyRef);
75
76    function wrap(min, max, v) {
77      const range = max - min;
78      const mod = (((v - min) % range) + range) % range;
79      return mod + min;
80    }
81
82    const x = useTransform(baseX, v => {
83      if (copyWidth === 0) return '0px';
84      return `${wrap(-copyWidth, 0, v)}px`;
85    });
86
87    const directionFactor = useRef(1);
88    useAnimationFrame((t, delta) => {
89      let moveBy = directionFactor.current * baseVelocity * (delta / 1000);
90
91      if (velocityFactor.get() < 0) {
92        directionFactor.current = -1;
93      } else if (velocityFactor.get() > 0) {
94        directionFactor.current = 1;
95      }
96
97      moveBy += directionFactor.current * moveBy * velocityFactor.get();
98      baseX.set(baseX.get() + moveBy);
99    });
100
101    const spans = [];
102    for (let i = 0; i < numCopies; i++) {
103      spans.push(
104        <span className={className} key={i} ref={i === 0 ? copyRef : null}>
105          {children}
106        </span>
107      );
108    }
109
110    return (
111      <div className={parallaxClassName} style={parallaxStyle}>
112        <motion.div className={scrollerClassName} style={{ x, ...scrollerStyle }}>
113          {spans}
114        </motion.div>
115      </div>
116    );
117  }
118
119  return (
120    <section>
121      {texts.map((text, index) => (
122        <VelocityText
123          key={index}
124          className={className}
125          baseVelocity={index % 2 !== 0 ? -velocity : velocity}
126          scrollContainerRef={scrollContainerRef}
127          damping={damping}
128          stiffness={stiffness}
129          numCopies={numCopies}
130          velocityMapping={velocityMapping}
131          parallaxClassName={parallaxClassName}
132          scrollerClassName={scrollerClassName}
133          parallaxStyle={parallaxStyle}
134          scrollerStyle={scrollerStyle}
135        >
136          {text}&nbsp;
137        </VelocityText>
138      ))}
139    </section>
140  );
141};
142
143export default ScrollVelocity;
144

Extra Config/Code:
1.parallax {
2  position: relative;
3  overflow: hidden;
4}
5
6.scroller {
7  display: flex;
8  white-space: nowrap;
9  text-align: center;
10  font-family: sans-serif;
11  font-size: 2.25rem;
12  font-weight: bold;
13  letter-spacing: -0.02em;
14  filter: drop-shadow(0 1px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1));
15}
16
17.scroller span {
18  flex-shrink: 0;
19}
20
21@media (min-width: 768px) {
22  .scroller {
23    font-size: 5rem;
24    line-height: 5rem;
25  }
26}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Variable Proximity

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/VariableProximity-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import { useRef } from 'react';
2import VariableProximity from './VariableProximity';
3
4const containerRef = useRef(null);
5
6<div
7ref={containerRef}
8style={{position: 'relative'}}
9>
10  <VariableProximity
11    label={'Hover me! And then star React Bits on GitHub, or else...'}
12    className={'variable-proximity-demo'}
13    fromFontVariationSettings="'wght' 400, 'opsz' 9"
14    toFontVariationSettings="'wght' 1000, 'opsz' 40"
15    containerRef={containerRef}
16    radius={100}
17    falloff='linear'
18    falloff="linear"
19/>
20</div>

Code:
1import { forwardRef, useMemo, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
2import { motion } from 'motion/react';
3import './VariableProximity.css';
4
5function useAnimationFrame(callback) {
6  useEffect(() => {
7    let frameId;
8    const loop = () => {
9      callback();
10      frameId = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
11    };
12    frameId = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
13    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(frameId);
14  }, [callback]);
15}
16
17function useMousePositionRef(containerRef) {
18  const positionRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
19
20  useEffect(() => {
21    const updatePosition = (x, y) => {
22      if (containerRef?.current) {
23        const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
24        positionRef.current = { x: x - rect.left, y: y - rect.top };
25      } else {
26        positionRef.current = { x, y };
27      }
28    };
29
30    const handleMouseMove = ev => updatePosition(ev.clientX, ev.clientY);
31    const handleTouchMove = ev => {
32      const touch = ev.touches[0];
33      updatePosition(touch.clientX, touch.clientY);
34    };
35
36    window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
37    window.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
38    return () => {
39      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
40      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
41    };
42  }, [containerRef]);
43
44  return positionRef;
45}
46
47const VariableProximity = forwardRef((props, ref) => {
48  const {
49    label,
50    fromFontVariationSettings,
51    toFontVariationSettings,
52    containerRef,
53    radius = 50,
54    falloff = 'linear',
55    className = '',
56    onClick,
57    style,
58    ...restProps
59  } = props;
60
61  const letterRefs = useRef([]);
62  const interpolatedSettingsRef = useRef([]);
63  const mousePositionRef = useMousePositionRef(containerRef);
64  const lastPositionRef = useRef({ x: null, y: null });
65
66  const parsedSettings = useMemo(() => {
67    const parseSettings = settingsStr =>
68      new Map(
69        settingsStr
70          .split(',')
71          .map(s => s.trim())
72          .map(s => {
73            const [name, value] = s.split(' ');
74            return [name.replace(/['"]/g, ''), parseFloat(value)];
75          })
76      );
77
78    const fromSettings = parseSettings(fromFontVariationSettings);
79    const toSettings = parseSettings(toFontVariationSettings);
80
81    return Array.from(fromSettings.entries()).map(([axis, fromValue]) => ({
82      axis,
83      fromValue,
84      toValue: toSettings.get(axis) ?? fromValue
85    }));
86  }, [fromFontVariationSettings, toFontVariationSettings]);
87
88  const calculateDistance = (x1, y1, x2, y2) => Math.sqrt((x2 - x1) ** 2 + (y2 - y1) ** 2);
89
90  const calculateFalloff = distance => {
91    const norm = Math.min(Math.max(1 - distance / radius, 0), 1);
92    switch (falloff) {
93      case 'exponential':
94        return norm ** 2;
95      case 'gaussian':
96        return Math.exp(-((distance / (radius / 2)) ** 2) / 2);
97      case 'linear':
98      default:
99        return norm;
100    }
101  };
102
103  useAnimationFrame(() => {
104    if (!containerRef?.current) return;
105    const containerRect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
106    const { x, y } = mousePositionRef.current;
107    if (lastPositionRef.current.x === x && lastPositionRef.current.y === y) {
108      return;
109    }
110    lastPositionRef.current = { x, y };
111
112    letterRefs.current.forEach((letterRef, index) => {
113      if (!letterRef) return;
114
115      const rect = letterRef.getBoundingClientRect();
116      const letterCenterX = rect.left + rect.width / 2 - containerRect.left;
117      const letterCenterY = rect.top + rect.height / 2 - containerRect.top;
118
119      const distance = calculateDistance(
120        mousePositionRef.current.x,
121        mousePositionRef.current.y,
122        letterCenterX,
123        letterCenterY
124      );
125
126      if (distance >= radius) {
127        letterRef.style.fontVariationSettings = fromFontVariationSettings;
128        return;
129      }
130
131      const falloffValue = calculateFalloff(distance);
132      const newSettings = parsedSettings
133        .map(({ axis, fromValue, toValue }) => {
134          const interpolatedValue = fromValue + (toValue - fromValue) * falloffValue;
135          return `'${axis}' ${interpolatedValue}`;
136        })
137        .join(', ');
138
139      interpolatedSettingsRef.current[index] = newSettings;
140      letterRef.style.fontVariationSettings = newSettings;
141    });
142  });
143
144  const words = label.split(' ');
145  let letterIndex = 0;
146
147  return (
148    <span
149      ref={ref}
150      className={`${className} variable-proximity`}
151      onClick={onClick}
152      style={{ display: 'inline', ...style }}
153      {...restProps}
154    >
155      {words.map((word, wordIndex) => (
156        <span key={wordIndex} style={{ display: 'inline-block', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}>
157          {word.split('').map(letter => {
158            const currentLetterIndex = letterIndex++;
159            return (
160              <motion.span
161                key={currentLetterIndex}
162                ref={el => {
163                  letterRefs.current[currentLetterIndex] = el;
164                }}
165                style={{
166                  display: 'inline-block',
167                  fontVariationSettings: interpolatedSettingsRef.current[currentLetterIndex]
168                }}
169                aria-hidden="true"
170              >
171                {letter}
172              </motion.span>
173            );
174          })}
175          {wordIndex < words.length - 1 && <span style={{ display: 'inline-block' }}>&nbsp;</span>}
176        </span>
177      ))}
178      <span className="sr-only">{label}</span>
179    </span>
180  );
181});
182
183VariableProximity.displayName = 'VariableProximity';
184export default VariableProximity;
185

Extra Config/Code:
1@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Roboto+Flex:opsz,wght@8..144,100..1000&display=swap');
2
3.variable-proximity {
4  font-family: 'Roboto Flex', sans-serif;
5}
6
7.sr-only {
8  position: absolute;
9  width: 1px;
10  height: 1px;
11  padding: 0;
12  margin: -1px;
13  overflow: hidden;
14  clip: rect(0, 0, 0, 0);
15  white-space: nowrap;
16  border: 0;
17}
