--------------------------------------------------

Component: Count Up

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/CountUp-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import CountUp from './CountUp'
2
3<CountUp
4  from={0}
5  to={100}
6  separator=","
7  direction="up"
8  duration={1}
9  className="count-up-text"
10  startCounting={false}
11/>

Code:
1import { useInView, useMotionValue, useSpring } from 'motion/react';
2import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
3
4export default function CountUp({
5  to,
6  from = 0,
7  direction = 'up',
8  delay = 0,
9  duration = 2,
10  className = '',
11  startWhen = true,
12  separator = '',
13  onStart,
14  onEnd
15}) {
16  const ref = useRef(null);
17  const motionValue = useMotionValue(direction === 'down' ? to : from);
18
19  const damping = 20 + 40 * (1 / duration);
20  const stiffness = 100 * (1 / duration);
21
22  const springValue = useSpring(motionValue, {
23    damping,
24    stiffness
25  });
26
27  const isInView = useInView(ref, { once: true, margin: '0px' });
28
29  const getDecimalPlaces = num => {
30    const str = num.toString();
31
32    if (str.includes('.')) {
33      const decimals = str.split('.')[1];
34
35      if (parseInt(decimals) !== 0) {
36        return decimals.length;
37      }
38    }
39
40    return 0;
41  };
42
43  const maxDecimals = Math.max(getDecimalPlaces(from), getDecimalPlaces(to));
44
45  const formatValue = useCallback(
46    latest => {
47      const hasDecimals = maxDecimals > 0;
48
49      const options = {
50        useGrouping: !!separator,
51        minimumFractionDigits: hasDecimals ? maxDecimals : 0,
52        maximumFractionDigits: hasDecimals ? maxDecimals : 0
53      };
54
55      const formattedNumber = Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', options).format(latest);
56
57      return separator ? formattedNumber.replace(/,/g, separator) : formattedNumber;
58    },
59    [maxDecimals, separator]
60  );
61
62  useEffect(() => {
63    if (ref.current) {
64      ref.current.textContent = formatValue(direction === 'down' ? to : from);
65    }
66  }, [from, to, direction, formatValue]);
67
68  useEffect(() => {
69    if (isInView && startWhen) {
70      if (typeof onStart === 'function') onStart();
71
72      const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
73        motionValue.set(direction === 'down' ? from : to);
74      }, delay * 1000);
75
76      const durationTimeoutId = setTimeout(
77        () => {
78          if (typeof onEnd === 'function') onEnd();
79        },
80        delay * 1000 + duration * 1000
81      );
82
83      return () => {
84        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
85        clearTimeout(durationTimeoutId);
86      };
87    }
88  }, [isInView, startWhen, motionValue, direction, from, to, delay, onStart, onEnd, duration]);
89
90  useEffect(() => {
91    const unsubscribe = springValue.on('change', latest => {
92      if (ref.current) {
93        ref.current.textContent = formatValue(latest);
94      }
95    });
96
97    return () => unsubscribe();
98  }, [springValue, formatValue]);
99
100  return <span className={className} ref={ref} />;
101}
102

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Animated Content

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/AnimatedContent-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import AnimatedContent from './AnimatedContent'
2
3<AnimatedContent
4  distance={100}
5  direction="vertical"
6  reverse={false}
7  duration={0.8}
8  ease="power3.out"
9  initialOpacity={0}
10  animateOpacity
11  scale={1}
12  threshold={0.1}
13  delay={0}
14>
15  <div>Content to Animate</div>
16</AnimatedContent>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4
5gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
6
7const AnimatedContent = ({
8  children,
9  container,
10  distance = 100,
11  direction = 'vertical',
12  reverse = false,
13  duration = 0.8,
14  ease = 'power3.out',
15  initialOpacity = 0,
16  animateOpacity = true,
17  scale = 1,
18  threshold = 0.1,
19  delay = 0,
20  disappearAfter = 0,
21  disappearDuration = 0.5,
22  disappearEase = 'power3.in',
23  onComplete,
24  onDisappearanceComplete,
25  className = '',
26  ...props
27}) => {
28  const ref = useRef(null);
29
30  useEffect(() => {
31    const el = ref.current;
32    if (!el) return;
33
34    let scrollerTarget = container || document.getElementById('snap-main-container') || null;
35
36    if (typeof scrollerTarget === 'string') {
37      scrollerTarget = document.querySelector(scrollerTarget);
38    }
39
40    const axis = direction === 'horizontal' ? 'x' : 'y';
41    const offset = reverse ? -distance : distance;
42    const startPct = (1 - threshold) * 100;
43
44    gsap.set(el, {
45      [axis]: offset,
46      scale,
47      opacity: animateOpacity ? initialOpacity : 1,
48      visibility: 'visible'
49    });
50
51    const tl = gsap.timeline({
52      paused: true,
53      delay,
54      onComplete: () => {
55        if (onComplete) onComplete();
56        if (disappearAfter > 0) {
57          gsap.to(el, {
58            [axis]: reverse ? distance : -distance,
59            scale: 0.8,
60            opacity: animateOpacity ? initialOpacity : 0,
61            delay: disappearAfter,
62            duration: disappearDuration,
63            ease: disappearEase,
64            onComplete: () => onDisappearanceComplete?.()
65          });
66        }
67      }
68    });
69
70    tl.to(el, {
71      [axis]: 0,
72      scale: 1,
73      opacity: 1,
74      duration,
75      ease
76    });
77
78    const st = ScrollTrigger.create({
79      trigger: el,
80      scroller: scrollerTarget,
81      start: `top ${startPct}%`,
82      once: true,
83      onEnter: () => tl.play()
84    });
85
86    return () => {
87      st.kill();
88      tl.kill();
89    };
90  }, [
91    container,
92    distance,
93    direction,
94    reverse,
95    duration,
96    ease,
97    initialOpacity,
98    animateOpacity,
99    scale,
100    threshold,
101    delay,
102    disappearAfter,
103    disappearDuration,
104    disappearEase,
105    onComplete,
106    onDisappearanceComplete
107  ]);
108
109  return (
110    <div ref={ref} className={className} style={{ visibility: 'hidden' }} {...props}>
111      {children}
112    </div>
113  );
114};
115
116export default AnimatedContent;
117

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Fade Content

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/FadeContent-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import FadeContent from './FadeContent'
2  
3<FadeContent blur={true} duration={1000} easing="ease-out" initialOpacity={0}>
4  {/* Anything placed inside this container will be fade into view */}
5</FadeContent>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger';
4
5gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
6
7const FadeContent = ({
8  children,
9  container,
10  blur = false,
11  duration = 1000,
12  ease = 'power2.out',
13  delay = 0,
14  threshold = 0.1,
15  initialOpacity = 0,
16  disappearAfter = 0,
17  disappearDuration = 0.5,
18  disappearEase = 'power2.in',
19  onComplete,
20  onDisappearanceComplete,
21  className = '',
22  style,
23  ...props
24}) => {
25  const ref = useRef(null);
26
27  useEffect(() => {
28    const el = ref.current;
29    if (!el) return;
30
31    let scrollerTarget = container || document.getElementById('snap-main-container') || null;
32    if (typeof scrollerTarget === 'string') {
33      scrollerTarget = document.querySelector(scrollerTarget);
34    }
35
36    const startPct = (1 - threshold) * 100;
37
38    const getSeconds = val => (typeof val === 'number' && val > 10 ? val / 1000 : val);
39
40    gsap.set(el, {
41      autoAlpha: initialOpacity,
42      filter: blur ? 'blur(10px)' : 'blur(0px)',
43      willChange: 'opacity, filter, transform'
44    });
45
46    const tl = gsap.timeline({
47      paused: true,
48      delay: getSeconds(delay),
49      onComplete: () => {
50        if (onComplete) onComplete();
51        if (disappearAfter > 0) {
52          gsap.to(el, {
53            autoAlpha: initialOpacity,
54            filter: blur ? 'blur(10px)' : 'blur(0px)',
55            delay: getSeconds(disappearAfter),
56            duration: getSeconds(disappearDuration),
57            ease: disappearEase,
58            onComplete: () => onDisappearanceComplete?.()
59          });
60        }
61      }
62    });
63
64    tl.to(el, {
65      autoAlpha: 1,
66      filter: 'blur(0px)',
67      duration: getSeconds(duration),
68      ease: ease
69    });
70
71    const st = ScrollTrigger.create({
72      trigger: el,
73      scroller: scrollerTarget || window,
74      start: `top ${startPct}%`,
75      once: true,
76      onEnter: () => tl.play()
77    });
78
79    return () => {
80      st.kill();
81      tl.kill();
82      gsap.killTweensOf(el);
83    };
84    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
85  }, []);
86
87  return (
88    <div ref={ref} className={className} style={style} {...props}>
89      {children}
90    </div>
91  );
92};
93
94export default FadeContent;
95

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Electric Border

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ElectricBorder-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// CREDIT
2// Component inspired by @BalintFerenczy on X
3// https://codepen.io/BalintFerenczy/pen/KwdoyEN
4  
5import ElectricBorder from './ElectricBorder'
6
7<ElectricBorder
8  color="#7df9ff"
9  speed={1}
10  chaos={0.12}
11  thickness={2}
12  style={{ borderRadius: 16 }}
13>
14  <div>
15    <p style={{ margin: '6px 0 0', opacity: 0.8 }}>
16      A glowing, animated border wrapper.
17    </p>
18  </div>
19</ElectricBorder>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
2import './ElectricBorder.css';
3
4const ElectricBorder = ({
5  children,
6  color = '#5227FF',
7  speed = 1,
8  chaos = 0.12,
9  borderRadius = 24,
10  className,
11  style
12}) => {
13  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
14  const containerRef = useRef(null);
15  const animationRef = useRef(null);
16  const timeRef = useRef(0);
17  const lastFrameTimeRef = useRef(0);
18
19  // Noise functions
20  const random = useCallback(x => {
21    return (Math.sin(x * 12.9898) * 43758.5453) % 1;
22  }, []);
23
24  const noise2D = useCallback(
25    (x, y) => {
26      const i = Math.floor(x);
27      const j = Math.floor(y);
28      const fx = x - i;
29      const fy = y - j;
30
31      const a = random(i + j * 57);
32      const b = random(i + 1 + j * 57);
33      const c = random(i + (j + 1) * 57);
34      const d = random(i + 1 + (j + 1) * 57);
35
36      const ux = fx * fx * (3.0 - 2.0 * fx);
37      const uy = fy * fy * (3.0 - 2.0 * fy);
38
39      return a * (1 - ux) * (1 - uy) + b * ux * (1 - uy) + c * (1 - ux) * uy + d * ux * uy;
40    },
41    [random]
42  );
43
44  const octavedNoise = useCallback(
45    (x, octaves, lacunarity, gain, baseAmplitude, baseFrequency, time, seed, baseFlatness) => {
46      let y = 0;
47      let amplitude = baseAmplitude;
48      let frequency = baseFrequency;
49
50      for (let i = 0; i < octaves; i++) {
51        let octaveAmplitude = amplitude;
52        if (i === 0) {
53          octaveAmplitude *= baseFlatness;
54        }
55        y += octaveAmplitude * noise2D(frequency * x + seed * 100, time * frequency * 0.3);
56        frequency *= lacunarity;
57        amplitude *= gain;
58      }
59
60      return y;
61    },
62    [noise2D]
63  );
64
65  const getCornerPoint = useCallback((centerX, centerY, radius, startAngle, arcLength, progress) => {
66    const angle = startAngle + progress * arcLength;
67    return {
68      x: centerX + radius * Math.cos(angle),
69      y: centerY + radius * Math.sin(angle)
70    };
71  }, []);
72
73  const getRoundedRectPoint = useCallback(
74    (t, left, top, width, height, radius) => {
75      const straightWidth = width - 2 * radius;
76      const straightHeight = height - 2 * radius;
77      const cornerArc = (Math.PI * radius) / 2;
78      const totalPerimeter = 2 * straightWidth + 2 * straightHeight + 4 * cornerArc;
79      const distance = t * totalPerimeter;
80
81      let accumulated = 0;
82
83      // Top edge
84      if (distance <= accumulated + straightWidth) {
85        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / straightWidth;
86        return { x: left + radius + progress * straightWidth, y: top };
87      }
88      accumulated += straightWidth;
89
90      // Top-right corner
91      if (distance <= accumulated + cornerArc) {
92        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / cornerArc;
93        return getCornerPoint(left + width - radius, top + radius, radius, -Math.PI / 2, Math.PI / 2, progress);
94      }
95      accumulated += cornerArc;
96
97      // Right edge
98      if (distance <= accumulated + straightHeight) {
99        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / straightHeight;
100        return { x: left + width, y: top + radius + progress * straightHeight };
101      }
102      accumulated += straightHeight;
103
104      // Bottom-right corner
105      if (distance <= accumulated + cornerArc) {
106        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / cornerArc;
107        return getCornerPoint(left + width - radius, top + height - radius, radius, 0, Math.PI / 2, progress);
108      }
109      accumulated += cornerArc;
110
111      // Bottom edge
112      if (distance <= accumulated + straightWidth) {
113        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / straightWidth;
114        return { x: left + width - radius - progress * straightWidth, y: top + height };
115      }
116      accumulated += straightWidth;
117
118      // Bottom-left corner
119      if (distance <= accumulated + cornerArc) {
120        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / cornerArc;
121        return getCornerPoint(left + radius, top + height - radius, radius, Math.PI / 2, Math.PI / 2, progress);
122      }
123      accumulated += cornerArc;
124
125      // Left edge
126      if (distance <= accumulated + straightHeight) {
127        const progress = (distance - accumulated) / straightHeight;
128        return { x: left, y: top + height - radius - progress * straightHeight };
129      }
130      accumulated += straightHeight;
131
132      // Top-left corner
133      const progress = (distance - accumulated) / cornerArc;
134      return getCornerPoint(left + radius, top + radius, radius, Math.PI, Math.PI / 2, progress);
135    },
136    [getCornerPoint]
137  );
138
139  useEffect(() => {
140    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
141    const container = containerRef.current;
142    if (!canvas || !container) return;
143
144    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
145    if (!ctx) return;
146
147    // Configuration
148    const octaves = 10;
149    const lacunarity = 1.6;
150    const gain = 0.7;
151    const amplitude = chaos;
152    const frequency = 10;
153    const baseFlatness = 0;
154    const displacement = 60;
155    const borderOffset = 60;
156
157    const updateSize = () => {
158      const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
159      const width = rect.width + borderOffset * 2;
160      const height = rect.height + borderOffset * 2;
161
162      // Use device pixel ratio for sharp rendering
163      const dpr = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2);
164      canvas.width = width * dpr;
165      canvas.height = height * dpr;
166      canvas.style.width = `${width}px`;
167      canvas.style.height = `${height}px`;
168      ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
169
170      return { width, height };
171    };
172
173    let { width, height } = updateSize();
174
175    const drawElectricBorder = currentTime => {
176      if (!canvas || !ctx) return;
177
178      const deltaTime = (currentTime - lastFrameTimeRef.current) / 1000;
179      timeRef.current += deltaTime * speed;
180      lastFrameTimeRef.current = currentTime;
181
182      // Clear canvas
183      const dpr = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2);
184      ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
185      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
186      ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
187
188      ctx.strokeStyle = color;
189      ctx.lineWidth = 1;
190      ctx.lineCap = 'round';
191      ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
192
193      const scale = displacement;
194      const left = borderOffset;
195      const top = borderOffset;
196      const borderWidth = width - 2 * borderOffset;
197      const borderHeight = height - 2 * borderOffset;
198      const maxRadius = Math.min(borderWidth, borderHeight) / 2;
199      const radius = Math.min(borderRadius, maxRadius);
200
201      const approximatePerimeter = 2 * (borderWidth + borderHeight) + 2 * Math.PI * radius;
202      const sampleCount = Math.floor(approximatePerimeter / 2);
203
204      ctx.beginPath();
205
206      for (let i = 0; i <= sampleCount; i++) {
207        const progress = i / sampleCount;
208
209        const point = getRoundedRectPoint(progress, left, top, borderWidth, borderHeight, radius);
210
211        const xNoise = octavedNoise(
212          progress * 8,
213          octaves,
214          lacunarity,
215          gain,
216          amplitude,
217          frequency,
218          timeRef.current,
219          0,
220          baseFlatness
221        );
222
223        const yNoise = octavedNoise(
224          progress * 8,
225          octaves,
226          lacunarity,
227          gain,
228          amplitude,
229          frequency,
230          timeRef.current,
231          1,
232          baseFlatness
233        );
234
235        const displacedX = point.x + xNoise * scale;
236        const displacedY = point.y + yNoise * scale;
237
238        if (i === 0) {
239          ctx.moveTo(displacedX, displacedY);
240        } else {
241          ctx.lineTo(displacedX, displacedY);
242        }
243      }
244
245      ctx.closePath();
246      ctx.stroke();
247
248      animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(drawElectricBorder);
249    };
250
251    // Handle resize
252    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(() => {
253      const newSize = updateSize();
254      width = newSize.width;
255      height = newSize.height;
256    });
257    resizeObserver.observe(container);
258
259    // Start animation
260    animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(drawElectricBorder);
261
262    return () => {
263      if (animationRef.current) {
264        cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
265      }
266      resizeObserver.disconnect();
267    };
268  }, [color, speed, chaos, borderRadius, octavedNoise, getRoundedRectPoint]);
269
270  const vars = {
271    '--electric-border-color': color,
272    borderRadius: borderRadius
273  };
274
275  return (
276    <div ref={containerRef} className={`electric-border ${className ?? ''}`} style={{ ...vars, ...style }}>
277      <div className="eb-canvas-container">
278        <canvas ref={canvasRef} className="eb-canvas" />
279      </div>
280      <div className="eb-layers">
281        <div className="eb-glow-1" />
282        <div className="eb-glow-2" />
283        <div className="eb-background-glow" />
284      </div>
285      <div className="eb-content">{children}</div>
286    </div>
287  );
288};
289
290export default ElectricBorder;
291

Component: Pixel Transition

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/PixelTransition-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import PixelTransition from './PixelTransition';
2
3<PixelTransition
4  firstContent={
5    <img
6      src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Cat03.jpg/1200px-Cat03.jpg"
7      alt="default pixel transition content, a cat!"
8      style={{ width: "100%", height: "100%", objectFit: "cover" }}
9    />
10  }
11  secondContent={
12    <div
13      style={{
14        width: "100%",
15        height: "100%",
16        display: "grid",
17        placeItems: "center",
18        backgroundColor: "#111"
19      }}
20    >
21      <p style={{ fontWeight: 900, fontSize: "3rem", color: "#ffffff" }}>Meow!</p>
22    </div>
23  }
24  gridSize={8}
25  pixelColor='#ffffff'
26  once={false}
27  animationStepDuration={0.4}
28  className="custom-pixel-card"
29  pixelColor="#ffffff"
30/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import './PixelTransition.css';
4
5function PixelTransition({
6  firstContent,
7  secondContent,
8  gridSize = 7,
9  pixelColor = 'currentColor',
10  animationStepDuration = 0.3,
11  once = false,
12  aspectRatio = '100%',
13  className = '',
14  style = {}
15}) {
16  const containerRef = useRef(null);
17  const pixelGridRef = useRef(null);
18  const activeRef = useRef(null);
19  const delayedCallRef = useRef(null);
20
21  const [isActive, setIsActive] = useState(false);
22
23  const isTouchDevice =
24    'ontouchstart' in window || navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0 || window.matchMedia('(pointer: coarse)').matches;
25
26  useEffect(() => {
27    const pixelGridEl = pixelGridRef.current;
28    if (!pixelGridEl) return;
29
30    pixelGridEl.innerHTML = '';
31
32    for (let row = 0; row < gridSize; row++) {
33      for (let col = 0; col < gridSize; col++) {
34        const pixel = document.createElement('div');
35        pixel.classList.add('pixelated-image-card__pixel');
36        pixel.style.backgroundColor = pixelColor;
37
38        const size = 100 / gridSize;
39        pixel.style.width = `${size}%`;
40        pixel.style.height = `${size}%`;
41        pixel.style.left = `${col * size}%`;
42        pixel.style.top = `${row * size}%`;
43        pixelGridEl.appendChild(pixel);
44      }
45    }
46  }, [gridSize, pixelColor]);
47
48  const animatePixels = activate => {
49    setIsActive(activate);
50
51    const pixelGridEl = pixelGridRef.current;
52    const activeEl = activeRef.current;
53    if (!pixelGridEl || !activeEl) return;
54
55    const pixels = pixelGridEl.querySelectorAll('.pixelated-image-card__pixel');
56    if (!pixels.length) return;
57
58    gsap.killTweensOf(pixels);
59    if (delayedCallRef.current) {
60      delayedCallRef.current.kill();
61    }
62
63    gsap.set(pixels, { display: 'none' });
64
65    const totalPixels = pixels.length;
66    const staggerDuration = animationStepDuration / totalPixels;
67
68    gsap.to(pixels, {
69      display: 'block',
70      duration: 0,
71      stagger: {
72        each: staggerDuration,
73        from: 'random'
74      }
75    });
76
77    delayedCallRef.current = gsap.delayedCall(animationStepDuration, () => {
78      activeEl.style.display = activate ? 'block' : 'none';
79      activeEl.style.pointerEvents = activate ? 'none' : '';
80    });
81
82    gsap.to(pixels, {
83      display: 'none',
84      duration: 0,
85      delay: animationStepDuration,
86      stagger: {
87        each: staggerDuration,
88        from: 'random'
89      }
90    });
91  };
92
93  const handleEnter = () => {
94    if (!isActive) animatePixels(true);
95  };
96  const handleLeave = () => {
97    if (isActive && !once) animatePixels(false);
98  };
99  const handleClick = () => {
100    if (!isActive) animatePixels(true);
101    else if (isActive && !once) animatePixels(false);
102  };
103
104  return (
105    <div
106      ref={containerRef}
107      className={`pixelated-image-card ${className}`}
108      style={style}
109      onMouseEnter={!isTouchDevice ? handleEnter : undefined}
110      onMouseLeave={!isTouchDevice ? handleLeave : undefined}
111      onClick={isTouchDevice ? handleClick : undefined}
112      onFocus={!isTouchDevice ? handleEnter : undefined}
113      onBlur={!isTouchDevice ? handleLeave : undefined}
114      tabIndex={0}
115    >
116      <div style={{ paddingTop: aspectRatio }} />
117      <div className="pixelated-image-card__default" aria-hidden={isActive}>
118        {firstContent}
119      </div>
120      <div className="pixelated-image-card__active" ref={activeRef} aria-hidden={!isActive}>
121        {secondContent}
122      </div>
123      <div className="pixelated-image-card__pixels" ref={pixelGridRef} />
124    </div>
125  );
126}
127
128export default PixelTransition;
129

Component: Glare Hover

Installation:

Usage:

5    glareColor="#ffffff"
6    glareOpacity={0.3}
7    glareAngle={-30}
8    glareSize={300}
9    transitionDuration={800}
10    playOnce={false}
11  >

13      Hover Me
14    </h2>
15  </GlareHover>
16</div>

Code:
1import './GlareHover.css';
2
3const GlareHover = ({
4  width = '500px',
5  height = '500px',
6  background = '#000',
7  borderRadius = '10px',
8  borderColor = '#333',
9  children,
10  glareColor = '#ffffff',
11  glareOpacity = 0.5,
12  glareAngle = -45,
13  glareSize = 250,
14  transitionDuration = 650,
15  playOnce = false,
16  className = '',
17  style = {}
18}) => {
19  const hex = glareColor.replace('#', '');
20  let rgba = glareColor;
21  if (/^[0-9A-Fa-f]{6}$/.test(hex)) {
22    const r = parseInt(hex.slice(0, 2), 16);
23    const g = parseInt(hex.slice(2, 4), 16);
24    const b = parseInt(hex.slice(4, 6), 16);
25    rgba = `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${glareOpacity})`;
26  } else if (/^[0-9A-Fa-f]{3}$/.test(hex)) {
27    const r = parseInt(hex[0] + hex[0], 16);
28    const g = parseInt(hex[1] + hex[1], 16);
29    const b = parseInt(hex[2] + hex[2], 16);
30    rgba = `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${glareOpacity})`;
31  }
32
33  const vars = {
34    '--gh-width': width,
35    '--gh-height': height,
36    '--gh-bg': background,
37    '--gh-br': borderRadius,
38    '--gh-angle': `${glareAngle}deg`,
39    '--gh-duration': `${transitionDuration}ms`,
40    '--gh-size': `${glareSize}%`,
41    '--gh-rgba': rgba,
42    '--gh-border': borderColor
43  };
44
45  return (
46    <div
47      className={`glare-hover ${playOnce ? 'glare-hover--play-once' : ''} ${className}`}
48      style={{ ...vars, ...style }}
49    >
50      {children}
51    </div>
52  );
53};
54
55export default GlareHover;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Antigravity

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Antigravity-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Antigravity from './Antigravity';
2
3<div style={{ width: '100%', height: '400px', position: 'relative' }}>
4  <Antigravity
5    count={300}
6    magnetRadius={6}
7    ringRadius={7}
8    waveSpeed={0.4}
9    waveAmplitude={1}
10    particleSize={1.5}
11    lerpSpeed={0.05}
12    color="#5227FF"
13    autoAnimate
14    particleVariance={1}
15    rotationSpeed={0}
16    depthFactor={1}
17    pulseSpeed={3}
18    particleShape="capsule"
19    fieldStrength={10}
20/>
21</div>

Code:
1/* eslint-disable react/no-unknown-property */
2import { Canvas, useFrame, useThree } from '@react-three/fiber';
3import { useMemo, useRef } from 'react';
4import * as THREE from 'three';
5
6const AntigravityInner = ({
7  count = 300,
8  magnetRadius = 10,
9  ringRadius = 10,
10  waveSpeed = 0.4,
11  waveAmplitude = 1,
12  particleSize = 2,
13  lerpSpeed = 0.1,
14  color = '#FF9FFC',
15  autoAnimate = false,
16  particleVariance = 1,
17  rotationSpeed = 0,
18  depthFactor = 1,
19  pulseSpeed = 3,
20  particleShape = 'capsule',
21  fieldStrength = 10
22}) => {
23  const meshRef = useRef(null);
24  const { viewport } = useThree();
25  const dummy = useMemo(() => new THREE.Object3D(), []);
26
27  const lastMousePos = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
28  const lastMouseMoveTime = useRef(0);
29  const virtualMouse = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
30
31  const particles = useMemo(() => {
32    const temp = [];
33    const width = viewport.width || 100;
34    const height = viewport.height || 100;
35
36    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
37      const t = Math.random() * 100;
38      const factor = 20 + Math.random() * 100;
39      const speed = 0.01 + Math.random() / 200;
40      const xFactor = -50 + Math.random() * 100;
41      const yFactor = -50 + Math.random() * 100;
42      const zFactor = -50 + Math.random() * 100;
43
44      const x = (Math.random() - 0.5) * width;
45      const y = (Math.random() - 0.5) * height;
46      const z = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20;
47
48      const randomRadiusOffset = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2;
49
50      temp.push({
51        t,
52        factor,
53        speed,
54        xFactor,
55        yFactor,
56        zFactor,
57        mx: x,
58        my: y,
59        mz: z,
60        cx: x,
61        cy: y,
62        cz: z,
63        vx: 0,
64        vy: 0,
65        vz: 0,
66        randomRadiusOffset
67      });
68    }
69    return temp;
70  }, [count, viewport.width, viewport.height]);
71
72  useFrame(state => {
73    const mesh = meshRef.current;
74    if (!mesh) return;
75
76    const { viewport: v, pointer: m } = state;
77
78    const mouseDist = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(m.x - lastMousePos.current.x, 2) + Math.pow(m.y - lastMousePos.current.y, 2));
79
80    if (mouseDist > 0.001) {
81      lastMouseMoveTime.current = Date.now();
82      lastMousePos.current = { x: m.x, y: m.y };
83    }
84
85    let destX = (m.x * v.width) / 2;
86    let destY = (m.y * v.height) / 2;
87
88    if (autoAnimate && Date.now() - lastMouseMoveTime.current > 2000) {
89      const time = state.clock.getElapsedTime();
90      destX = Math.sin(time * 0.5) * (v.width / 4);
91      destY = Math.cos(time * 0.5 * 2) * (v.height / 4);
92    }
93
94    const smoothFactor = 0.05;
95    virtualMouse.current.x += (destX - virtualMouse.current.x) * smoothFactor;
96    virtualMouse.current.y += (destY - virtualMouse.current.y) * smoothFactor;
97
98    const targetX = virtualMouse.current.x;
99    const targetY = virtualMouse.current.y;
100
101    const globalRotation = state.clock.getElapsedTime() * rotationSpeed;
102
103    particles.forEach((particle, i) => {
104      let { t, speed, mx, my, mz, cz, randomRadiusOffset } = particle;
105
106      t = particle.t += speed / 2;
107
108      const projectionFactor = 1 - cz / 50;
109      const projectedTargetX = targetX * projectionFactor;
110      const projectedTargetY = targetY * projectionFactor;
111
112      const dx = mx - projectedTargetX;
113      const dy = my - projectedTargetY;
114      const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
115
116      let targetPos = { x: mx, y: my, z: mz * depthFactor };
117
118      if (dist < magnetRadius) {
119        const angle = Math.atan2(dy, dx) + globalRotation;
120
121        const wave = Math.sin(t * waveSpeed + angle) * (0.5 * waveAmplitude);
122        const deviation = randomRadiusOffset * (5 / (fieldStrength + 0.1));
123
124        const currentRingRadius = ringRadius + wave + deviation;
125
126        targetPos.x = projectedTargetX + currentRingRadius * Math.cos(angle);
127        targetPos.y = projectedTargetY + currentRingRadius * Math.sin(angle);
128        targetPos.z = mz * depthFactor + Math.sin(t) * (1 * waveAmplitude * depthFactor);
129      }
130
131      particle.cx += (targetPos.x - particle.cx) * lerpSpeed;
132      particle.cy += (targetPos.y - particle.cy) * lerpSpeed;
133      particle.cz += (targetPos.z - particle.cz) * lerpSpeed;
134
135      dummy.position.set(particle.cx, particle.cy, particle.cz);
136
137      dummy.lookAt(projectedTargetX, projectedTargetY, particle.cz);
138      dummy.rotateX(Math.PI / 2);
139
140      const currentDistToMouse = Math.sqrt(
141        Math.pow(particle.cx - projectedTargetX, 2) + Math.pow(particle.cy - projectedTargetY, 2)
142      );
143
144      const distFromRing = Math.abs(currentDistToMouse - ringRadius);
145      let scaleFactor = 1 - distFromRing / 10;
146
147      scaleFactor = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, scaleFactor));
148
149      const finalScale = scaleFactor * (0.8 + Math.sin(t * pulseSpeed) * 0.2 * particleVariance) * particleSize;
150      dummy.scale.set(finalScale, finalScale, finalScale);
151
152      dummy.updateMatrix();
153
154      mesh.setMatrixAt(i, dummy.matrix);
155    });
156
157    mesh.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;
158  });
159
160  return (
161    <instancedMesh ref={meshRef} args={[undefined, undefined, count]}>
162      {particleShape === 'capsule' && <capsuleGeometry args={[0.1, 0.4, 4, 8]} />}
163      {particleShape === 'sphere' && <sphereGeometry args={[0.2, 16, 16]} />}
164      {particleShape === 'box' && <boxGeometry args={[0.3, 0.3, 0.3]} />}
165      {particleShape === 'tetrahedron' && <tetrahedronGeometry args={[0.3]} />}
166      <meshBasicMaterial color={color} />
167    </instancedMesh>
168  );
169};
170
171const Antigravity = props => {
172  return (
173    <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0, 50], fov: 35 }}>
174      <AntigravityInner {...props} />
175    </Canvas>
176  );
177};
178
179export default Antigravity;
180

Code:
1import { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState, memo } from 'react';
2import './LogoLoop.css';
3
4const ANIMATION_CONFIG = { SMOOTH_TAU: 0.25, MIN_COPIES: 2, COPY_HEADROOM: 2 };
5
6const toCssLength = value => (typeof value === 'number' ? `${value}px` : (value ?? undefined));
7
8const useResizeObserver = (callback, elements, dependencies) => {
9  useEffect(() => {
10    if (!window.ResizeObserver) {
11      const handleResize = () => callback();
12      window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
13      callback();
14      return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
15    }
16    const observers = elements.map(ref => {
17      if (!ref.current) return null;
18      const observer = new ResizeObserver(callback);
19      observer.observe(ref.current);
20      return observer;
21    });
22    callback();
23    return () => {
24      observers.forEach(observer => observer?.disconnect());
25    };
26  }, [callback, elements, dependencies]);
27};
28
29const useImageLoader = (seqRef, onLoad, dependencies) => {
30  useEffect(() => {
31    const images = seqRef.current?.querySelectorAll('img') ?? [];
32    if (images.length === 0) {
33      onLoad();
34      return;
35    }
36    let remainingImages = images.length;
37    const handleImageLoad = () => {
38      remainingImages -= 1;
39      if (remainingImages === 0) onLoad();
40    };
41    images.forEach(img => {
42      const htmlImg = img;
43      if (htmlImg.complete) {
44        handleImageLoad();
45      } else {
46        htmlImg.addEventListener('load', handleImageLoad, { once: true });
47        htmlImg.addEventListener('error', handleImageLoad, { once: true });
48      }
49    });
50    return () => {
51      images.forEach(img => {
52        img.removeEventListener('load', handleImageLoad);
53        img.removeEventListener('error', handleImageLoad);
54      });
55    };
56  }, [onLoad, seqRef, dependencies]);
57};
58
59const useAnimationLoop = (trackRef, targetVelocity, seqWidth, seqHeight, isHovered, hoverSpeed, isVertical) => {
60  const rafRef = useRef(null);
61  const lastTimestampRef = useRef(null);
62  const offsetRef = useRef(0);
63  const velocityRef = useRef(0);
64
65  useEffect(() => {
66    const track = trackRef.current;
67    if (!track) return;
68
69    const seqSize = isVertical ? seqHeight : seqWidth;
70
71    if (seqSize > 0) {
72      offsetRef.current = ((offsetRef.current % seqSize) + seqSize) % seqSize;
73      const transformValue = isVertical
74        ? `translate3d(0, ${-offsetRef.current}px, 0)`
75        : `translate3d(${-offsetRef.current}px, 0, 0)`;
76      track.style.transform = transformValue;
77    }
78
79    const animate = timestamp => {
80      if (lastTimestampRef.current === null) {
81        lastTimestampRef.current = timestamp;
82      }
83
84      const deltaTime = Math.max(0, timestamp - lastTimestampRef.current) / 1000;
85      lastTimestampRef.current = timestamp;
86
87      const target = isHovered && hoverSpeed !== undefined ? hoverSpeed : targetVelocity;
88
89      const easingFactor = 1 - Math.exp(-deltaTime / ANIMATION_CONFIG.SMOOTH_TAU);
90      velocityRef.current += (target - velocityRef.current) * easingFactor;
91
92      if (seqSize > 0) {
93        let nextOffset = offsetRef.current + velocityRef.current * deltaTime;
94        nextOffset = ((nextOffset % seqSize) + seqSize) % seqSize;
95        offsetRef.current = nextOffset;
96
97        const transformValue = isVertical
98          ? `translate3d(0, ${-offsetRef.current}px, 0)`
99          : `translate3d(${-offsetRef.current}px, 0, 0)`;
100        track.style.transform = transformValue;
101      }
102
103      rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
104    };
105
106    rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
107
108    return () => {
109      if (rafRef.current !== null) {
110        cancelAnimationFrame(rafRef.current);
111        rafRef.current = null;
112      }
113      lastTimestampRef.current = null;
114    };
115  }, [targetVelocity, seqWidth, seqHeight, isHovered, hoverSpeed, isVertical, trackRef]);
116};
117
118export const LogoLoop = memo(
119  ({
120    logos,
121    speed = 120,
122    direction = 'left',
123    width = '100%',
124    logoHeight = 28,
125    gap = 32,
126    pauseOnHover,
127    hoverSpeed,
128    fadeOut = false,
129    fadeOutColor,
130    scaleOnHover = false,
131    renderItem,
132    ariaLabel = 'Partner logos',
133    className,
134    style
135  }) => {
136    const containerRef = useRef(null);
137    const trackRef = useRef(null);
138    const seqRef = useRef(null);
139
140    const [seqWidth, setSeqWidth] = useState(0);
141    const [seqHeight, setSeqHeight] = useState(0);
142    const [copyCount, setCopyCount] = useState(ANIMATION_CONFIG.MIN_COPIES);
143    const [isHovered, setIsHovered] = useState(false);
144
145    const effectiveHoverSpeed = useMemo(() => {
146      if (hoverSpeed !== undefined) return hoverSpeed;
147      if (pauseOnHover === true) return 0;
148      if (pauseOnHover === false) return undefined;
149      return 0;
150    }, [hoverSpeed, pauseOnHover]);
151
152    const isVertical = direction === 'up' || direction === 'down';
153
154    const targetVelocity = useMemo(() => {
155      const magnitude = Math.abs(speed);
156      let directionMultiplier;
157      if (isVertical) {
158        directionMultiplier = direction === 'up' ? 1 : -1;
159      } else {
160        directionMultiplier = direction === 'left' ? 1 : -1;
161      }
162      const speedMultiplier = speed < 0 ? -1 : 1;
163      return magnitude * directionMultiplier * speedMultiplier;
164    }, [speed, direction, isVertical]);
165
166    const updateDimensions = useCallback(() => {
167      const containerWidth = containerRef.current?.clientWidth ?? 0;
168      const sequenceRect = seqRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect?.();
169      const sequenceWidth = sequenceRect?.width ?? 0;
170      const sequenceHeight = sequenceRect?.height ?? 0;
171      if (isVertical) {
172        const parentHeight = containerRef.current?.parentElement?.clientHeight ?? 0;
173        if (containerRef.current && parentHeight > 0) {
174          const targetHeight = Math.ceil(parentHeight);
175          if (containerRef.current.style.height !== `${targetHeight}px`)
176            containerRef.current.style.height = `${targetHeight}px`;
177        }
178        if (sequenceHeight > 0) {
179          setSeqHeight(Math.ceil(sequenceHeight));
180          const viewport = containerRef.current?.clientHeight ?? parentHeight ?? sequenceHeight;
181          const copiesNeeded = Math.ceil(viewport / sequenceHeight) + ANIMATION_CONFIG.COPY_HEADROOM;
182          setCopyCount(Math.max(ANIMATION_CONFIG.MIN_COPIES, copiesNeeded));
183        }
184      } else if (sequenceWidth > 0) {
185        setSeqWidth(Math.ceil(sequenceWidth));
186        const copiesNeeded = Math.ceil(containerWidth / sequenceWidth) + ANIMATION_CONFIG.COPY_HEADROOM;
187        setCopyCount(Math.max(ANIMATION_CONFIG.MIN_COPIES, copiesNeeded));
188      }
189    }, [isVertical]);
190
191    useResizeObserver(updateDimensions, [containerRef, seqRef], [logos, gap, logoHeight, isVertical]);
192
193    useImageLoader(seqRef, updateDimensions, [logos, gap, logoHeight, isVertical]);
194
195    useAnimationLoop(trackRef, targetVelocity, seqWidth, seqHeight, isHovered, effectiveHoverSpeed, isVertical);
196
197    const cssVariables = useMemo(
198      () => ({
199        '--logoloop-gap': `${gap}px`,
200        '--logoloop-logoHeight': `${logoHeight}px`,
201        ...(fadeOutColor && { '--logoloop-fadeColor': fadeOutColor })
202      }),
203      [gap, logoHeight, fadeOutColor]
204    );
205
206    const rootClassName = useMemo(
207      () =>
208        [
209          'logoloop',
210          isVertical ? 'logoloop--vertical' : 'logoloop--horizontal',
211          fadeOut && 'logoloop--fade',
212          scaleOnHover && 'logoloop--scale-hover',
213          className
214        ]
215          .filter(Boolean)
216          .join(' '),
217      [isVertical, fadeOut, scaleOnHover, className]
218    );
219
220    const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
221      if (effectiveHoverSpeed !== undefined) setIsHovered(true);
222    }, [effectiveHoverSpeed]);
223    const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
224      if (effectiveHoverSpeed !== undefined) setIsHovered(false);
225    }, [effectiveHoverSpeed]);
226
227    const renderLogoItem = useCallback(
228      (item, key) => {
229        if (renderItem) {
230          return (
231            <li className="logoloop__item" key={key} role="listitem">
232              {renderItem(item, key)}
233            </li>
234          );
235        }
236        const isNodeItem = 'node' in item;
237        const content = isNodeItem ? (
238          <span className="logoloop__node" aria-hidden={!!item.href && !item.ariaLabel}>
239            {item.node}
240          </span>
241        ) : (
242          <img
243            src={item.src}
244            srcSet={item.srcSet}
245            sizes={item.sizes}
246            width={item.width}
247            height={item.height}
248            alt={item.alt ?? ''}
249            title={item.title}
250            loading="lazy"
251            decoding="async"
252            draggable={false}
253          />
254        );
255        const itemAriaLabel = isNodeItem ? (item.ariaLabel ?? item.title) : (item.alt ?? item.title);
256        const itemContent = item.href ? (
257          <a
258            className="logoloop__link"
259            href={item.href}
260            aria-label={itemAriaLabel || 'logo link'}
261            target="_blank"
262            rel="noreferrer noopener"
263          >
264            {content}
265          </a>
266        ) : (
267          content
268        );
269        return (
270          <li className="logoloop__item" key={key} role="listitem">
271            {itemContent}
272          </li>
273        );
274      },
275      [renderItem]
276    );
277
278    const logoLists = useMemo(
279      () =>
280        Array.from({ length: copyCount }, (_, copyIndex) => (
281          <ul
282            className="logoloop__list"
283            key={`copy-${copyIndex}`}
284            role="list"
285            aria-hidden={copyIndex > 0}
286            ref={copyIndex === 0 ? seqRef : undefined}
287          >
288            {logos.map((item, itemIndex) => renderLogoItem(item, `${copyIndex}-${itemIndex}`))}
289          </ul>
290        )),
291      [copyCount, logos, renderLogoItem]
292    );
293
294    const containerStyle = useMemo(
295      () => ({
296        width: isVertical
297          ? toCssLength(width) === '100%'
298            ? undefined
299            : toCssLength(width)
300          : (toCssLength(width) ?? '100%'),
301        ...cssVariables,
302        ...style
303      }),
304      [width, cssVariables, style, isVertical]
305    );
306
307    return (
308      <div ref={containerRef} className={rootClassName} style={containerStyle} role="region" aria-label={ariaLabel}>
309        <div className="logoloop__track" ref={trackRef} onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter} onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}>
310          {logoLists}
311        </div>
312      </div>
313    );
314  }
315);
316
317LogoLoop.displayName = 'LogoLoop';
318
319export default LogoLoop;
320

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Target Cursor

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/TargetCursor-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import TargetCursor from './TargetCursor';
2
3export default function App() {
4  return (
5    <div>
6      <TargetCursor 
7        spinDuration={2}
8        hideDefaultCursor
9        parallaxOn
10  hoverDuration={0.2}
11/>
12      
13      <h1>Hover over the elements below</h1>
14      <button className="cursor-target">Click me!</button>
15      <div className="cursor-target">Hover target</div>
16    </div>
17  );
18}

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import './TargetCursor.css';
4
5const TargetCursor = ({
6  targetSelector = '.cursor-target',
7  spinDuration = 2,
8  hideDefaultCursor = true,
9  hoverDuration = 0.2,
10  parallaxOn = true
11}) => {
12  const cursorRef = useRef(null);
13  const cornersRef = useRef(null);
14  const spinTl = useRef(null);
15  const dotRef = useRef(null);
16
17  const isActiveRef = useRef(false);
18  const targetCornerPositionsRef = useRef(null);
19  const tickerFnRef = useRef(null);
20  const activeStrengthRef = useRef(0);
21
22  const isMobile = useMemo(() => {
23    const hasTouchScreen = 'ontouchstart' in window || navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0;
24    const isSmallScreen = window.innerWidth <= 768;
25    const userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;
26    const mobileRegex = /android|webos|iphone|ipad|ipod|blackberry|iemobile|opera mini/i;
27    const isMobileUserAgent = mobileRegex.test(userAgent.toLowerCase());
28    return (hasTouchScreen && isSmallScreen) || isMobileUserAgent;
29  }, []);
30
31  const constants = useMemo(
32    () => ({
33      borderWidth: 3,
34      cornerSize: 12
35    }),
36    []
37  );
38
39  const moveCursor = useCallback((x, y) => {
40    if (!cursorRef.current) return;
41    gsap.to(cursorRef.current, {
42      x,
43      y,
44      duration: 0.1,
45      ease: 'power3.out'
46    });
47  }, []);
48
49  useEffect(() => {
50    if (isMobile || !cursorRef.current) return;
51
52    const originalCursor = document.body.style.cursor;
53    if (hideDefaultCursor) {
54      document.body.style.cursor = 'none';
55    }
56
57    const cursor = cursorRef.current;
58    cornersRef.current = cursor.querySelectorAll('.target-cursor-corner');
59
60    let activeTarget = null;
61    let currentLeaveHandler = null;
62    let resumeTimeout = null;
63
64    const cleanupTarget = target => {
65      if (currentLeaveHandler) {
66        target.removeEventListener('mouseleave', currentLeaveHandler);
67      }
68      currentLeaveHandler = null;
69    };
70
71    gsap.set(cursor, {
72      xPercent: -50,
73      yPercent: -50,
74      x: window.innerWidth / 2,
75      y: window.innerHeight / 2
76    });
77
78    const createSpinTimeline = () => {
79      if (spinTl.current) {
80        spinTl.current.kill();
81      }
82      spinTl.current = gsap
83        .timeline({ repeat: -1 })
84        .to(cursor, { rotation: '+=360', duration: spinDuration, ease: 'none' });
85    };
86
87    createSpinTimeline();
88
89    const tickerFn = () => {
90      if (!targetCornerPositionsRef.current || !cursorRef.current || !cornersRef.current) {
91        return;
92      }
93
94      const strength = activeStrengthRef.current;
95      if (strength === 0) return;
96
97      const cursorX = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'x');
98      const cursorY = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'y');
99
100      const corners = Array.from(cornersRef.current);
101      corners.forEach((corner, i) => {
102        const currentX = gsap.getProperty(corner, 'x');
103        const currentY = gsap.getProperty(corner, 'y');
104
105        const targetX = targetCornerPositionsRef.current[i].x - cursorX;
106        const targetY = targetCornerPositionsRef.current[i].y - cursorY;
107
108        const finalX = currentX + (targetX - currentX) * strength;
109        const finalY = currentY + (targetY - currentY) * strength;
110
111        const duration = strength >= 0.99 ? (parallaxOn ? 0.2 : 0) : 0.05;
112
113        gsap.to(corner, {
114          x: finalX,
115          y: finalY,
116          duration: duration,
117          ease: duration === 0 ? 'none' : 'power1.out',
118          overwrite: 'auto'
119        });
120      });
121    };
122
123    tickerFnRef.current = tickerFn;
124
125    const moveHandler = e => moveCursor(e.clientX, e.clientY);
126    window.addEventListener('mousemove', moveHandler);
127
128    const scrollHandler = () => {
129      if (!activeTarget || !cursorRef.current) return;
130      const mouseX = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'x');
131      const mouseY = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'y');
132      const elementUnderMouse = document.elementFromPoint(mouseX, mouseY);
133      const isStillOverTarget =
134        elementUnderMouse &&
135        (elementUnderMouse === activeTarget || elementUnderMouse.closest(targetSelector) === activeTarget);
136      if (!isStillOverTarget) {
137        if (currentLeaveHandler) {
138          currentLeaveHandler();
139        }
140      }
141    };
142    window.addEventListener('scroll', scrollHandler, { passive: true });
143
144    const mouseDownHandler = () => {
145      if (!dotRef.current) return;
146      gsap.to(dotRef.current, { scale: 0.7, duration: 0.3 });
147      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 0.9, duration: 0.2 });
148    };
149
150    const mouseUpHandler = () => {
151      if (!dotRef.current) return;
152      gsap.to(dotRef.current, { scale: 1, duration: 0.3 });
153      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 1, duration: 0.2 });
154    };
155
156    window.addEventListener('mousedown', mouseDownHandler);
157    window.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
158
159    const enterHandler = e => {
160      const directTarget = e.target;
161      const allTargets = [];
162      let current = directTarget;
163      while (current && current !== document.body) {
164        if (current.matches(targetSelector)) {
165          allTargets.push(current);
166        }
167        current = current.parentElement;
168      }
169      const target = allTargets[0] || null;
170      if (!target || !cursorRef.current || !cornersRef.current) return;
171      if (activeTarget === target) return;
172      if (activeTarget) {
173        cleanupTarget(activeTarget);
174      }
175      if (resumeTimeout) {
176        clearTimeout(resumeTimeout);
177        resumeTimeout = null;
178      }
179
180      activeTarget = target;
181      const corners = Array.from(cornersRef.current);
182      corners.forEach(corner => gsap.killTweensOf(corner));
183
184      gsap.killTweensOf(cursorRef.current, 'rotation');
185      spinTl.current?.pause();
186      gsap.set(cursorRef.current, { rotation: 0 });
187
188      const rect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
189      const { borderWidth, cornerSize } = constants;
190      const cursorX = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'x');
191      const cursorY = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'y');
192
193      targetCornerPositionsRef.current = [
194        { x: rect.left - borderWidth, y: rect.top - borderWidth },
195        { x: rect.right + borderWidth - cornerSize, y: rect.top - borderWidth },
196        { x: rect.right + borderWidth - cornerSize, y: rect.bottom + borderWidth - cornerSize },
197        { x: rect.left - borderWidth, y: rect.bottom + borderWidth - cornerSize }
198      ];
199
200      isActiveRef.current = true;
201      gsap.ticker.add(tickerFnRef.current);
202
203      gsap.to(activeStrengthRef, {
204        current: 1,
205        duration: hoverDuration,
206        ease: 'power2.out'
207      });
208
209      corners.forEach((corner, i) => {
210        gsap.to(corner, {
211          x: targetCornerPositionsRef.current[i].x - cursorX,
212          y: targetCornerPositionsRef.current[i].y - cursorY,
213          duration: 0.2,
214          ease: 'power2.out'
215        });
216      });
217
218      const leaveHandler = () => {
219        gsap.ticker.remove(tickerFnRef.current);
220
221        isActiveRef.current = false;
222        targetCornerPositionsRef.current = null;
223        gsap.set(activeStrengthRef, { current: 0, overwrite: true });
224        activeTarget = null;
225
226        if (cornersRef.current) {
227          const corners = Array.from(cornersRef.current);
228          gsap.killTweensOf(corners);
229          const { cornerSize } = constants;
230          const positions = [
231            { x: -cornerSize * 1.5, y: -cornerSize * 1.5 },
232            { x: cornerSize * 0.5, y: -cornerSize * 1.5 },
233            { x: cornerSize * 0.5, y: cornerSize * 0.5 },
234            { x: -cornerSize * 1.5, y: cornerSize * 0.5 }
235          ];
236          const tl = gsap.timeline();
237          corners.forEach((corner, index) => {
238            tl.to(
239              corner,
240              {
241                x: positions[index].x,
242                y: positions[index].y,
243                duration: 0.3,
244                ease: 'power3.out'
245              },
246              0
247            );
248          });
249        }
250
251        resumeTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
252          if (!activeTarget && cursorRef.current && spinTl.current) {
253            const currentRotation = gsap.getProperty(cursorRef.current, 'rotation');
254            const normalizedRotation = currentRotation % 360;
255            spinTl.current.kill();
256            spinTl.current = gsap
257              .timeline({ repeat: -1 })
258              .to(cursorRef.current, { rotation: '+=360', duration: spinDuration, ease: 'none' });
259            gsap.to(cursorRef.current, {
260              rotation: normalizedRotation + 360,
261              duration: spinDuration * (1 - normalizedRotation / 360),
262              ease: 'none',
263              onComplete: () => {
264                spinTl.current?.restart();
265              }
266            });
267          }
268          resumeTimeout = null;
269        }, 50);
270
271        cleanupTarget(target);
272      };
273
274      currentLeaveHandler = leaveHandler;
275      target.addEventListener('mouseleave', leaveHandler);
276    };
277
278    window.addEventListener('mouseover', enterHandler, { passive: true });
279
280    return () => {
281      if (tickerFnRef.current) {
282        gsap.ticker.remove(tickerFnRef.current);
283      }
284
285      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', moveHandler);
286      window.removeEventListener('mouseover', enterHandler);
287      window.removeEventListener('scroll', scrollHandler);
288      window.removeEventListener('mousedown', mouseDownHandler);
289      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
290
291      if (activeTarget) {
292        cleanupTarget(activeTarget);
293      }
294
295      spinTl.current?.kill();
296      document.body.style.cursor = originalCursor;
297
298      isActiveRef.current = false;
299      targetCornerPositionsRef.current = null;
300      activeStrengthRef.current = 0;
301    };
302  }, [targetSelector, spinDuration, moveCursor, constants, hideDefaultCursor, isMobile, hoverDuration, parallaxOn]);
303
304  useEffect(() => {
305    if (isMobile || !cursorRef.current || !spinTl.current) return;
306    if (spinTl.current.isActive()) {
307      spinTl.current.kill();
308      spinTl.current = gsap
309        .timeline({ repeat: -1 })
310        .to(cursorRef.current, { rotation: '+=360', duration: spinDuration, ease: 'none' });
311    }
312  }, [spinDuration, isMobile]);
313
314  if (isMobile) {
315    return null;
316  }
317
318  return (
319    <div ref={cursorRef} className="target-cursor-wrapper">
320      <div ref={dotRef} className="target-cursor-dot" />
321      <div className="target-cursor-corner corner-tl" />
322      <div className="target-cursor-corner corner-tr" />
323      <div className="target-cursor-corner corner-br" />
324      <div className="target-cursor-corner corner-bl" />
325    </div>
326  );
327};
328
329export default TargetCursor;
330

Component: Magnet Lines

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/MagnetLines-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import MagnetLines from './MagnetLines';
2
3<MagnetLines
4  rows={10}
5  columns={12}
6  containerSize="40vmin"
7  lineColor="tomato"
8  lineWidth="2px"
9  lineHeight="30px"
10  baseAngle={0}
11  style={{ margin: "2rem auto" }}
12/>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
2import './MagnetLines.css';
3
4export default function MagnetLines({
5  rows = 9,
6  columns = 9,
7  containerSize = '80vmin',
8  lineColor = '#efefef',
9  lineWidth = '1vmin',
10  lineHeight = '6vmin',
11  baseAngle = -10,
12  className = '',
13  style = {}
14}) {
15  const containerRef = useRef(null);
16
17  useEffect(() => {
18    const container = containerRef.current;
19    if (!container) return;
20
21    const items = container.querySelectorAll('span');
22
23    const onPointerMove = pointer => {
24      items.forEach(item => {
25        const rect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
26        const centerX = rect.x + rect.width / 2;
27        const centerY = rect.y + rect.height / 2;
28
29        const b = pointer.x - centerX;
30        const a = pointer.y - centerY;
31        const c = Math.sqrt(a * a + b * b) || 1;
32        const r = ((Math.acos(b / c) * 180) / Math.PI) * (pointer.y > centerY ? 1 : -1);
33
34        item.style.setProperty('--rotate', `${r}deg`);
35      });
36    };
37
38    window.addEventListener('pointermove', onPointerMove);
39
40    if (items.length) {
41      const middleIndex = Math.floor(items.length / 2);
42      const rect = items[middleIndex].getBoundingClientRect();
43      onPointerMove({ x: rect.x, y: rect.y });
44    }
45
46    return () => {
47      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', onPointerMove);
48    };
49  }, []);
50
51  const total = rows * columns;
52  const spans = Array.from({ length: total }, (_, i) => (
53    <span
54      key={i}
55      style={{
56        '--rotate': `${baseAngle}deg`,
57        backgroundColor: lineColor,
58        width: lineWidth,
59        height: lineHeight
60      }}
61    />
62  ));
63
64  return (
65    <div
66      ref={containerRef}
67      className={`magnetLines-container ${className}`}
68      style={{
69        display: 'grid',
70        gridTemplateColumns: `repeat(${columns}, 1fr)`,
71        gridTemplateRows: `repeat(${rows}, 1fr)`,
72        width: containerSize,
73        height: containerSize,
74        ...style
75      }}
76    >
77      {spans}
78    </div>
79  );
80}
81

Extra Config/Code:
1.magnetLines-container {
2  display: grid;
3  grid-template-columns: repeat(var(--columns), 1fr);
4  grid-template-rows: repeat(var(--rows), 1fr);
5
6  justify-items: center;
7  align-items: center;
8
9  width: 80vmin;
10  height: 80vmin;
11}
12
13.magnetLines-container span {
14  display: block;
15  transform-origin: center;
16  will-change: transform;
17  transform: rotate(var(--rotate));
18}

Component: Gradual Blur

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/GradualBlur-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// Component added by Ansh - github.com/ansh-dhanani
2
3import GradualBlur from './GradualBlur';
4
5<section style={{position: 'relative',height: 500,overflow: 'hidden'}}>
6  <div style={{ height: '100%',overflowY: 'auto',padding: '6rem 2rem' }}>
7    <!-- Content Here - such as an image or text -->
8  </div>
9
10  <GradualBlur
11    target="parent"
12    position="bottom"
13    height="7rem"
14    strength={2}
15    divCount={5}
16    curve="bezier"
17    exponential
18    opacity={1}
19  />
20</section>

Code:
1import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState, useMemo } from 'react';
2import * as math from 'mathjs';
3
4import './GradualBlur.css';
5
6const DEFAULT_CONFIG = {
7  position: 'bottom',
8  strength: 2,
9  height: '6rem',
10  divCount: 5,
11  exponential: false,
12  zIndex: 1000,
13  animated: false,
14  duration: '0.3s',
15  easing: 'ease-out',
16  opacity: 1,
17  curve: 'linear',
18  responsive: false,
19  target: 'parent',
20  className: '',
21  style: {}
22};
23
24const PRESETS = {
25  top: { position: 'top', height: '6rem' },
26  bottom: { position: 'bottom', height: '6rem' },
27  left: { position: 'left', height: '6rem' },
28  right: { position: 'right', height: '6rem' },
29  subtle: { height: '4rem', strength: 1, opacity: 0.8, divCount: 3 },
30  intense: { height: '10rem', strength: 4, divCount: 8, exponential: true },
31  smooth: { height: '8rem', curve: 'bezier', divCount: 10 },
32  sharp: { height: '5rem', curve: 'linear', divCount: 4 },
33  header: { position: 'top', height: '8rem', curve: 'ease-out' },
34  footer: { position: 'bottom', height: '8rem', curve: 'ease-out' },
35  sidebar: { position: 'left', height: '6rem', strength: 2.5 },
36  'page-header': { position: 'top', height: '10rem', target: 'page', strength: 3 },
37  'page-footer': { position: 'bottom', height: '10rem', target: 'page', strength: 3 }
38};
39
40const CURVE_FUNCTIONS = {
41  linear: p => p,
42  bezier: p => p * p * (3 - 2 * p),
43  'ease-in': p => p * p,
44  'ease-out': p => 1 - Math.pow(1 - p, 2),
45  'ease-in-out': p => (p < 0.5 ? 2 * p * p : 1 - Math.pow(-2 * p + 2, 2) / 2)
46};
47
48const mergeConfigs = (...configs) => configs.reduce((acc, c) => ({ ...acc, ...c }), {});
49const getGradientDirection = position =>
50  ({
51    top: 'to top',
52    bottom: 'to bottom',
53    left: 'to left',
54    right: 'to right'
55  })[position] || 'to bottom';
56
57const debounce = (fn, wait) => {
58  let t;
59  return (...a) => {
60    clearTimeout(t);
61    t = setTimeout(() => fn(...a), wait);
62  };
63};
64
65const useResponsiveDimension = (responsive, config, key) => {
66  const [value, setValue] = useState(config[key]);
67  useEffect(() => {
68    if (!responsive) return;
69    const calc = () => {
70      const w = window.innerWidth;
71      let v = config[key];
72      if (w <= 480 && config[`mobile${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`])
73        v = config[`mobile${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`];
74      else if (w <= 768 && config[`tablet${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`])
75        v = config[`tablet${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`];
76      else if (w <= 1024 && config[`desktop${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`])
77        v = config[`desktop${key[0].toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`];
78      setValue(v);
79    };
80    const debounced = debounce(calc, 100);
81    calc();
82    window.addEventListener('resize', debounced);
83    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', debounced);
84  }, [responsive, config, key]);
85  return responsive ? value : config[key];
86};
87
88const useIntersectionObserver = (ref, shouldObserve = false) => {
89  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(!shouldObserve);
90
91  useEffect(() => {
92    if (!shouldObserve || !ref.current) return;
93
94    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(([entry]) => setIsVisible(entry.isIntersecting), { threshold: 0.1 });
95
96    observer.observe(ref.current);
97    return () => observer.disconnect();
98  }, [ref, shouldObserve]);
99
100  return isVisible;
101};
102
103function GradualBlur(props) {
104  const containerRef = useRef(null);
105  const [isHovered, setIsHovered] = useState(false);
106
107  const config = useMemo(() => {
108    const presetConfig = props.preset && PRESETS[props.preset] ? PRESETS[props.preset] : {};
109    return mergeConfigs(DEFAULT_CONFIG, presetConfig, props);
110  }, [props]);
111
112  const responsiveHeight = useResponsiveDimension(config.responsive, config, 'height');
113  const responsiveWidth = useResponsiveDimension(config.responsive, config, 'width');
114
115  const isVisible = useIntersectionObserver(containerRef, config.animated === 'scroll');
116
117  const blurDivs = useMemo(() => {
118    const divs = [];
119    const increment = 100 / config.divCount;
120    const currentStrength =
121      isHovered && config.hoverIntensity ? config.strength * config.hoverIntensity : config.strength;
122
123    const curveFunc = CURVE_FUNCTIONS[config.curve] || CURVE_FUNCTIONS.linear;
124
125    for (let i = 1; i <= config.divCount; i++) {
126      let progress = i / config.divCount;
127      progress = curveFunc(progress);
128
129      let blurValue;
130      if (config.exponential) {
131        blurValue = math.pow(2, progress * 4) * 0.0625 * currentStrength;
132      } else {
133        blurValue = 0.0625 * (progress * config.divCount + 1) * currentStrength;
134      }
135
136      const p1 = math.round((increment * i - increment) * 10) / 10;
137      const p2 = math.round(increment * i * 10) / 10;
138      const p3 = math.round((increment * i + increment) * 10) / 10;
139      const p4 = math.round((increment * i + increment * 2) * 10) / 10;
140
141      let gradient = `transparent ${p1}%, black ${p2}%`;
142      if (p3 <= 100) gradient += `, black ${p3}%`;
143      if (p4 <= 100) gradient += `, transparent ${p4}%`;
144
145      const direction = getGradientDirection(config.position);
146
147      const divStyle = {
148        position: 'absolute',
149        inset: '0',
150        maskImage: `linear-gradient(${direction}, ${gradient})`,
151        WebkitMaskImage: `linear-gradient(${direction}, ${gradient})`,
152        backdropFilter: `blur(${blurValue.toFixed(3)}rem)`,
153        WebkitBackdropFilter: `blur(${blurValue.toFixed(3)}rem)`,
154        opacity: config.opacity,
155        transition:
156          config.animated && config.animated !== 'scroll'
157            ? `backdrop-filter ${config.duration} ${config.easing}`
158            : undefined
159      };
160
161      divs.push(<div key={i} style={divStyle} />);
162    }
163
164    return divs;
165  }, [config, isHovered]);
166
167  const containerStyle = useMemo(() => {
168    const isVertical = ['top', 'bottom'].includes(config.position);
169    const isHorizontal = ['left', 'right'].includes(config.position);
170    const isPageTarget = config.target === 'page';
171
172    const baseStyle = {
173      position: isPageTarget ? 'fixed' : 'absolute',
174      pointerEvents: config.hoverIntensity ? 'auto' : 'none',
175      opacity: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
176      transition: config.animated ? `opacity ${config.duration} ${config.easing}` : undefined,
177      zIndex: isPageTarget ? config.zIndex + 100 : config.zIndex,
178      ...config.style
179    };
180
181    if (isVertical) {
182      baseStyle.height = responsiveHeight;
183      baseStyle.width = responsiveWidth || '100%';
184      baseStyle[config.position] = 0;
185      baseStyle.left = 0;
186      baseStyle.right = 0;
187    } else if (isHorizontal) {
188      baseStyle.width = responsiveWidth || responsiveHeight;
189      baseStyle.height = '100%';
190      baseStyle[config.position] = 0;
191      baseStyle.top = 0;
192      baseStyle.bottom = 0;
193    }
194
195    return baseStyle;
196  }, [config, responsiveHeight, responsiveWidth, isVisible]);
197
198  const { hoverIntensity, animated, onAnimationComplete, duration } = config;
199
200  useEffect(() => {
201    if (isVisible && animated === 'scroll' && onAnimationComplete) {
202      const ms = parseFloat(duration) * 1000;
203      const t = setTimeout(() => onAnimationComplete(), ms);
204      return () => clearTimeout(t);
205    }
206  }, [isVisible, animated, onAnimationComplete, duration]);
207
208  return (
209    <div
210      ref={containerRef}
211      className={`gradual-blur ${config.target === 'page' ? 'gradual-blur-page' : 'gradual-blur-parent'} ${config.className}`}
212      style={containerStyle}
213      onMouseEnter={hoverIntensity ? () => setIsHovered(true) : undefined}
214      onMouseLeave={hoverIntensity ? () => setIsHovered(false) : undefined}
215    >
216      <div
217        className="gradual-blur-inner"
218        style={{
219          position: 'relative',
220          width: '100%',
221          height: '100%'
222        }}
223      >
224        {blurDivs}
225      </div>
226    </div>
227  );
228}
229
230const GradualBlurMemo = React.memo(GradualBlur);
231GradualBlurMemo.displayName = 'GradualBlur';
232GradualBlurMemo.PRESETS = PRESETS;
233GradualBlurMemo.CURVE_FUNCTIONS = CURVE_FUNCTIONS;
234export default GradualBlurMemo;
235
236const injectStyles = () => {
237  if (typeof document === 'undefined') return;
238
239  const styleId = 'gradual-blur-styles';
240  if (document.getElementById(styleId)) return;
241
242  const styleElement = document.createElement('style');
243  styleElement.id = styleId;
244  styleElement.textContent = `
245  .gradual-blur { pointer-events: none; transition: opacity 0.3s ease-out; }
246  .gradual-blur-parent { overflow: hidden; }
247  .gradual-blur-inner { pointer-events: none; }`;
248
249  document.head.appendChild(styleElement);
250};
251
252if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {
253  injectStyles();
254}
255

Extra Config/Code:
1.gradual-blur-inner {
2  position: relative;
3  width: 100%;
4  height: 100%;
5}
6
7.gradual-blur-inner > div {
8  -webkit-backdrop-filter: inherit;
9  backdrop-filter: inherit;
10}
11
12.gradual-blur {
13  isolation: isolate;
14}
15
16@supports not (backdrop-filter: blur(1px)) {
17  .gradual-blur-inner > div {
18    background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);
19    opacity: 0.5;
20  }
21}
22
23.gradual-blur-fixed {
24  position: fixed !important;
25  top: 0;
26  left: 0;
27  right: 0;
28  bottom: 0;
29  pointer-events: none;
30  z-index: 1000;
31}
