Code:
1import { useLayoutEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3// use your own icon import if react-icons is not available
4import { GoArrowUpRight } from 'react-icons/go';
5import './CardNav.css';
6
7const CardNav = ({
8  logo,
9  logoAlt = 'Logo',
10  items,
11  className = '',
12  ease = 'power3.out',
13  baseColor = '#fff',
14  menuColor,
15  buttonBgColor,
16  buttonTextColor
17}) => {
18  const [isHamburgerOpen, setIsHamburgerOpen] = useState(false);
19  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);
20  const navRef = useRef(null);
21  const cardsRef = useRef([]);
22  const tlRef = useRef(null);
23
24  const calculateHeight = () => {
25    const navEl = navRef.current;
26    if (!navEl) return 260;
27
28    const isMobile = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 768px)').matches;
29    if (isMobile) {
30      const contentEl = navEl.querySelector('.card-nav-content');
31      if (contentEl) {
32        const wasVisible = contentEl.style.visibility;
33        const wasPointerEvents = contentEl.style.pointerEvents;
34        const wasPosition = contentEl.style.position;
35        const wasHeight = contentEl.style.height;
36
37        contentEl.style.visibility = 'visible';
38        contentEl.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
39        contentEl.style.position = 'static';
40        contentEl.style.height = 'auto';
41
42        contentEl.offsetHeight;
43
44        const topBar = 60;
45        const padding = 16;
46        const contentHeight = contentEl.scrollHeight;
47
48        contentEl.style.visibility = wasVisible;
49        contentEl.style.pointerEvents = wasPointerEvents;
50        contentEl.style.position = wasPosition;
51        contentEl.style.height = wasHeight;
52
53        return topBar + contentHeight + padding;
54      }
55    }
56    return 260;
57  };
58
59  const createTimeline = () => {
60    const navEl = navRef.current;
61    if (!navEl) return null;
62
63    gsap.set(navEl, { height: 60, overflow: 'hidden' });
64    gsap.set(cardsRef.current, { y: 50, opacity: 0 });
65
66    const tl = gsap.timeline({ paused: true });
67
68    tl.to(navEl, {
69      height: calculateHeight,
70      duration: 0.4,
71      ease
72    });
73
74    tl.to(cardsRef.current, { y: 0, opacity: 1, duration: 0.4, ease, stagger: 0.08 }, '-=0.1');
75
76    return tl;
77  };
78
79  useLayoutEffect(() => {
80    const tl = createTimeline();
81    tlRef.current = tl;
82
83    return () => {
84      tl?.kill();
85      tlRef.current = null;
86    };
87    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
88  }, [ease, items]);
89
90  useLayoutEffect(() => {
91    const handleResize = () => {
92      if (!tlRef.current) return;
93
94      if (isExpanded) {
95        const newHeight = calculateHeight();
96        gsap.set(navRef.current, { height: newHeight });
97
98        tlRef.current.kill();
99        const newTl = createTimeline();
100        if (newTl) {
101          newTl.progress(1);
102          tlRef.current = newTl;
103        }
104      } else {
105        tlRef.current.kill();
106        const newTl = createTimeline();
107        if (newTl) {
108          tlRef.current = newTl;
109        }
110      }
111    };
112
113    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
114    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
115    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
116  }, [isExpanded]);
117
118  const toggleMenu = () => {
119    const tl = tlRef.current;
120    if (!tl) return;
121    if (!isExpanded) {
122      setIsHamburgerOpen(true);
123      setIsExpanded(true);
124      tl.play(0);
125    } else {
126      setIsHamburgerOpen(false);
127      tl.eventCallback('onReverseComplete', () => setIsExpanded(false));
128      tl.reverse();
129    }
130  };
131
132  const setCardRef = i => el => {
133    if (el) cardsRef.current[i] = el;
134  };
135
136  return (
137    <div className={`card-nav-container ${className}`}>
138      <nav ref={navRef} className={`card-nav ${isExpanded ? 'open' : ''}`} style={{ backgroundColor: baseColor }}>
139        <div className="card-nav-top">
140          <div
141            className={`hamburger-menu ${isHamburgerOpen ? 'open' : ''}`}
142            onClick={toggleMenu}
143            role="button"
144            aria-label={isExpanded ? 'Close menu' : 'Open menu'}
145            tabIndex={0}
146            style={{ color: menuColor || '#000' }}
147          >
148            <div className="hamburger-line" />
149            <div className="hamburger-line" />
150          </div>
151
152          <div className="logo-container">
153            <img src={logo} alt={logoAlt} className="logo" />
154          </div>
155
156          <button
157            type="button"
158            className="card-nav-cta-button"
159            style={{ backgroundColor: buttonBgColor, color: buttonTextColor }}
160          >
161            Get Started
162          </button>
163        </div>
164
165        <div className="card-nav-content" aria-hidden={!isExpanded}>
166          {(items || []).slice(0, 3).map((item, idx) => (
167            <div
168              key={`${item.label}-${idx}`}
169              className="nav-card"
170              ref={setCardRef(idx)}
171              style={{ backgroundColor: item.bgColor, color: item.textColor }}
172            >
173              <div className="nav-card-label">{item.label}</div>
174              <div className="nav-card-links">
175                {item.links?.map((lnk, i) => (
176                  <a key={`${lnk.label}-${i}`} className="nav-card-link" href={lnk.href} aria-label={lnk.ariaLabel}>
177                    <GoArrowUpRight className="nav-card-link-icon" aria-hidden="true" />
178                    {lnk.label}
179                  </a>
180                ))}
181              </div>
182            </div>
183          ))}
184        </div>
185      </nav>
186    </div>
187  );
188};
189
190export default CardNav;
191

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Stack

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Stack-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Stack from './Stack'
2
3const images = [
4  "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1480074568708-e7b720bb3f09?q=80&w=500&auto=format",
5  "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1449844908441-8829872d2607?q=80&w=500&auto=format",
6  "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1452626212852-811d58933cae?q=80&w=500&auto=format",
7  "https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1572120360610-d971b9d7767c?q=80&w=500&auto=format"
8];
9
10<div style={{ width: 208, height: 208 }}>
11  <Stack
12    randomRotation={false}
13    sensitivity={200}
14    sendToBackOnClick={true}
15    cards={images.map((src, i) => (
16      <img 
17        key={i} 
18        src={src} 
19        alt={`card-${i + 1}`} 
20        style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', objectFit: 'cover' }} 
21      />
22    ))}
23    autoplay={false}
24    autoplayDelay={3000}
25    pauseOnHover={false}
26/>
27</div>

Code:
1import { motion, useMotionValue, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
2import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
3import './Stack.css';
4
5function CardRotate({ children, onSendToBack, sensitivity, disableDrag = false }) {
6  const x = useMotionValue(0);
7  const y = useMotionValue(0);
8  const rotateX = useTransform(y, [-100, 100], [60, -60]);
9  const rotateY = useTransform(x, [-100, 100], [-60, 60]);
10
11  function handleDragEnd(_, info) {
12    if (Math.abs(info.offset.x) > sensitivity || Math.abs(info.offset.y) > sensitivity) {
13      onSendToBack();
14    } else {
15      x.set(0);
16      y.set(0);
17    }
18  }
19
20  if (disableDrag) {
21    return (
22      <motion.div className="card-rotate-disabled" style={{ x: 0, y: 0 }}>
23        {children}
24      </motion.div>
25    );
26  }
27
28  return (
29    <motion.div
30      className="card-rotate"
31      style={{ x, y, rotateX, rotateY }}
32      drag
33      dragConstraints={{ top: 0, right: 0, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}
34      dragElastic={0.6}
35      whileTap={{ cursor: 'grabbing' }}
36      onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}
37    >
38      {children}
39    </motion.div>
40  );
41}
42
43export default function Stack({
44  randomRotation = false,
45  sensitivity = 200,
46  cards = [],
47  animationConfig = { stiffness: 260, damping: 20 },
48  sendToBackOnClick = false,
49  autoplay = false,
50  autoplayDelay = 3000,
51  pauseOnHover = false,
52  mobileClickOnly = false,
53  mobileBreakpoint = 768
54}) {
55  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = useState(false);
56  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);
57
58  useEffect(() => {
59    const checkMobile = () => {
60      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < mobileBreakpoint);
61    };
62
63    checkMobile();
64    window.addEventListener('resize', checkMobile);
65    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', checkMobile);
66  }, [mobileBreakpoint]);
67
68  const shouldDisableDrag = mobileClickOnly && isMobile;
69  const shouldEnableClick = sendToBackOnClick || shouldDisableDrag;
70
71  const [stack, setStack] = useState(() => {
72    if (cards.length) {
73      return cards.map((content, index) => ({ id: index + 1, content }));
74    } else {
75      return [
76        {
77          id: 1,
78          content: (
79            <img
80              src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1480074568708-e7b720bb3f09?q=80&w=500&auto=format"
81              alt="card-1"
82              className="card-image"
83            />
84          )
85        },
86        {
87          id: 2,
88          content: (
89            <img
90              src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1449844908441-8829872d2607?q=80&w=500&auto=format"
91              alt="card-2"
92              className="card-image"
93            />
94          )
95        },
96        {
97          id: 3,
98          content: (
99            <img
100              src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1452626212852-811d58933cae?q=80&w=500&auto=format"
101              alt="card-3"
102              className="card-image"
103            />
104          )
105        },
106        {
107          id: 4,
108          content: (
109            <img
110              src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1572120360610-d971b9d7767c?q=80&w=500&auto=format"
111              alt="card-4"
112              className="card-image"
113            />
114          )
115        }
116      ];
117    }
118  });
119
120  useEffect(() => {
121    if (cards.length) {
122      setStack(cards.map((content, index) => ({ id: index + 1, content })));
123    }
124  }, [cards]);
125
126  const sendToBack = id => {
127    setStack(prev => {
128      const newStack = [...prev];
129      const index = newStack.findIndex(card => card.id === id);
130      const [card] = newStack.splice(index, 1);
131      newStack.unshift(card);
132      return newStack;
133    });
134  };
135
136  useEffect(() => {
137    if (autoplay && stack.length > 1 && !isPaused) {
138      const interval = setInterval(() => {
139        const topCardId = stack[stack.length - 1].id;
140        sendToBack(topCardId);
141      }, autoplayDelay);
142
143      return () => clearInterval(interval);
144    }
145  }, [autoplay, autoplayDelay, stack, isPaused]);
146
147  return (
148    <div
149      className="stack-container"
150      onMouseEnter={() => pauseOnHover && setIsPaused(true)}
151      onMouseLeave={() => pauseOnHover && setIsPaused(false)}
152    >
153      {stack.map((card, index) => {
154        const randomRotate = randomRotation ? Math.random() * 10 - 5 : 0;
155        return (
156          <CardRotate
157            key={card.id}
158            onSendToBack={() => sendToBack(card.id)}
159            sensitivity={sensitivity}
160            disableDrag={shouldDisableDrag}
161          >
162            <motion.div
163              className="card"
164              onClick={() => shouldEnableClick && sendToBack(card.id)}
165              animate={{
166                rotateZ: (stack.length - index - 1) * 4 + randomRotate,
167                scale: 1 + index * 0.06 - stack.length * 0.06,
168                transformOrigin: '90% 90%'
169              }}
170              initial={false}
171              transition={{
172                type: 'spring',
173                stiffness: animationConfig.stiffness,
174                damping: animationConfig.damping
175              }}
176            >
177              {card.content}
178            </motion.div>
179          </CardRotate>
180        );
181      })}
182    </div>
183  );
184}
185

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Fluid Glass

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/FluidGlass-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// IMPORTANT INFO BELOW
2// This component requires a 3D model to function correctly.
3// You can find three example models in the 'public/assets/3d' directory of the repository:
4// - 'lens.glb'
5// - 'bar.glb'
6// - 'cube.glb'
7// Make sure to place these models in the correct directory or update the paths accordingly.
8
9import FluidGlass from './FluidGlass'
10
11<div style={{ height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
12  <FluidGlass 
13    mode="lens" // or "bar", "cube"
14    lensProps={{
15      scale: 0.25,
16      ior: 1.15,
17      thickness: 5,
18      chromaticAberration: 0.1,
19      anisotropy: 0.01  
20    }}
21    barProps={} // add specific props if using bar mode
22    cubeProps={} // add specific props if using cube mode
23    mode="lens"
24    scale={0.25}
25    ior={1.15}
26    thickness={2}
27    transmission={1}
28    roughness={0}
29    chromaticAberration={0.05}
30    anisotropy={0.01}
31/>
32</div>

Code:
1/* eslint-disable react/no-unknown-property */
2import * as THREE from 'three';
3import { useRef, useState, useEffect, memo } from 'react';
4import { Canvas, createPortal, useFrame, useThree } from '@react-three/fiber';
5import {
6  useFBO,
7  useGLTF,
8  useScroll,
9  Image,
10  Scroll,
11  Preload,
12  ScrollControls,
13  MeshTransmissionMaterial,
14  Text
15} from '@react-three/drei';
16import { easing } from 'maath';
17
18export default function FluidGlass({ mode = 'lens', lensProps = {}, barProps = {}, cubeProps = {} }) {
19  const Wrapper = mode === 'bar' ? Bar : mode === 'cube' ? Cube : Lens;
20  const rawOverrides = mode === 'bar' ? barProps : mode === 'cube' ? cubeProps : lensProps;
21
22  const {
23    navItems = [
24      { label: 'Home', link: '' },
25      { label: 'About', link: '' },
26      { label: 'Contact', link: '' }
27    ],
28    ...modeProps
29  } = rawOverrides;
30
31  return (
32    <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0, 20], fov: 15 }} gl={{ alpha: true }}>
33      <ScrollControls damping={0.2} pages={3} distance={0.4}>
34        {mode === 'bar' && <NavItems items={navItems} />}
35        <Wrapper modeProps={modeProps}>
36          <Scroll>
37            <Typography />
38            <Images />
39          </Scroll>
40          <Scroll html />
41          <Preload />
42        </Wrapper>
43      </ScrollControls>
44    </Canvas>
45  );
46}
47
48const ModeWrapper = memo(function ModeWrapper({
49  children,
50  glb,
51  geometryKey,
52  lockToBottom = false,
53  followPointer = true,
54  modeProps = {},
55  ...props
56}) {
57  const ref = useRef();
58  const { nodes } = useGLTF(glb);
59  const buffer = useFBO();
60  const { viewport: vp } = useThree();
61  const [scene] = useState(() => new THREE.Scene());
62  const geoWidthRef = useRef(1);
63
64  useEffect(() => {
65    const geo = nodes[geometryKey]?.geometry;
66    geo.computeBoundingBox();
67    geoWidthRef.current = geo.boundingBox.max.x - geo.boundingBox.min.x || 1;
68  }, [nodes, geometryKey]);
69
70  useFrame((state, delta) => {
71    const { gl, viewport, pointer, camera } = state;
72    const v = viewport.getCurrentViewport(camera, [0, 0, 15]);
73
74    const destX = followPointer ? (pointer.x * v.width) / 2 : 0;
75    const destY = lockToBottom ? -v.height / 2 + 0.2 : followPointer ? (pointer.y * v.height) / 2 : 0;
76    easing.damp3(ref.current.position, [destX, destY, 15], 0.15, delta);
77
78    if (modeProps.scale == null) {
79      const maxWorld = v.width * 0.9;
80      const desired = maxWorld / geoWidthRef.current;
81      ref.current.scale.setScalar(Math.min(0.15, desired));
82    }
83
84    gl.setRenderTarget(buffer);
85    gl.render(scene, camera);
86    gl.setRenderTarget(null);
87
88    // Background Color
89    gl.setClearColor(0x5227ff, 1);
90  });
91
92  const { scale, ior, thickness, anisotropy, chromaticAberration, ...extraMat } = modeProps;
93
94  return (
95    <>
96      {createPortal(children, scene)}
97      <mesh scale={[vp.width, vp.height, 1]}>
98        <planeGeometry />
99        <meshBasicMaterial map={buffer.texture} transparent />
100      </mesh>
101      <mesh ref={ref} scale={scale ?? 0.15} rotation-x={Math.PI / 2} geometry={nodes[geometryKey]?.geometry} {...props}>
102        <MeshTransmissionMaterial
103          buffer={buffer.texture}
104          ior={ior ?? 1.15}
105          thickness={thickness ?? 5}
106          anisotropy={anisotropy ?? 0.01}
107          chromaticAberration={chromaticAberration ?? 0.1}
108          {...extraMat}
109        />
110      </mesh>
111    </>
112  );
113});
114
115function Lens({ modeProps, ...p }) {
116  return <ModeWrapper glb="/assets/3d/lens.glb" geometryKey="Cylinder" followPointer modeProps={modeProps} {...p} />;
117}
118
119function Cube({ modeProps, ...p }) {
120  return <ModeWrapper glb="/assets/3d/cube.glb" geometryKey="Cube" followPointer modeProps={modeProps} {...p} />;
121}
122
123function Bar({ modeProps = {}, ...p }) {
124  const defaultMat = {
125    transmission: 1,
126    roughness: 0,
127    thickness: 10,
128    ior: 1.15,
129    color: '#ffffff',
130    attenuationColor: '#ffffff',
131    attenuationDistance: 0.25
132  };
133
134  return (
135    <ModeWrapper
136      glb="/assets/3d/bar.glb"
137      geometryKey="Cube"
138      lockToBottom
139      followPointer={false}
140      modeProps={{ ...defaultMat, ...modeProps }}
141      {...p}
142    />
143  );
144}
145
146function NavItems({ items }) {
147  const group = useRef();
148  const { viewport, camera } = useThree();
149
150  const DEVICE = {
151    mobile: { max: 639, spacing: 0.2, fontSize: 0.035 },
152    tablet: { max: 1023, spacing: 0.24, fontSize: 0.035 },
153    desktop: { max: Infinity, spacing: 0.3, fontSize: 0.035 }
154  };
155  const getDevice = () => {
156    const w = window.innerWidth;
157    return w <= DEVICE.mobile.max ? 'mobile' : w <= DEVICE.tablet.max ? 'tablet' : 'desktop';
158  };
159
160  const [device, setDevice] = useState(getDevice());
161
162  useEffect(() => {
163    const onResize = () => setDevice(getDevice());
164    window.addEventListener('resize', onResize);
165    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', onResize);
166    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
167  }, []);
168
169  const { spacing, fontSize } = DEVICE[device];
170
171  useFrame(() => {
172    if (!group.current) return;
173    const v = viewport.getCurrentViewport(camera, [0, 0, 15]);
174    group.current.position.set(0, -v.height / 2 + 0.2, 15.1);
175
176    group.current.children.forEach((child, i) => {
177      child.position.x = (i - (items.length - 1) / 2) * spacing;
178    });
179  });
180
181  const handleNavigate = link => {
182    if (!link) return;
183    link.startsWith('#') ? (window.location.hash = link) : (window.location.href = link);
184  };
185
186  return (
187    <group ref={group} renderOrder={10}>
188      {items.map(({ label, link }) => (
189        <Text
190          key={label}
191          fontSize={fontSize}
192          color="white"
193          anchorX="center"
194          anchorY="middle"
195          depthWrite={false}
196          outlineWidth={0}
197          outlineBlur="20%"
198          outlineColor="#000"
199          outlineOpacity={0.5}
200          depthTest={false}
201          renderOrder={10}
202          onClick={e => {
203            e.stopPropagation();
204            handleNavigate(link);
205          }}
206          onPointerOver={() => (document.body.style.cursor = 'pointer')}
207          onPointerOut={() => (document.body.style.cursor = 'auto')}
208        >
209          {label}
210        </Text>
211      ))}
212    </group>
213  );
214}
215
216function Images() {
217  const group = useRef();
218  const data = useScroll();
219  const { height } = useThree(s => s.viewport);
220
221  useFrame(() => {
222    group.current.children[0].material.zoom = 1 + data.range(0, 1 / 3) / 3;
223    group.current.children[1].material.zoom = 1 + data.range(0, 1 / 3) / 3;
224    group.current.children[2].material.zoom = 1 + data.range(1.15 / 3, 1 / 3) / 2;
225    group.current.children[3].material.zoom = 1 + data.range(1.15 / 3, 1 / 3) / 2;
226    group.current.children[4].material.zoom = 1 + data.range(1.15 / 3, 1 / 3) / 2;
227  });
228
229  return (
230    <group ref={group}>
231      <Image position={[-2, 0, 0]} scale={[3, height / 1.1, 1]} url="/assets/demo/cs1.webp" />
232      <Image position={[2, 0, 3]} scale={3} url="/assets/demo/cs2.webp" />
233      <Image position={[-2.05, -height, 6]} scale={[1, 3, 1]} url="/assets/demo/cs3.webp" />
234      <Image position={[-0.6, -height, 9]} scale={[1, 2, 1]} url="/assets/demo/cs1.webp" />
235      <Image position={[0.75, -height, 10.5]} scale={1.5} url="/assets/demo/cs2.webp" />
236    </group>
237  );
238}
239
240function Typography() {
241  const DEVICE = {
242    mobile: { fontSize: 0.2 },
243    tablet: { fontSize: 0.4 },
244    desktop: { fontSize: 0.6 }
245  };
246  const getDevice = () => {
247    const w = window.innerWidth;
248    return w <= 639 ? 'mobile' : w <= 1023 ? 'tablet' : 'desktop';
249  };
250
251  const [device, setDevice] = useState(getDevice());
252
253  useEffect(() => {
254    const onResize = () => setDevice(getDevice());
255    window.addEventListener('resize', onResize);
256    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', onResize);
257  }, []);
258
259  const { fontSize } = DEVICE[device];
260
261  return (
262    <Text
263      position={[0, 0, 12]}
264      fontSize={fontSize}
265      letterSpacing={-0.05}
266      outlineWidth={0}
267      outlineBlur="20%"
268      outlineColor="#000"
269      outlineOpacity={0.5}
270      color="white"
271      anchorX="center"
272      anchorY="middle"
273    >
274      React Bits
275    </Text>
276  );
277}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Pill Nav

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/PillNav-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import PillNav from './PillNav';
2import logo from '/path/to/logo.svg';
3
4<PillNav
5  logo={logo}
6  logoAlt="Company Logo"
7  items={[
8    { label: 'Home', href: '/' },
9    { label: 'About', href: '/about' },
10    { label: 'Services', href: '/services' },
11    { label: 'Contact', href: '/contact' }
12  ]}
13  activeHref="/"
14  className="custom-nav"
15  ease="power2.easeOut"
16  baseColor="#000000"
17  pillColor="#ffffff"
18  hoveredPillTextColor="#ffffff"
19  pillTextColor="#000000"
20  theme="light"
21  initialLoadAnimation={false}
22/>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { Link } from 'react-router-dom';
3import { gsap } from 'gsap';
4import './PillNav.css';
5
6const PillNav = ({
7  logo,
8  logoAlt = 'Logo',
9  items,
10  activeHref,
11  className = '',
12  ease = 'power3.easeOut',
13  baseColor = '#fff',
14  pillColor = '#060010',
15  hoveredPillTextColor = '#060010',
16  pillTextColor,
17  onMobileMenuClick,
18  initialLoadAnimation = true
19}) => {
20  const resolvedPillTextColor = pillTextColor ?? baseColor;
21  const [isMobileMenuOpen, setIsMobileMenuOpen] = useState(false);
22  const circleRefs = useRef([]);
23  const tlRefs = useRef([]);
24  const activeTweenRefs = useRef([]);
25  const logoImgRef = useRef(null);
26  const logoTweenRef = useRef(null);
27  const hamburgerRef = useRef(null);
28  const mobileMenuRef = useRef(null);
29  const navItemsRef = useRef(null);
30  const logoRef = useRef(null);
31
32  useEffect(() => {
33    const layout = () => {
34      circleRefs.current.forEach(circle => {
35        if (!circle?.parentElement) return;
36
37        const pill = circle.parentElement;
38        const rect = pill.getBoundingClientRect();
39        const { width: w, height: h } = rect;
40        const R = ((w * w) / 4 + h * h) / (2 * h);
41        const D = Math.ceil(2 * R) + 2;
42        const delta = Math.ceil(R - Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, R * R - (w * w) / 4))) + 1;
43        const originY = D - delta;
44
45        circle.style.width = `${D}px`;
46        circle.style.height = `${D}px`;
47        circle.style.bottom = `-${delta}px`;
48
49        gsap.set(circle, {
50          xPercent: -50,
51          scale: 0,
52          transformOrigin: `50% ${originY}px`
53        });
54
55        const label = pill.querySelector('.pill-label');
56        const white = pill.querySelector('.pill-label-hover');
57
58        if (label) gsap.set(label, { y: 0 });
59        if (white) gsap.set(white, { y: h + 12, opacity: 0 });
60
61        const index = circleRefs.current.indexOf(circle);
62        if (index === -1) return;
63
64        tlRefs.current[index]?.kill();
65        const tl = gsap.timeline({ paused: true });
66
67        tl.to(circle, { scale: 1.2, xPercent: -50, duration: 2, ease, overwrite: 'auto' }, 0);
68
69        if (label) {
70          tl.to(label, { y: -(h + 8), duration: 2, ease, overwrite: 'auto' }, 0);
71        }
72
73        if (white) {
74          gsap.set(white, { y: Math.ceil(h + 100), opacity: 0 });
75          tl.to(white, { y: 0, opacity: 1, duration: 2, ease, overwrite: 'auto' }, 0);
76        }
77
78        tlRefs.current[index] = tl;
79      });
80    };
81
82    layout();
83
84    const onResize = () => layout();
85    window.addEventListener('resize', onResize);
86
87    if (document.fonts?.ready) {
88      document.fonts.ready.then(layout).catch(() => {});
89    }
90
91    const menu = mobileMenuRef.current;
92    if (menu) {
93      gsap.set(menu, { visibility: 'hidden', opacity: 0, scaleY: 1 });
94    }
95
96    if (initialLoadAnimation) {
97      const logo = logoRef.current;
98      const navItems = navItemsRef.current;
99
100      if (logo) {
101        gsap.set(logo, { scale: 0 });
102        gsap.to(logo, {
103          scale: 1,
104          duration: 0.6,
105          ease
106        });
107      }
108
109      if (navItems) {
110        gsap.set(navItems, { width: 0, overflow: 'hidden' });
111        gsap.to(navItems, {
112          width: 'auto',
113          duration: 0.6,
114          ease
115        });
116      }
117    }
118
119    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', onResize);
120  }, [items, ease, initialLoadAnimation]);
121
122  const handleEnter = i => {
123    const tl = tlRefs.current[i];
124    if (!tl) return;
125    activeTweenRefs.current[i]?.kill();
126    activeTweenRefs.current[i] = tl.tweenTo(tl.duration(), {
127      duration: 0.3,
128      ease,
129      overwrite: 'auto'
130    });
131  };
132
133  const handleLeave = i => {
134    const tl = tlRefs.current[i];
135    if (!tl) return;
136    activeTweenRefs.current[i]?.kill();
137    activeTweenRefs.current[i] = tl.tweenTo(0, {
138      duration: 0.2,
139      ease,
140      overwrite: 'auto'
141    });
142  };
143
144  const handleLogoEnter = () => {
145    const img = logoImgRef.current;
146    if (!img) return;
147    logoTweenRef.current?.kill();
148    gsap.set(img, { rotate: 0 });
149    logoTweenRef.current = gsap.to(img, {
150      rotate: 360,
151      duration: 0.2,
152      ease,
153      overwrite: 'auto'
154    });
155  };
156
157  const toggleMobileMenu = () => {
158    const newState = !isMobileMenuOpen;
159    setIsMobileMenuOpen(newState);
160
161    const hamburger = hamburgerRef.current;
162    const menu = mobileMenuRef.current;
163
164    if (hamburger) {
165      const lines = hamburger.querySelectorAll('.hamburger-line');
166      if (newState) {
167        gsap.to(lines[0], { rotation: 45, y: 3, duration: 0.3, ease });
168        gsap.to(lines[1], { rotation: -45, y: -3, duration: 0.3, ease });
169      } else {
170        gsap.to(lines[0], { rotation: 0, y: 0, duration: 0.3, ease });
171        gsap.to(lines[1], { rotation: 0, y: 0, duration: 0.3, ease });
172      }
173    }
174
175    if (menu) {
176      if (newState) {
177        gsap.set(menu, { visibility: 'visible' });
178        gsap.fromTo(
179          menu,
180          { opacity: 0, y: 10, scaleY: 1 },
181          {
182            opacity: 1,
183            y: 0,
184            scaleY: 1,
185            duration: 0.3,
186            ease,
187            transformOrigin: 'top center'
188          }
189        );
190      } else {
191        gsap.to(menu, {
192          opacity: 0,
193          y: 10,
194          scaleY: 1,
195          duration: 0.2,
196          ease,
197          transformOrigin: 'top center',
198          onComplete: () => {
199            gsap.set(menu, { visibility: 'hidden' });
200          }
201        });
202      }
203    }
204
205    onMobileMenuClick?.();
206  };
207
208  const isExternalLink = href =>
209    href.startsWith('http://') ||
210    href.startsWith('https://') ||
211    href.startsWith('//') ||
212    href.startsWith('mailto:') ||
213    href.startsWith('tel:') ||
214    href.startsWith('#');
215
216  const isRouterLink = href => href && !isExternalLink(href);
217
218  const cssVars = {
219    ['--base']: baseColor,
220    ['--pill-bg']: pillColor,
221    ['--hover-text']: hoveredPillTextColor,
222    ['--pill-text']: resolvedPillTextColor
223  };
224
225  return (
226    <div className="pill-nav-container">
227      <nav className={`pill-nav ${className}`} aria-label="Primary" style={cssVars}>
228        {isRouterLink(items?.[0]?.href) ? (
229          <Link
230            className="pill-logo"
231            to={items[0].href}
232            aria-label="Home"
233            onMouseEnter={handleLogoEnter}
234            role="menuitem"
235            ref={el => {
236              logoRef.current = el;
237            }}
238          >
239            <img src={logo} alt={logoAlt} ref={logoImgRef} />
240          </Link>
241        ) : (
242          <a
243            className="pill-logo"
244            href={items?.[0]?.href || '#'}
245            aria-label="Home"
246            onMouseEnter={handleLogoEnter}
247            ref={el => {
248              logoRef.current = el;
249            }}
250          >
251            <img src={logo} alt={logoAlt} ref={logoImgRef} />
252          </a>
253        )}
254
255        <div className="pill-nav-items desktop-only" ref={navItemsRef}>
256          <ul className="pill-list" role="menubar">
257            {items.map((item, i) => (
258              <li key={item.href || `item-${i}`} role="none">
259                {isRouterLink(item.href) ? (
260                  <Link
261                    role="menuitem"
262                    to={item.href}
263                    className={`pill${activeHref === item.href ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
264                    aria-label={item.ariaLabel || item.label}
265                    onMouseEnter={() => handleEnter(i)}
266                    onMouseLeave={() => handleLeave(i)}
267                  >
268                    <span
269                      className="hover-circle"
270                      aria-hidden="true"
271                      ref={el => {
272                        circleRefs.current[i] = el;
273                      }}
274                    />
275                    <span className="label-stack">
276                      <span className="pill-label">{item.label}</span>
277                      <span className="pill-label-hover" aria-hidden="true">
278                        {item.label}
279                      </span>
280                    </span>
281                  </Link>
282                ) : (
283                  <a
284                    role="menuitem"
285                    href={item.href}
286                    className={`pill${activeHref === item.href ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
287                    aria-label={item.ariaLabel || item.label}
288                    onMouseEnter={() => handleEnter(i)}
289                    onMouseLeave={() => handleLeave(i)}
290                  >
291                    <span
292                      className="hover-circle"
293                      aria-hidden="true"
294                      ref={el => {
295                        circleRefs.current[i] = el;
296                      }}
297                    />
298                    <span className="label-stack">
299                      <span className="pill-label">{item.label}</span>
300                      <span className="pill-label-hover" aria-hidden="true">
301                        {item.label}
302                      </span>
303                    </span>
304                  </a>
305                )}
306              </li>
307            ))}
308          </ul>
309        </div>
310
311        <button
312          className="mobile-menu-button mobile-only"
313          onClick={toggleMobileMenu}
314          aria-label="Toggle menu"
315          ref={hamburgerRef}
316        >
317          <span className="hamburger-line" />
318          <span className="hamburger-line" />
319        </button>
320      </nav>
321
322      <div className="mobile-menu-popover mobile-only" ref={mobileMenuRef} style={cssVars}>
323        <ul className="mobile-menu-list">
324          {items.map((item, i) => (
325            <li key={item.href || `mobile-item-${i}`}>
326              {isRouterLink(item.href) ? (
327                <Link
328                  to={item.href}
329                  className={`mobile-menu-link${activeHref === item.href ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
330                  onClick={() => setIsMobileMenuOpen(false)}
331                >
332                  {item.label}
333                </Link>
334              ) : (
335                <a
336                  href={item.href}
337                  className={`mobile-menu-link${activeHref === item.href ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
338                  onClick={() => setIsMobileMenuOpen(false)}
339                >
340                  {item.label}
341                </a>
342              )}
343            </li>
344          ))}
345        </ul>
346      </div>
347    </div>
348  );
349};
350
351export default PillNav;
352

Component: Tilted Card

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/TiltedCard-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import TiltedCard from './TiltedCard';
2
3<TiltedCard
4  imageSrc="https://i.scdn.co/image/ab67616d0000b273d9985092cd88bffd97653b58"
5  altText="Kendrick Lamar - GNX Album Cover"
6  captionText="Kendrick Lamar - GNX"
7  containerHeight="300px"
8  containerWidth="300px"
9  imageHeight="300px"
10  imageWidth="300px"
11  rotateAmplitude={12}
12  scaleOnHover={1.05}
13  showMobileWarning={false}
14  showTooltip
15  displayOverlayContent
16  overlayContent={
17    <p className="tilted-card-demo-text">
18      Kendrick Lamar - GNX
19    </p>
20  }
21/>
22  

Code:
1import { useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { motion, useMotionValue, useSpring } from 'motion/react';
3import './TiltedCard.css';
4
5const springValues = {
6  damping: 30,
7  stiffness: 100,
8  mass: 2
9};
10
11export default function TiltedCard({
12  imageSrc,
13  altText = 'Tilted card image',
14  captionText = '',
15  containerHeight = '300px',
16  containerWidth = '100%',
17  imageHeight = '300px',
18  imageWidth = '300px',
19  scaleOnHover = 1.1,
20  rotateAmplitude = 14,
21  showMobileWarning = true,
22  showTooltip = true,
23  overlayContent = null,
24  displayOverlayContent = false
25}) {
26  const ref = useRef(null);
27
28  const x = useMotionValue();
29  const y = useMotionValue();
30  const rotateX = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springValues);
31  const rotateY = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springValues);
32  const scale = useSpring(1, springValues);
33  const opacity = useSpring(0);
34  const rotateFigcaption = useSpring(0, {
35    stiffness: 350,
36    damping: 30,
37    mass: 1
38  });
39
40  const [lastY, setLastY] = useState(0);
41
42  function handleMouse(e) {
43    if (!ref.current) return;
44
45    const rect = ref.current.getBoundingClientRect();
46    const offsetX = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2;
47    const offsetY = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2;
48
49    const rotationX = (offsetY / (rect.height / 2)) * -rotateAmplitude;
50    const rotationY = (offsetX / (rect.width / 2)) * rotateAmplitude;
51
52    rotateX.set(rotationX);
53    rotateY.set(rotationY);
54
55    x.set(e.clientX - rect.left);
56    y.set(e.clientY - rect.top);
57
58    const velocityY = offsetY - lastY;
59    rotateFigcaption.set(-velocityY * 0.6);
60    setLastY(offsetY);
61  }
62
63  function handleMouseEnter() {
64    scale.set(scaleOnHover);
65    opacity.set(1);
66  }
67
68  function handleMouseLeave() {
69    opacity.set(0);
70    scale.set(1);
71    rotateX.set(0);
72    rotateY.set(0);
73    rotateFigcaption.set(0);
74  }
75
76  return (
77    <figure
78      ref={ref}
79      className="tilted-card-figure"
80      style={{
81        height: containerHeight,
82        width: containerWidth
83      }}
84      onMouseMove={handleMouse}
85      onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter}
86      onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
87    >
88      {showMobileWarning && (
89        <div className="tilted-card-mobile-alert">This effect is not optimized for mobile. Check on desktop.</div>
90      )}
91
92      <motion.div
93        className="tilted-card-inner"
94        style={{
95          width: imageWidth,
96          height: imageHeight,
97          rotateX,
98          rotateY,
99          scale
100        }}
101      >
102        <motion.img
103          src={imageSrc}
104          alt={altText}
105          className="tilted-card-img"
106          style={{
107            width: imageWidth,
108            height: imageHeight
109          }}
110        />
111
112        {displayOverlayContent && overlayContent && (
113          <motion.div className="tilted-card-overlay">{overlayContent}</motion.div>
114        )}
115      </motion.div>
116
117      {showTooltip && (
118        <motion.figcaption
119          className="tilted-card-caption"
120          style={{
121            x,
122            y,
123            opacity,
124            rotate: rotateFigcaption
125          }}
126        >
127          {captionText}
128        </motion.figcaption>
129      )}
130    </figure>
131  );
132}
133

23  }

Component: Masonry

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Glass Surface

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/GlassSurface-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import GlassSurface from './GlassSurface'
2
3// Basic usage
4<GlassSurface 
5  width={300} 
6  height={200}
7  borderRadius={50}
8  className="my-custom-class"
9>
10  <h2>Glass Surface Content</h2>
11</GlassSurface>
12
13// Custom displacement effects
14<GlassSurface
15  displace={0.5}
16  distortionScale={-180}
17  redOffset={0}
18  greenOffset={10}
19  blueOffset={20}
20  brightness={50}
21  opacity={0.93}
22  mixBlendMode="screen"
23>
24  <span>Advanced Glass Distortion</span>
25</GlassSurface>

Code:
1/* eslint-disable react-hooks/exhaustive-deps */
2import { useEffect, useState, useRef, useId } from 'react';
3import './GlassSurface.css';
4
5const GlassSurface = ({
6  children,
7  width = 200,
8  height = 80,
9  borderRadius = 20,
10  borderWidth = 0.07,
11  brightness = 50,
12  opacity = 0.93,
13  blur = 11,
14  displace = 0,
15  backgroundOpacity = 0,
16  saturation = 1,
17  distortionScale = -180,
18  redOffset = 0,
19  greenOffset = 10,
20  blueOffset = 20,
21  xChannel = 'R',
22  yChannel = 'G',
23  mixBlendMode = 'difference',
24  className = '',
25  style = {}
26}) => {
27  const uniqueId = useId().replace(/:/g, '-');
28  const filterId = `glass-filter-${uniqueId}`;
29  const redGradId = `red-grad-${uniqueId}`;
30  const blueGradId = `blue-grad-${uniqueId}`;
31
32  const [svgSupported, setSvgSupported] = useState(false);
33
34  const containerRef = useRef(null);
35  const feImageRef = useRef(null);
36  const redChannelRef = useRef(null);
37  const greenChannelRef = useRef(null);
38  const blueChannelRef = useRef(null);
39  const gaussianBlurRef = useRef(null);
40
41  const generateDisplacementMap = () => {
42    const rect = containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
43    const actualWidth = rect?.width || 400;
44    const actualHeight = rect?.height || 200;
45    const edgeSize = Math.min(actualWidth, actualHeight) * (borderWidth * 0.5);
46
47    const svgContent = `
48      <svg viewBox="0 0 ${actualWidth} ${actualHeight}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
49        <defs>
50          <linearGradient id="${redGradId}" x1="100%" y1="0%" x2="0%" y2="0%">
51            <stop offset="0%" stop-color="#0000"/>
52            <stop offset="100%" stop-color="red"/>
53          </linearGradient>
54          <linearGradient id="${blueGradId}" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="0%" y2="100%">
55            <stop offset="0%" stop-color="#0000"/>
56            <stop offset="100%" stop-color="blue"/>
57          </linearGradient>
58        </defs>
59        <rect x="0" y="0" width="${actualWidth}" height="${actualHeight}" fill="black"></rect>
60        <rect x="0" y="0" width="${actualWidth}" height="${actualHeight}" rx="${borderRadius}" fill="url(#${redGradId})" />
61        <rect x="0" y="0" width="${actualWidth}" height="${actualHeight}" rx="${borderRadius}" fill="url(#${blueGradId})" style="mix-blend-mode: ${mixBlendMode}" />
62        <rect x="${edgeSize}" y="${edgeSize}" width="${actualWidth - edgeSize * 2}" height="${actualHeight - edgeSize * 2}" rx="${borderRadius}" fill="hsl(0 0% ${brightness}% / ${opacity})" style="filter:blur(${blur}px)" />
63      </svg>
64    `;
65
66    return `data:image/svg+xml,${encodeURIComponent(svgContent)}`;
67  };
68
69  const updateDisplacementMap = () => {
70    feImageRef.current?.setAttribute('href', generateDisplacementMap());
71  };
72
73  useEffect(() => {
74    updateDisplacementMap();
75    [
76      { ref: redChannelRef, offset: redOffset },
77      { ref: greenChannelRef, offset: greenOffset },
78      { ref: blueChannelRef, offset: blueOffset }
79    ].forEach(({ ref, offset }) => {
80      if (ref.current) {
81        ref.current.setAttribute('scale', (distortionScale + offset).toString());
82        ref.current.setAttribute('xChannelSelector', xChannel);
83        ref.current.setAttribute('yChannelSelector', yChannel);
84      }
85    });
86
87    gaussianBlurRef.current?.setAttribute('stdDeviation', displace.toString());
88  }, [
89    width,
90    height,
91    borderRadius,
92    borderWidth,
93    brightness,
94    opacity,
95    blur,
96    displace,
97    distortionScale,
98    redOffset,
99    greenOffset,
100    blueOffset,
101    xChannel,
102    yChannel,
103    mixBlendMode
104  ]);
105
106  useEffect(() => {
107    if (!containerRef.current) return;
108
109    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(() => {
110      setTimeout(updateDisplacementMap, 0);
111    });
112
113    resizeObserver.observe(containerRef.current);
114
115    return () => {
116      resizeObserver.disconnect();
117    };
118  }, []);
119
120  useEffect(() => {
121    if (!containerRef.current) return;
122
123    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(() => {
124      setTimeout(updateDisplacementMap, 0);
125    });
126
127    resizeObserver.observe(containerRef.current);
128
129    return () => {
130      resizeObserver.disconnect();
131    };
132  }, []);
133
134  useEffect(() => {
135    setTimeout(updateDisplacementMap, 0);
136  }, [width, height]);
137
138  useEffect(() => {
139    setSvgSupported(supportsSVGFilters());
140  }, []);
141
142  const supportsSVGFilters = () => {
143    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || typeof document === 'undefined') {
144      return false;
145    }
146
147    const isWebkit = /Safari/.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/Chrome/.test(navigator.userAgent);
148    const isFirefox = /Firefox/.test(navigator.userAgent);
149
150    if (isWebkit || isFirefox) {
151      return false;
152    }
153
154    const div = document.createElement('div');
155    div.style.backdropFilter = `url(#${filterId})`;
156
157    return div.style.backdropFilter !== '';
158  };
159
160  const containerStyle = {
161    ...style,
162    width: typeof width === 'number' ? `${width}px` : width,
163    height: typeof height === 'number' ? `${height}px` : height,
164    borderRadius: `${borderRadius}px`,
165    '--glass-frost': backgroundOpacity,
166    '--glass-saturation': saturation,
167    '--filter-id': `url(#${filterId})`
168  };
169
170  return (
171    <div
172      ref={containerRef}
173      className={`glass-surface ${svgSupported ? 'glass-surface--svg' : 'glass-surface--fallback'} ${className}`}
174      style={containerStyle}
175    >
176      <svg className="glass-surface__filter" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
177        <defs>
178          <filter id={filterId} colorInterpolationFilters="sRGB" x="0%" y="0%" width="100%" height="100%">
179            <feImage ref={feImageRef} x="0" y="0" width="100%" height="100%" preserveAspectRatio="none" result="map" />
180
181            <feDisplacementMap ref={redChannelRef} in="SourceGraphic" in2="map" id="redchannel" result="dispRed" />
182            <feColorMatrix
183              in="dispRed"
184              type="matrix"
185              values="1 0 0 0 0
186                      0 0 0 0 0
187                      0 0 0 0 0
188                      0 0 0 1 0"
189              result="red"
190            />
191
192            <feDisplacementMap
193              ref={greenChannelRef}
194              in="SourceGraphic"
195              in2="map"
196              id="greenchannel"
197              result="dispGreen"
198            />
199            <feColorMatrix
200              in="dispGreen"
201              type="matrix"
202              values="0 0 0 0 0
203                      0 1 0 0 0
204                      0 0 0 0 0
205                      0 0 0 1 0"
206              result="green"
207            />
208
209            <feDisplacementMap ref={blueChannelRef} in="SourceGraphic" in2="map" id="bluechannel" result="dispBlue" />
210            <feColorMatrix
211              in="dispBlue"
212              type="matrix"
213              values="0 0 0 0 0
214                      0 0 0 0 0
215                      0 0 1 0 0
216                      0 0 0 1 0"
217              result="blue"
218            />
219
220            <feBlend in="red" in2="green" mode="screen" result="rg" />
221            <feBlend in="rg" in2="blue" mode="screen" result="output" />
222            <feGaussianBlur ref={gaussianBlurRef} in="output" stdDeviation="0.7" />
223          </filter>
224        </defs>
225      </svg>
226
227      <div className="glass-surface__content">{children}</div>
228    </div>
229  );
230};
231
232export default GlassSurface;
233

Extra Config/Code:

2  position: relative;

5  justify-content: center;
6  overflow: hidden;

8}
9
10.glass-surface__filter {
11  width: 100%;
12  height: 100%;
13  pointer-events: none;
14  position: absolute;
15  inset: 0;
16  opacity: 0;
17  z-index: -1;
18}
19
20.glass-surface__content {
21  width: 100%;
22  height: 100%;
23  display: flex;
24  align-items: center;
25  justify-content: center;
26  padding: 0.5rem;
27  border-radius: inherit;
28  position: relative;
29  z-index: 1;
30}
31
32.glass-surface--svg {
33  background: light-dark(hsl(0 0% 100% / var(--glass-frost, 0)), hsl(0 0% 0% / var(--glass-frost, 0)));
34  backdrop-filter: var(--filter-id, url(#glass-filter)) saturate(var(--glass-saturation, 1));
35  box-shadow:
36    0 0 2px 1px light-dark(color-mix(in oklch, black, transparent 85%), color-mix(in oklch, white, transparent 65%))
37      inset,
38    0 0 10px 4px light-dark(color-mix(in oklch, black, transparent 90%), color-mix(in oklch, white, transparent 85%))
39      inset,
40    0px 4px 16px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05),
41    0px 8px 24px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05),
42    0px 16px 56px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05),
43    0px 4px 16px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05) inset,
44    0px 8px 24px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05) inset,
45    0px 16px 56px rgba(17, 17, 26, 0.05) inset;
46}
47
48.glass-surface--fallback {
49  background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25);
50  backdrop-filter: blur(12px) saturate(1.8) brightness(1.1);
51  -webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(12px) saturate(1.8) brightness(1.1);
52  border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3);
53  box-shadow:
54    0 8px 32px 0 rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.2),
55    0 2px 16px 0 rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.1),
56    inset 0 1px 0 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.4),
57    inset 0 -1px 0 0 rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2);
58}
59
60@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {

Component: Dome Gallery

1import { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
2import { useGesture } from '@use-gesture/react';

33const DEFAULTS = {
34  maxVerticalRotationDeg: 5,
35  dragSensitivity: 20,
36  enlargeTransitionMs: 300,
37  segments: 35
38};
39
40const clamp = (v, min, max) => Math.min(Math.max(v, min), max);
41const normalizeAngle = d => ((d % 360) + 360) % 360;
42const wrapAngleSigned = deg => {
43  const a = (((deg + 180) % 360) + 360) % 360;
44  return a - 180;
45};
46const getDataNumber = (el, name, fallback) => {
47  const attr = el.dataset[name] ?? el.getAttribute(`data-${name}`);
48  const n = attr == null ? NaN : parseFloat(attr);
49  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
50};
51
52function buildItems(pool, seg) {
53  const xCols = Array.from({ length: seg }, (_, i) => -37 + i * 2);
54  const evenYs = [-4, -2, 0, 2, 4];
55  const oddYs = [-3, -1, 1, 3, 5];
56
57  const coords = xCols.flatMap((x, c) => {
58    const ys = c % 2 === 0 ? evenYs : oddYs;
59    return ys.map(y => ({ x, y, sizeX: 2, sizeY: 2 }));
60  });
61
62  const totalSlots = coords.length;
63  if (pool.length === 0) {
64    return coords.map(c => ({ ...c, src: '', alt: '' }));
65  }
66  if (pool.length > totalSlots) {
67    console.warn(
68      `[DomeGallery] Provided image count (${pool.length}) exceeds available tiles (${totalSlots}). Some images will not be shown.`
69    );
70  }
71
72  const normalizedImages = pool.map(image => {
73    if (typeof image === 'string') {
74      return { src: image, alt: '' };
75    }
76    return { src: image.src || '', alt: image.alt || '' };
77  });
78
79  const usedImages = Array.from({ length: totalSlots }, (_, i) => normalizedImages[i % normalizedImages.length]);
80
81  for (let i = 1; i < usedImages.length; i++) {
82    if (usedImages[i].src === usedImages[i - 1].src) {
83      for (let j = i + 1; j < usedImages.length; j++) {
84        if (usedImages[j].src !== usedImages[i].src) {
85          const tmp = usedImages[i];
86          usedImages[i] = usedImages[j];
87          usedImages[j] = tmp;
88          break;
89        }
90      }
91    }
92  }
93
94  return coords.map((c, i) => ({
95    ...c,
96    src: usedImages[i].src,
97    alt: usedImages[i].alt
98  }));
99}
100
101function computeItemBaseRotation(offsetX, offsetY, sizeX, sizeY, segments) {
102  const unit = 360 / segments / 2;
103  const rotateY = unit * (offsetX + (sizeX - 1) / 2);
104  const rotateX = unit * (offsetY - (sizeY - 1) / 2);
105  return { rotateX, rotateY };
106}
107
108export default function DomeGallery({
109  images = DEFAULT_IMAGES,
110  fit = 0.5,
111  fitBasis = 'auto',
112  minRadius = 600,
113  maxRadius = Infinity,
114  padFactor = 0.25,
115  overlayBlurColor = '#060010',
116  maxVerticalRotationDeg = DEFAULTS.maxVerticalRotationDeg,
117  dragSensitivity = DEFAULTS.dragSensitivity,
118  enlargeTransitionMs = DEFAULTS.enlargeTransitionMs,
119  segments = DEFAULTS.segments,
120  dragDampening = 2,
121  openedImageWidth = '250px',
122  openedImageHeight = '350px',
123  imageBorderRadius = '30px',
124  openedImageBorderRadius = '30px',
125  grayscale = true
126}) {
127  const rootRef = useRef(null);
128  const mainRef = useRef(null);
129  const sphereRef = useRef(null);
130  const frameRef = useRef(null);
131  const viewerRef = useRef(null);
132  const scrimRef = useRef(null);
133  const focusedElRef = useRef(null);
134  const originalTilePositionRef = useRef(null);
135
136  const rotationRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
137  const startRotRef = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
138  const startPosRef = useRef(null);
139  const draggingRef = useRef(false);
140  const movedRef = useRef(false);
141  const inertiaRAF = useRef(null);
142  const openingRef = useRef(false);
143  const openStartedAtRef = useRef(0);
144  const lastDragEndAt = useRef(0);
145
146  const scrollLockedRef = useRef(false);
147  const lockScroll = useCallback(() => {
148    if (scrollLockedRef.current) return;
149    scrollLockedRef.current = true;
150    document.body.classList.add('dg-scroll-lock');
151  }, []);
152  const unlockScroll = useCallback(() => {
153    if (!scrollLockedRef.current) return;
154    if (rootRef.current?.getAttribute('data-enlarging') === 'true') return;
155    scrollLockedRef.current = false;
156    document.body.classList.remove('dg-scroll-lock');
157  }, []);
158
159  const items = useMemo(() => buildItems(images, segments), [images, segments]);
160
161  const applyTransform = (xDeg, yDeg) => {
162    const el = sphereRef.current;
163    if (el) {
164      el.style.transform = `translateZ(calc(var(--radius) * -1)) rotateX(${xDeg}deg) rotateY(${yDeg}deg)`;
165    }
166  };
167
168  const lockedRadiusRef = useRef(null);
169
170  useEffect(() => {
171    const root = rootRef.current;
172    if (!root) return;
173    const ro = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
174      const cr = entries[0].contentRect;
175      const w = Math.max(1, cr.width),
176        h = Math.max(1, cr.height);
177      const minDim = Math.min(w, h),
178        maxDim = Math.max(w, h),
179        aspect = w / h;
180      let basis;
181      switch (fitBasis) {
182        case 'min':
183          basis = minDim;
184          break;
185        case 'max':
186          basis = maxDim;
187          break;
188        case 'width':
189          basis = w;
190          break;
191        case 'height':
192          basis = h;
193          break;
194        default:
195          basis = aspect >= 1.3 ? w : minDim;
196      }
197      let radius = basis * fit;
198      const heightGuard = h * 1.35;
199      radius = Math.min(radius, heightGuard);
200      radius = clamp(radius, minRadius, maxRadius);
201      lockedRadiusRef.current = Math.round(radius);
202
203      const viewerPad = Math.max(8, Math.round(minDim * padFactor));
204      root.style.setProperty('--radius', `${lockedRadiusRef.current}px`);
205      root.style.setProperty('--viewer-pad', `${viewerPad}px`);
206      root.style.setProperty('--overlay-blur-color', overlayBlurColor);
207      root.style.setProperty('--tile-radius', imageBorderRadius);
208      root.style.setProperty('--enlarge-radius', openedImageBorderRadius);
209      root.style.setProperty('--image-filter', grayscale ? 'grayscale(1)' : 'none');
210      applyTransform(rotationRef.current.x, rotationRef.current.y);
211
212      const enlargedOverlay = viewerRef.current?.querySelector('.enlarge');
213      if (enlargedOverlay && frameRef.current && mainRef.current) {
214        const frameR = frameRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
215        const mainR = mainRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
216
217        const hasCustomSize = openedImageWidth && openedImageHeight;
218        if (hasCustomSize) {
219          const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
220          tempDiv.style.cssText = `position: absolute; width: ${openedImageWidth}; height: ${openedImageHeight}; visibility: hidden;`;
221          document.body.appendChild(tempDiv);
222          const tempRect = tempDiv.getBoundingClientRect();
223          document.body.removeChild(tempDiv);
224
225          const centeredLeft = frameR.left - mainR.left + (frameR.width - tempRect.width) / 2;
226          const centeredTop = frameR.top - mainR.top + (frameR.height - tempRect.height) / 2;
227
228          enlargedOverlay.style.left = `${centeredLeft}px`;
229          enlargedOverlay.style.top = `${centeredTop}px`;
230        } else {
231          enlargedOverlay.style.left = `${frameR.left - mainR.left}px`;
232          enlargedOverlay.style.top = `${frameR.top - mainR.top}px`;
233          enlargedOverlay.style.width = `${frameR.width}px`;
234          enlargedOverlay.style.height = `${frameR.height}px`;
235        }
236      }
237    });
238    ro.observe(root);
239    return () => ro.disconnect();
240  }, [
241    fit,
242    fitBasis,
243    minRadius,
244    maxRadius,
245    padFactor,
246    overlayBlurColor,
247    grayscale,
248    imageBorderRadius,
249    openedImageBorderRadius,
250    openedImageWidth,
251    openedImageHeight
252  ]);
253
254  useEffect(() => {
255    applyTransform(rotationRef.current.x, rotationRef.current.y);
256  }, []);
257
258  const stopInertia = useCallback(() => {
259    if (inertiaRAF.current) {
260      cancelAnimationFrame(inertiaRAF.current);
261      inertiaRAF.current = null;
262    }
263  }, []);
264
265  const startInertia = useCallback(
266    (vx, vy) => {
267      const MAX_V = 1.4;
268      let vX = clamp(vx, -MAX_V, MAX_V) * 80;
269      let vY = clamp(vy, -MAX_V, MAX_V) * 80;
270      let frames = 0;
271      const d = clamp(dragDampening ?? 0.6, 0, 1);
272      const frictionMul = 0.94 + 0.055 * d;
273      const stopThreshold = 0.015 - 0.01 * d;
274      const maxFrames = Math.round(90 + 270 * d);
275      const step = () => {
276        vX *= frictionMul;
277        vY *= frictionMul;
278        if (Math.abs(vX) < stopThreshold && Math.abs(vY) < stopThreshold) {
279          inertiaRAF.current = null;
280          return;
281        }
282        if (++frames > maxFrames) {
283          inertiaRAF.current = null;
284          return;
285        }
286        const nextX = clamp(rotationRef.current.x - vY / 200, -maxVerticalRotationDeg, maxVerticalRotationDeg);
287        const nextY = wrapAngleSigned(rotationRef.current.y + vX / 200);
288        rotationRef.current = { x: nextX, y: nextY };
289        applyTransform(nextX, nextY);
290        inertiaRAF.current = requestAnimationFrame(step);
291      };
292      stopInertia();
293      inertiaRAF.current = requestAnimationFrame(step);
294    },
295    [dragDampening, maxVerticalRotationDeg, stopInertia]
296  );
297
298  useGesture(
299    {
300      onDragStart: ({ event }) => {
301        if (focusedElRef.current) return;
302        stopInertia();
303        const evt = event;
304        draggingRef.current = true;
305        movedRef.current = false;
306        startRotRef.current = { ...rotationRef.current };
307        startPosRef.current = { x: evt.clientX, y: evt.clientY };
308      },
309      onDrag: ({ event, last, velocity = [0, 0], direction = [0, 0], movement }) => {
310        if (focusedElRef.current || !draggingRef.current || !startPosRef.current) return;
311        const evt = event;
312        const dxTotal = evt.clientX - startPosRef.current.x;
313        const dyTotal = evt.clientY - startPosRef.current.y;
314        if (!movedRef.current) {
315          const dist2 = dxTotal * dxTotal + dyTotal * dyTotal;
316          if (dist2 > 16) movedRef.current = true;
317        }
318        const nextX = clamp(
319          startRotRef.current.x - dyTotal / dragSensitivity,
320          -maxVerticalRotationDeg,
321          maxVerticalRotationDeg
322        );
323        const nextY = wrapAngleSigned(startRotRef.current.y + dxTotal / dragSensitivity);
324        if (rotationRef.current.x !== nextX || rotationRef.current.y !== nextY) {
325          rotationRef.current = { x: nextX, y: nextY };
326          applyTransform(nextX, nextY);
327        }
328        if (last) {
329          draggingRef.current = false;
330          let [vMagX, vMagY] = velocity;
331          const [dirX, dirY] = direction;
332          let vx = vMagX * dirX;
333          let vy = vMagY * dirY;
334          if (Math.abs(vx) < 0.001 && Math.abs(vy) < 0.001 && Array.isArray(movement)) {
335            const [mx, my] = movement;
336            vx = clamp((mx / dragSensitivity) * 0.02, -1.2, 1.2);
337            vy = clamp((my / dragSensitivity) * 0.02, -1.2, 1.2);
338          }
339          if (Math.abs(vx) > 0.005 || Math.abs(vy) > 0.005) startInertia(vx, vy);
340          if (movedRef.current) lastDragEndAt.current = performance.now();
341          movedRef.current = false;
342        }
343      }
344    },
345    { target: mainRef, eventOptions: { passive: true } }
346  );
347
348  useEffect(() => {
349    const scrim = scrimRef.current;
350    if (!scrim) return;
351    const close = () => {
352      if (performance.now() - openStartedAtRef.current < 250) return;
353      const el = focusedElRef.current;
354      if (!el) return;
355      const parent = el.parentElement;
356      const overlay = viewerRef.current?.querySelector('.enlarge');
357      if (!overlay) return;
358      const refDiv = parent.querySelector('.item__image--reference');
359      const originalPos = originalTilePositionRef.current;
360      if (!originalPos) {
361        overlay.remove();
362        if (refDiv) refDiv.remove();
363        parent.style.setProperty('--rot-y-delta', '0deg');
364        parent.style.setProperty('--rot-x-delta', '0deg');
365        el.style.visibility = '';
366        el.style.zIndex = 0;
367        focusedElRef.current = null;
368        rootRef.current?.removeAttribute('data-enlarging');
369        openingRef.current = false;
370        unlockScroll();
371        return;
372      }
373      const currentRect = overlay.getBoundingClientRect();
374      const rootRect = rootRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
375      const originalPosRelativeToRoot = {
376        left: originalPos.left - rootRect.left,
377        top: originalPos.top - rootRect.top,
378        width: originalPos.width,
379        height: originalPos.height
380      };
381      const overlayRelativeToRoot = {
382        left: currentRect.left - rootRect.left,
383        top: currentRect.top - rootRect.top,
384        width: currentRect.width,
385        height: currentRect.height
386      };
387      const animatingOverlay = document.createElement('div');
388      animatingOverlay.className = 'enlarge-closing';
389      animatingOverlay.style.cssText = `position:absolute;left:${overlayRelativeToRoot.left}px;top:${overlayRelativeToRoot.top}px;width:${overlayRelativeToRoot.width}px;height:${overlayRelativeToRoot.height}px;z-index:9999;border-radius: var(--enlarge-radius, 32px);overflow:hidden;box-shadow:0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,.35);transition:all ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease-out;pointer-events:none;margin:0;transform:none;`;
390      const originalImg = overlay.querySelector('img');
391      if (originalImg) {
392        const img = originalImg.cloneNode();
393        img.style.cssText = 'width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;';
394        animatingOverlay.appendChild(img);
395      }
396      overlay.remove();
397      rootRef.current.appendChild(animatingOverlay);
398      void animatingOverlay.getBoundingClientRect();
399      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
400        animatingOverlay.style.left = originalPosRelativeToRoot.left + 'px';
401        animatingOverlay.style.top = originalPosRelativeToRoot.top + 'px';
402        animatingOverlay.style.width = originalPosRelativeToRoot.width + 'px';
403        animatingOverlay.style.height = originalPosRelativeToRoot.height + 'px';
404        animatingOverlay.style.opacity = '0';
405      });
406      const cleanup = () => {
407        animatingOverlay.remove();
408        originalTilePositionRef.current = null;
409        if (refDiv) refDiv.remove();
410        parent.style.transition = 'none';
411        el.style.transition = 'none';
412        parent.style.setProperty('--rot-y-delta', '0deg');
413        parent.style.setProperty('--rot-x-delta', '0deg');
414        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
415          el.style.visibility = '';
416          el.style.opacity = '0';
417          el.style.zIndex = 0;
418          focusedElRef.current = null;
419          rootRef.current?.removeAttribute('data-enlarging');
420          requestAnimationFrame(() => {
421            parent.style.transition = '';
422            el.style.transition = 'opacity 300ms ease-out';
423            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
424              el.style.opacity = '1';
425              setTimeout(() => {
426                el.style.transition = '';
427                el.style.opacity = '';
428                openingRef.current = false;
429                if (!draggingRef.current && rootRef.current?.getAttribute('data-enlarging') !== 'true')
430                  document.body.classList.remove('dg-scroll-lock');
431              }, 300);
432            });
433          });
434        });
435      };
436      animatingOverlay.addEventListener('transitionend', cleanup, { once: true });
437    };
438    scrim.addEventListener('click', close);
439    const onKey = e => {
440      if (e.key === 'Escape') close();
441    };
442    window.addEventListener('keydown', onKey);
443    return () => {
444      scrim.removeEventListener('click', close);
445      window.removeEventListener('keydown', onKey);
446    };
447  }, [enlargeTransitionMs, unlockScroll]);
448
449  const openItemFromElement = useCallback(
450    el => {
451      if (openingRef.current) return;
452      openingRef.current = true;
453      openStartedAtRef.current = performance.now();
454      lockScroll();
455      const parent = el.parentElement;
456      focusedElRef.current = el;
457      el.setAttribute('data-focused', 'true');
458      const offsetX = getDataNumber(parent, 'offsetX', 0);
459      const offsetY = getDataNumber(parent, 'offsetY', 0);
460      const sizeX = getDataNumber(parent, 'sizeX', 2);
461      const sizeY = getDataNumber(parent, 'sizeY', 2);
462      const parentRot = computeItemBaseRotation(offsetX, offsetY, sizeX, sizeY, segments);
463      const parentY = normalizeAngle(parentRot.rotateY);
464      const globalY = normalizeAngle(rotationRef.current.y);
465      let rotY = -(parentY + globalY) % 360;
466      if (rotY < -180) rotY += 360;
467      const rotX = -parentRot.rotateX - rotationRef.current.x;
468      parent.style.setProperty('--rot-y-delta', `${rotY}deg`);
469      parent.style.setProperty('--rot-x-delta', `${rotX}deg`);
470      const refDiv = document.createElement('div');
471      refDiv.className = 'item__image item__image--reference';
472      refDiv.style.opacity = '0';
473      refDiv.style.transform = `rotateX(${-parentRot.rotateX}deg) rotateY(${-parentRot.rotateY}deg)`;
474      parent.appendChild(refDiv);
475
476      void refDiv.offsetHeight;
477
478      const tileR = refDiv.getBoundingClientRect();
479      const mainR = mainRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
480      const frameR = frameRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
481
482      if (!mainR || !frameR || tileR.width <= 0 || tileR.height <= 0) {
483        openingRef.current = false;
484        focusedElRef.current = null;
485        parent.removeChild(refDiv);
486        unlockScroll();
487        return;
488      }
489
490      originalTilePositionRef.current = { left: tileR.left, top: tileR.top, width: tileR.width, height: tileR.height };
491      el.style.visibility = 'hidden';
492      el.style.zIndex = 0;
493      const overlay = document.createElement('div');
494      overlay.className = 'enlarge';
495      overlay.style.position = 'absolute';
496      overlay.style.left = frameR.left - mainR.left + 'px';
497      overlay.style.top = frameR.top - mainR.top + 'px';
498      overlay.style.width = frameR.width + 'px';
499      overlay.style.height = frameR.height + 'px';
500      overlay.style.opacity = '0';
501      overlay.style.zIndex = '30';
502      overlay.style.willChange = 'transform, opacity';
503      overlay.style.transformOrigin = 'top left';
504      overlay.style.transition = `transform ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease, opacity ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease`;
505      const rawSrc = parent.dataset.src || el.querySelector('img')?.src || '';
506      const img = document.createElement('img');
507      img.src = rawSrc;
508      overlay.appendChild(img);
509      viewerRef.current.appendChild(overlay);
510      const tx0 = tileR.left - frameR.left;
511      const ty0 = tileR.top - frameR.top;
512      const sx0 = tileR.width / frameR.width;
513      const sy0 = tileR.height / frameR.height;
514
515      const validSx0 = isFinite(sx0) && sx0 > 0 ? sx0 : 1;
516      const validSy0 = isFinite(sy0) && sy0 > 0 ? sy0 : 1;
517
518      overlay.style.transform = `translate(${tx0}px, ${ty0}px) scale(${validSx0}, ${validSy0})`;
519
520      setTimeout(() => {
521        if (!overlay.parentElement) return;
522        overlay.style.opacity = '1';
523        overlay.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) scale(1, 1)';
524        rootRef.current?.setAttribute('data-enlarging', 'true');
525      }, 16);
526
527      const wantsResize = openedImageWidth || openedImageHeight;
528      if (wantsResize) {
529        const onFirstEnd = ev => {
530          if (ev.propertyName !== 'transform') return;
531          overlay.removeEventListener('transitionend', onFirstEnd);
532          const prevTransition = overlay.style.transition;
533          overlay.style.transition = 'none';
534          const tempWidth = openedImageWidth || `${frameR.width}px`;
535          const tempHeight = openedImageHeight || `${frameR.height}px`;
536          overlay.style.width = tempWidth;
537          overlay.style.height = tempHeight;
538          const newRect = overlay.getBoundingClientRect();
539          overlay.style.width = frameR.width + 'px';
540          overlay.style.height = frameR.height + 'px';
541          void overlay.offsetWidth;
542          overlay.style.transition = `left ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease, top ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease, width ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease, height ${enlargeTransitionMs}ms ease`;
543          const centeredLeft = frameR.left - mainR.left + (frameR.width - newRect.width) / 2;
544          const centeredTop = frameR.top - mainR.top + (frameR.height - newRect.height) / 2;
545          requestAnimationFrame(() => {
546            overlay.style.left = `${centeredLeft}px`;
547            overlay.style.top = `${centeredTop}px`;
548            overlay.style.width = tempWidth;
549            overlay.style.height = tempHeight;
550          });
551          const cleanupSecond = () => {
552            overlay.removeEventListener('transitionend', cleanupSecond);
553            overlay.style.transition = prevTransition;
554          };
555          overlay.addEventListener('transitionend', cleanupSecond, { once: true });
556        };
557        overlay.addEventListener('transitionend', onFirstEnd);
558      }
559    },
560    [enlargeTransitionMs, lockScroll, openedImageHeight, openedImageWidth, segments, unlockScroll]
561  );
562
563  const onTileClick = useCallback(
564    e => {
565      if (draggingRef.current) return;
566      if (movedRef.current) return;
567      if (performance.now() - lastDragEndAt.current < 80) return;
568      if (openingRef.current) return;
569      openItemFromElement(e.currentTarget);
570    },
571    [openItemFromElement]
572  );
573
574  const onTilePointerUp = useCallback(
575    e => {
576      if (e.pointerType !== 'touch') return;
577      if (draggingRef.current) return;
578      if (movedRef.current) return;
579      if (performance.now() - lastDragEndAt.current < 80) return;
580      if (openingRef.current) return;
581      openItemFromElement(e.currentTarget);
582    },
583    [openItemFromElement]
584  );
585
586  useEffect(() => {
587    return () => {
588      document.body.classList.remove('dg-scroll-lock');
589    };
590  }, []);
591
592  return (
593    <div
594      ref={rootRef}
595      className="sphere-root"
596      style={{
597        ['--segments-x']: segments,
598        ['--segments-y']: segments,
599        ['--overlay-blur-color']: overlayBlurColor,
600        ['--tile-radius']: imageBorderRadius,
601        ['--enlarge-radius']: openedImageBorderRadius,
602        ['--image-filter']: grayscale ? 'grayscale(1)' : 'none'
603      }}
604    >
605      <main ref={mainRef} className="sphere-main">
606        <div className="stage">
607          <div ref={sphereRef} className="sphere">
608            {items.map((it, i) => (
609              <div
610                key={`${it.x},${it.y},${i}`}
611                className="item"
612                data-src={it.src}
613                data-offset-x={it.x}
614                data-offset-y={it.y}
615                data-size-x={it.sizeX}
616                data-size-y={it.sizeY}
617                style={{
618                  ['--offset-x']: it.x,
619                  ['--offset-y']: it.y,
620                  ['--item-size-x']: it.sizeX,
621                  ['--item-size-y']: it.sizeY
622                }}
623              >
624                <div
625                  className="item__image"
626                  role="button"
627                  tabIndex={0}
628                  aria-label={it.alt || 'Open image'}
629                  onClick={onTileClick}
630                  onPointerUp={onTilePointerUp}
631                >
632                  <img src={it.src} draggable={false} alt={it.alt} />
633                </div>
634              </div>
635            ))}
636          </div>
637        </div>
638
639        <div className="overlay" />
640        <div className="overlay overlay--blur" />
641        <div className="edge-fade edge-fade--top" />
642        <div className="edge-fade edge-fade--bottom" />
643
644        <div className="viewer" ref={viewerRef}>
645          <div ref={scrimRef} className="scrim" />
646          <div ref={frameRef} className="frame" />
647        </div>
648      </main>
649    </div>
650  );
651}
652

Component: Folder

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Folder-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Folder from './Folder'
2
3<div style={{ height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
4  <Folder size={2} color="#5227FF" className="custom-folder"
5  color="#5227FF"
6  size={2}
7/>
8</div>

Code:
1import { useState } from 'react';
2import './Folder.css';
3
4const darkenColor = (hex, percent) => {
5  let color = hex.startsWith('#') ? hex.slice(1) : hex;
6  if (color.length === 3) {
7    color = color
8      .split('')
9      .map(c => c + c)
10      .join('');
11  }
12  const num = parseInt(color, 16);
13  let r = (num >> 16) & 0xff;
14  let g = (num >> 8) & 0xff;
15  let b = num & 0xff;
16  r = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, Math.floor(r * (1 - percent))));
17  g = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, Math.floor(g * (1 - percent))));
18  b = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, Math.floor(b * (1 - percent))));
19  return '#' + ((1 << 24) + (r << 16) + (g << 8) + b).toString(16).slice(1).toUpperCase();
20};
21
22const Folder = ({ color = '#5227FF', size = 1, items = [], className = '' }) => {
23  const maxItems = 3;
24  const papers = items.slice(0, maxItems);
25  while (papers.length < maxItems) {
26    papers.push(null);
27  }
28
29  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
30  const [paperOffsets, setPaperOffsets] = useState(Array.from({ length: maxItems }, () => ({ x: 0, y: 0 })));
31
32  const folderBackColor = darkenColor(color, 0.08);
33  const paper1 = darkenColor('#ffffff', 0.1);
34  const paper2 = darkenColor('#ffffff', 0.05);
35  const paper3 = '#ffffff';
36
37  const handleClick = () => {
38    setOpen(prev => !prev);
39    if (open) {
40      setPaperOffsets(Array.from({ length: maxItems }, () => ({ x: 0, y: 0 })));
41    }
42  };
43
44  const handlePaperMouseMove = (e, index) => {
45    if (!open) return;
46    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
47    const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
48    const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
49    const offsetX = (e.clientX - centerX) * 0.15;
50    const offsetY = (e.clientY - centerY) * 0.15;
51    setPaperOffsets(prev => {
52      const newOffsets = [...prev];
53      newOffsets[index] = { x: offsetX, y: offsetY };
54      return newOffsets;
55    });
56  };
57
58  const handlePaperMouseLeave = (e, index) => {
59    setPaperOffsets(prev => {
60      const newOffsets = [...prev];
61      newOffsets[index] = { x: 0, y: 0 };
62      return newOffsets;
63    });
64  };
65
66  const folderStyle = {
67    '--folder-color': color,
68    '--folder-back-color': folderBackColor,
69    '--paper-1': paper1,
70    '--paper-2': paper2,
71    '--paper-3': paper3
72  };
73
74  const folderClassName = `folder ${open ? 'open' : ''}`.trim();
75  const scaleStyle = { transform: `scale(${size})` };
76
77  return (
78    <div style={scaleStyle} className={className}>
79      <div className={folderClassName} style={folderStyle} onClick={handleClick}>
80        <div className="folder__back">
81          {papers.map((item, i) => (
82            <div
83              key={i}
84              className={`paper paper-${i + 1}`}
85              onMouseMove={e => handlePaperMouseMove(e, i)}
86              onMouseLeave={e => handlePaperMouseLeave(e, i)}
87              style={
88                open
89                  ? {
90                      '--magnet-x': `${paperOffsets[i]?.x || 0}px`,
91                      '--magnet-y': `${paperOffsets[i]?.y || 0}px`
92                    }
93                  : {}
94              }
95            >
96              {item}
97            </div>
98          ))}
99          <div className="folder__front"></div>
100          <div className="folder__front right"></div>
101        </div>
102      </div>
103    </div>
104  );
105};
106
107export default Folder;
108
