--------------------------------------------------

Component: Staggered Menu

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/StaggeredMenu-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import StaggeredMenu from './StaggeredMenu';
2
3const menuItems = [
4  { label: 'Home', ariaLabel: 'Go to home page', link: '/' },
5  { label: 'About', ariaLabel: 'Learn about us', link: '/about' },
6  { label: 'Services', ariaLabel: 'View our services', link: '/services' },
7  { label: 'Contact', ariaLabel: 'Get in touch', link: '/contact' }
8];
9
10const socialItems = [
11  { label: 'Twitter', link: 'https://twitter.com' },
12  { label: 'GitHub', link: 'https://github.com' },
13  { label: 'LinkedIn', link: 'https://linkedin.com' }
14];
15
16<div style={{ height: '100vh', background: '#1a1a1a' }}>
17  <StaggeredMenu
18    position="right"
19    items={menuItems}
20    socialItems={socialItems}
21    displaySocials
22    displayItemNumbering={true}
23    menuButtonColor="#ffffff"
24    openMenuButtonColor="#fff"
25    changeMenuColorOnOpen={true}
26    colors={['#B19EEF', '#5227FF']}
27    logoUrl="/path-to-your-logo.svg"
28    accentColor="#5227FF"
29    onMenuOpen={() => console.log('Menu opened')}
30    onMenuClose={() => console.log('Menu closed')}
31  />
32</div>

Code:
1import React, { useCallback, useLayoutEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3import './StaggeredMenu.css';
4
5export const StaggeredMenu = ({
6  position = 'right',
7  colors = ['#B19EEF', '#5227FF'],
8  items = [],
9  socialItems = [],
10  displaySocials = true,
11  displayItemNumbering = true,
12  className,
13  logoUrl = '/src/assets/logos/reactbits-gh-white.svg',
14  menuButtonColor = '#fff',
15  openMenuButtonColor = '#fff',
16  accentColor = '#5227FF',
17  changeMenuColorOnOpen = true,
18  isFixed = false,
19  closeOnClickAway = true,
20  onMenuOpen,
21  onMenuClose
22}) => {
23  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
24  const openRef = useRef(false);
25  const panelRef = useRef(null);
26  const preLayersRef = useRef(null);
27  const preLayerElsRef = useRef([]);
28  const plusHRef = useRef(null);
29  const plusVRef = useRef(null);
30  const iconRef = useRef(null);
31  const textInnerRef = useRef(null);
32  const textWrapRef = useRef(null);
33  const [textLines, setTextLines] = useState(['Menu', 'Close']);
34
35  const openTlRef = useRef(null);
36  const closeTweenRef = useRef(null);
37  const spinTweenRef = useRef(null);
38  const textCycleAnimRef = useRef(null);
39  const colorTweenRef = useRef(null);
40  const toggleBtnRef = useRef(null);
41  const busyRef = useRef(false);
42  const itemEntranceTweenRef = useRef(null);
43
44  useLayoutEffect(() => {
45    const ctx = gsap.context(() => {
46      const panel = panelRef.current;
47      const preContainer = preLayersRef.current;
48      const plusH = plusHRef.current;
49      const plusV = plusVRef.current;
50      const icon = iconRef.current;
51      const textInner = textInnerRef.current;
52      if (!panel || !plusH || !plusV || !icon || !textInner) return;
53
54      let preLayers = [];
55      if (preContainer) {
56        preLayers = Array.from(preContainer.querySelectorAll('.sm-prelayer'));
57      }
58      preLayerElsRef.current = preLayers;
59
60      const offscreen = position === 'left' ? -100 : 100;
61      gsap.set([panel, ...preLayers], { xPercent: offscreen });
62      gsap.set(plusH, { transformOrigin: '50% 50%', rotate: 0 });
63      gsap.set(plusV, { transformOrigin: '50% 50%', rotate: 90 });
64      gsap.set(icon, { rotate: 0, transformOrigin: '50% 50%' });
65      gsap.set(textInner, { yPercent: 0 });
66      if (toggleBtnRef.current) gsap.set(toggleBtnRef.current, { color: menuButtonColor });
67    });
68    return () => ctx.revert();
69  }, [menuButtonColor, position]);
70
71  const buildOpenTimeline = useCallback(() => {
72    const panel = panelRef.current;
73    const layers = preLayerElsRef.current;
74    if (!panel) return null;
75
76    openTlRef.current?.kill();
77    if (closeTweenRef.current) {
78      closeTweenRef.current.kill();
79      closeTweenRef.current = null;
80    }
81    itemEntranceTweenRef.current?.kill();
82
83    const itemEls = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-panel-itemLabel'));
84    const numberEls = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-panel-list[data-numbering] .sm-panel-item'));
85    const socialTitle = panel.querySelector('.sm-socials-title');
86    const socialLinks = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-socials-link'));
87
88    const layerStates = layers.map(el => ({ el, start: Number(gsap.getProperty(el, 'xPercent')) }));
89    const panelStart = Number(gsap.getProperty(panel, 'xPercent'));
90
91    if (itemEls.length) {
92      gsap.set(itemEls, { yPercent: 140, rotate: 10 });
93    }
94    if (numberEls.length) {
95      gsap.set(numberEls, { '--sm-num-opacity': 0 });
96    }
97    if (socialTitle) {
98      gsap.set(socialTitle, { opacity: 0 });
99    }
100    if (socialLinks.length) {
101      gsap.set(socialLinks, { y: 25, opacity: 0 });
102    }
103
104    const tl = gsap.timeline({ paused: true });
105
106    layerStates.forEach((ls, i) => {
107      tl.fromTo(ls.el, { xPercent: ls.start }, { xPercent: 0, duration: 0.5, ease: 'power4.out' }, i * 0.07);
108    });
109    const lastTime = layerStates.length ? (layerStates.length - 1) * 0.07 : 0;
110    const panelInsertTime = lastTime + (layerStates.length ? 0.08 : 0);
111    const panelDuration = 0.65;
112    tl.fromTo(
113      panel,
114      { xPercent: panelStart },
115      { xPercent: 0, duration: panelDuration, ease: 'power4.out' },
116      panelInsertTime
117    );
118
119    if (itemEls.length) {
120      const itemsStartRatio = 0.15;
121      const itemsStart = panelInsertTime + panelDuration * itemsStartRatio;
122      tl.to(
123        itemEls,
124        {
125          yPercent: 0,
126          rotate: 0,
127          duration: 1,
128          ease: 'power4.out',
129          stagger: { each: 0.1, from: 'start' }
130        },
131        itemsStart
132      );
133      if (numberEls.length) {
134        tl.to(
135          numberEls,
136          {
137            duration: 0.6,
138            ease: 'power2.out',
139            '--sm-num-opacity': 1,
140            stagger: { each: 0.08, from: 'start' }
141          },
142          itemsStart + 0.1
143        );
144      }
145    }
146
147    if (socialTitle || socialLinks.length) {
148      const socialsStart = panelInsertTime + panelDuration * 0.4;
149      if (socialTitle) {
150        tl.to(
151          socialTitle,
152          {
153            opacity: 1,
154            duration: 0.5,
155            ease: 'power2.out'
156          },
157          socialsStart
158        );
159      }
160      if (socialLinks.length) {
161        tl.to(
162          socialLinks,
163          {
164            y: 0,
165            opacity: 1,
166            duration: 0.55,
167            ease: 'power3.out',
168            stagger: { each: 0.08, from: 'start' },
169            onComplete: () => {
170              gsap.set(socialLinks, { clearProps: 'opacity' });
171            }
172          },
173          socialsStart + 0.04
174        );
175      }
176    }
177
178    openTlRef.current = tl;
179    return tl;
180  }, []);
181
182  const playOpen = useCallback(() => {
183    if (busyRef.current) return;
184    busyRef.current = true;
185    const tl = buildOpenTimeline();
186    if (tl) {
187      tl.eventCallback('onComplete', () => {
188        busyRef.current = false;
189      });
190      tl.play(0);
191    } else {
192      busyRef.current = false;
193    }
194  }, [buildOpenTimeline]);
195
196  const playClose = useCallback(() => {
197    openTlRef.current?.kill();
198    openTlRef.current = null;
199    itemEntranceTweenRef.current?.kill();
200
201    const panel = panelRef.current;
202    const layers = preLayerElsRef.current;
203    if (!panel) return;
204
205    const all = [...layers, panel];
206    closeTweenRef.current?.kill();
207    const offscreen = position === 'left' ? -100 : 100;
208    closeTweenRef.current = gsap.to(all, {
209      xPercent: offscreen,
210      duration: 0.32,
211      ease: 'power3.in',
212      overwrite: 'auto',
213      onComplete: () => {
214        const itemEls = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-panel-itemLabel'));
215        if (itemEls.length) {
216          gsap.set(itemEls, { yPercent: 140, rotate: 10 });
217        }
218        const numberEls = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-panel-list[data-numbering] .sm-panel-item'));
219        if (numberEls.length) {
220          gsap.set(numberEls, { '--sm-num-opacity': 0 });
221        }
222        const socialTitle = panel.querySelector('.sm-socials-title');
223        const socialLinks = Array.from(panel.querySelectorAll('.sm-socials-link'));
224        if (socialTitle) gsap.set(socialTitle, { opacity: 0 });
225        if (socialLinks.length) gsap.set(socialLinks, { y: 25, opacity: 0 });
226        busyRef.current = false;
227      }
228    });
229  }, [position]);
230
231  const animateIcon = useCallback(opening => {
232    const icon = iconRef.current;
233    if (!icon) return;
234    spinTweenRef.current?.kill();
235    if (opening) {
236      spinTweenRef.current = gsap.to(icon, { rotate: 225, duration: 0.8, ease: 'power4.out', overwrite: 'auto' });
237    } else {
238      spinTweenRef.current = gsap.to(icon, { rotate: 0, duration: 0.35, ease: 'power3.inOut', overwrite: 'auto' });
239    }
240  }, []);
241
242  const animateColor = useCallback(
243    opening => {
244      const btn = toggleBtnRef.current;
245      if (!btn) return;
246      colorTweenRef.current?.kill();
247      if (changeMenuColorOnOpen) {
248        const targetColor = opening ? openMenuButtonColor : menuButtonColor;
249        colorTweenRef.current = gsap.to(btn, {
250          color: targetColor,
251          delay: 0.18,
252          duration: 0.3,
253          ease: 'power2.out'
254        });
255      } else {
256        gsap.set(btn, { color: menuButtonColor });
257      }
258    },
259    [openMenuButtonColor, menuButtonColor, changeMenuColorOnOpen]
260  );
261
262  React.useEffect(() => {
263    if (toggleBtnRef.current) {
264      if (changeMenuColorOnOpen) {
265        const targetColor = openRef.current ? openMenuButtonColor : menuButtonColor;
266        gsap.set(toggleBtnRef.current, { color: targetColor });
267      } else {
268        gsap.set(toggleBtnRef.current, { color: menuButtonColor });
269      }
270    }
271  }, [changeMenuColorOnOpen, menuButtonColor, openMenuButtonColor]);
272
273  const animateText = useCallback(opening => {
274    const inner = textInnerRef.current;
275    if (!inner) return;
276    textCycleAnimRef.current?.kill();
277
278    const currentLabel = opening ? 'Menu' : 'Close';
279    const targetLabel = opening ? 'Close' : 'Menu';
280    const cycles = 3;
281    const seq = [currentLabel];
282    let last = currentLabel;
283    for (let i = 0; i < cycles; i++) {
284      last = last === 'Menu' ? 'Close' : 'Menu';
285      seq.push(last);
286    }
287    if (last !== targetLabel) seq.push(targetLabel);
288    seq.push(targetLabel);
289    setTextLines(seq);
290
291    gsap.set(inner, { yPercent: 0 });
292    const lineCount = seq.length;
293    const finalShift = ((lineCount - 1) / lineCount) * 100;
294    textCycleAnimRef.current = gsap.to(inner, {
295      yPercent: -finalShift,
296      duration: 0.5 + lineCount * 0.07,
297      ease: 'power4.out'
298    });
299  }, []);
300
301  const toggleMenu = useCallback(() => {
302    const target = !openRef.current;
303    openRef.current = target;
304    setOpen(target);
305    if (target) {
306      onMenuOpen?.();
307      playOpen();
308    } else {
309      onMenuClose?.();
310      playClose();
311    }
312    animateIcon(target);
313    animateColor(target);
314    animateText(target);
315  }, [playOpen, playClose, animateIcon, animateColor, animateText, onMenuOpen, onMenuClose]);
316
317  const closeMenu = useCallback(() => {
318    if (openRef.current) {
319      openRef.current = false;
320      setOpen(false);
321      onMenuClose?.();
322      playClose();
323      animateIcon(false);
324      animateColor(false);
325      animateText(false);
326    }
327  }, [playClose, animateIcon, animateColor, animateText, onMenuClose]);
328
329  React.useEffect(() => {
330    if (!closeOnClickAway || !open) return;
331
332    const handleClickOutside = event => {
333      if (
334        panelRef.current &&
335        !panelRef.current.contains(event.target) &&
336        toggleBtnRef.current &&
337        !toggleBtnRef.current.contains(event.target)
338      ) {
339        closeMenu();
340      }
341    };
342
343    document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
344    return () => {
345      document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
346    };
347  }, [closeOnClickAway, open, closeMenu]);
348
349  return (
350    <div
351      className={(className ? className + ' ' : '') + 'staggered-menu-wrapper' + (isFixed ? ' fixed-wrapper' : '')}
352      style={accentColor ? { ['--sm-accent']: accentColor } : undefined}
353      data-position={position}
354      data-open={open || undefined}
355    >
356      <div ref={preLayersRef} className="sm-prelayers" aria-hidden="true">
357        {(() => {
358          const raw = colors && colors.length ? colors.slice(0, 4) : ['#1e1e22', '#35353c'];
359          let arr = [...raw];
360          if (arr.length >= 3) {
361            const mid = Math.floor(arr.length / 2);
362            arr.splice(mid, 1);
363          }
364          return arr.map((c, i) => <div key={i} className="sm-prelayer" style={{ background: c }} />);
365        })()}
366      </div>
367      <header className="staggered-menu-header" aria-label="Main navigation header">
368        <div className="sm-logo" aria-label="Logo">
369          <img
370            src={logoUrl || '/src/assets/logos/reactbits-gh-white.svg'}
371            alt="Logo"
372            className="sm-logo-img"
373            draggable={false}
374            width={110}
375            height={24}
376          />
377        </div>
378        <button
379          ref={toggleBtnRef}
380          className="sm-toggle"
381          aria-label={open ? 'Close menu' : 'Open menu'}
382          aria-expanded={open}
383          aria-controls="staggered-menu-panel"
384          onClick={toggleMenu}
385          type="button"
386        >
387          <span ref={textWrapRef} className="sm-toggle-textWrap" aria-hidden="true">
388            <span ref={textInnerRef} className="sm-toggle-textInner">
389              {textLines.map((l, i) => (
390                <span className="sm-toggle-line" key={i}>
391                  {l}
392                </span>
393              ))}
394            </span>
395          </span>
396          <span ref={iconRef} className="sm-icon" aria-hidden="true">
397            <span ref={plusHRef} className="sm-icon-line" />
398            <span ref={plusVRef} className="sm-icon-line sm-icon-line-v" />
399          </span>
400        </button>
401      </header>
402
403      <aside id="staggered-menu-panel" ref={panelRef} className="staggered-menu-panel" aria-hidden={!open}>
404        <div className="sm-panel-inner">
405          <ul className="sm-panel-list" role="list" data-numbering={displayItemNumbering || undefined}>
406            {items && items.length ? (
407              items.map((it, idx) => (
408                <li className="sm-panel-itemWrap" key={it.label + idx}>
409                  <a className="sm-panel-item" href={it.link} aria-label={it.ariaLabel} data-index={idx + 1}>
410                    <span className="sm-panel-itemLabel">{it.label}</span>
411                  </a>
412                </li>
413              ))
414            ) : (
415              <li className="sm-panel-itemWrap" aria-hidden="true">
416                <span className="sm-panel-item">
417                  <span className="sm-panel-itemLabel">No items</span>
418                </span>
419              </li>
420            )}
421          </ul>
422          {displaySocials && socialItems && socialItems.length > 0 && (
423            <div className="sm-socials" aria-label="Social links">
424              <h3 className="sm-socials-title">Socials</h3>
425              <ul className="sm-socials-list" role="list">
426                {socialItems.map((s, i) => (
427                  <li key={s.label + i} className="sm-socials-item">
428                    <a href={s.link} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" className="sm-socials-link">
429                      {s.label}
430                    </a>
431                  </li>
432                ))}
433              </ul>
434            </div>
435          )}
436        </div>
437      </aside>
438    </div>
439  );
440};
441
442export default StaggeredMenu;
443

Component: Model Viewer

Component: Lanyard

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Lanyard-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Lanyard from './Lanyard'
2
3<Lanyard position={[0, 0, 20]} gravity={[0, -40, 0]} />
4
5/* IMPORTANT INFO BELOW
6
71. You MUST have the card.glb and lanyard.png files in your project and import them
8- these can be downloaded from the repo's files, under src/assets/lanyard
9
102. You can edit your card.glb file in this online .glb editor and change the texture:
11- https://modelviewer.dev/editor/
12
134. The png file is the texture for the lanyard's band and can be edited in any image editor
14
155. Your Vite configuration must be updated to include the following in vite.config.js:
16assetsInclude: ['**/*.glb']
17
186. For TS users, you might need these changes:
19
20- src/global.d.ts
21export { };
22
23declare module '*.glb';
24declare module '*.png';
25
26declare module 'meshline' {
27  export const MeshLineGeometry: any;
28  export const MeshLineMaterial: any;
29}
30
31declare global {
32  namespace JSX {
33    interface IntrinsicElements {
34      meshLineGeometry: any;
35      meshLineMaterial: any;
36    }
37  }
38}
39
40- src/vite-env.d.ts
41/// <reference types="vite/client"
42  position={[0,0,24]}
43  gravity={[0,-40,0]}
44/>
45declare module '*.glb';
46declare module '*.png';
47*/

Code:
1/* eslint-disable react/no-unknown-property */
2'use client';
3import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
4import { Canvas, extend, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber';
5import { useGLTF, useTexture, Environment, Lightformer } from '@react-three/drei';
6import { BallCollider, CuboidCollider, Physics, RigidBody, useRopeJoint, useSphericalJoint } from '@react-three/rapier';
7import { MeshLineGeometry, MeshLineMaterial } from 'meshline';
8
9// replace with your own imports, see the usage snippet for details
10import cardGLB from './card.glb';
11import lanyard from './lanyard.png';
12
13import * as THREE from 'three';
14import './Lanyard.css';
15
16extend({ MeshLineGeometry, MeshLineMaterial });
17
18export default function Lanyard({ position = [0, 0, 30], gravity = [0, -40, 0], fov = 20, transparent = true }) {
19  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = useState(() => typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.innerWidth < 768);
20
21  useEffect(() => {
22    const handleResize = () => setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < 768);
23    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
24    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
25  }, []);
26
27  return (
28    <div className="lanyard-wrapper">
29      <Canvas
30        camera={{ position: position, fov: fov }}
31        dpr={[1, isMobile ? 1.5 : 2]}
32        gl={{ alpha: transparent }}
33        onCreated={({ gl }) => gl.setClearColor(new THREE.Color(0x000000), transparent ? 0 : 1)}
34      >
35        <ambientLight intensity={Math.PI} />
36        <Physics gravity={gravity} timeStep={isMobile ? 1 / 30 : 1 / 60}>
37          <Band isMobile={isMobile} />
38        </Physics>
39        <Environment blur={0.75}>
40          <Lightformer
41            intensity={2}
42            color="white"
43            position={[0, -1, 5]}
44            rotation={[0, 0, Math.PI / 3]}
45            scale={[100, 0.1, 1]}
46          />
47          <Lightformer
48            intensity={3}
49            color="white"
50            position={[-1, -1, 1]}
51            rotation={[0, 0, Math.PI / 3]}
52            scale={[100, 0.1, 1]}
53          />
54          <Lightformer
55            intensity={3}
56            color="white"
57            position={[1, 1, 1]}
58            rotation={[0, 0, Math.PI / 3]}
59            scale={[100, 0.1, 1]}
60          />
61          <Lightformer
62            intensity={10}
63            color="white"
64            position={[-10, 0, 14]}
65            rotation={[0, Math.PI / 2, Math.PI / 3]}
66            scale={[100, 10, 1]}
67          />
68        </Environment>
69      </Canvas>
70    </div>
71  );
72}
73function Band({ maxSpeed = 50, minSpeed = 0, isMobile = false }) {
74  const band = useRef(),
75    fixed = useRef(),
76    j1 = useRef(),
77    j2 = useRef(),
78    j3 = useRef(),
79    card = useRef();
80  const vec = new THREE.Vector3(),
81    ang = new THREE.Vector3(),
82    rot = new THREE.Vector3(),
83    dir = new THREE.Vector3();
84  const segmentProps = { type: 'dynamic', canSleep: true, colliders: false, angularDamping: 4, linearDamping: 4 };
85  const { nodes, materials } = useGLTF(cardGLB);
86  const texture = useTexture(lanyard);
87  const [curve] = useState(
88    () =>
89      new THREE.CatmullRomCurve3([new THREE.Vector3(), new THREE.Vector3(), new THREE.Vector3(), new THREE.Vector3()])
90  );
91  const [dragged, drag] = useState(false);
92  const [hovered, hover] = useState(false);
93
94  useRopeJoint(fixed, j1, [[0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0], 1]);
95  useRopeJoint(j1, j2, [[0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0], 1]);
96  useRopeJoint(j2, j3, [[0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0], 1]);
97  useSphericalJoint(j3, card, [
98    [0, 0, 0],
99    [0, 1.5, 0]
100  ]);
101
102  useEffect(() => {
103    if (hovered) {
104      document.body.style.cursor = dragged ? 'grabbing' : 'grab';
105      return () => void (document.body.style.cursor = 'auto');
106    }
107  }, [hovered, dragged]);
108
109  useFrame((state, delta) => {
110    if (dragged) {
111      vec.set(state.pointer.x, state.pointer.y, 0.5).unproject(state.camera);
112      dir.copy(vec).sub(state.camera.position).normalize();
113      vec.add(dir.multiplyScalar(state.camera.position.length()));
114      [card, j1, j2, j3, fixed].forEach(ref => ref.current?.wakeUp());
115      card.current?.setNextKinematicTranslation({ x: vec.x - dragged.x, y: vec.y - dragged.y, z: vec.z - dragged.z });
116    }
117    if (fixed.current) {
118      [j1, j2].forEach(ref => {
119        if (!ref.current.lerped) ref.current.lerped = new THREE.Vector3().copy(ref.current.translation());
120        const clampedDistance = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1, ref.current.lerped.distanceTo(ref.current.translation())));
121        ref.current.lerped.lerp(
122          ref.current.translation(),
123          delta * (minSpeed + clampedDistance * (maxSpeed - minSpeed))
124        );
125      });
126      curve.points[0].copy(j3.current.translation());
127      curve.points[1].copy(j2.current.lerped);
128      curve.points[2].copy(j1.current.lerped);
129      curve.points[3].copy(fixed.current.translation());
130      band.current.geometry.setPoints(curve.getPoints(isMobile ? 16 : 32));
131      ang.copy(card.current.angvel());
132      rot.copy(card.current.rotation());
133      card.current.setAngvel({ x: ang.x, y: ang.y - rot.y * 0.25, z: ang.z });
134    }
135  });
136
137  curve.curveType = 'chordal';
138  texture.wrapS = texture.wrapT = THREE.RepeatWrapping;
139
140  return (
141    <>
142      <group position={[0, 4, 0]}>
143        <RigidBody ref={fixed} {...segmentProps} type="fixed" />
144        <RigidBody position={[0.5, 0, 0]} ref={j1} {...segmentProps}>
145          <BallCollider args={[0.1]} />
146        </RigidBody>
147        <RigidBody position={[1, 0, 0]} ref={j2} {...segmentProps}>
148          <BallCollider args={[0.1]} />
149        </RigidBody>
150        <RigidBody position={[1.5, 0, 0]} ref={j3} {...segmentProps}>
151          <BallCollider args={[0.1]} />
152        </RigidBody>
153        <RigidBody position={[2, 0, 0]} ref={card} {...segmentProps} type={dragged ? 'kinematicPosition' : 'dynamic'}>
154          <CuboidCollider args={[0.8, 1.125, 0.01]} />
155          <group
156            scale={2.25}
157            position={[0, -1.2, -0.05]}
158            onPointerOver={() => hover(true)}
159            onPointerOut={() => hover(false)}
160            onPointerUp={e => (e.target.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId), drag(false))}
161            onPointerDown={e => (
162              e.target.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId),
163              drag(new THREE.Vector3().copy(e.point).sub(vec.copy(card.current.translation())))
164            )}
165          >
166            <mesh geometry={nodes.card.geometry}>
167              <meshPhysicalMaterial
168                map={materials.base.map}
169                map-anisotropy={16}
170                clearcoat={isMobile ? 0 : 1}
171                clearcoatRoughness={0.15}
172                roughness={0.9}
173                metalness={0.8}
174              />
175            </mesh>
176            <mesh geometry={nodes.clip.geometry} material={materials.metal} material-roughness={0.3} />
177            <mesh geometry={nodes.clamp.geometry} material={materials.metal} />
178          </group>
179        </RigidBody>
180      </group>
181      <mesh ref={band}>
182        <meshLineGeometry />
183        <meshLineMaterial
184          color="white"
185          depthTest={false}
186          resolution={isMobile ? [1000, 2000] : [1000, 1000]}
187          useMap
188          map={texture}
189          repeat={[-4, 1]}
190          lineWidth={1}
191        />
192      </mesh>
193    </>
194  );
195}
196

Component: Profile Card

Usage:
1import ProfileCard from './ProfileCard'
2  
3<ProfileCard
4  name="Javi A. Torres"
5  title="Software Engineer"
6  handle="javicodes"
7  status="Online"
8  contactText="Contact Me"
9  avatarUrl="/path/to/avatar.jpg"

11  enableTilt={true}
12  enableMobileTilt={false}

Code:
1import React, { useEffect, useRef, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
2import './ProfileCard.css';
3
4const DEFAULT_INNER_GRADIENT = 'linear-gradient(145deg,#60496e8c 0%,#71C4FF44 100%)';
5
6const ANIMATION_CONFIG = {
7  INITIAL_DURATION: 1200,
8  INITIAL_X_OFFSET: 70,
9  INITIAL_Y_OFFSET: 60,
10  DEVICE_BETA_OFFSET: 20,
11  ENTER_TRANSITION_MS: 180
12};
13
14const clamp = (v, min = 0, max = 100) => Math.min(Math.max(v, min), max);
15const round = (v, precision = 3) => parseFloat(v.toFixed(precision));
16const adjust = (v, fMin, fMax, tMin, tMax) => round(tMin + ((tMax - tMin) * (v - fMin)) / (fMax - fMin));
17
18const ProfileCardComponent = ({
19  avatarUrl = '<Placeholder for avatar URL>',
20  iconUrl = '<Placeholder for icon URL>',
21  grainUrl = '<Placeholder for grain URL>',
22  innerGradient,
23  behindGlowEnabled = true,
24  behindGlowColor,
25  behindGlowSize,
26  className = '',
27  enableTilt = true,
28  enableMobileTilt = false,
29  mobileTiltSensitivity = 5,
30  miniAvatarUrl,
31  name = 'Javi A. Torres',
32  title = 'Software Engineer',
33  handle = 'javicodes',
34  status = 'Online',
35  contactText = 'Contact',
36  showUserInfo = true,
37  onContactClick
38}) => {
39  const wrapRef = useRef(null);
40  const shellRef = useRef(null);
41
42  const enterTimerRef = useRef(null);
43  const leaveRafRef = useRef(null);
44
45  const tiltEngine = useMemo(() => {
46    if (!enableTilt) return null;
47
48    let rafId = null;
49    let running = false;
50    let lastTs = 0;
51
52    let currentX = 0;
53    let currentY = 0;
54    let targetX = 0;
55    let targetY = 0;
56
57    const DEFAULT_TAU = 0.14;
58    const INITIAL_TAU = 0.6;
59    let initialUntil = 0;
60
61    const setVarsFromXY = (x, y) => {
62      const shell = shellRef.current;
63      const wrap = wrapRef.current;
64      if (!shell || !wrap) return;
65
66      const width = shell.clientWidth || 1;
67      const height = shell.clientHeight || 1;
68
69      const percentX = clamp((100 / width) * x);
70      const percentY = clamp((100 / height) * y);
71
72      const centerX = percentX - 50;
73      const centerY = percentY - 50;
74
75      const properties = {
76        '--pointer-x': `${percentX}%`,
77        '--pointer-y': `${percentY}%`,
78        '--background-x': `${adjust(percentX, 0, 100, 35, 65)}%`,
79        '--background-y': `${adjust(percentY, 0, 100, 35, 65)}%`,
80        '--pointer-from-center': `${clamp(Math.hypot(percentY - 50, percentX - 50) / 50, 0, 1)}`,
81        '--pointer-from-top': `${percentY / 100}`,
82        '--pointer-from-left': `${percentX / 100}`,
83        '--rotate-x': `${round(-(centerX / 5))}deg`,
84        '--rotate-y': `${round(centerY / 4)}deg`
85      };
86
87      for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(properties)) wrap.style.setProperty(k, v);
88    };
89
90    const step = ts => {
91      if (!running) return;
92      if (lastTs === 0) lastTs = ts;
93      const dt = (ts - lastTs) / 1000;
94      lastTs = ts;
95
96      const tau = ts < initialUntil ? INITIAL_TAU : DEFAULT_TAU;
97      const k = 1 - Math.exp(-dt / tau);
98
99      currentX += (targetX - currentX) * k;
100      currentY += (targetY - currentY) * k;
101
102      setVarsFromXY(currentX, currentY);
103
104      const stillFar = Math.abs(targetX - currentX) > 0.05 || Math.abs(targetY - currentY) > 0.05;
105
106      if (stillFar || document.hasFocus()) {
107        rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
108      } else {
109        running = false;
110        lastTs = 0;
111        if (rafId) {
112          cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
113          rafId = null;
114        }
115      }
116    };
117
118    const start = () => {
119      if (running) return;
120      running = true;
121      lastTs = 0;
122      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
123    };
124
125    return {
126      setImmediate(x, y) {
127        currentX = x;
128        currentY = y;
129        setVarsFromXY(currentX, currentY);
130      },
131      setTarget(x, y) {
132        targetX = x;
133        targetY = y;
134        start();
135      },
136      toCenter() {
137        const shell = shellRef.current;
138        if (!shell) return;
139        this.setTarget(shell.clientWidth / 2, shell.clientHeight / 2);
140      },
141      beginInitial(durationMs) {
142        initialUntil = performance.now() + durationMs;
143        start();
144      },
145      getCurrent() {
146        return { x: currentX, y: currentY, tx: targetX, ty: targetY };
147      },
148      cancel() {
149        if (rafId) cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
150        rafId = null;
151        running = false;
152        lastTs = 0;
153      }
154    };
155  }, [enableTilt]);
156
157  const getOffsets = (evt, el) => {
158    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
159    return { x: evt.clientX - rect.left, y: evt.clientY - rect.top };
160  };
161
162  const handlePointerMove = useCallback(
163    event => {
164      const shell = shellRef.current;
165      if (!shell || !tiltEngine) return;
166      const { x, y } = getOffsets(event, shell);
167      tiltEngine.setTarget(x, y);
168    },
169    [tiltEngine]
170  );
171
172  const handlePointerEnter = useCallback(
173    event => {
174      const shell = shellRef.current;
175      if (!shell || !tiltEngine) return;
176
177      shell.classList.add('active');
178      shell.classList.add('entering');
179      if (enterTimerRef.current) window.clearTimeout(enterTimerRef.current);
180      enterTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
181        shell.classList.remove('entering');
182      }, ANIMATION_CONFIG.ENTER_TRANSITION_MS);
183
184      const { x, y } = getOffsets(event, shell);
185      tiltEngine.setTarget(x, y);
186    },
187    [tiltEngine]
188  );
189
190  const handlePointerLeave = useCallback(() => {
191    const shell = shellRef.current;
192    if (!shell || !tiltEngine) return;
193
194    tiltEngine.toCenter();
195
196    const checkSettle = () => {
197      const { x, y, tx, ty } = tiltEngine.getCurrent();
198      const settled = Math.hypot(tx - x, ty - y) < 0.6;
199      if (settled) {
200        shell.classList.remove('active');
201        leaveRafRef.current = null;
202      } else {
203        leaveRafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(checkSettle);
204      }
205    };
206    if (leaveRafRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(leaveRafRef.current);
207    leaveRafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(checkSettle);
208  }, [tiltEngine]);
209
210  const handleDeviceOrientation = useCallback(
211    event => {
212      const shell = shellRef.current;
213      if (!shell || !tiltEngine) return;
214
215      const { beta, gamma } = event;
216      if (beta == null || gamma == null) return;
217
218      const centerX = shell.clientWidth / 2;
219      const centerY = shell.clientHeight / 2;
220      const x = clamp(centerX + gamma * mobileTiltSensitivity, 0, shell.clientWidth);
221      const y = clamp(
222        centerY + (beta - ANIMATION_CONFIG.DEVICE_BETA_OFFSET) * mobileTiltSensitivity,
223        0,
224        shell.clientHeight
225      );
226
227      tiltEngine.setTarget(x, y);
228    },
229    [tiltEngine, mobileTiltSensitivity]
230  );
231
232  useEffect(() => {
233    if (!enableTilt || !tiltEngine) return;
234
235    const shell = shellRef.current;
236    if (!shell) return;
237
238    const pointerMoveHandler = handlePointerMove;
239    const pointerEnterHandler = handlePointerEnter;
240    const pointerLeaveHandler = handlePointerLeave;
241    const deviceOrientationHandler = handleDeviceOrientation;
242
243    shell.addEventListener('pointerenter', pointerEnterHandler);
244    shell.addEventListener('pointermove', pointerMoveHandler);
245    shell.addEventListener('pointerleave', pointerLeaveHandler);
246
247    const handleClick = () => {
248      if (!enableMobileTilt || location.protocol !== 'https:') return;
249      const anyMotion = window.DeviceMotionEvent;
250      if (anyMotion && typeof anyMotion.requestPermission === 'function') {
251        anyMotion
252          .requestPermission()
253          .then(state => {
254            if (state === 'granted') {
255              window.addEventListener('deviceorientation', deviceOrientationHandler);
256            }
257          })
258          .catch(console.error);
259      } else {
260        window.addEventListener('deviceorientation', deviceOrientationHandler);
261      }
262    };
263    shell.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
264
265    const initialX = (shell.clientWidth || 0) - ANIMATION_CONFIG.INITIAL_X_OFFSET;
266    const initialY = ANIMATION_CONFIG.INITIAL_Y_OFFSET;
267    tiltEngine.setImmediate(initialX, initialY);
268    tiltEngine.toCenter();
269    tiltEngine.beginInitial(ANIMATION_CONFIG.INITIAL_DURATION);
270
271    return () => {
272      shell.removeEventListener('pointerenter', pointerEnterHandler);
273      shell.removeEventListener('pointermove', pointerMoveHandler);
274      shell.removeEventListener('pointerleave', pointerLeaveHandler);
275      shell.removeEventListener('click', handleClick);
276      window.removeEventListener('deviceorientation', deviceOrientationHandler);
277      if (enterTimerRef.current) window.clearTimeout(enterTimerRef.current);
278      if (leaveRafRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(leaveRafRef.current);
279      tiltEngine.cancel();
280      shell.classList.remove('entering');
281    };
282  }, [
283    enableTilt,
284    enableMobileTilt,
285    tiltEngine,
286    handlePointerMove,
287    handlePointerEnter,
288    handlePointerLeave,
289    handleDeviceOrientation
290  ]);
291
292  const cardStyle = useMemo(
293    () => ({
294      '--icon': iconUrl ? `url(${iconUrl})` : 'none',
295      '--grain': grainUrl ? `url(${grainUrl})` : 'none',
296      '--inner-gradient': innerGradient ?? DEFAULT_INNER_GRADIENT,
297      '--behind-glow-color': behindGlowColor ?? 'rgba(125, 190, 255, 0.67)',
298      '--behind-glow-size': behindGlowSize ?? '50%'
299    }),
300    [iconUrl, grainUrl, innerGradient, behindGlowColor, behindGlowSize]
301  );
302
303  const handleContactClick = useCallback(() => {
304    onContactClick?.();
305  }, [onContactClick]);
306
307  return (
308    <div ref={wrapRef} className={`pc-card-wrapper ${className}`.trim()} style={cardStyle}>
309      {behindGlowEnabled && <div className="pc-behind" />}
310      <div ref={shellRef} className="pc-card-shell">
311        <section className="pc-card">
312          <div className="pc-inside">
313            <div className="pc-shine" />
314            <div className="pc-glare" />
315            <div className="pc-content pc-avatar-content">
316              <img
317                className="avatar"
318                src={avatarUrl}
319                alt={`${name || 'User'} avatar`}
320                loading="lazy"
321                onError={e => {
322                  const t = e.target;
323                  t.style.display = 'none';
324                }}
325              />
326              {showUserInfo && (
327                <div className="pc-user-info">
328                  <div className="pc-user-details">
329                    <div className="pc-mini-avatar">
330                      <img
331                        src={miniAvatarUrl || avatarUrl}
332                        alt={`${name || 'User'} mini avatar`}
333                        loading="lazy"
334                        onError={e => {
335                          const t = e.target;
336                          t.style.opacity = '0.5';
337                          t.src = avatarUrl;
338                        }}
339                      />
340                    </div>
341                    <div className="pc-user-text">
342                      <div className="pc-handle">@{handle}</div>
343                      <div className="pc-status">{status}</div>
344                    </div>
345                  </div>
346                  <button
347                    className="pc-contact-btn"
348                    onClick={handleContactClick}
349                    style={{ pointerEvents: 'auto' }}
350                    type="button"
351                    aria-label={`Contact ${name || 'user'}`}
352                  >
353                    {contactText}
354                  </button>
355                </div>
356              )}
357            </div>
358            <div className="pc-content">
359              <div className="pc-details">
360                <h3>{name}</h3>
361                <p>{title}</p>
362              </div>
363            </div>
364          </div>
365        </section>
366      </div>
367    </div>
368  );
369};
370
371const ProfileCard = React.memo(ProfileCardComponent);
372export default ProfileCard;
373

31}

47    var(--behind-glow-color) 0%,
48    transparent var(--behind-glow-size)
49  );
50  filter: blur(50px) saturate(1.1);
51  opacity: calc(0.8 * var(--card-opacity));
52  transition: opacity 200ms ease;
53}
54
55.pc-card-wrapper:hover,
56.pc-card-wrapper.active {

58}
59
60.pc-card {
61  height: 80svh;
62  max-height: 540px;
63  display: grid;
64  aspect-ratio: 0.718;
65  border-radius: var(--card-radius);
66  position: relative;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Dock

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Dock-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Dock from './Dock';
2
3  const items = [
4    { icon: <VscHome size={18} />, label: 'Home', onClick: () => alert('Home!') },
5    { icon: <VscArchive size={18} />, label: 'Archive', onClick: () => alert('Archive!') },
6    { icon: <VscAccount size={18} />, label: 'Profile', onClick: () => alert('Profile!') },
7    { icon: <VscSettingsGear size={18} />, label: 'Settings', onClick: () => alert('Settings!') },
8  ];
9
10  <Dock 
11    items={items}
12    panelHeight={68}
13    baseItemSize={50}
14    magnification={70}
15  />

Code:
1'use client';
2
3import { motion, useMotionValue, useSpring, useTransform, AnimatePresence } from 'motion/react';
4import { Children, cloneElement, useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
5
6import './Dock.css';
7
8function DockItem({ children, className = '', onClick, mouseX, spring, distance, magnification, baseItemSize }) {
9  const ref = useRef(null);
10  const isHovered = useMotionValue(0);
11
12  const mouseDistance = useTransform(mouseX, val => {
13    const rect = ref.current?.getBoundingClientRect() ?? {
14      x: 0,
15      width: baseItemSize
16    };
17    return val - rect.x - baseItemSize / 2;
18  });
19
20  const targetSize = useTransform(mouseDistance, [-distance, 0, distance], [baseItemSize, magnification, baseItemSize]);
21  const size = useSpring(targetSize, spring);
22
23  return (
24    <motion.div
25      ref={ref}
26      style={{
27        width: size,
28        height: size
29      }}
30      onHoverStart={() => isHovered.set(1)}
31      onHoverEnd={() => isHovered.set(0)}
32      onFocus={() => isHovered.set(1)}
33      onBlur={() => isHovered.set(0)}
34      onClick={onClick}
35      className={`dock-item ${className}`}
36      tabIndex={0}
37      role="button"
38      aria-haspopup="true"
39    >
40      {Children.map(children, child => cloneElement(child, { isHovered }))}
41    </motion.div>
42  );
43}
44
45function DockLabel({ children, className = '', ...rest }) {
46  const { isHovered } = rest;
47  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
48
49  useEffect(() => {
50    const unsubscribe = isHovered.on('change', latest => {
51      setIsVisible(latest === 1);
52    });
53    return () => unsubscribe();
54  }, [isHovered]);
55
56  return (
57    <AnimatePresence>
58      {isVisible && (
59        <motion.div
60          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 0 }}
61          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: -10 }}
62          exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 0 }}
63          transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
64          className={`dock-label ${className}`}
65          role="tooltip"
66          style={{ x: '-50%' }}
67        >
68          {children}
69        </motion.div>
70      )}
71    </AnimatePresence>
72  );
73}
74
75function DockIcon({ children, className = '' }) {
76  return <div className={`dock-icon ${className}`}>{children}</div>;
77}
78
79export default function Dock({
80  items,
81  className = '',
82  spring = { mass: 0.1, stiffness: 150, damping: 12 },
83  magnification = 70,
84  distance = 200,
85  panelHeight = 68,
86  dockHeight = 256,
87  baseItemSize = 50
88}) {
89  const mouseX = useMotionValue(Infinity);
90  const isHovered = useMotionValue(0);
91
92  const maxHeight = useMemo(
93    () => Math.max(dockHeight, magnification + magnification / 2 + 4),
94    [magnification, dockHeight]
95  );
96  const heightRow = useTransform(isHovered, [0, 1], [panelHeight, maxHeight]);
97  const height = useSpring(heightRow, spring);
98
99  return (
100    <motion.div style={{ height, scrollbarWidth: 'none' }} className="dock-outer">
101      <motion.div
102        onMouseMove={({ pageX }) => {
103          isHovered.set(1);
104          mouseX.set(pageX);
105        }}
106        onMouseLeave={() => {
107          isHovered.set(0);
108          mouseX.set(Infinity);
109        }}
110        className={`dock-panel ${className}`}
111        style={{ height: panelHeight }}
112        role="toolbar"
113        aria-label="Application dock"
114      >
115        {items.map((item, index) => (
116          <DockItem
117            key={index}
118            onClick={item.onClick}
119            className={item.className}
120            mouseX={mouseX}
121            spring={spring}
122            distance={distance}
123            magnification={magnification}
124            baseItemSize={baseItemSize}
125          >
126            <DockIcon>{item.icon}</DockIcon>
127            <DockLabel>{item.label}</DockLabel>
128          </DockItem>
129        ))}
130      </motion.div>
131    </motion.div>
132  );
133}
134

Extra Config/Code:

4  max-width: 100%;
5  align-items: center;
6}
7

10  bottom: 0.5rem;
11  left: 50%;
12  transform: translateX(-50%);
13  display: flex;
14  align-items: flex-end;
15  width: fit-content;
16  gap: 1rem;
17  border-radius: 1rem;
18  background-color: #060010;
19  border: 1px solid #222;
20  padding: 0 0.5rem 0.5rem;
21}
22
23.dock-item {
24  position: relative;
25  display: inline-flex;
26  align-items: center;
27  justify-content: center;
28  border-radius: 10px;
29  background-color: #060010;
30  border: 1px solid #222;
31  box-shadow:
32    0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1),
33    0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06);
34  cursor: pointer;
35  outline: none;
36}
37
38.dock-icon {
39  display: flex;
40  align-items: center;
41  justify-content: center;
42}
43
44.dock-label {
45  position: absolute;
46  top: -1.5rem;
47  left: 50%;
48  width: fit-content;
49  white-space: pre;
50  border-radius: 0.375rem;
51  border: 1px solid #222;
52  background-color: #060010;
53  padding: 0.125rem 0.5rem;
54  font-size: 0.75rem;
55  color: #fff;
56  transform: translateX(-50%);
57}

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Gooey Nav

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/GooeyNav-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import GooeyNav from './GooeyNav'
2
3// update with your own items
4const items = [
5  { label: "Home", href: "#" },
6  { label: "About", href: "#" },
7  { label: "Contact", href: "#" },
8];
9
10<div style={{ height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
11  <GooeyNav
12    items={items}
13    particleCount={15}
14    particleDistances={[90, 10]}
15    particleR={100}
16    initialActiveIndex={0}
17    animationTime={600}
18    timeVariance={300}
19    colors={[1, 2, 3, 1, 2, 3, 1, 4]}
20  />
21</div>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
2import './GooeyNav.css';
3
4const GooeyNav = ({
5  items,
6  animationTime = 600,
7  particleCount = 15,
8  particleDistances = [90, 10],
9  particleR = 100,
10  timeVariance = 300,
11  colors = [1, 2, 3, 1, 2, 3, 1, 4],
12  initialActiveIndex = 0
13}) => {
14  const containerRef = useRef(null);
15  const navRef = useRef(null);
16  const filterRef = useRef(null);
17  const textRef = useRef(null);
18  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(initialActiveIndex);
19
20  const noise = (n = 1) => n / 2 - Math.random() * n;
21
22  const getXY = (distance, pointIndex, totalPoints) => {
23    const angle = ((360 + noise(8)) / totalPoints) * pointIndex * (Math.PI / 180);
24    return [distance * Math.cos(angle), distance * Math.sin(angle)];
25  };
26
27  const createParticle = (i, t, d, r) => {
28    let rotate = noise(r / 10);
29    return {
30      start: getXY(d[0], particleCount - i, particleCount),
31      end: getXY(d[1] + noise(7), particleCount - i, particleCount),
32      time: t,
33      scale: 1 + noise(0.2),
34      color: colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)],
35      rotate: rotate > 0 ? (rotate + r / 20) * 10 : (rotate - r / 20) * 10
36    };
37  };
38
39  const makeParticles = element => {
40    const d = particleDistances;
41    const r = particleR;
42    const bubbleTime = animationTime * 2 + timeVariance;
43    element.style.setProperty('--time', `${bubbleTime}ms`);
44
45    for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
46      const t = animationTime * 2 + noise(timeVariance * 2);
47      const p = createParticle(i, t, d, r);
48      element.classList.remove('active');
49
50      setTimeout(() => {
51        const particle = document.createElement('span');
52        const point = document.createElement('span');
53        particle.classList.add('particle');
54        particle.style.setProperty('--start-x', `${p.start[0]}px`);
55        particle.style.setProperty('--start-y', `${p.start[1]}px`);
56        particle.style.setProperty('--end-x', `${p.end[0]}px`);
57        particle.style.setProperty('--end-y', `${p.end[1]}px`);
58        particle.style.setProperty('--time', `${p.time}ms`);
59        particle.style.setProperty('--scale', `${p.scale}`);
60        particle.style.setProperty('--color', `var(--color-${p.color}, white)`);
61        particle.style.setProperty('--rotate', `${p.rotate}deg`);
62
63        point.classList.add('point');
64        particle.appendChild(point);
65        element.appendChild(particle);
66        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
67          element.classList.add('active');
68        });
69        setTimeout(() => {
70          try {
71            element.removeChild(particle);
72          } catch {
73            // Do nothing
74          }
75        }, t);
76      }, 30);
77    }
78  };
79
80  const updateEffectPosition = element => {
81    if (!containerRef.current || !filterRef.current || !textRef.current) return;
82    const containerRect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
83    const pos = element.getBoundingClientRect();
84
85    const styles = {
86      left: `${pos.x - containerRect.x}px`,
87      top: `${pos.y - containerRect.y}px`,
88      width: `${pos.width}px`,
89      height: `${pos.height}px`
90    };
91    Object.assign(filterRef.current.style, styles);
92    Object.assign(textRef.current.style, styles);
93    textRef.current.innerText = element.innerText;
94  };
95
96  const handleClick = (e, index) => {
97    const liEl = e.currentTarget;
98    if (activeIndex === index) return;
99
100    setActiveIndex(index);
101    updateEffectPosition(liEl);
102
103    if (filterRef.current) {
104      const particles = filterRef.current.querySelectorAll('.particle');
105      particles.forEach(p => filterRef.current.removeChild(p));
106    }
107
108    if (textRef.current) {
109      textRef.current.classList.remove('active');
110
111      void textRef.current.offsetWidth;
112      textRef.current.classList.add('active');
113    }
114
115    if (filterRef.current) {
116      makeParticles(filterRef.current);
117    }
118  };
119
120  const handleKeyDown = (e, index) => {
121    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
122      e.preventDefault();
123      const liEl = e.currentTarget.parentElement;
124      if (liEl) {
125        handleClick({ currentTarget: liEl }, index);
126      }
127    }
128  };
129
130  useEffect(() => {
131    if (!navRef.current || !containerRef.current) return;
132    const activeLi = navRef.current.querySelectorAll('li')[activeIndex];
133    if (activeLi) {
134      updateEffectPosition(activeLi);
135      textRef.current?.classList.add('active');
136    }
137
138    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(() => {
139      const currentActiveLi = navRef.current?.querySelectorAll('li')[activeIndex];
140      if (currentActiveLi) {
141        updateEffectPosition(currentActiveLi);
142      }
143    });
144
145    resizeObserver.observe(containerRef.current);
146    return () => resizeObserver.disconnect();
147  }, [activeIndex]);
148
149  return (
150    <div className="gooey-nav-container" ref={containerRef}>
151      <nav>
152        <ul ref={navRef}>
153          {items.map((item, index) => (
154            <li key={index} className={activeIndex === index ? 'active' : ''}>
155              <a href={item.href} onClick={e => handleClick(e, index)} onKeyDown={e => handleKeyDown(e, index)}>
156                {item.label}
157              </a>
158            </li>
159          ))}
160        </ul>
161      </nav>
162      <span className="effect filter" ref={filterRef} />
163      <span className="effect text" ref={textRef} />
164    </div>
165  );
166};
167
168export default GooeyNav;

Component: Pixel Card

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/PixelCard-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import PixelCard from './PixelCard';
2
3<PixelCard variant="pink">
4  // your card content (use position: absolute)
5</PixelCard>
6

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import './PixelCard.css';
3
4class Pixel {
5  constructor(canvas, context, x, y, color, speed, delay) {
6    this.width = canvas.width;
7    this.height = canvas.height;
8    this.ctx = context;
9    this.x = x;
10    this.y = y;
11    this.color = color;
12    this.speed = this.getRandomValue(0.1, 0.9) * speed;
13    this.size = 0;
14    this.sizeStep = Math.random() * 0.4;
15    this.minSize = 0.5;
16    this.maxSizeInteger = 2;
17    this.maxSize = this.getRandomValue(this.minSize, this.maxSizeInteger);
18    this.delay = delay;
19    this.counter = 0;
20    this.counterStep = Math.random() * 4 + (this.width + this.height) * 0.01;
21    this.isIdle = false;
22    this.isReverse = false;
23    this.isShimmer = false;
24  }
25
26  getRandomValue(min, max) {
27    return Math.random() * (max - min) + min;
28  }
29
30  draw() {
31    const centerOffset = this.maxSizeInteger * 0.5 - this.size * 0.5;
32    this.ctx.fillStyle = this.color;
33    this.ctx.fillRect(this.x + centerOffset, this.y + centerOffset, this.size, this.size);
34  }
35
36  appear() {
37    this.isIdle = false;
38    if (this.counter <= this.delay) {
39      this.counter += this.counterStep;
40      return;
41    }
42    if (this.size >= this.maxSize) {
43      this.isShimmer = true;
44    }
45    if (this.isShimmer) {
46      this.shimmer();
47    } else {
48      this.size += this.sizeStep;
49    }
50    this.draw();
51  }
52
53  disappear() {
54    this.isShimmer = false;
55    this.counter = 0;
56    if (this.size <= 0) {
57      this.isIdle = true;
58      return;
59    } else {
60      this.size -= 0.1;
61    }
62    this.draw();
63  }
64
65  shimmer() {
66    if (this.size >= this.maxSize) {
67      this.isReverse = true;
68    } else if (this.size <= this.minSize) {
69      this.isReverse = false;
70    }
71    if (this.isReverse) {
72      this.size -= this.speed;
73    } else {
74      this.size += this.speed;
75    }
76  }
77}
78
79function getEffectiveSpeed(value, reducedMotion) {
80  const min = 0;
81  const max = 100;
82  const throttle = 0.001;
83  const parsed = parseInt(value, 10);
84
85  if (parsed <= min || reducedMotion) {
86    return min;
87  } else if (parsed >= max) {
88    return max * throttle;
89  } else {
90    return parsed * throttle;
91  }
92}
93
94const VARIANTS = {
95  default: {
96    activeColor: null,
97    gap: 5,
98    speed: 35,
99    colors: '#f8fafc,#f1f5f9,#cbd5e1',
100    noFocus: false
101  },
102  blue: {
103    activeColor: '#e0f2fe',
104    gap: 10,
105    speed: 25,
106    colors: '#e0f2fe,#7dd3fc,#0ea5e9',
107    noFocus: false
108  },
109  yellow: {
110    activeColor: '#fef08a',
111    gap: 3,
112    speed: 20,
113    colors: '#fef08a,#fde047,#eab308',
114    noFocus: false
115  },
116  pink: {
117    activeColor: '#fecdd3',
118    gap: 6,
119    speed: 80,
120    colors: '#fecdd3,#fda4af,#e11d48',
121    noFocus: true
122  }
123};
124
125export default function PixelCard({ variant = 'default', gap, speed, colors, noFocus, className = '', children }) {
126  const containerRef = useRef(null);
127  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
128  const pixelsRef = useRef([]);
129  const animationRef = useRef(null);
130  const timePreviousRef = useRef(performance.now());
131  const reducedMotion = useRef(window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches).current;
132
133  const variantCfg = VARIANTS[variant] || VARIANTS.default;
134  const finalGap = gap ?? variantCfg.gap;
135  const finalSpeed = speed ?? variantCfg.speed;
136  const finalColors = colors ?? variantCfg.colors;
137  const finalNoFocus = noFocus ?? variantCfg.noFocus;
138
139  const initPixels = () => {
140    if (!containerRef.current || !canvasRef.current) return;
141
142    const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
143    const width = Math.floor(rect.width);
144    const height = Math.floor(rect.height);
145    const ctx = canvasRef.current.getContext('2d');
146
147    canvasRef.current.width = width;
148    canvasRef.current.height = height;
149    canvasRef.current.style.width = `${width}px`;
150    canvasRef.current.style.height = `${height}px`;
151
152    const colorsArray = finalColors.split(',');
153    const pxs = [];
154    for (let x = 0; x < width; x += parseInt(finalGap, 10)) {
155      for (let y = 0; y < height; y += parseInt(finalGap, 10)) {
156        const color = colorsArray[Math.floor(Math.random() * colorsArray.length)];
157
158        const dx = x - width / 2;
159        const dy = y - height / 2;
160        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
161        const delay = reducedMotion ? 0 : distance;
162
163        pxs.push(new Pixel(canvasRef.current, ctx, x, y, color, getEffectiveSpeed(finalSpeed, reducedMotion), delay));
164      }
165    }
166    pixelsRef.current = pxs;
167  };
168
169  const doAnimate = fnName => {
170    animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(() => doAnimate(fnName));
171    const timeNow = performance.now();
172    const timePassed = timeNow - timePreviousRef.current;
173    const timeInterval = 1000 / 60;
174
175    if (timePassed < timeInterval) return;
176    timePreviousRef.current = timeNow - (timePassed % timeInterval);
177
178    const ctx = canvasRef.current?.getContext('2d');
179    if (!ctx || !canvasRef.current) return;
180
181    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvasRef.current.width, canvasRef.current.height);
182
183    let allIdle = true;
184    for (let i = 0; i < pixelsRef.current.length; i++) {
185      const pixel = pixelsRef.current[i];
186      pixel[fnName]();
187      if (!pixel.isIdle) {
188        allIdle = false;
189      }
190    }
191    if (allIdle) {
192      cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
193    }
194  };
195
196  const handleAnimation = name => {
197    cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
198    animationRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(() => doAnimate(name));
199  };
200
201  const onMouseEnter = () => handleAnimation('appear');
202  const onMouseLeave = () => handleAnimation('disappear');
203  const onFocus = e => {
204    if (e.currentTarget.contains(e.relatedTarget)) return;
205    handleAnimation('appear');
206  };
207  const onBlur = e => {
208    if (e.currentTarget.contains(e.relatedTarget)) return;
209    handleAnimation('disappear');
210  };
211
212  useEffect(() => {
213    initPixels();
214    const observer = new ResizeObserver(() => {
215      initPixels();
216    });
217    if (containerRef.current) {
218      observer.observe(containerRef.current);
219    }
220    return () => {
221      observer.disconnect();
222      cancelAnimationFrame(animationRef.current);
223    };
224    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
225  }, [finalGap, finalSpeed, finalColors, finalNoFocus]);
226
227  return (
228    <div
229      ref={containerRef}
230      className={`pixel-card ${className}`}
231      onMouseEnter={onMouseEnter}
232      onMouseLeave={onMouseLeave}
233      onFocus={finalNoFocus ? undefined : onFocus}
234      onBlur={finalNoFocus ? undefined : onBlur}
235      tabIndex={finalNoFocus ? -1 : 0}
236    >
237      <canvas className="pixel-canvas" ref={canvasRef} />
238      {children}
239    </div>
240  );
241}
242

Component: Carousel

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Carousel-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Carousel from './Carousel'
2
3<div style={{ height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
4  <Carousel
5    baseWidth={300}
6    autoplay={false}
7    autoplayDelay={3000}
8    pauseOnHover={false}
9    loop={false}
10    round={false}
11  />
12</div>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2import { motion, useMotionValue, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
3// replace icons with your own if needed
4import { FiCircle, FiCode, FiFileText, FiLayers, FiLayout } from 'react-icons/fi';
5
6import './Carousel.css';
7
8const DEFAULT_ITEMS = [
9  {
10    title: 'Text Animations',
11    description: 'Cool text animations for your projects.',
12    id: 1,
13    icon: <FiFileText className="carousel-icon" />
14  },
15  {
16    title: 'Animations',
17    description: 'Smooth animations for your projects.',
18    id: 2,
19    icon: <FiCircle className="carousel-icon" />
20  },
21  {
22    title: 'Components',
23    description: 'Reusable components for your projects.',
24    id: 3,
25    icon: <FiLayers className="carousel-icon" />
26  },
27  {
28    title: 'Backgrounds',
29    description: 'Beautiful backgrounds and patterns for your projects.',
30    id: 4,
31    icon: <FiLayout className="carousel-icon" />
32  },
33  {
34    title: 'Common UI',
35    description: 'Common UI components are coming soon!',
36    id: 5,
37    icon: <FiCode className="carousel-icon" />
38  }
39];
40
41const DRAG_BUFFER = 0;
42const VELOCITY_THRESHOLD = 500;
43const GAP = 16;
44const SPRING_OPTIONS = { type: 'spring', stiffness: 300, damping: 30 };
45
46function CarouselItem({ item, index, itemWidth, round, trackItemOffset, x, transition }) {
47  const range = [-(index + 1) * trackItemOffset, -index * trackItemOffset, -(index - 1) * trackItemOffset];
48  const outputRange = [90, 0, -90];
49  const rotateY = useTransform(x, range, outputRange, { clamp: false });
50
51  return (
52    <motion.div
53      key={`${item?.id ?? index}-${index}`}
54      className={`carousel-item ${round ? 'round' : ''}`}
55      style={{
56        width: itemWidth,
57        height: round ? itemWidth : '100%',
58        rotateY: rotateY,
59        ...(round && { borderRadius: '50%' })
60      }}
61      transition={transition}
62    >
63      <div className={`carousel-item-header ${round ? 'round' : ''}`}>
64        <span className="carousel-icon-container">{item.icon}</span>
65      </div>
66      <div className="carousel-item-content">
67        <div className="carousel-item-title">{item.title}</div>
68        <p className="carousel-item-description">{item.description}</p>
69      </div>
70    </motion.div>
71  );
72}
73
74export default function Carousel({
75  items = DEFAULT_ITEMS,
76  baseWidth = 300,
77  autoplay = false,
78  autoplayDelay = 3000,
79  pauseOnHover = false,
80  loop = false,
81  round = false
82}) {
83  const containerPadding = 16;
84  const itemWidth = baseWidth - containerPadding * 2;
85  const trackItemOffset = itemWidth + GAP;
86  const itemsForRender = useMemo(() => {
87    if (!loop) return items;
88    if (items.length === 0) return [];
89    return [items[items.length - 1], ...items, items[0]];
90  }, [items, loop]);
91
92  const [position, setPosition] = useState(loop ? 1 : 0);
93  const x = useMotionValue(0);
94  const [isHovered, setIsHovered] = useState(false);
95  const [isJumping, setIsJumping] = useState(false);
96  const [isAnimating, setIsAnimating] = useState(false);
97
98  const containerRef = useRef(null);
99  useEffect(() => {
100    if (pauseOnHover && containerRef.current) {
101      const container = containerRef.current;
102      const handleMouseEnter = () => setIsHovered(true);
103      const handleMouseLeave = () => setIsHovered(false);
104      container.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
105      container.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
106      return () => {
107        container.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
108        container.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
109      };
110    }
111  }, [pauseOnHover]);
112
113  useEffect(() => {
114    if (!autoplay || itemsForRender.length <= 1) return undefined;
115    if (pauseOnHover && isHovered) return undefined;
116
117    const timer = setInterval(() => {
118      setPosition(prev => Math.min(prev + 1, itemsForRender.length - 1));
119    }, autoplayDelay);
120
121    return () => clearInterval(timer);
122  }, [autoplay, autoplayDelay, isHovered, pauseOnHover, itemsForRender.length]);
123
124  useEffect(() => {
125    const startingPosition = loop ? 1 : 0;
126    setPosition(startingPosition);
127    x.set(-startingPosition * trackItemOffset);
128  }, [items.length, loop, trackItemOffset, x]);
129
130  useEffect(() => {
131    if (!loop && position > itemsForRender.length - 1) {
132      setPosition(Math.max(0, itemsForRender.length - 1));
133    }
134  }, [itemsForRender.length, loop, position]);
135
136  const effectiveTransition = isJumping ? { duration: 0 } : SPRING_OPTIONS;
137
138  const handleAnimationStart = () => {
139    setIsAnimating(true);
140  };
141
142  const handleAnimationComplete = () => {
143    if (!loop || itemsForRender.length <= 1) {
144      setIsAnimating(false);
145      return;
146    }
147    const lastCloneIndex = itemsForRender.length - 1;
148
149    if (position === lastCloneIndex) {
150      setIsJumping(true);
151      const target = 1;
152      setPosition(target);
153      x.set(-target * trackItemOffset);
154      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
155        setIsJumping(false);
156        setIsAnimating(false);
157      });
158      return;
159    }
160
161    if (position === 0) {
162      setIsJumping(true);
163      const target = items.length;
164      setPosition(target);
165      x.set(-target * trackItemOffset);
166      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
167        setIsJumping(false);
168        setIsAnimating(false);
169      });
170      return;
171    }
172
173    setIsAnimating(false);
174  };
175
176  const handleDragEnd = (_, info) => {
177    const { offset, velocity } = info;
178    const direction =
179      offset.x < -DRAG_BUFFER || velocity.x < -VELOCITY_THRESHOLD
180        ? 1
181        : offset.x > DRAG_BUFFER || velocity.x > VELOCITY_THRESHOLD
182          ? -1
183          : 0;
184
185    if (direction === 0) return;
186
187    setPosition(prev => {
188      const next = prev + direction;
189      const max = itemsForRender.length - 1;
190      return Math.max(0, Math.min(next, max));
191    });
192  };
193
194  const dragProps = loop
195    ? {}
196    : {
197        dragConstraints: {
198          left: -trackItemOffset * Math.max(itemsForRender.length - 1, 0),
199          right: 0
200        }
201      };
202
203  const activeIndex =
204    items.length === 0 ? 0 : loop ? (position - 1 + items.length) % items.length : Math.min(position, items.length - 1);
205
206  return (
207    <div
208      ref={containerRef}
209      className={`carousel-container ${round ? 'round' : ''}`}
210      style={{
211        width: `${baseWidth}px`,
212        ...(round && { height: `${baseWidth}px`, borderRadius: '50%' })
213      }}
214    >
215      <motion.div
216        className="carousel-track"
217        drag={isAnimating ? false : 'x'}
218        {...dragProps}
219        style={{
220          width: itemWidth,
221          gap: `${GAP}px`,
222          perspective: 1000,
223          perspectiveOrigin: `${position * trackItemOffset + itemWidth / 2}px 50%`,
224          x
225        }}
226        onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}
227        animate={{ x: -(position * trackItemOffset) }}
228        transition={effectiveTransition}
229        onAnimationStart={handleAnimationStart}
230        onAnimationComplete={handleAnimationComplete}
231      >
232        {itemsForRender.map((item, index) => (
233          <CarouselItem
234            key={`${item?.id ?? index}-${index}`}
235            item={item}
236            index={index}
237            itemWidth={itemWidth}
238            round={round}
239            trackItemOffset={trackItemOffset}
240            x={x}
241            transition={effectiveTransition}
242          />
243        ))}
244      </motion.div>
245      <div className={`carousel-indicators-container ${round ? 'round' : ''}`}>
246        <div className="carousel-indicators">
247          {items.map((_, index) => (
248            <motion.div
249              key={index}
250              className={`carousel-indicator ${activeIndex === index ? 'active' : 'inactive'}`}
251              animate={{
252                scale: activeIndex === index ? 1.2 : 1
253              }}
254              onClick={() => setPosition(loop ? index + 1 : index)}
255              transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
256            />
257          ))}
258        </div>
259      </div>
260    </div>
261  );
262}
263

Component: Spotlight Card

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/SpotlightCard-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import SpotlightCard from './SpotlightCard';
2  
3<SpotlightCard className="custom-spotlight-card" spotlightColor="rgba(0, 229, 255, 0.2)">
4  // Content goes here
5</SpotlightCard>

Code:
1import { useRef } from 'react';
2import './SpotlightCard.css';
3
4const SpotlightCard = ({ children, className = '', spotlightColor = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25)' }) => {
5  const divRef = useRef(null);
6
7  const handleMouseMove = e => {
8    const rect = divRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
9    const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
10    const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
11
12    divRef.current.style.setProperty('--mouse-x', `${x}px`);
13    divRef.current.style.setProperty('--mouse-y', `${y}px`);
14    divRef.current.style.setProperty('--spotlight-color', spotlightColor);
15  };
16
17  return (
18    <div ref={divRef} onMouseMove={handleMouseMove} className={`card-spotlight ${className}`}>
19      {children}
20    </div>
21  );
22};
23
24export default SpotlightCard;
25

9  --mouse-y: 50%;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Card Swap

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/CardSwap-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import CardSwap, { Card } from './CardSwap'
2
3<div style={{ height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
4  <CardSwap
5    cardDistance={60}
6    verticalDistance={70}
7    delay={5000}
8    pauseOnHover={false}
9  >
10    <Card>
11      <h3>Card 1</h3>
12      <p>Your content here</p>
13    </Card>
14    <Card>
15      <h3>Card 2</h3>
16      <p>Your content here</p>
17    </Card>
18    <Card>
19      <h3>Card 3</h3>
20      <p>Your content here</p>
21    </Card>
22  </CardSwap>
23</div>

Code:
1import React, { Children, cloneElement, forwardRef, isValidElement, useEffect, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';
2import gsap from 'gsap';
3import './CardSwap.css';
4
5export const Card = forwardRef(({ customClass, ...rest }, ref) => (
6  <div ref={ref} {...rest} className={`card ${customClass ?? ''} ${rest.className ?? ''}`.trim()} />
7));
8Card.displayName = 'Card';
9
10const makeSlot = (i, distX, distY, total) => ({
11  x: i * distX,
12  y: -i * distY,
13  z: -i * distX * 1.5,
14  zIndex: total - i
15});
16const placeNow = (el, slot, skew) =>
17  gsap.set(el, {
18    x: slot.x,
19    y: slot.y,
20    z: slot.z,
21    xPercent: -50,
22    yPercent: -50,
23    skewY: skew,
24    transformOrigin: 'center center',
25    zIndex: slot.zIndex,
26    force3D: true
27  });
28
29const CardSwap = ({
30  width = 500,
31  height = 400,
32  cardDistance = 60,
33  verticalDistance = 70,
34  delay = 5000,
35  pauseOnHover = false,
36  onCardClick,
37  skewAmount = 6,
38  easing = 'elastic',
39  children
40}) => {
41  const config =
42    easing === 'elastic'
43      ? {
44          ease: 'elastic.out(0.6,0.9)',
45          durDrop: 2,
46          durMove: 2,
47          durReturn: 2,
48          promoteOverlap: 0.9,
49          returnDelay: 0.05
50        }
51      : {
52          ease: 'power1.inOut',
53          durDrop: 0.8,
54          durMove: 0.8,
55          durReturn: 0.8,
56          promoteOverlap: 0.45,
57          returnDelay: 0.2
58        };
59
60  const childArr = useMemo(() => Children.toArray(children), [children]);
61  const refs = useMemo(
62    () => childArr.map(() => React.createRef()),
63    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
64    [childArr.length]
65  );
66
67  const order = useRef(Array.from({ length: childArr.length }, (_, i) => i));
68
69  const tlRef = useRef(null);
70  const intervalRef = useRef();
71  const container = useRef(null);
72
73  useEffect(() => {
74    const total = refs.length;
75    refs.forEach((r, i) => placeNow(r.current, makeSlot(i, cardDistance, verticalDistance, total), skewAmount));
76
77    const swap = () => {
78      if (order.current.length < 2) return;
79
80      const [front, ...rest] = order.current;
81      const elFront = refs[front].current;
82      const tl = gsap.timeline();
83      tlRef.current = tl;
84
85      tl.to(elFront, {
86        y: '+=500',
87        duration: config.durDrop,
88        ease: config.ease
89      });
90
91      tl.addLabel('promote', `-=${config.durDrop * config.promoteOverlap}`);
92      rest.forEach((idx, i) => {
93        const el = refs[idx].current;
94        const slot = makeSlot(i, cardDistance, verticalDistance, refs.length);
95        tl.set(el, { zIndex: slot.zIndex }, 'promote');
96        tl.to(
97          el,
98          {
99            x: slot.x,
100            y: slot.y,
101            z: slot.z,
102            duration: config.durMove,
103            ease: config.ease
104          },
105          `promote+=${i * 0.15}`
106        );
107      });
108
109      const backSlot = makeSlot(refs.length - 1, cardDistance, verticalDistance, refs.length);
110      tl.addLabel('return', `promote+=${config.durMove * config.returnDelay}`);
111      tl.call(
112        () => {
113          gsap.set(elFront, { zIndex: backSlot.zIndex });
114        },
115        undefined,
116        'return'
117      );
118      tl.to(
119        elFront,
120        {
121          x: backSlot.x,
122          y: backSlot.y,
123          z: backSlot.z,
124          duration: config.durReturn,
125          ease: config.ease
126        },
127        'return'
128      );
129
130      tl.call(() => {
131        order.current = [...rest, front];
132      });
133    };
134
135    swap();
136    intervalRef.current = window.setInterval(swap, delay);
137
138    if (pauseOnHover) {
139      const node = container.current;
140      const pause = () => {
141        tlRef.current?.pause();
142        clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
143      };
144      const resume = () => {
145        tlRef.current?.play();
146        intervalRef.current = window.setInterval(swap, delay);
147      };
148      node.addEventListener('mouseenter', pause);
149      node.addEventListener('mouseleave', resume);
150      return () => {
151        node.removeEventListener('mouseenter', pause);
152        node.removeEventListener('mouseleave', resume);
153        clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
154      };
155    }
156    return () => clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
157    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
158  }, [cardDistance, verticalDistance, delay, pauseOnHover, skewAmount, easing]);
159
160  const rendered = childArr.map((child, i) =>
161    isValidElement(child)
162      ? cloneElement(child, {
163          key: i,
164          ref: refs[i],
165          style: { width, height, ...(child.props.style ?? {}) },
166          onClick: e => {
167            child.props.onClick?.(e);
168            onCardClick?.(i);
169          }
170        })
171      : child
172  );
173
174  return (
175    <div ref={container} className="card-swap-container" style={{ width, height }}>
176      {rendered}
177    </div>
178  );
179};
180
181export default CardSwap;
182

Extra Config/Code:

2  position: absolute;
3  bottom: 0;
4  right: 0;
5  transform: translate(5%, 20%);
6  transform-origin: bottom right;
7
8  perspective: 900px;
9  overflow: visible;
10}
11
12.card {
13  position: absolute;
14  top: 50%;
15  left: 50%;
16  border-radius: 12px;
17  border: 1px solid #fff;
18  background: #000;
19
20  transform-style: preserve-3d;
21  will-change: transform;
22  backface-visibility: hidden;
23  -webkit-backface-visibility: hidden;
24}
25
26@media (max-width: 768px) {
27  .card-swap-container {
28    transform: scale(0.75) translate(25%, 25%);
29  }
30}
31
32@media (max-width: 480px) {
33  .card-swap-container {
34    transform: scale(0.55) translate(25%, 25%);
35  }

Code:
1import './GlassIcons.css';
2
3const gradientMapping = {
4  blue: 'linear-gradient(hsl(223, 90%, 50%), hsl(208, 90%, 50%))',
5  purple: 'linear-gradient(hsl(283, 90%, 50%), hsl(268, 90%, 50%))',
6  red: 'linear-gradient(hsl(3, 90%, 50%), hsl(348, 90%, 50%))',
7  indigo: 'linear-gradient(hsl(253, 90%, 50%), hsl(238, 90%, 50%))',
8  orange: 'linear-gradient(hsl(43, 90%, 50%), hsl(28, 90%, 50%))',
9  green: 'linear-gradient(hsl(123, 90%, 40%), hsl(108, 90%, 40%))'
10};
11
12const GlassIcons = ({ items, className }) => {
13  const getBackgroundStyle = color => {
14    if (gradientMapping[color]) {
15      return { background: gradientMapping[color] };
16    }
17    return { background: color };
18  };
19
20  return (
21    <div className={`icon-btns ${className || ''}`}>
22      {items.map((item, index) => (
23        <button key={index} className={`icon-btn ${item.customClass || ''}`} aria-label={item.label} type="button">
24          <span className="icon-btn__back" style={getBackgroundStyle(item.color)}></span>
25          <span className="icon-btn__front">
26            <span className="icon-btn__icon" aria-hidden="true">
27              {item.icon}
28            </span>
29          </span>
30          <span className="icon-btn__label">{item.label}</span>
31        </button>
32      ))}
33    </div>
34  );
35};
36
37export default GlassIcons;
