--------------------------------------------------

Component: Decay Card

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/DecayCard-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import DecayCard from './DecayCard';
2
3<DecayCard width={200} height={300} image="https://picsum.photos/300/400?grayscale">
4  <h2>Decay<br/>Card</h2>
5</DecayCard>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import { gsap } from 'gsap';
3
4import './DecayCard.css';
5
6const DecayCard = ({ width = 300, height = 400, image = 'https://picsum.photos/300/400?grayscale', children }) => {
7  const svgRef = useRef(null);
8  const displacementMapRef = useRef(null);
9  const cursor = useRef({ x: window.innerWidth / 2, y: window.innerHeight / 2 });
10  const cachedCursor = useRef({ ...cursor.current });
11  const winsize = useRef({ width: window.innerWidth, height: window.innerHeight });
12
13  useEffect(() => {
14    const lerp = (a, b, n) => (1 - n) * a + n * b;
15
16    const map = (x, a, b, c, d) => ((x - a) * (d - c)) / (b - a) + c;
17
18    const distance = (x1, x2, y1, y2) => {
19      const a = x1 - x2;
20      const b = y1 - y2;
21      return Math.hypot(a, b);
22    };
23
24    const handleResize = () => {
25      winsize.current = { width: window.innerWidth, height: window.innerHeight };
26    };
27
28    const handleMouseMove = ev => {
29      cursor.current = { x: ev.clientX, y: ev.clientY };
30    };
31
32    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
33    window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
34
35    const imgValues = {
36      imgTransforms: { x: 0, y: 0, rz: 0 },
37      displacementScale: 0
38    };
39
40    const render = () => {
41      let targetX = lerp(imgValues.imgTransforms.x, map(cursor.current.x, 0, winsize.current.width, -120, 120), 0.1);
42      let targetY = lerp(imgValues.imgTransforms.y, map(cursor.current.y, 0, winsize.current.height, -120, 120), 0.1);
43      let targetRz = lerp(imgValues.imgTransforms.rz, map(cursor.current.x, 0, winsize.current.width, -10, 10), 0.1);
44
45      const bound = 50;
46
47      if (targetX > bound) targetX = bound + (targetX - bound) * 0.2;
48      if (targetX < -bound) targetX = -bound + (targetX + bound) * 0.2;
49      if (targetY > bound) targetY = bound + (targetY - bound) * 0.2;
50      if (targetY < -bound) targetY = -bound + (targetY + bound) * 0.2;
51
52      imgValues.imgTransforms.x = targetX;
53      imgValues.imgTransforms.y = targetY;
54      imgValues.imgTransforms.rz = targetRz;
55
56      if (svgRef.current) {
57        gsap.set(svgRef.current, {
58          x: imgValues.imgTransforms.x,
59          y: imgValues.imgTransforms.y,
60          rotateZ: imgValues.imgTransforms.rz
61        });
62      }
63
64      const cursorTravelledDistance = distance(
65        cachedCursor.current.x,
66        cursor.current.x,
67        cachedCursor.current.y,
68        cursor.current.y
69      );
70      imgValues.displacementScale = lerp(
71        imgValues.displacementScale,
72        map(cursorTravelledDistance, 0, 200, 0, 400),
73        0.06
74      );
75
76      if (displacementMapRef.current) {
77        gsap.set(displacementMapRef.current, { attr: { scale: imgValues.displacementScale } });
78      }
79
80      cachedCursor.current = { ...cursor.current };
81
82      requestAnimationFrame(render);
83    };
84
85    render();
86
87    return () => {
88      window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
89      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
90    };
91  }, []);
92
93  return (
94    <div className="content" style={{ width: `${width}px`, height: `${height}px` }} ref={svgRef}>
95      <svg viewBox="-60 -75 720 900" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid slice" className="svg">
96        <filter id="imgFilter">
97          <feTurbulence
98            type="turbulence"
99            baseFrequency="0.015"
100            numOctaves="5"
101            seed="4"
102            stitchTiles="stitch"
103            x="0%"
104            y="0%"
105            width="100%"
106            height="100%"
107            result="turbulence1"
108          />
109          <feDisplacementMap
110            ref={displacementMapRef}
111            in="SourceGraphic"
112            in2="turbulence1"
113            scale="0"
114            xChannelSelector="R"
115            yChannelSelector="B"
116            x="0%"
117            y="0%"
118            width="100%"
119            height="100%"
120            result="displacementMap3"
121          />
122        </filter>
123        <g>
124          <image
125            href={image}
126            x="0"
127            y="0"
128            width="600"
129            height="750"
130            filter="url(#imgFilter)"
131            preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid slice"
132          />
133        </g>
134      </svg>
135      <div className="card-text">{children}</div>
136    </div>
137  );
138};
139
140export default DecayCard;
141

Component: Elastic Slider

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ElasticSlider-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import ElasticSlider from './ElasticSlider'
2  
3<ElasticSlider
4  leftIcon={<>...your icon...</>}
5  rightIcon={<>...your icon...</>}
6  startingValue={0}
7  defaultValue={50}
8  maxValue={100}
9  isStepped={false}
10  stepSize={1}
11/>

Code:
1import { animate, motion, useMotionValue, useMotionValueEvent, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
2import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
3import { Icon } from '@chakra-ui/react';
4import { RiVolumeDownFill, RiVolumeUpFill } from 'react-icons/ri';
5
6import './ElasticSlider.css';
7
8const MAX_OVERFLOW = 50;
9
10export default function ElasticSlider({
11  defaultValue = 50,
12  startingValue = 0,
13  maxValue = 100,
14  className = '',
15  isStepped = false,
16  stepSize = 1,
17  leftIcon = <Icon as={RiVolumeDownFill} />,
18  rightIcon = <Icon as={RiVolumeUpFill} />
19}) {
20  return (
21    <div className={`slider-container ${className}`}>
22      <Slider
23        defaultValue={defaultValue}
24        startingValue={startingValue}
25        maxValue={maxValue}
26        isStepped={isStepped}
27        stepSize={stepSize}
28        leftIcon={leftIcon}
29        rightIcon={rightIcon}
30      />
31    </div>
32  );
33}
34
35function Slider({ defaultValue, startingValue, maxValue, isStepped, stepSize, leftIcon, rightIcon }) {
36  const [value, setValue] = useState(defaultValue);
37  const sliderRef = useRef(null);
38  const [region, setRegion] = useState('middle');
39  const clientX = useMotionValue(0);
40  const overflow = useMotionValue(0);
41  const scale = useMotionValue(1);
42
43  useEffect(() => {
44    setValue(defaultValue);
45  }, [defaultValue]);
46
47  useMotionValueEvent(clientX, 'change', latest => {
48    if (sliderRef.current) {
49      const { left, right } = sliderRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
50      let newValue;
51
52      if (latest < left) {
53        setRegion('left');
54        newValue = left - latest;
55      } else if (latest > right) {
56        setRegion('right');
57        newValue = latest - right;
58      } else {
59        setRegion('middle');
60        newValue = 0;
61      }
62
63      overflow.jump(decay(newValue, MAX_OVERFLOW));
64    }
65  });
66
67  const handlePointerMove = e => {
68    if (e.buttons > 0 && sliderRef.current) {
69      const { left, width } = sliderRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
70      let newValue = startingValue + ((e.clientX - left) / width) * (maxValue - startingValue);
71
72      if (isStepped) {
73        newValue = Math.round(newValue / stepSize) * stepSize;
74      }
75
76      newValue = Math.min(Math.max(newValue, startingValue), maxValue);
77      setValue(newValue);
78      clientX.jump(e.clientX);
79    }
80  };
81
82  const handlePointerDown = e => {
83    handlePointerMove(e);
84    e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
85  };
86
87  const handlePointerUp = () => {
88    animate(overflow, 0, { type: 'spring', bounce: 0.5 });
89  };
90
91  const getRangePercentage = () => {
92    const totalRange = maxValue - startingValue;
93    if (totalRange === 0) return 0;
94
95    return ((value - startingValue) / totalRange) * 100;
96  };
97
98  return (
99    <>
100      <motion.div
101        onHoverStart={() => animate(scale, 1.2)}
102        onHoverEnd={() => animate(scale, 1)}
103        onTouchStart={() => animate(scale, 1.2)}
104        onTouchEnd={() => animate(scale, 1)}
105        style={{
106          scale,
107          opacity: useTransform(scale, [1, 1.2], [0.7, 1])
108        }}
109        className="slider-wrapper"
110      >
111        <motion.div
112          animate={{
113            scale: region === 'left' ? [1, 1.4, 1] : 1,
114            transition: { duration: 0.25 }
115          }}
116          style={{
117            x: useTransform(() => (region === 'left' ? -overflow.get() / scale.get() : 0))
118          }}
119        >
120          {leftIcon}
121        </motion.div>
122
123        <div
124          ref={sliderRef}
125          className="slider-root"
126          onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
127          onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
128          onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
129        >
130          <motion.div
131            style={{
132              scaleX: useTransform(() => {
133                if (sliderRef.current) {
134                  const { width } = sliderRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
135                  return 1 + overflow.get() / width;
136                }
137              }),
138              scaleY: useTransform(overflow, [0, MAX_OVERFLOW], [1, 0.8]),
139              transformOrigin: useTransform(() => {
140                if (sliderRef.current) {
141                  const { left, width } = sliderRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
142                  return clientX.get() < left + width / 2 ? 'right' : 'left';
143                }
144              }),
145              height: useTransform(scale, [1, 1.2], [6, 12]),
146              marginTop: useTransform(scale, [1, 1.2], [0, -3]),
147              marginBottom: useTransform(scale, [1, 1.2], [0, -3])
148            }}
149            className="slider-track-wrapper"
150          >
151            <div className="slider-track">
152              <div className="slider-range" style={{ width: `${getRangePercentage()}%` }} />
153            </div>
154          </motion.div>
155        </div>
156
157        <motion.div
158          animate={{
159            scale: region === 'right' ? [1, 1.4, 1] : 1,
160            transition: { duration: 0.25 }
161          }}
162          style={{
163            x: useTransform(() => (region === 'right' ? overflow.get() / scale.get() : 0))
164          }}
165        >
166          {rightIcon}
167        </motion.div>
168      </motion.div>
169      <p className="value-indicator">{Math.round(value)}</p>
170    </>
171  );
172}
173
174function decay(value, max) {
175  if (max === 0) {
176    return 0;
177  }
178
179  const entry = value / max;
180  const sigmoid = 2 * (1 / (1 + Math.exp(-entry)) - 0.5);
181
182  return sigmoid * max;
183}
184

Component: Counter

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Counter-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Counter from './Counter';
2
3<Counter
4  value={1}
5  places={[100, 10, 1]}
6  fontSize={80}
7  padding={5}
8  gap={10}
9  textColor="white"
10  fontWeight={900}
11  digitPlaceHolders
12/>

Code:
1import { motion, useSpring, useTransform } from 'motion/react';
2import { useEffect } from 'react';
3
4import './Counter.css';
5
6function Number({ mv, number, height }) {
7  let y = useTransform(mv, latest => {
8    let placeValue = latest % 10;
9    let offset = (10 + number - placeValue) % 10;
10    let memo = offset * height;
11    if (offset > 5) {
12      memo -= 10 * height;
13    }
14    return memo;
15  });
16  return (
17    <motion.span className="counter-number" style={{ y }}>
18      {number}
19    </motion.span>
20  );
21}
22
23function normalizeNearInteger(num) {
24  const nearest = Math.round(num);
25  const tolerance = 1e-9 * Math.max(1, Math.abs(num));
26  return Math.abs(num - nearest) < tolerance ? nearest : num;
27}
28
29function getValueRoundedToPlace(value, place) {
30  const scaled = value / place;
31  return Math.floor(normalizeNearInteger(scaled));
32}
33
34function Digit({ place, value, height, digitStyle }) {
35  const isDecimal = place === '.';
36  const valueRoundedToPlace = isDecimal ? 0 : getValueRoundedToPlace(value, place);
37  const animatedValue = useSpring(valueRoundedToPlace);
38
39  useEffect(() => {
40    if (!isDecimal) {
41      animatedValue.set(valueRoundedToPlace);
42    }
43  }, [animatedValue, valueRoundedToPlace, isDecimal]);
44
45  if (isDecimal) {
46    return (
47      <span className="counter-digit" style={{ height, ...digitStyle, width: 'fit-content' }}>
48        .
49      </span>
50    );
51  }
52
53  return (
54    <span className="counter-digit" style={{ height, ...digitStyle }}>
55      {Array.from({ length: 10 }, (_, i) => (
56        <Number key={i} mv={animatedValue} number={i} height={height} />
57      ))}
58    </span>
59  );
60}
61
62export default function Counter({
63  value,
64  fontSize = 100,
65  padding = 0,
66  places = [...value.toString()].map((ch, i, a) => {
67    ch == '.';
68    if (ch === '.') {
69      return '.';
70    } else {
71      return (
72        10 **
73        (a.indexOf('.') === -1 ? a.length - i - 1 : i < a.indexOf('.') ? a.indexOf('.') - i - 1 : -(i - a.indexOf('.')))
74      );
75    }
76  }),
77  gap = 8,
78  borderRadius = 4,
79  horizontalPadding = 8,
80  textColor = 'inherit',
81  fontWeight = 'inherit',
82  containerStyle,
83  counterStyle,
84  digitStyle,
85  gradientHeight = 16,
86  gradientFrom = 'black',
87  gradientTo = 'transparent',
88  topGradientStyle,
89  bottomGradientStyle
90}) {
91  const height = fontSize + padding;
92  const defaultCounterStyle = {
93    fontSize,
94    gap: gap,
95    borderRadius: borderRadius,
96    paddingLeft: horizontalPadding,
97    paddingRight: horizontalPadding,
98    color: textColor,
99    fontWeight: fontWeight
100  };
101  const defaultTopGradientStyle = {
102    height: gradientHeight,
103    background: `linear-gradient(to bottom, ${gradientFrom}, ${gradientTo})`
104  };
105  const defaultBottomGradientStyle = {
106    height: gradientHeight,
107    background: `linear-gradient(to top, ${gradientFrom}, ${gradientTo})`
108  };
109  return (
110    <span className="counter-container" style={containerStyle}>
111      <span className="counter-counter" style={{ ...defaultCounterStyle, ...counterStyle }}>
112        {places.map(place => (
113          <Digit key={place} place={place} value={value} height={height} digitStyle={digitStyle} />
114        ))}
115      </span>
116      <span className="gradient-container">
117        <span className="top-gradient" style={topGradientStyle ? topGradientStyle : defaultTopGradientStyle}></span>
118        <span
119          className="bottom-gradient"
120          style={bottomGradientStyle ? bottomGradientStyle : defaultBottomGradientStyle}
121        ></span>
122      </span>
123    </span>
124  );
125}
126

Component: Stepper

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/Stepper-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import Stepper, { Step } from './Stepper';
2  
3<Stepper
4  initialStep={1}
5  onStepChange={(step) => {
6    console.log(step);
7  }}
8  onFinalStepCompleted={() => console.log("All steps completed!")}
9  backButtonText="Previous"
10  nextButtonText="Next"
11>
12  <Step>
13    <h2>Welcome to the React Bits stepper!</h2>
14    <p>Check out the next step!</p>
15  </Step>
16  <Step>
17    <h2>Step 2</h2>
18    <img style={{ height: '100px', width: '100%', objectFit: 'cover', objectPosition: 'center -70px', borderRadius: '15px', marginTop: '1em' }} src="https://www.purrfectcatgifts.co.uk/cdn/shop/collections/Funny_Cat_Cards_640x640.png?v=1663150894" />
19    <p>Custom step content!</p>
20  </Step>
21  <Step>
22    <h2>How about an input?</h2>
23    <input value={name} onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)} placeholder="Your name?" />
24  </Step>
25  <Step>
26    <h2>Final Step</h2>
27    <p>You made it!</p>
28  </Step>
29</Stepper>

Code:
1import React, { useState, Children, useRef, useLayoutEffect } from 'react';
2import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'motion/react';
3
4import './Stepper.css';
5
6export default function Stepper({
7  children,
8  initialStep = 1,
9  onStepChange = () => {},
10  onFinalStepCompleted = () => {},
11  stepCircleContainerClassName = '',
12  stepContainerClassName = '',
13  contentClassName = '',
14  footerClassName = '',
15  backButtonProps = {},
16  nextButtonProps = {},
17  backButtonText = 'Back',
18  nextButtonText = 'Continue',
19  disableStepIndicators = false,
20  renderStepIndicator,
21  ...rest
22}) {
23  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(initialStep);
24  const [direction, setDirection] = useState(0);
25  const stepsArray = Children.toArray(children);
26  const totalSteps = stepsArray.length;
27  const isCompleted = currentStep > totalSteps;
28  const isLastStep = currentStep === totalSteps;
29
30  const updateStep = newStep => {
31    setCurrentStep(newStep);
32    if (newStep > totalSteps) {
33      onFinalStepCompleted();
34    } else {
35      onStepChange(newStep);
36    }
37  };
38
39  const handleBack = () => {
40    if (currentStep > 1) {
41      setDirection(-1);
42      updateStep(currentStep - 1);
43    }
44  };
45
46  const handleNext = () => {
47    if (!isLastStep) {
48      setDirection(1);
49      updateStep(currentStep + 1);
50    }
51  };
52
53  const handleComplete = () => {
54    setDirection(1);
55    updateStep(totalSteps + 1);
56  };
57
58  return (
59    <div className="outer-container" {...rest}>
60      <div className={`step-circle-container ${stepCircleContainerClassName}`} style={{ border: '1px solid #222' }}>
61        <div className={`step-indicator-row ${stepContainerClassName}`}>
62          {stepsArray.map((_, index) => {
63            const stepNumber = index + 1;
64            const isNotLastStep = index < totalSteps - 1;
65            return (
66              <React.Fragment key={stepNumber}>
67                {renderStepIndicator ? (
68                  renderStepIndicator({
69                    step: stepNumber,
70                    currentStep,
71                    onStepClick: clicked => {
72                      setDirection(clicked > currentStep ? 1 : -1);
73                      updateStep(clicked);
74                    }
75                  })
76                ) : (
77                  <StepIndicator
78                    step={stepNumber}
79                    disableStepIndicators={disableStepIndicators}
80                    currentStep={currentStep}
81                    onClickStep={clicked => {
82                      setDirection(clicked > currentStep ? 1 : -1);
83                      updateStep(clicked);
84                    }}
85                  />
86                )}
87                {isNotLastStep && <StepConnector isComplete={currentStep > stepNumber} />}
88              </React.Fragment>
89            );
90          })}
91        </div>
92
93        <StepContentWrapper
94          isCompleted={isCompleted}
95          currentStep={currentStep}
96          direction={direction}
97          className={`step-content-default ${contentClassName}`}
98        >
99          {stepsArray[currentStep - 1]}
100        </StepContentWrapper>
101
102        {!isCompleted && (
103          <div className={`footer-container ${footerClassName}`}>
104            <div className={`footer-nav ${currentStep !== 1 ? 'spread' : 'end'}`}>
105              {currentStep !== 1 && (
106                <button
107                  onClick={handleBack}
108                  className={`back-button ${currentStep === 1 ? 'inactive' : ''}`}
109                  {...backButtonProps}
110                >
111                  {backButtonText}
112                </button>
113              )}
114              <button onClick={isLastStep ? handleComplete : handleNext} className="next-button" {...nextButtonProps}>
115                {isLastStep ? 'Complete' : nextButtonText}
116              </button>
117            </div>
118          </div>
119        )}
120      </div>
121    </div>
122  );
123}
124
125function StepContentWrapper({ isCompleted, currentStep, direction, children, className }) {
126  const [parentHeight, setParentHeight] = useState(0);
127
128  return (
129    <motion.div
130      className={className}
131      style={{ position: 'relative', overflow: 'hidden' }}
132      animate={{ height: isCompleted ? 0 : parentHeight }}
133      transition={{ type: 'spring', duration: 0.4 }}
134    >
135      <AnimatePresence initial={false} mode="sync" custom={direction}>
136        {!isCompleted && (
137          <SlideTransition key={currentStep} direction={direction} onHeightReady={h => setParentHeight(h)}>
138            {children}
139          </SlideTransition>
140        )}
141      </AnimatePresence>
142    </motion.div>
143  );
144}
145
146function SlideTransition({ children, direction, onHeightReady }) {
147  const containerRef = useRef(null);
148
149  useLayoutEffect(() => {
150    if (containerRef.current) onHeightReady(containerRef.current.offsetHeight);
151  }, [children, onHeightReady]);
152
153  return (
154    <motion.div
155      ref={containerRef}
156      custom={direction}
157      variants={stepVariants}
158      initial="enter"
159      animate="center"
160      exit="exit"
161      transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
162      style={{ position: 'absolute', left: 0, right: 0, top: 0 }}
163    >
164      {children}
165    </motion.div>
166  );
167}
168
169const stepVariants = {
170  enter: dir => ({
171    x: dir >= 0 ? '-100%' : '100%',
172    opacity: 0
173  }),
174  center: {
175    x: '0%',
176    opacity: 1
177  },
178  exit: dir => ({
179    x: dir >= 0 ? '50%' : '-50%',
180    opacity: 0
181  })
182};
183
184export function Step({ children }) {
185  return <div className="step-default">{children}</div>;
186}
187
188function StepIndicator({ step, currentStep, onClickStep, disableStepIndicators }) {
189  const status = currentStep === step ? 'active' : currentStep < step ? 'inactive' : 'complete';
190
191  const handleClick = () => {
192    if (step !== currentStep && !disableStepIndicators) onClickStep(step);
193  };
194
195  return (
196    <motion.div onClick={handleClick} className="step-indicator" animate={status} initial={false}>
197      <motion.div
198        variants={{
199          inactive: { scale: 1, backgroundColor: '#222', color: '#a3a3a3' },
200          active: { scale: 1, backgroundColor: '#5227FF', color: '#5227FF' },
201          complete: { scale: 1, backgroundColor: '#5227FF', color: '#3b82f6' }
202        }}
203        transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
204        className="step-indicator-inner"
205      >
206        {status === 'complete' ? (
207          <CheckIcon className="check-icon" />
208        ) : status === 'active' ? (
209          <div className="active-dot" />
210        ) : (
211          <span className="step-number">{step}</span>
212        )}
213      </motion.div>
214    </motion.div>
215  );
216}
217
218function StepConnector({ isComplete }) {
219  const lineVariants = {
220    incomplete: { width: 0, backgroundColor: 'transparent' },
221    complete: { width: '100%', backgroundColor: '#5227FF' }
222  };
223
224  return (
225    <div className="step-connector">
226      <motion.div
227        className="step-connector-inner"
228        variants={lineVariants}
229        initial={false}
230        animate={isComplete ? 'complete' : 'incomplete'}
231        transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
232      />
233    </div>
234  );
235}
236
237function CheckIcon(props) {
238  return (
239    <svg {...props} fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth={2} viewBox="0 0 24 24">
240      <motion.path
241        initial={{ pathLength: 0 }}
242        animate={{ pathLength: 1 }}
243        transition={{ delay: 0.1, type: 'tween', ease: 'easeOut', duration: 0.3 }}
244        strokeLinecap="round"
245        strokeLinejoin="round"
246        d="M5 13l4 4L19 7"
247      />
248    </svg>
249  );
250}

30vec3 hueShiftRGB(vec3 col,float deg){

56    buf[0]=sigmoid(buf[0]);
57    return vec4(buf[0].x,buf[0].y,buf[0].z,1.);
58}
59
60void mainImage(out vec4 fragColor,in vec2 fragCoord){
61    vec2 uv=fragCoord/uResolution.xy*2.-1.;
62    uv.y*=-1.;
63    uv+=uWarp*vec2(sin(uv.y*6.283+uTime*0.5),cos(uv.x*6.283+uTime*0.5))*0.05;
64    fragColor=cppn_fn(uv,0.1*sin(0.3*uTime),0.1*sin(0.69*uTime),0.1*sin(0.44*uTime));
65}
66
67void main(){
68    vec4 col;mainImage(col,gl_FragCoord.xy);
69    col.rgb=hueShiftRGB(col.rgb,uHueShift);
70    float scanline_val=sin(gl_FragCoord.y*uScanFreq)*0.5+0.5;
71    col.rgb*=1.-(scanline_val*scanline_val)*uScan;
72    col.rgb+=(rand(gl_FragCoord.xy+uTime)-0.5)*uNoise;
73    gl_FragColor=vec4(clamp(col.rgb,0.0,1.0),1.0);
74}
75`;
76
77export default function DarkVeil({
78  hueShift = 0,
79  noiseIntensity = 0,
80  scanlineIntensity = 0,
81  speed = 0.5,
82  scanlineFrequency = 0,
83  warpAmount = 0,
84  resolutionScale = 1
85}) {
86  const ref = useRef(null);
87  useEffect(() => {
88    const canvas = ref.current;
89    const parent = canvas.parentElement;
90
91    const renderer = new Renderer({
92      dpr: Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2),
93      canvas
94    });
95
96    const gl = renderer.gl;
97    const geometry = new Triangle(gl);
98
99    const program = new Program(gl, {
100      vertex,
101      fragment,
102      uniforms: {
103        uTime: { value: 0 },
104        uResolution: { value: new Vec2() },
105        uHueShift: { value: hueShift },
106        uNoise: { value: noiseIntensity },
107        uScan: { value: scanlineIntensity },
108        uScanFreq: { value: scanlineFrequency },
109        uWarp: { value: warpAmount }
110      }
111    });
112
113    const mesh = new Mesh(gl, { geometry, program });
114
115    const resize = () => {
116      const w = parent.clientWidth,
117        h = parent.clientHeight;
118      renderer.setSize(w * resolutionScale, h * resolutionScale);
119      program.uniforms.uResolution.value.set(w, h);
120    };
121
122    window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
123    resize();
124
125    const start = performance.now();
126    let frame = 0;
127
128    const loop = () => {
129      program.uniforms.uTime.value = ((performance.now() - start) / 1000) * speed;
130      program.uniforms.uHueShift.value = hueShift;
131      program.uniforms.uNoise.value = noiseIntensity;
132      program.uniforms.uScan.value = scanlineIntensity;
133      program.uniforms.uScanFreq.value = scanlineFrequency;
134      program.uniforms.uWarp.value = warpAmount;
135      renderer.render({ scene: mesh });
136      frame = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
137    };
138
139    loop();
140
141    return () => {
142      cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
143      window.removeEventListener('resize', resize);
144    };
145  }, [hueShift, noiseIntensity, scanlineIntensity, speed, scanlineFrequency, warpAmount, resolutionScale]);
146  return <canvas ref={ref} className="darkveil-canvas" />;
147}
148

Extra Config/Code:

2  width: 100%;
3  height: 100%;
4  display: block;
5}

Component: Silk

Installation:

Usage:

Code:
1npm install three @react-three/fiber

Extra Config/Code:
1/* eslint-disable react/no-unknown-property */
2import { Canvas, useFrame, useThree } from '@react-three/fiber';
3import { forwardRef, useRef, useMemo, useLayoutEffect } from 'react';
4import { Color } from 'three';
5
6const hexToNormalizedRGB = hex => {
7  hex = hex.replace('#', '');
8  return [
9    parseInt(hex.slice(0, 2), 16) / 255,
10    parseInt(hex.slice(2, 4), 16) / 255,
11    parseInt(hex.slice(4, 6), 16) / 255
12  ];
13};
14
15const vertexShader = `
16varying vec2 vUv;
17varying vec3 vPosition;
18
19void main() {
20  vPosition = position;
21  vUv = uv;
22  gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);
23}
24`;
25
26const fragmentShader = `
27varying vec2 vUv;
28varying vec3 vPosition;
29
30uniform float uTime;
31uniform vec3  uColor;
32uniform float uSpeed;
33uniform float uScale;
34uniform float uRotation;
35uniform float uNoiseIntensity;
36
37const float e = 2.71828182845904523536;
38
39float noise(vec2 texCoord) {
40  float G = e;
41  vec2  r = (G * sin(G * texCoord));
42  return fract(r.x * r.y * (1.0 + texCoord.x));
43}
44
45vec2 rotateUvs(vec2 uv, float angle) {
46  float c = cos(angle);
47  float s = sin(angle);
48  mat2  rot = mat2(c, -s, s, c);
49  return rot * uv;
50}
51
52void main() {
53  float rnd        = noise(gl_FragCoord.xy);
54  vec2  uv         = rotateUvs(vUv * uScale, uRotation);
55  vec2  tex        = uv * uScale;
56  float tOffset    = uSpeed * uTime;
57
58  tex.y += 0.03 * sin(8.0 * tex.x - tOffset);
59
60  float pattern = 0.6 +
61                  0.4 * sin(5.0 * (tex.x + tex.y +
62                                   cos(3.0 * tex.x + 5.0 * tex.y) +
63                                   0.02 * tOffset) +
64                           sin(20.0 * (tex.x + tex.y - 0.1 * tOffset)));
65
66  vec4 col = vec4(uColor, 1.0) * vec4(pattern) - rnd / 15.0 * uNoiseIntensity;
67  col.a = 1.0;
68  gl_FragColor = col;
69}
70`;
71
72const SilkPlane = forwardRef(function SilkPlane({ uniforms }, ref) {
73  const { viewport } = useThree();
74
75  useLayoutEffect(() => {
76    if (ref.current) {
77      ref.current.scale.set(viewport.width, viewport.height, 1);
78    }
79  }, [ref, viewport]);
80
81  useFrame((_, delta) => {
82    ref.current.material.uniforms.uTime.value += 0.1 * delta;
83  });
84
85  return (
86    <mesh ref={ref}>
87      <planeGeometry args={[1, 1, 1, 1]} />
88      <shaderMaterial uniforms={uniforms} vertexShader={vertexShader} fragmentShader={fragmentShader} />
89    </mesh>
90  );
91});
92SilkPlane.displayName = 'SilkPlane';
93
94const Silk = ({ speed = 5, scale = 1, color = '#7B7481', noiseIntensity = 1.5, rotation = 0 }) => {
95  const meshRef = useRef();
96
97  const uniforms = useMemo(
98    () => ({
99      uSpeed: { value: speed },
100      uScale: { value: scale },
101      uNoiseIntensity: { value: noiseIntensity },
102      uColor: { value: new Color(...hexToNormalizedRGB(color)) },
103      uRotation: { value: rotation },
104      uTime: { value: 0 }
105    }),
106    [speed, scale, noiseIntensity, color, rotation]
107  );
108
109  return (
110    <Canvas dpr={[1, 2]} frameloop="always">
111      <SilkPlane ref={meshRef} uniforms={uniforms} />
112    </Canvas>
113  );
114};
115
116export default Silk;

Component: Light Rays

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/LightRays-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import LightRays from './LightRays';
2
3<div style={{ width: '100%', height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>
4  <LightRays
5    raysOrigin="top-center"
6    raysColor="#ffffff"
7    raysSpeed={1}
8    lightSpread={0.5}
9    rayLength={3}
10    followMouse={true}
11    mouseInfluence={0.1}
12    noiseAmount={0}
13    distortion={0}
14    className="custom-rays"
15    pulsating={false}
16    fadeDistance={1}
17    saturation={1}
18/>
19</div>

Code:
1import { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
2import { Renderer, Program, Triangle, Mesh } from 'ogl';
3import './LightRays.css';
4
5const DEFAULT_COLOR = '#ffffff';
6
7const hexToRgb = hex => {
8  const m = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(hex);
9  return m ? [parseInt(m[1], 16) / 255, parseInt(m[2], 16) / 255, parseInt(m[3], 16) / 255] : [1, 1, 1];
10};
11
12const getAnchorAndDir = (origin, w, h) => {
13  const outside = 0.2;
14  switch (origin) {
15    case 'top-left':
16      return { anchor: [0, -outside * h], dir: [0, 1] };
17    case 'top-right':
18      return { anchor: [w, -outside * h], dir: [0, 1] };
19    case 'left':
20      return { anchor: [-outside * w, 0.5 * h], dir: [1, 0] };
21    case 'right':
22      return { anchor: [(1 + outside) * w, 0.5 * h], dir: [-1, 0] };
23    case 'bottom-left':
24      return { anchor: [0, (1 + outside) * h], dir: [0, -1] };
25    case 'bottom-center':
26      return { anchor: [0.5 * w, (1 + outside) * h], dir: [0, -1] };
27    case 'bottom-right':
28      return { anchor: [w, (1 + outside) * h], dir: [0, -1] };
29    default: // "top-center"
30      return { anchor: [0.5 * w, -outside * h], dir: [0, 1] };
31  }
32};
33
34const LightRays = ({
35  raysOrigin = 'top-center',
36  raysColor = DEFAULT_COLOR,
37  raysSpeed = 1,
38  lightSpread = 1,
39  rayLength = 2,
40  pulsating = false,
41  fadeDistance = 1.0,
42  saturation = 1.0,
43  followMouse = true,
44  mouseInfluence = 0.1,
45  noiseAmount = 0.0,
46  distortion = 0.0,
47  className = ''
48}) => {
49  const containerRef = useRef(null);
50  const uniformsRef = useRef(null);
51  const rendererRef = useRef(null);
52  const mouseRef = useRef({ x: 0.5, y: 0.5 });
53  const smoothMouseRef = useRef({ x: 0.5, y: 0.5 });
54  const animationIdRef = useRef(null);
55  const meshRef = useRef(null);
56  const cleanupFunctionRef = useRef(null);
57  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
58  const observerRef = useRef(null);
59
60  useEffect(() => {
61    if (!containerRef.current) return;
62
63    observerRef.current = new IntersectionObserver(
64      entries => {
65        const entry = entries[0];
66        setIsVisible(entry.isIntersecting);
67      },
68      { threshold: 0.1 }
69    );
70
71    observerRef.current.observe(containerRef.current);
72
73    return () => {
74      if (observerRef.current) {
75        observerRef.current.disconnect();
76        observerRef.current = null;
77      }
78    };
79  }, []);
80
81  useEffect(() => {
82    if (!isVisible || !containerRef.current) return;
83
84    if (cleanupFunctionRef.current) {
85      cleanupFunctionRef.current();
86      cleanupFunctionRef.current = null;
87    }
88
89    const initializeWebGL = async () => {
90      if (!containerRef.current) return;
91
92      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10));
93
94      if (!containerRef.current) return;
95
96      const renderer = new Renderer({
97        dpr: Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2),
98        alpha: true
99      });
100      rendererRef.current = renderer;
101
102      const gl = renderer.gl;
103      gl.canvas.style.width = '100%';
104      gl.canvas.style.height = '100%';
105
106      while (containerRef.current.firstChild) {
107        containerRef.current.removeChild(containerRef.current.firstChild);
108      }
109      containerRef.current.appendChild(gl.canvas);
110
111      const vert = `
112attribute vec2 position;
113varying vec2 vUv;
114void main() {
115  vUv = position * 0.5 + 0.5;
116  gl_Position = vec4(position, 0.0, 1.0);
117}`;
118
119      const frag = `precision highp float;
120
121uniform float iTime;
122uniform vec2  iResolution;
123
124uniform vec2  rayPos;
125uniform vec2  rayDir;
126uniform vec3  raysColor;
127uniform float raysSpeed;
128uniform float lightSpread;
129uniform float rayLength;
130uniform float pulsating;
131uniform float fadeDistance;
132uniform float saturation;
133uniform vec2  mousePos;
134uniform float mouseInfluence;
135uniform float noiseAmount;
136uniform float distortion;
137
138varying vec2 vUv;
139
140float noise(vec2 st) {
141  return fract(sin(dot(st.xy, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453123);
142}
143
144float rayStrength(vec2 raySource, vec2 rayRefDirection, vec2 coord,
145                  float seedA, float seedB, float speed) {
146  vec2 sourceToCoord = coord - raySource;
147  vec2 dirNorm = normalize(sourceToCoord);
148  float cosAngle = dot(dirNorm, rayRefDirection);
149
150  float distortedAngle = cosAngle + distortion * sin(iTime * 2.0 + length(sourceToCoord) * 0.01) * 0.2;
151  
152  float spreadFactor = pow(max(distortedAngle, 0.0), 1.0 / max(lightSpread, 0.001));
153
154  float distance = length(sourceToCoord);
155  float maxDistance = iResolution.x * rayLength;
156  float lengthFalloff = clamp((maxDistance - distance) / maxDistance, 0.0, 1.0);
157  
158  float fadeFalloff = clamp((iResolution.x * fadeDistance - distance) / (iResolution.x * fadeDistance), 0.5, 1.0);
159  float pulse = pulsating > 0.5 ? (0.8 + 0.2 * sin(iTime * speed * 3.0)) : 1.0;
160
161  float baseStrength = clamp(
162    (0.45 + 0.15 * sin(distortedAngle * seedA + iTime * speed)) +
163    (0.3 + 0.2 * cos(-distortedAngle * seedB + iTime * speed)),
164    0.0, 1.0
165  );
166
167  return baseStrength * lengthFalloff * fadeFalloff * spreadFactor * pulse;
168}
169
170void mainImage(out vec4 fragColor, in vec2 fragCoord) {
171  vec2 coord = vec2(fragCoord.x, iResolution.y - fragCoord.y);
172  
173  vec2 finalRayDir = rayDir;
174  if (mouseInfluence > 0.0) {
175    vec2 mouseScreenPos = mousePos * iResolution.xy;
176    vec2 mouseDirection = normalize(mouseScreenPos - rayPos);
177    finalRayDir = normalize(mix(rayDir, mouseDirection, mouseInfluence));
178  }
179
180  vec4 rays1 = vec4(1.0) *
181               rayStrength(rayPos, finalRayDir, coord, 36.2214, 21.11349,
182                           1.5 * raysSpeed);
183  vec4 rays2 = vec4(1.0) *
184               rayStrength(rayPos, finalRayDir, coord, 22.3991, 18.0234,
185                           1.1 * raysSpeed);
186
187  fragColor = rays1 * 0.5 + rays2 * 0.4;
188
189  if (noiseAmount > 0.0) {
190    float n = noise(coord * 0.01 + iTime * 0.1);
191    fragColor.rgb *= (1.0 - noiseAmount + noiseAmount * n);
192  }
193
194  float brightness = 1.0 - (coord.y / iResolution.y);
195  fragColor.x *= 0.1 + brightness * 0.8;
196  fragColor.y *= 0.3 + brightness * 0.6;
197  fragColor.z *= 0.5 + brightness * 0.5;
198
199  if (saturation != 1.0) {
200    float gray = dot(fragColor.rgb, vec3(0.299, 0.587, 0.114));
201    fragColor.rgb = mix(vec3(gray), fragColor.rgb, saturation);
202  }
203
204  fragColor.rgb *= raysColor;
205}
206
207void main() {
208  vec4 color;
209  mainImage(color, gl_FragCoord.xy);
210  gl_FragColor  = color;
211}`;
212
213      const uniforms = {
214        iTime: { value: 0 },
215        iResolution: { value: [1, 1] },
216
217        rayPos: { value: [0, 0] },
218        rayDir: { value: [0, 1] },
219
220        raysColor: { value: hexToRgb(raysColor) },
221        raysSpeed: { value: raysSpeed },
222        lightSpread: { value: lightSpread },
223        rayLength: { value: rayLength },
224        pulsating: { value: pulsating ? 1.0 : 0.0 },
225        fadeDistance: { value: fadeDistance },
226        saturation: { value: saturation },
227        mousePos: { value: [0.5, 0.5] },
228        mouseInfluence: { value: mouseInfluence },
229        noiseAmount: { value: noiseAmount },
230        distortion: { value: distortion }
231      };
232      uniformsRef.current = uniforms;
233
234      const geometry = new Triangle(gl);
235      const program = new Program(gl, {
236        vertex: vert,
237        fragment: frag,
238        uniforms
239      });
240      const mesh = new Mesh(gl, { geometry, program });
241      meshRef.current = mesh;
242
243      const updatePlacement = () => {
244        if (!containerRef.current || !renderer) return;
245
246        renderer.dpr = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2);
247
248        const { clientWidth: wCSS, clientHeight: hCSS } = containerRef.current;
249        renderer.setSize(wCSS, hCSS);
250
251        const dpr = renderer.dpr;
252        const w = wCSS * dpr;
253        const h = hCSS * dpr;
254
255        uniforms.iResolution.value = [w, h];
256
257        const { anchor, dir } = getAnchorAndDir(raysOrigin, w, h);
258        uniforms.rayPos.value = anchor;
259        uniforms.rayDir.value = dir;
260      };
261
262      const loop = t => {
263        if (!rendererRef.current || !uniformsRef.current || !meshRef.current) {
264          return;
265        }
266
267        uniforms.iTime.value = t * 0.001;
268
269        if (followMouse && mouseInfluence > 0.0) {
270          const smoothing = 0.92;
271
272          smoothMouseRef.current.x = smoothMouseRef.current.x * smoothing + mouseRef.current.x * (1 - smoothing);
273          smoothMouseRef.current.y = smoothMouseRef.current.y * smoothing + mouseRef.current.y * (1 - smoothing);
274
275          uniforms.mousePos.value = [smoothMouseRef.current.x, smoothMouseRef.current.y];
276        }
277
278        try {
279          renderer.render({ scene: mesh });
280          animationIdRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
281        } catch (error) {
282          console.warn('WebGL rendering error:', error);
283          return;
284        }
285      };
286
287      window.addEventListener('resize', updatePlacement);
288      updatePlacement();
289      animationIdRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
290
291      cleanupFunctionRef.current = () => {
292        if (animationIdRef.current) {
293          cancelAnimationFrame(animationIdRef.current);
294          animationIdRef.current = null;
295        }
296
297        window.removeEventListener('resize', updatePlacement);
298
299        if (renderer) {
300          try {
301            const canvas = renderer.gl.canvas;
302            const loseContextExt = renderer.gl.getExtension('WEBGL_lose_context');
303            if (loseContextExt) {
304              loseContextExt.loseContext();
305            }
306
307            if (canvas && canvas.parentNode) {
308              canvas.parentNode.removeChild(canvas);
309            }
310          } catch (error) {
311            console.warn('Error during WebGL cleanup:', error);
312          }
313        }
314
315        rendererRef.current = null;
316        uniformsRef.current = null;
317        meshRef.current = null;
318      };
319    };
320
321    initializeWebGL();
322
323    return () => {
324      if (cleanupFunctionRef.current) {
325        cleanupFunctionRef.current();
326        cleanupFunctionRef.current = null;
327      }
328    };
329  }, [
330    isVisible,
331    raysOrigin,
332    raysColor,
333    raysSpeed,
334    lightSpread,
335    rayLength,
336    pulsating,
337    fadeDistance,
338    saturation,
339    followMouse,
340    mouseInfluence,
341    noiseAmount,
342    distortion
343  ]);
344
345  useEffect(() => {
346    if (!uniformsRef.current || !containerRef.current || !rendererRef.current) return;
347
348    const u = uniformsRef.current;
349    const renderer = rendererRef.current;
350
351    u.raysColor.value = hexToRgb(raysColor);
352    u.raysSpeed.value = raysSpeed;
353    u.lightSpread.value = lightSpread;
354    u.rayLength.value = rayLength;
355    u.pulsating.value = pulsating ? 1.0 : 0.0;
356    u.fadeDistance.value = fadeDistance;
357    u.saturation.value = saturation;
358    u.mouseInfluence.value = mouseInfluence;
359    u.noiseAmount.value = noiseAmount;
360    u.distortion.value = distortion;
361
362    const { clientWidth: wCSS, clientHeight: hCSS } = containerRef.current;
363    const dpr = renderer.dpr;
364    const { anchor, dir } = getAnchorAndDir(raysOrigin, wCSS * dpr, hCSS * dpr);
365    u.rayPos.value = anchor;
366    u.rayDir.value = dir;
367  }, [
368    raysColor,
369    raysSpeed,
370    lightSpread,
371    raysOrigin,
372    rayLength,
373    pulsating,
374    fadeDistance,
375    saturation,
376    mouseInfluence,
377    noiseAmount,
378    distortion
379  ]);
380
381  useEffect(() => {
382    const handleMouseMove = e => {
383      if (!containerRef.current || !rendererRef.current) return;
384      const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
385      const x = (e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width;
386      const y = (e.clientY - rect.top) / rect.height;
387      mouseRef.current = { x, y };
388    };
389
390    if (followMouse) {
391      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
392      return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
393    }
394  }, [followMouse]);
395
396  return <div ref={containerRef} className={`light-rays-container ${className}`.trim()} />;
397};
398
399export default LightRays;

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Pixel Blast

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/PixelBlast-JS-CSS

Usage:
1// Component inspired by github.com/zavalit/bayer-dithering-webgl-demo
2  
3import PixelBlast from './PixelBlast';
4
5<div style={{ width: '100%', height: '600px', position: 'relative' }}>

7    variant="square"
8    pixelSize={4}

11    patternDensity={1}

17    liquid={false}

19    liquidRadius={1.2}
20    liquidWobbleSpeed={5}

22    edgeFade={0.25}

24  />

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import * as THREE from 'three';
3import { EffectComposer, EffectPass, RenderPass, Effect } from 'postprocessing';
4import './PixelBlast.css';
5
6const createTouchTexture = () => {
7  const size = 64;
8  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
9  canvas.width = size;
10  canvas.height = size;
11  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
12  if (!ctx) throw new Error('2D context not available');
13  ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
14  ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
15  const texture = new THREE.Texture(canvas);
16  texture.minFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
17  texture.magFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
18  texture.generateMipmaps = false;
19  const trail = [];
20  let last = null;
21  const maxAge = 64;
22  let radius = 0.1 * size;
23  const speed = 1 / maxAge;
24  const clear = () => {
25    ctx.fillStyle = 'black';
26    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
27  };
28  const drawPoint = p => {
29    const pos = { x: p.x * size, y: (1 - p.y) * size };
30    let intensity = 1;
31    const easeOutSine = t => Math.sin((t * Math.PI) / 2);
32    const easeOutQuad = t => -t * (t - 2);
33    if (p.age < maxAge * 0.3) intensity = easeOutSine(p.age / (maxAge * 0.3));
34    else intensity = easeOutQuad(1 - (p.age - maxAge * 0.3) / (maxAge * 0.7)) || 0;
35    intensity *= p.force;
36    const color = `${((p.vx + 1) / 2) * 255}, ${((p.vy + 1) / 2) * 255}, ${intensity * 255}`;
37    const offset = size * 5;
38    ctx.shadowOffsetX = offset;
39    ctx.shadowOffsetY = offset;
40    ctx.shadowBlur = radius;
41    ctx.shadowColor = `rgba(${color},${0.22 * intensity})`;
42    ctx.beginPath();
43    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,0,0,1)';
44    ctx.arc(pos.x - offset, pos.y - offset, radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
45    ctx.fill();
46  };
47  const addTouch = norm => {
48    let force = 0;
49    let vx = 0;
50    let vy = 0;
51    if (last) {
52      const dx = norm.x - last.x;
53      const dy = norm.y - last.y;
54      if (dx === 0 && dy === 0) return;
55      const dd = dx * dx + dy * dy;
56      const d = Math.sqrt(dd);
57      vx = dx / (d || 1);
58      vy = dy / (d || 1);
59      force = Math.min(dd * 10000, 1);
60    }
61    last = { x: norm.x, y: norm.y };
62    trail.push({ x: norm.x, y: norm.y, age: 0, force, vx, vy });
63  };
64  const update = () => {
65    clear();
66    for (let i = trail.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
67      const point = trail[i];
68      const f = point.force * speed * (1 - point.age / maxAge);
69      point.x += point.vx * f;
70      point.y += point.vy * f;
71      point.age++;
72      if (point.age > maxAge) trail.splice(i, 1);
73    }
74    for (let i = 0; i < trail.length; i++) drawPoint(trail[i]);
75    texture.needsUpdate = true;
76  };
77  return {
78    canvas,
79    texture,
80    addTouch,
81    update,
82    set radiusScale(v) {
83      radius = 0.1 * size * v;
84    },
85    get radiusScale() {
86      return radius / (0.1 * size);
87    },
88    size
89  };
90};
91
92const createLiquidEffect = (texture, opts) => {
93  const fragment = `
94    uniform sampler2D uTexture;
95    uniform float uStrength;
96    uniform float uTime;
97    uniform float uFreq;
98
99    void mainUv(inout vec2 uv) {
100      vec4 tex = texture2D(uTexture, uv);
101      float vx = tex.r * 2.0 - 1.0;
102      float vy = tex.g * 2.0 - 1.0;
103      float intensity = tex.b;
104
105      float wave = 0.5 + 0.5 * sin(uTime * uFreq + intensity * 6.2831853);
106
107      float amt = uStrength * intensity * wave;
108
109      uv += vec2(vx, vy) * amt;
110    }
111    `;
112  return new Effect('LiquidEffect', fragment, {
113    uniforms: new Map([
114      ['uTexture', new THREE.Uniform(texture)],
115      ['uStrength', new THREE.Uniform(opts?.strength ?? 0.025)],
116      ['uTime', new THREE.Uniform(0)],
117      ['uFreq', new THREE.Uniform(opts?.freq ?? 4.5)]
118    ])
119  });
120};
121
122const SHAPE_MAP = {
123  square: 0,
124  circle: 1,
125  triangle: 2,
126  diamond: 3
127};
128
129const VERTEX_SRC = `
130void main() {
131  gl_Position = vec4(position, 1.0);
132}
133`;
134
135const FRAGMENT_SRC = `
136precision highp float;
137
138uniform vec3  uColor;
139uniform vec2  uResolution;
140uniform float uTime;
141uniform float uPixelSize;
142uniform float uScale;
143uniform float uDensity;
144uniform float uPixelJitter;
145uniform int   uEnableRipples;
146uniform float uRippleSpeed;
147uniform float uRippleThickness;
148uniform float uRippleIntensity;
149uniform float uEdgeFade;
150
151uniform int   uShapeType;
152const int SHAPE_SQUARE   = 0;
153const int SHAPE_CIRCLE   = 1;
154const int SHAPE_TRIANGLE = 2;
155const int SHAPE_DIAMOND  = 3;
156
157const int   MAX_CLICKS = 10;
158
159uniform vec2  uClickPos  [MAX_CLICKS];
160uniform float uClickTimes[MAX_CLICKS];
161
162out vec4 fragColor;
163
164float Bayer2(vec2 a) {
165  a = floor(a);
166  return fract(a.x / 2. + a.y * a.y * .75);
167}
168#define Bayer4(a) (Bayer2(.5*(a))*0.25 + Bayer2(a))
169#define Bayer8(a) (Bayer4(.5*(a))*0.25 + Bayer2(a))
170
171#define FBM_OCTAVES     5
172#define FBM_LACUNARITY  1.25
173#define FBM_GAIN        1.0
174
175float hash11(float n){ return fract(sin(n)*43758.5453); }
176
177float vnoise(vec3 p){
178  vec3 ip = floor(p);
179  vec3 fp = fract(p);
180  float n000 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(0.0,0.0,0.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
181  float n100 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(1.0,0.0,0.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
182  float n010 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(0.0,1.0,0.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
183  float n110 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(1.0,1.0,0.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
184  float n001 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(0.0,0.0,1.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
185  float n101 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(1.0,0.0,1.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
186  float n011 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(0.0,1.0,1.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
187  float n111 = hash11(dot(ip + vec3(1.0,1.0,1.0), vec3(1.0,57.0,113.0)));
188  vec3 w = fp*fp*fp*(fp*(fp*6.0-15.0)+10.0);
189  float x00 = mix(n000, n100, w.x);
190  float x10 = mix(n010, n110, w.x);
191  float x01 = mix(n001, n101, w.x);
192  float x11 = mix(n011, n111, w.x);
193  float y0  = mix(x00, x10, w.y);
194  float y1  = mix(x01, x11, w.y);
195  return mix(y0, y1, w.z) * 2.0 - 1.0;
196}
197
198float fbm2(vec2 uv, float t){
199  vec3 p = vec3(uv * uScale, t);
200  float amp = 1.0;
201  float freq = 1.0;
202  float sum = 1.0;
203  for (int i = 0; i < FBM_OCTAVES; ++i){
204    sum  += amp * vnoise(p * freq);
205    freq *= FBM_LACUNARITY;
206    amp  *= FBM_GAIN;
207  }
208  return sum * 0.5 + 0.5;
209}
210
211float maskCircle(vec2 p, float cov){
212  float r = sqrt(cov) * .25;
213  float d = length(p - 0.5) - r;
214  float aa = 0.5 * fwidth(d);
215  return cov * (1.0 - smoothstep(-aa, aa, d * 2.0));
216}
217
218float maskTriangle(vec2 p, vec2 id, float cov){
219  bool flip = mod(id.x + id.y, 2.0) > 0.5;
220  if (flip) p.x = 1.0 - p.x;
221  float r = sqrt(cov);
222  float d  = p.y - r*(1.0 - p.x);
223  float aa = fwidth(d);
224  return cov * clamp(0.5 - d/aa, 0.0, 1.0);
225}
226
227float maskDiamond(vec2 p, float cov){
228  float r = sqrt(cov) * 0.564;
229  return step(abs(p.x - 0.49) + abs(p.y - 0.49), r);
230}
231
232void main(){
233  float pixelSize = uPixelSize;
234  vec2 fragCoord = gl_FragCoord.xy - uResolution * .5;
235  float aspectRatio = uResolution.x / uResolution.y;
236
237  vec2 pixelId = floor(fragCoord / pixelSize);
238  vec2 pixelUV = fract(fragCoord / pixelSize);
239
240  float cellPixelSize = 8.0 * pixelSize;
241  vec2 cellId = floor(fragCoord / cellPixelSize);
242  vec2 cellCoord = cellId * cellPixelSize;
243  vec2 uv = cellCoord / uResolution * vec2(aspectRatio, 1.0);
244
245  float base = fbm2(uv, uTime * 0.05);
246  base = base * 0.5 - 0.65;
247
248  float feed = base + (uDensity - 0.5) * 0.3;
249
250  float speed     = uRippleSpeed;
251  float thickness = uRippleThickness;
252  const float dampT     = 1.0;
253  const float dampR     = 10.0;
254
255  if (uEnableRipples == 1) {
256    for (int i = 0; i < MAX_CLICKS; ++i){
257      vec2 pos = uClickPos[i];
258      if (pos.x < 0.0) continue;
259      float cellPixelSize = 8.0 * pixelSize;
260      vec2 cuv = (((pos - uResolution * .5 - cellPixelSize * .5) / (uResolution))) * vec2(aspectRatio, 1.0);
261      float t = max(uTime - uClickTimes[i], 0.0);
262      float r = distance(uv, cuv);
263      float waveR = speed * t;
264      float ring  = exp(-pow((r - waveR) / thickness, 2.0));
265      float atten = exp(-dampT * t) * exp(-dampR * r);
266      feed = max(feed, ring * atten * uRippleIntensity);
267    }
268  }
269
270  float bayer = Bayer8(fragCoord / uPixelSize) - 0.5;
271  float bw = step(0.5, feed + bayer);
272
273  float h = fract(sin(dot(floor(fragCoord / uPixelSize), vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453);
274  float jitterScale = 1.0 + (h - 0.5) * uPixelJitter;
275  float coverage = bw * jitterScale;
276  float M;
277  if      (uShapeType == SHAPE_CIRCLE)   M = maskCircle (pixelUV, coverage);
278  else if (uShapeType == SHAPE_TRIANGLE) M = maskTriangle(pixelUV, pixelId, coverage);
279  else if (uShapeType == SHAPE_DIAMOND)  M = maskDiamond(pixelUV, coverage);
280  else                                   M = coverage;
281
282  if (uEdgeFade > 0.0) {
283    vec2 norm = gl_FragCoord.xy / uResolution;
284    float edge = min(min(norm.x, norm.y), min(1.0 - norm.x, 1.0 - norm.y));
285    float fade = smoothstep(0.0, uEdgeFade, edge);
286    M *= fade;
287  }
288
289  vec3 color = uColor;
290
291  // sRGB gamma correction - convert linear to sRGB for accurate color output
292  vec3 srgbColor = mix(
293    color * 12.92,
294    1.055 * pow(color, vec3(1.0 / 2.4)) - 0.055,
295    step(0.0031308, color)
296  );
297
298  fragColor = vec4(srgbColor, M);
299}
300`;
301
302const MAX_CLICKS = 10;
303
304const PixelBlast = ({
305  variant = 'square',
306  pixelSize = 3,
307  color = '#B19EEF',
308  className,
309  style,
310  antialias = true,
311  patternScale = 2,
312  patternDensity = 1,
313  liquid = false,
314  liquidStrength = 0.1,
315  liquidRadius = 1,
316  pixelSizeJitter = 0,
317  enableRipples = true,
318  rippleIntensityScale = 1,
319  rippleThickness = 0.1,
320  rippleSpeed = 0.3,
321  liquidWobbleSpeed = 4.5,
322  autoPauseOffscreen = true,
323  speed = 0.5,
324  transparent = true,
325  edgeFade = 0.5,
326  noiseAmount = 0
327}) => {
328  const containerRef = useRef(null);
329  const visibilityRef = useRef({ visible: true });
330  const speedRef = useRef(speed);
331
332  const threeRef = useRef(null);
333  const prevConfigRef = useRef(null);
334  useEffect(() => {
335    const container = containerRef.current;
336    if (!container) return;
337    speedRef.current = speed;
338    const needsReinitKeys = ['antialias', 'liquid', 'noiseAmount'];
339    const cfg = { antialias, liquid, noiseAmount };
340    let mustReinit = false;
341    if (!threeRef.current) mustReinit = true;
342    else if (prevConfigRef.current) {
343      for (const k of needsReinitKeys)
344        if (prevConfigRef.current[k] !== cfg[k]) {
345          mustReinit = true;
346          break;
347        }
348    }
349    if (mustReinit) {
350      if (threeRef.current) {
351        const t = threeRef.current;
352        t.resizeObserver?.disconnect();
353        cancelAnimationFrame(t.raf);
354        t.quad?.geometry.dispose();
355        t.material.dispose();
356        t.composer?.dispose();
357        t.renderer.dispose();
358        if (t.renderer.domElement.parentElement === container) container.removeChild(t.renderer.domElement);
359        threeRef.current = null;
360      }
361      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
362      const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({
363        canvas,
364        antialias,
365        alpha: true,
366        powerPreference: 'high-performance'
367      });
368      renderer.domElement.style.width = '100%';
369      renderer.domElement.style.height = '100%';
370      renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2));
371      container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);
372      if (transparent) renderer.setClearAlpha(0);
373      else renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, 1);
374      const uniforms = {
375        uResolution: { value: new THREE.Vector2(0, 0) },
376        uTime: { value: 0 },
377        uColor: { value: new THREE.Color(color) },
378        uClickPos: {
379          value: Array.from({ length: MAX_CLICKS }, () => new THREE.Vector2(-1, -1))
380        },
381        uClickTimes: { value: new Float32Array(MAX_CLICKS) },
382        uShapeType: { value: SHAPE_MAP[variant] ?? 0 },
383        uPixelSize: { value: pixelSize * renderer.getPixelRatio() },
384        uScale: { value: patternScale },
385        uDensity: { value: patternDensity },
386        uPixelJitter: { value: pixelSizeJitter },
387        uEnableRipples: { value: enableRipples ? 1 : 0 },
388        uRippleSpeed: { value: rippleSpeed },
389        uRippleThickness: { value: rippleThickness },
390        uRippleIntensity: { value: rippleIntensityScale },
391        uEdgeFade: { value: edgeFade }
392      };
393      const scene = new THREE.Scene();
394      const camera = new THREE.OrthographicCamera(-1, 1, 1, -1, 0, 1);
395      const material = new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
396        vertexShader: VERTEX_SRC,
397        fragmentShader: FRAGMENT_SRC,
398        uniforms,
399        transparent: true,
400        depthTest: false,
401        depthWrite: false,
402        glslVersion: THREE.GLSL3
403      });
404      const quadGeom = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(2, 2);
405      const quad = new THREE.Mesh(quadGeom, material);
406      scene.add(quad);
407      const clock = new THREE.Clock();
408      const setSize = () => {
409        const w = container.clientWidth || 1;
410        const h = container.clientHeight || 1;
411        renderer.setSize(w, h, false);
412        uniforms.uResolution.value.set(renderer.domElement.width, renderer.domElement.height);
413        if (threeRef.current?.composer)
414          threeRef.current.composer.setSize(renderer.domElement.width, renderer.domElement.height);
415        uniforms.uPixelSize.value = pixelSize * renderer.getPixelRatio();
416      };
417      setSize();
418      const ro = new ResizeObserver(setSize);
419      ro.observe(container);
420      const randomFloat = () => {
421        if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.crypto?.getRandomValues) {
422          const u32 = new Uint32Array(1);
423          window.crypto.getRandomValues(u32);
424          return u32[0] / 0xffffffff;
425        }
426        return Math.random();
427      };
428      const timeOffset = randomFloat() * 1000;
429      let composer;
430      let touch;
431      let liquidEffect;
432      if (liquid) {
433        touch = createTouchTexture();
434        touch.radiusScale = liquidRadius;
435        composer = new EffectComposer(renderer);
436        const renderPass = new RenderPass(scene, camera);
437        liquidEffect = createLiquidEffect(touch.texture, {
438          strength: liquidStrength,
439          freq: liquidWobbleSpeed
440        });
441        const effectPass = new EffectPass(camera, liquidEffect);
442        effectPass.renderToScreen = true;
443        composer.addPass(renderPass);
444        composer.addPass(effectPass);
445      }
446      if (noiseAmount > 0) {
447        if (!composer) {
448          composer = new EffectComposer(renderer);
449          composer.addPass(new RenderPass(scene, camera));
450        }
451        const noiseEffect = new Effect(
452          'NoiseEffect',
453          `uniform float uTime; uniform float uAmount; float hash(vec2 p){ return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1,311.7))) * 43758.5453);} void mainUv(inout vec2 uv){} void mainImage(const in vec4 inputColor,const in vec2 uv,out vec4 outputColor){ float n=hash(floor(uv*vec2(1920.0,1080.0))+floor(uTime*60.0)); float g=(n-0.5)*uAmount; outputColor=inputColor+vec4(vec3(g),0.0);} `,
454          {
455            uniforms: new Map([
456              ['uTime', new THREE.Uniform(0)],
457              ['uAmount', new THREE.Uniform(noiseAmount)]
458            ])
459          }
460        );
461        const noisePass = new EffectPass(camera, noiseEffect);
462        noisePass.renderToScreen = true;
463        if (composer && composer.passes.length > 0) composer.passes.forEach(p => (p.renderToScreen = false));
464        composer.addPass(noisePass);
465      }
466      if (composer) composer.setSize(renderer.domElement.width, renderer.domElement.height);
467      const mapToPixels = e => {
468        const rect = renderer.domElement.getBoundingClientRect();
469        const scaleX = renderer.domElement.width / rect.width;
470        const scaleY = renderer.domElement.height / rect.height;
471        const fx = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
472        const fy = (rect.height - (e.clientY - rect.top)) * scaleY;
473        return {
474          fx,
475          fy,
476          w: renderer.domElement.width,
477          h: renderer.domElement.height
478        };
479      };
480      const onPointerDown = e => {
481        const { fx, fy } = mapToPixels(e);
482        const ix = threeRef.current?.clickIx ?? 0;
483        uniforms.uClickPos.value[ix].set(fx, fy);
484        uniforms.uClickTimes.value[ix] = uniforms.uTime.value;
485        if (threeRef.current) threeRef.current.clickIx = (ix + 1) % MAX_CLICKS;
486      };
487      const onPointerMove = e => {
488        if (!touch) return;
489        const { fx, fy, w, h } = mapToPixels(e);
490        touch.addTouch({ x: fx / w, y: fy / h });
491      };
492      renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointerdown', onPointerDown, {
493        passive: true
494      });
495      renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointermove', onPointerMove, {
496        passive: true
497      });
498      let raf = 0;
499      const animate = () => {
500        if (autoPauseOffscreen && !visibilityRef.current.visible) {
501          raf = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
502          return;
503        }
504        uniforms.uTime.value = timeOffset + clock.getElapsedTime() * speedRef.current;
505        if (liquidEffect) liquidEffect.uniforms.get('uTime').value = uniforms.uTime.value;
506        if (composer) {
507          if (touch) touch.update();
508          composer.passes.forEach(p => {
509            const effs = p.effects;
510            if (effs)
511              effs.forEach(eff => {
512                const u = eff.uniforms?.get('uTime');
513                if (u) u.value = uniforms.uTime.value;
514              });
515          });
516          composer.render();
517        } else renderer.render(scene, camera);
518        raf = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
519      };
520      raf = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
521      threeRef.current = {
522        renderer,
523        scene,
524        camera,
525        material,
526        clock,
527        clickIx: 0,
528        uniforms,
529        resizeObserver: ro,
530        raf,
531        quad,
532        timeOffset,
533        composer,
534        touch,
535        liquidEffect
536      };
537    } else {
538      const t = threeRef.current;
539      t.uniforms.uShapeType.value = SHAPE_MAP[variant] ?? 0;
540      t.uniforms.uPixelSize.value = pixelSize * t.renderer.getPixelRatio();
541      t.uniforms.uColor.value.set(color);
542      t.uniforms.uScale.value = patternScale;
543      t.uniforms.uDensity.value = patternDensity;
544      t.uniforms.uPixelJitter.value = pixelSizeJitter;
545      t.uniforms.uEnableRipples.value = enableRipples ? 1 : 0;
546      t.uniforms.uRippleIntensity.value = rippleIntensityScale;
547      t.uniforms.uRippleThickness.value = rippleThickness;
548      t.uniforms.uRippleSpeed.value = rippleSpeed;
549      t.uniforms.uEdgeFade.value = edgeFade;
550      if (transparent) t.renderer.setClearAlpha(0);
551      else t.renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, 1);
552      if (t.liquidEffect) {
553        const uStrength = t.liquidEffect;
554        if (uStrength) uStrength.value = liquidStrength;
555        const uFreq = t.liquidEffect.uniforms.get('uFreq');
556        if (uFreq) uFreq.value = liquidWobbleSpeed;
557      }
558      if (t.touch) t.touch.radiusScale = liquidRadius;
559    }
560    prevConfigRef.current = cfg;
561    return () => {
562      if (threeRef.current && mustReinit) return;
563      if (!threeRef.current) return;
564      const t = threeRef.current;
565      t.resizeObserver?.disconnect();
566      cancelAnimationFrame(t.raf);
567      t.quad?.geometry.dispose();
568      t.material.dispose();
569      t.composer?.dispose();
570      t.renderer.dispose();
571      if (t.renderer.domElement.parentElement === container) container.removeChild(t.renderer.domElement);
572      threeRef.current = null;
573    };
574  }, [
575    antialias,
576    liquid,
577    noiseAmount,
578    pixelSize,
579    patternScale,
580    patternDensity,
581    enableRipples,
582    rippleIntensityScale,
583    rippleThickness,
584    rippleSpeed,
585    pixelSizeJitter,
586    edgeFade,
587    transparent,
588    liquidStrength,
589    liquidRadius,
590    liquidWobbleSpeed,
591    autoPauseOffscreen,
592    variant,
593    color,
594    speed
595  ]);
596
597  return (
598    <div
599      ref={containerRef}
600      className={`pixel-blast-container ${className ?? ''}`}
601      style={style}
602      aria-label="PixelBlast interactive background"
603    />
604  );
605};
606
607export default PixelBlast;
608

Extra Config/Code:
1.pixel-blast-container {
2  width: 100%;
3  height: 100%;
4  position: relative;
5  overflow: hidden;
6}
7

--------------------------------------------------

Component: Color Bends

Installation:
npx shadcn@latest add @react-bits/ColorBends-JS-CSS

Usage:
1import ColorBends from './ColorBends';
2  
3<ColorBends
4  colors={["#ff5c7a", "#8a5cff", "#00ffd1"]}
5  rotation={0}
6  speed={0.2}
7  scale={1}
8  frequency={1}
9  warpStrength={1}
10  mouseInfluence={1}
11  parallax={0.5}
12  noise={0.1}
13  transparent
14  autoRotate={0}
15  color=""
16/>

Code:
1import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2import * as THREE from 'three';
3import './ColorBends.css';
4
5const MAX_COLORS = 8;
6
7const frag = `
8#define MAX_COLORS ${MAX_COLORS}
9uniform vec2 uCanvas;
10uniform float uTime;
11uniform float uSpeed;
12uniform vec2 uRot;
13uniform int uColorCount;
14uniform vec3 uColors[MAX_COLORS];
15uniform int uTransparent;
16uniform float uScale;
17uniform float uFrequency;
18uniform float uWarpStrength;
19uniform vec2 uPointer; // in NDC [-1,1]
20uniform float uMouseInfluence;
21uniform float uParallax;
22uniform float uNoise;
23varying vec2 vUv;
24
25void main() {
26  float t = uTime * uSpeed;
27  vec2 p = vUv * 2.0 - 1.0;
28  p += uPointer * uParallax * 0.1;
29  vec2 rp = vec2(p.x * uRot.x - p.y * uRot.y, p.x * uRot.y + p.y * uRot.x);
30  vec2 q = vec2(rp.x * (uCanvas.x / uCanvas.y), rp.y);
31  q /= max(uScale, 0.0001);
32  q /= 0.5 + 0.2 * dot(q, q);
33  q += 0.2 * cos(t) - 7.56;
34  vec2 toward = (uPointer - rp);
35  q += toward * uMouseInfluence * 0.2;
36
37    vec3 col = vec3(0.0);
38    float a = 1.0;
39
40    if (uColorCount > 0) {
41      vec2 s = q;
42      vec3 sumCol = vec3(0.0);
43      float cover = 0.0;
44      for (int i = 0; i < MAX_COLORS; ++i) {
45            if (i >= uColorCount) break;
46            s -= 0.01;
47            vec2 r = sin(1.5 * (s.yx * uFrequency) + 2.0 * cos(s * uFrequency));
48            float m0 = length(r + sin(5.0 * r.y * uFrequency - 3.0 * t + float(i)) / 4.0);
49            float kBelow = clamp(uWarpStrength, 0.0, 1.0);
50            float kMix = pow(kBelow, 0.3); // strong response across 0..1
51            float gain = 1.0 + max(uWarpStrength - 1.0, 0.0); // allow >1 to amplify displacement
52            vec2 disp = (r - s) * kBelow;
53            vec2 warped = s + disp * gain;
54            float m1 = length(warped + sin(5.0 * warped.y * uFrequency - 3.0 * t + float(i)) / 4.0);
55            float m = mix(m0, m1, kMix);
56            float w = 1.0 - exp(-6.0 / exp(6.0 * m));
57            sumCol += uColors[i] * w;
58            cover = max(cover, w);
59      }
60      col = clamp(sumCol, 0.0, 1.0);
61      a = uTransparent > 0 ? cover : 1.0;
62    } else {
63        vec2 s = q;
64        for (int k = 0; k < 3; ++k) {
65            s -= 0.01;
66            vec2 r = sin(1.5 * (s.yx * uFrequency) + 2.0 * cos(s * uFrequency));
67            float m0 = length(r + sin(5.0 * r.y * uFrequency - 3.0 * t + float(k)) / 4.0);
68            float kBelow = clamp(uWarpStrength, 0.0, 1.0);
69            float kMix = pow(kBelow, 0.3);
70            float gain = 1.0 + max(uWarpStrength - 1.0, 0.0);
71            vec2 disp = (r - s) * kBelow;
72            vec2 warped = s + disp * gain;
73            float m1 = length(warped + sin(5.0 * warped.y * uFrequency - 3.0 * t + float(k)) / 4.0);
74            float m = mix(m0, m1, kMix);
75            col[k] = 1.0 - exp(-6.0 / exp(6.0 * m));
76        }
77        a = uTransparent > 0 ? max(max(col.r, col.g), col.b) : 1.0;
78    }
79
80    if (uNoise > 0.0001) {
81      float n = fract(sin(dot(gl_FragCoord.xy + vec2(uTime), vec2(12.9898, 78.233))) * 43758.5453123);
82      col += (n - 0.5) * uNoise;
83      col = clamp(col, 0.0, 1.0);
84    }
85
86    vec3 rgb = (uTransparent > 0) ? col * a : col;
87    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, a);
88}
89`;
90
91const vert = `
92varying vec2 vUv;
93void main() {
94  vUv = uv;
95  gl_Position = vec4(position, 1.0);
96}
97`;
98
99export default function ColorBends({
100  className,
101  style,
102  rotation = 45,
103  speed = 0.2,
104  colors = [],
105  transparent = true,
106  autoRotate = 0,
107  scale = 1,
108  frequency = 1,
109  warpStrength = 1,
110  mouseInfluence = 1,
111  parallax = 0.5,
112  noise = 0.1
113}) {
114  const containerRef = useRef(null);
115  const rendererRef = useRef(null);
116  const rafRef = useRef(null);
117  const materialRef = useRef(null);
118  const resizeObserverRef = useRef(null);
119  const rotationRef = useRef(rotation);
120  const autoRotateRef = useRef(autoRotate);
121  const pointerTargetRef = useRef(new THREE.Vector2(0, 0));
122  const pointerCurrentRef = useRef(new THREE.Vector2(0, 0));
123  const pointerSmoothRef = useRef(8);
124
125  useEffect(() => {
126    const container = containerRef.current;
127    const scene = new THREE.Scene();
128    const camera = new THREE.OrthographicCamera(-1, 1, 1, -1, 0, 1);
129
130    const geometry = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(2, 2);
131    const uColorsArray = Array.from({ length: MAX_COLORS }, () => new THREE.Vector3(0, 0, 0));
132    const material = new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
133      vertexShader: vert,
134      fragmentShader: frag,
135      uniforms: {
136        uCanvas: { value: new THREE.Vector2(1, 1) },
137        uTime: { value: 0 },
138        uSpeed: { value: speed },
139        uRot: { value: new THREE.Vector2(1, 0) },
140        uColorCount: { value: 0 },
141        uColors: { value: uColorsArray },
142        uTransparent: { value: transparent ? 1 : 0 },
143        uScale: { value: scale },
144        uFrequency: { value: frequency },
145        uWarpStrength: { value: warpStrength },
146        uPointer: { value: new THREE.Vector2(0, 0) },
147        uMouseInfluence: { value: mouseInfluence },
148        uParallax: { value: parallax },
149        uNoise: { value: noise }
150      },
151      premultipliedAlpha: true,
152      transparent: true
153    });
154    materialRef.current = material;
155
156    const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
157    scene.add(mesh);
158
159    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({
160      antialias: false,
161      powerPreference: 'high-performance',
162      alpha: true
163    });
164    rendererRef.current = renderer;
165    renderer.outputColorSpace = THREE.SRGBColorSpace;
166    renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2));
167    renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, transparent ? 0 : 1);
168    renderer.domElement.style.width = '100%';
169    renderer.domElement.style.height = '100%';
170    renderer.domElement.style.display = 'block';
171    container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);
172
173    const clock = new THREE.Clock();
174
175    const handleResize = () => {
176      const w = container.clientWidth || 1;
177      const h = container.clientHeight || 1;
178      renderer.setSize(w, h, false);
179      material.uniforms.uCanvas.value.set(w, h);
180    };
181
182    handleResize();
183
184    if ('ResizeObserver' in window) {
185      const ro = new ResizeObserver(handleResize);
186      ro.observe(container);
187      resizeObserverRef.current = ro;
188    } else {
189      window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
190    }
191
192    const loop = () => {
193      const dt = clock.getDelta();
194      const elapsed = clock.elapsedTime;
195      material.uniforms.uTime.value = elapsed;
196
197      const deg = (rotationRef.current % 360) + autoRotateRef.current * elapsed;
198      const rad = (deg * Math.PI) / 180;
199      const c = Math.cos(rad);
200      const s = Math.sin(rad);
201      material.uniforms.uRot.value.set(c, s);
202
203      const cur = pointerCurrentRef.current;
204      const tgt = pointerTargetRef.current;
205      const amt = Math.min(1, dt * pointerSmoothRef.current);
206      cur.lerp(tgt, amt);
207      material.uniforms.uPointer.value.copy(cur);
208      renderer.render(scene, camera);
209      rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
210    };
211    rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(loop);
212
213    return () => {
214      if (rafRef.current !== null) cancelAnimationFrame(rafRef.current);
215      if (resizeObserverRef.current) resizeObserverRef.current.disconnect();
216      else window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
217      geometry.dispose();
218      material.dispose();
219      renderer.dispose();
220      if (renderer.domElement && renderer.domElement.parentElement === container) {
221        container.removeChild(renderer.domElement);
222      }
223    };
224  }, [frequency, mouseInfluence, noise, parallax, scale, speed, transparent, warpStrength]);
225
226  useEffect(() => {
227    const material = materialRef.current;
228    const renderer = rendererRef.current;
229    if (!material) return;
230
231    rotationRef.current = rotation;
232    autoRotateRef.current = autoRotate;
233    material.uniforms.uSpeed.value = speed;
234    material.uniforms.uScale.value = scale;
235    material.uniforms.uFrequency.value = frequency;
236    material.uniforms.uWarpStrength.value = warpStrength;
237    material.uniforms.uMouseInfluence.value = mouseInfluence;
238    material.uniforms.uParallax.value = parallax;
239    material.uniforms.uNoise.value = noise;
240
241    const toVec3 = hex => {
242      const h = hex.replace('#', '').trim();
243      const v =
244        h.length === 3
245          ? [parseInt(h[0] + h[0], 16), parseInt(h[1] + h[1], 16), parseInt(h[2] + h[2], 16)]
246          : [parseInt(h.slice(0, 2), 16), parseInt(h.slice(2, 4), 16), parseInt(h.slice(4, 6), 16)];
247      return new THREE.Vector3(v[0] / 255, v[1] / 255, v[2] / 255);
248    };
249
250    const arr = (colors || []).filter(Boolean).slice(0, MAX_COLORS).map(toVec3);
251    for (let i = 0; i < MAX_COLORS; i++) {
252      const vec = material.uniforms.uColors.value[i];
253      if (i < arr.length) vec.copy(arr[i]);
254      else vec.set(0, 0, 0);
255    }
256    material.uniforms.uColorCount.value = arr.length;
257
258    material.uniforms.uTransparent.value = transparent ? 1 : 0;
259    if (renderer) renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, transparent ? 0 : 1);
260  }, [
261    rotation,
262    autoRotate,
263    speed,
264    scale,
265    frequency,
266    warpStrength,
267    mouseInfluence,
268    parallax,
269    noise,
270    colors,
271    transparent
272  ]);
273
274  useEffect(() => {
275    const material = materialRef.current;
276    const container = containerRef.current;
277    if (!material || !container) return;
278
279    const handlePointerMove = e => {
280      const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
281      const x = ((e.clientX - rect.left) / (rect.width || 1)) * 2 - 1;
282      const y = -(((e.clientY - rect.top) / (rect.height || 1)) * 2 - 1);
283      pointerTargetRef.current.set(x, y);
284    };
285
286    container.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
287    return () => {
288      container.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
289    };
290  }, []);
291
292  return <div ref={containerRef} className={`color-bends-container ${className}`} style={style} />;
293}
294

2  position: relative;
3  width: 100%;
4  height: 100%;
5  overflow: hidden;
6}
